### B396 вАФ Dependency connectors: keep the CURVE, bind it to the bars (revert B395's orthogonal elbow) `[Scheduler / Gantt]` (bug)  *(owner feedback right after B395 shipped: "the serpentine things were fine, i preferred those, revert, the issue was just that they weren't bound to anything")*
`[x]` **Fixed + headless-verified + shipped the SAME session per STANDING RULE #1 (branch `claude/zen-ramanujan-14sak9`).** B395 had replaced the curved (cubic-b√©zier) dependency connectors with orthogonal elbows вАФ but the owner preferred the curves; the real defect was that the connectors **floated at the row's vertical mid-line** while the on-screen bars sit at the **bottom** of the row, so a curve looked unbound (it left from / arrived at empty space above the bar).
- **Reverted to the curved b√©zier** in both render paths (`GanttView` `depLines` render + `buildGanttSVG`); removed the `depElbow`/`depElbowD`/`DEP_DIRS` elbow router entirely.
- **The actual fix вАФ bind to the bar:** each endpoint's **y is now the bar's true vertical center per kind** (`depYCenter` in `GanttView`; `ycOf` in `buildGanttSVG`) вАФ leaf bars at the row bottom, summaries on their span, milestones on the diamond вАФ instead of the old `ROW_H/2` row-center. So a curve now cleanly leaves the predecessor bar and enters the successor bar. x still anchors to the correct bar edge per type (FS/SS/FF/SF); arrowhead direction by `x2вЙ•x1`. Pure geometry from the row index, so off-screen virtualized rows still compute.
- **Supersedes B395's visual** (the elbow); keeps the SS color `#7c3aed`, dashed `4 3`, layer order (z3, under bars), and the blank-date guard (`verify-unscheduled-deps` still 1/1, no phantom NaN).
- **Verified:** build green ¬Ј JSX OK ¬Ј headless **V114** (`ui-audit/verify-gantt-labels-deps.mjs`, updated): every connector is a curve (not an elbow), **0** NaN, and every endpoint binds to the bar band (below the row mid-line) on screen + in the print SVG, across right/center/left.

No text fades toward the background.

Data labels (start/end/owner/%) are cleared via `padBefore/padAfter` so the name never overlaps them.

Control surfaced in the Settings panel ("Task name alignment", 3-way, edits the active project).

### B395 вАФ Dependency arrows route as clean orthogonal elbows, not serpentine zig-zags `[Scheduler / Gantt]` (bug)  *(owner-dropped from chat as "NEW-3" 2026-06-22; first minted B392, **renumbered B395** вАФ PR #293 collision)*
`[x]` **вЪ†пЄП SUPERSEDED by B396 (same session):** the owner preferred the original curved connectors вАФ B396 reverts the orthogonal elbow and instead fixes the real defect (binding the curve's endpoints to the bar centers). This block records what B395 shipped before that feedback. вАФ **Filed AND fixed + headless-verified + shipped the SAME session per STANDING RULE #1 (branch `claude/zen-ramanujan-14sak9`).** The dashed dependency links were single cubic b√©ziers with direction-flipped handles that wandered into multi-bend serpentine shapes. Replaced the path generation in BOTH the `GanttView` `depLines` useMemo and the `buildGanttSVG` connector emitter with a deterministic **orthogonal elbow router** (`depElbow` + `depElbowD`, pure, shared) keyed on dependency type via `DEP_DIRS` (FS `[1,1]` / SS `[-1,1]` / FF `[1,-1]` / SF `[-1,-1]` exit/entry directions).
- **Shape:** short exit stub off the predecessor edge вЖТ a single vertical run вЖТ a horizontal into the successor edge, arrowhead pointing along the entry direction. A **normal forward link is вЙ§2 bends**; a **backward link** (the successor's entry edge sits on the far side) routes out вЖТ vertical вЖТ back across вЖТ in (вЙ§4 bends), around the bars вАФ never diagonally through them.
- **Edge cases:** milestone endpoints anchor to the **diamond tip** (center ¬± half-width in the travel direction), not a bar edge; endpoints are pure geometry from `tasks.indexOf`, so a link whose row is scrolled out of the virtualized window still computes and clips at the viewport; adjacent rows give a minimal vertical run; many-row spans give one straight vertical run, not per-row jogs. Kept the layer/paint order (connectors z3, under bars) and the per-type colors incl. SS `#7c3aed`; still dashed `4 3`.
- **Verified (part of V114 + the existing `verify-unscheduled-deps`):** `depElbow` unit-checked per type (every segment orthogonal for forward AND backward geometry, forward вЙ§2 bends, backward вЙ§4, no NaN in `depElbowD`); the live on-screen scenario draws 4 connectors all orthogonal/no-NaN incl. a backward link routing around; the print path likewise. `verify-unscheduled-deps` still passes (exactly 1 connector, no phantom NaN paths) вАФ the blank-date guard is intact.

### B392 вАФ Drag-to-resize columns in the PDF/Print Exhibit `[Scheduler]` (feature)  *(owner-dropped from chat as "NEW-3" 2026-06-22; filed B387, **renumbered B392** вАФ concurrent `main` (PRs #290/#291/#292) took B385вАУB389 while this exhibit batch was in flight, so B390вАУB392 are the real next free IDs; branch commit titles still read B385/B386/B387)*
`[x]` **Filed AND fixed + headless-verified (V113, 10/10) + merged via PR #293 the SAME session per STANDING RULE #1 (branch `claude/practical-edison-ggcm1k`).** The exhibit columns can now be tuned by dragging a column's right edge in the preview вАФ the same interaction as resizing a column in the live schedule grid вАФ with the preview reflowing live and the tuned layout persisting.
- **Handles + live drag (`buildPDFHtml`, `public/sequence/index.html`):** every column header in the **preview** (never the print output вАФ `@media print{.col-rs{display:none}}` + emitted only when `forPreview`) carries an absolutely-positioned `.col-rs` `col-resize` handle on its right edge. A small preview-only script tracks the drag and resizes the dragged column **live across every paginated page** (sets the width on all `th[data-k]` + each `.split-table`/`.split-gantt`), trading the delta against the Gantt вАФ which keeps `EXHIBIT_MIN_GANTT` (240px) вАФ and clamping to the column's `[min,max]`. On release it posts `{type:'planarColResize',key,w}` to the parent.
- **Persistence (`PDFExportModal`):** a `planarColResize` message handler stashes the width as a per-column override (`cfg.colWidths[key]`), flushes the preview immediately (like the collapse-toggle path), and writes through `setData` to **`data.exportColWidths`** so a tuned exhibit comes back next time the modal opens (`cfg.colWidths` is seeded from it). A **Reset** affordance under the Columns section clears the overrides back to content-fit. (Persisted at schedule-data level вАФ the exhibit renders one shared column layout across all selected projects, so a per-project-keyed store wouldn't apply; this is "comes back the way you left it" at the right granularity.)
- **Starts from B390's auto-fit:** an override wins for its column; everything else stays content-fit. Drag handles render only in the split (Gantt) view, where the table-vs-Gantt trade-off is well-defined (the reported screenshot).
- **Pagination fix bundled:** the paginator rebuilds the split and the Gantt container had **lost its `.split-gantt` class** (a no-class `div`); restored it so the live width-trade (and any `.split-gantt` selector) lands on the real post-paginate element instead of pushing/overflowing the chart.
- **DEDUPE / RECONCILE with B160 (left Open):** B160 is a single *ratio slider* for the whole table-vs-Gantt split; B392's **per-column** drag now changes the table block's total directly and the Gantt auto-takes the remainder (вЙ• MIN_GANTT) вАФ complementary, not a duplicate. B392 sets the default total from content-fit; if B160's slider is built later it sets the overall budget B392's columns fit within. Added a reconcile note to B160 in `BACKLOG.md`; not built here (it wasn't in this drop and is a distinct control).
- **Verified:** see the shared verification note under B390.

### B391 вАФ Year-boundary divider lines on the exhibit Gantt timeline `[Scheduler]` (feature)  *(owner-dropped from chat as "NEW-2" 2026-06-22; filed B386, **renumbered B391** вАФ concurrent `main` took B385вАУB389 while this batch was in flight)*
`[x]` **Filed AND fixed + headless-verified (V113, 10/10) + merged via PR #293 the SAME session per STANDING RULE #1 (branch `claude/practical-edison-ggcm1k`).** A multi-year exhibit Gantt (the example spanned 2025вЖТ2027) had no visual break between calendar years.
- **Root cause (read the code, not the brief):** `buildGanttSVG`'s month gridlines were drawn **behind** the opaque per-row background bands (`<rect width=svgWidth fill=bg>`), so in the chart **body** they were invisible вАФ only the dark header strip showed month labels. There were effectively no body gridlines at all, year or month.
- **Fix:** a new `yearLines` string drawn **over** the row bands (in the return, `${gridLines}${rows}${yearLines}${arrows}${todayLine}`): a heavier solid **medium-slate `#7b8290`, 1.3px** vertical at each Jan 1 (`yearMarkers`, the existing `m.mo===0` filter), so the split between years reads at a glance. Solid slate keeps it distinct from the red **dashed** Today line and the colored **dashed** dependency arrows. Also **emphasized the January month-axis labels** (bold + white vs the faint `#e8e8e8` other months) so each year's start is legible on the axis itself (doubles as the year label). A single-year exhibit (no January boundary in range) gets no divider вАФ correct.
- **Scope:** the exhibit only (the explicit request вАФ "the Gantt's result вА¶ should at least have divisions between the years"). Mirroring onto the on-screen `GanttView` was deferred (different render path; not requested).
- **Verified:** see the shared verification note under B390.

### B390 вАФ PDF/Print Exhibit table columns mis-sized: oversized Task-Name gap + truncated Start/End/Duration `[Scheduler]` (bug)  *(owner-dropped from chat as "NEW-1" 2026-06-22; filed B385, **renumbered B390** вАФ concurrent `main` (PRs #290/#291/#292) took B385вАУB389 while this batch was in flight, so B390вАУB392 are the real next free IDs)*
`[x]` **Filed AND fixed + headless-verified (V113, 10/10) + merged via PR #293 the SAME session per STANDING RULE #1 (branch `claude/practical-edison-ggcm1k`).** Three symptoms, **one** cause: in the split-view (table + Gantt) exhibit the columns were sized by **fixed widths, not fitted to content** вАФ a large dead band between TASK NAME and START, Start/End rendering clipped (`06/2вА¶`, `09/0вА¶`), and DUR clipped (`1вА¶`, `4вА¶`).
- **Root cause:** the split table used `table-layout:fixed` at a hardcoded ~50%-of-page width, with fixed per-column px from `COL_DEFS` and the **Task-Name column at `w:null`** вАФ so Name absorbed ALL the leftover width (the giant gap) while the fixed **42px** Start/End and **28px** Duration columns were too narrow for `MM/DD/YY` / multi-digit durations and clipped via `overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis`.
- **Fix вАФ content-fit width model.** New pure, DOM-free module-scope helpers (above `buildPDFHtml`, so preview + print + tests agree): `approxTextPx(str,fs)` approximates rendered width from per-character advances for the exhibit's Inter face (deliberately generous so a fixed-format value never clips); `layoutExhibitCols(specs,opts)` lays columns out from their content-fit base, lets a user drag-override win, clamps each to `[min,max]`, makes the **table block exactly its columns' total**, and gives the Gantt the rest вАФ never below `EXHIBIT_MIN_GANTT` (240px), shrinking the **flexible** columns (name/owner/predecessors/cost) toward their min, then a uniform scale, only if the columns would crowd the chart. `buildPDFHtml` measures each visible column's widest value across **all** selected projects (the exhibit stacks them under one shared header) via a plain-text `cellText` + a `COL_FIT` profile (font px, clamp range, flex flag, the Status dot+gap extra), then sizes the split from the result.
- **Per the brief:** the short fixed-format columns (Start/End/Duration/%/Status) are **NOT flexible** вАФ a date is never the value that gets clipped to make room; only Name/Owner/Predecessors/Cost cap + ellipsize. **Respects the column on/off checkboxes** (only the turned-on `colDefs` are measured/sized). Tables-only mode (no Gantt) is **untouched** вАФ its auto-layout already content-fits, so the bug was split-only; the fix is scoped there.
- **Shared verification (B390/B391/B392):** lint **0 errors** ¬Ј **1210 tests** (1201 + 9 new in `test/exhibitCols.test.js`, with a faithful copy in `ui-audit/stress/exhibit-cols.mjs` + anti-drift guards) ¬Ј build green ¬Ј JSX transpiles (`jsxcheck-sequence`) ¬Ј `Scheduler` lazy chunk intact. Headless **V113** (`ui-audit/verify-exhibit-columns.mjs`, **10/10**, drives page вЖТ sequence iframe вЖТ preview iframe on the real app): Start **and** End dates render in full with no ellipsis clip (`12/27/26`, `07/23/25`, `02/02/27`); Duration full (`389d`, `21d`); Task-Name content-capped (no runaway gap, name=280px); Gantt keeps a real share (322px); year-boundary divider lines present; a resize handle drags **live** (53вЖТ87px) and the new width **round-trips/persists** through the parent re-render. Screenshot: `ui-audit/screens/exhibit-fixed-zoom.png`. (Re-verified after merging `main` вАФ main's B388 Schedule-toolbar lift moved the Export control into the shell header, so the harness opens it there; still 10/10.)

`[x]` **Filed AND fixed + headless-verified the SAME session per STANDING RULE #1 (branch `claude/inspiring-bohr-46gql9`).** The Light/Dark/System picker that lived in the row-1 вЪЩ gear (B342) now lives in the **account вЖТ Settings** panel (`AuthPanel`), next to Change password вАФ where a signed-in user expects their preferences.
- **One picker, one home, no duplication:** extracted the picker UI into a shared `src/shared/theme/ThemePicker.jsx` (self-contained вАФ reads/sets the ThemeProvider via `useTheme`, theme tokens only, no raw hex). `AuthPanel`'s Settings tab renders it; the row-1 gear (`AppHeader` `SettingsMenu`) now renders the SAME component (no copy-paste).
- **Signed-out access preserved (B342):** the row-1 gear is kept **only when signed out** (`{!accountActive && <SettingsMenu/>}`) вАФ a logged-out visitor can still switch theme, a signed-in user finds it in account вЖТ Settings, and it's never duplicated. `accountActive` is `!!user` from the Shell, threaded to every AppHeader, so the gate is reliable. (Owner trade-off, flagged: signed-out is now the only place the standalone gear shows; signed-in is account вЖТ Settings.)
- **Code:** new `ThemePicker.jsx`; `AppHeader.jsx` (gear вЖТ shared picker, gated on `!accountActive`, dropped the now-unused `mode`/`setMode`/`THEME_OPTS`); `AuthPanel.jsx` (Settings tab renders `<ThemePicker/>`). Pure relocation вАФ the ThemeProvider, the `data-theme` mechanism, and the System matchMedia listener are unchanged.
- **Verified:** lint 0 ¬Ј **1201 tests** ¬Ј build green; headless **V112** (`ui-audit/verify-b389-theme-in-profile.mjs` + `theme-in-profile-harness.{html,jsx}`, **7/7** вАФ signed-out gear present, signed-in gear gone, the Settings-tab picker offers Light/Dark/System and clicking Dark/Light actually flips `<html data-theme>`, 0 page errors). The B387 (9/9) + B388 (17/17) harnesses still pass вАФ the logged-out gear they rely on is preserved.

### B388 вАФ Lift the Schedule toolbar into the unified AppHeader over the iframe bridge `[Scheduler / Header-Nav]` (feature) вАФ built on B387  *(owner-dropped from chat as "NEW-2" 2026-06-22; filed B386, **renumbered B388** вАФ a concurrent `main` (PRs #289/#290) took B385/B386 while this was in flight, so B387/B388 are the real next free IDs. The branch commit titles still read "B385/B386" вАФ written before the collision surfaced; the canonical IDs are **B387/B388**.)*
`[x]` **Filed AND fully built + headless-verified the SAME session per STANDING RULE #1 (branch `claude/inspiring-bohr-46gql9`).** Schedule's two stacked header rows are now one: the embedded Gantt app's action toolbar (`public/sequence/index.html`) is LIFTED up into the shell's unified `AppHeader` Row 2 over the existing postMessage bridge (B203), so Schedule matches Site/Markup вАФ one header, no double toolbar.

Consumes B387's `toolbarCenter`.

### B386 вАФ Dependency connectors draw phantom arrows to unscheduled (blank-date) tasks `[Scheduler]` (bug)  *(owner-reported 2026-06-22; arrived as cross-chat "NEW-1"; filed B385, **renumbered B386** вАФ a concurrent `main` (PR #289) took B385 for the Site Planner parcel-identify feature while this was in flight, so B386 is the real next free ID)*
`[x]` **Filed AND fixed + headless-verified + SHIPPED the same session per STANDING RULE #1 вАФ merged to `main` via PR #290 (squash `e4fdb2f`), branch `claude/gifted-rubin-0adp7h`.** (The PR/commit title still reads "B385" вАФ written before the concurrent-collision renumber surfaced; the canonical ID is **B386**.)

**Repro (Pappadoupolos, Schedule вЖТ Split/Gantt):** the "Wastewater Treatment Plant Design" branch (rows 11вАУ13) are *unscheduled stubs* вАФ blank start/finish, 0d, so no bar and no milestone diamond. A dependency link still terminated at/from one of them and the arrow was drawn into empty space (the "purple pointing at nothing" the owner saw).

**Diagnostic fork (done first, as the brief required) вЖТ branch #1: genuine unscheduled stubs, NOT a silent date-calc failure.** Blank/unscheduled tasks are a deliberate, first-class state: `mkt` creates them (`start=""`, `dur=""`), `rollupParentDates` leaves a parent blank when *all* its children are blank (so the blank parent over blank children in rows 11вАУ13 is the *designed* outcome), `cascadeDates` leaves a task blank when no predecessor yields a start, and BOTH the bar renderer (`isBlankDates` guard) and the PDF-export connector loop (`!pt.start||!pt.end||!t.start||!t.end`) already skip blank-date geometry. The date engine is correct вАФ the rows are intentionally undated. The single defect: the live `GanttView.depLines` was the one draw path *missing* that guard, so it computed `xOf("")` вЖТ `NaN` and emitted a phantom path.

**Fix (`public/sequence/index.html`):** (1) `depLines` now skips any link whose predecessor OR successor has blank dates вАФ exactly the guard the export already uses, so no connector is drawn to no-geometry. (2) Per the "don't silently hide it" preference, each blank-date Gantt row now shows an explicit, horizontally-sticky **"Unscheduled"** tag, so the empty row reads as intentional rather than a glitch. 0-day *dated* milestones (rows 10, 16) keep their diamond AND their links (`start===end`, both truthy) вАФ no regression.

**Verified:** headless **V109** (`ui-audit/verify-unscheduled-deps.mjs`) вАФ phantom connectors gone (dep-line count **1**, **zero** `NaN` paths), the one fully-dated link still draws, both blank rows tagged & visible; **proven to FAIL with the guard reverted** (3 dep paths, 3 `NaN` coords, 0 tags). lint **0 errors** ¬Ј **1201** unit tests green ¬Ј build green ¬Ј `Scheduler` lazy chunk intact ¬Ј existing scheduler harnesses still pass (no-crash 6/6, bugfixes ALL PASS, picker 8/8, rowfill-bars PASS). Cloudflare Pages deploy succeeded on the PR.

**Deduped вАФ NET-NEW.** Not B380 (Scheduler.jsx nav-state render-crash вАФ different file/cause), not B381 (toolbar hidden by a CSS over-reach вАФ different surface), and NOT the concurrent **B385** (Site Planner parcel-identify вАФ a different module entirely, just an ID collision). No existing Open or Done item covers dependency-connector geometry.

The `+` add cursor shows while armed.

- **Gotcha fixed during verify:** a selected parcel's interior is a hit target AND its acreage label (`startAcChip`) stops propagation, so clicks on an existing lot never reached the background handler вАФ both `startMoveParcel` and `startAcChip` now defer to a shared `beginIdentifyPress` in identify mode, so clicking anywhere on a lot toggles it.

(The live county host is CORS-blocked in the sandbox, hence the route-fulfil mock.)

### B383 вАФ "Add parcel" action in the Parcel left-hand panel `[Site Planner]` (feature)  *(owner-dropped from chat as "NEW-1" 2026-06-22; minted **B383** вАФ highest B# across both files was B382)*

### B382 вАФ Parcels in the Fort Bend / Harris seam "take forever to load" then "can't be clicked" while a county CAD host is down `[Site Planner / Map]` (bug)  *(owner-reported from chat 2026-06-22 вАФ "Fort Bend, Cadd вА¶ isn't working вА¶ takes forever to load, and then вА¶ it doesn't work"; minted **B382** вАФ highest B# across both files was B381 (concurrent main PR #285 took B381 for the Schedule-toolbar restore while this was in flight); a recurrence of B244/B137 territory, deduped against them)*
`[x]` **Filed AND fixed + headless-verified the SAME session per STANDING RULE #1 (branch `claude/confident-meitner-j3tv25`).** Two symptoms, ONE upstream cause confirmed with LIVE probes (not guessed): **FBCAD (`gis.fbcad.org`) was down again** вАФ timed out / slow-503 at 12вАУ15s from both Node and headless Chromium вАФ while HCAD and the statewide TxGIO host were up (the exact B244 condition, recurred 2026-06-22). The two existing mitigations didn't fully cover it:
- **Symptom 1 ("forever to load") вАФ the DISPLAY layer had no timeout.** B244's 8s `AbortController` lives only in `fetchJson` (the click/identify path). The visible purple parcel outlines are an esri-leaflet `featureLayer` (`makeParcelLayer`, `MapFinder.jsx`) that bypasses `fetchJson`, so when FBCAD hangs the outline layer spins with no recovery. **Fix:** `addDisplay` now arms an 8s hang-guard for a real county layer (armed on the layer's `requeststart`, disarmed by `load`, so a below-outline-zoom view never false-flags); on timeout/`requesterror` it pulls the dead layer, records the host as failing (feeds the breaker so CLICKS skip it too), and leans on the always-present statewide TxGIO outlines for that ground вАФ keeping what you SEE == what you can SELECT (the B137 rule). The **statewide layer is exempt** from the guard: a slow statewide outline is allowed to finish rather than be pulled (a slow outline beats no outline вАФ that "took a while but worked" wait IS this layer; pulling it would leave nothing to see OR click).
- **Symptom 2 ("can't click the lots") вАФ every click waited on the hung host.** `identifyParcelDetailed` used `Promise.allSettled`, which waits for EVERY candidate вАФ so even though TxGIO answered, each click stalled the full 8s on FBCAD's timeout before resolving, reading as "clicking does nothing." **Fix:** new `identifyParcelEager` (`lib/arcgis.js`) resolves the moment the FIRST source returns a lot (real CADs are queried before the statewide fallback, so a healthy county still answers first), and feeds the circuit breaker the full per-source health via an `onSettled` callback once the slow ones finish (so the next click skips the dead host). The no-hit verdict still waits for all to settle, so "reached a server, no parcel" vs "couldn't reach any server" stay honest (B245). `handleClick` + the address-search `selectParcelAt` both switched to it.
- **Tests/verify:** +3 unit (`test/arcgis.test.js`) вАФ eager returns the hit WITHOUT tripping/awaiting the hung source's timeout then feeds the breaker for both; the no-hit path reports responded/errors honestly; a real-CAD hit is preferred over the statewide one. Full suite **1201 green** (unchanged after merging main вАФ PR #285 added a Playwright harness, no vitest tests), build green, esri-leaflet 3.0.19 `requeststart`/`load`/`requesterror` event contract confirmed present. Headless **V107** (`ui-audit/verify-parcel-resilience.mjs`) вАФ run against the LIVE failing hosts tonight: select mode loads with **0 uncaught errors**, the map stays alive through the full FBCAD hang window (no freeze), and a click resolves in a **bounded 8.1s** (the AbortController cap on the worst-case no-hit path) instead of the open-ended 12вАУ30s+ the raw hung hosts give. (A real lot with a fast source resolves in ~1вАУ4s, per the unit tests.)
- **Forward note:** tonight the statewide TxGIO *query* op was itself slow (its metadata was fast, but spatial queries timed out 30s+ from Node) вАФ so when FBCAD is down AND TxGIO query is degraded, even the universal fallback is slow. This fix makes the click *bounded and non-freezing* and keeps see==click, but it can't make a slow statewide host fast. If TxGIO-query slowness becomes chronic, the roadmap **GIS layer caching** item (stale-while-revalidate parcel outlines) is the durable answer.

### B381 вАФ Restore the missing Schedule toolbar controls (regression) `[Schedule]` (bug)  *(arrived as cross-chat "NEW-1" 2026-06-22; first filed B380, renumbered **B381** вАФ concurrent main PR #284 took B380 for the Schedule render-crash fix while this was in flight, so B381 is the real next free ID; net-new, the completion of B203)*
`[x]` **Filed AND fixed + headless-verified (V106, 15/15) + merged the SAME session per STANDING RULE #1 (branch `claude/vigilant-newton-rovl4l`).** Owner: opening the Schedule module on any project, the Gantt/timeline toolbar was reduced to the **single floating Columns button** above the grid вАФ timeline zoom, Contacts, Export (PDF/print), Version History, the Grid/Split/Gantt view switcher, Automation, Settings and the Review toggle were all gone.
- **Root cause вАФ hidden, NOT deleted (read the code + git, not the brief).** The Schedule module embeds the standalone sequence app (`public/sequence/index.html`) in an **iframe**; the shell's Row-1 breadcrumb takes over project nav, so the sequence app hides its own duplicated nav when `.in-iframe` (the embed app even documents this at the postMessage bridge: "runs in an iframe with its OWN header вА¶ hidden"). But the rule was `html.in-iframe .app-header { display:none }` вАФ it hid the **ENTIRE** header, and the whole action toolbar (view switch, Review, Format, Zoom, Export, Save, Version History, Contacts, Automation, Settings) lives inside that same `.app-header`. So every tool vanished; only the in-grid **Columns** button (rendered inside `GridView`, not the header) survived вАФ exactly the reported symptom. All handlers were intact the whole time; a pure CSS over-reach. Confirmed hidden vs deleted (the fix is re-show, not re-add).
- **Fix (`public/sequence/index.html`, 2 small edits).** Narrowed the `.in-iframe` rule to hide ONLY the genuinely-duplicated branding/nav вАФ the logo (gave it a new `.hdr-logo` class), the Dashboard/Projects toggle (`.hdr-mode`) and the project picker (`.hdr-project`), all of which the shell breadcrumb already provides (bridged via the B203 postMessage nav). The rest of `.app-header` (view switcher + Review + the full action group) is visible again, in its original position, with its original handlers вАФ no re-wiring needed because nothing was ever removed.
- **Authoritative restored set (from the actual `.app-header` markup, not the brief):** Grid/Split/Gantt view switcher ¬Ј Review toggle ¬Ј Format ¬Ј timeline Zoom вИТ/%/+ (shown in split/gantt) ¬Ј Export (PDF¬ЈPrint Exhibit / Web Snapshot) ¬Ј Save indicator ¬Ј Version History ¬Ј Contacts ¬Ј Automation ¬Ј Settings. **The brief's speculative "fit-to-view / today-date-jump / status-filter" controls do NOT exist in this app** вАФ none were ever shipped, so none were restored (per "do not rebuild from a guessed list").
- **Verified working, not just present (V106, `ui-audit/verify-schedule-toolbar.mjs`, 15/15 headless):** toolbar visible in the iframe; logo/mode/project correctly hidden; every action control renders; switching to Gantt reveals the zoom controls; zoom-in changes the % (17вЖТ33, proving the handler is wired, not a no-op); Contacts opens its panel. New Playwright regression harness so this can't silently regress again. **Site + Markup checked вАФ NOT affected** (they aren't iframes; they feed their toolbars through the shell's `toolbarContent` slot, which `.in-iframe` can't reach). lint **0 errors** ¬Ј **1186 tests** green (1198 after merging main's B380) ¬Ј build green ¬Ј `Scheduler` lazy chunk intact.
- **Dedup:** NET-NEW, the **completion of B203** (DONE). B203 diagnosed this same `.in-iframe .app-header{display:none}` hide and bridged the **nav half** (project picker + Dashboard/Projects toggle) up to the shell breadcrumb вАФ but the **action-toolbar half** the same rule hid was never re-homed and stayed dark; B381 restores it. NOT a dup of main's **B380** (a separate intermittent Schedule *render-crash* race in `Scheduler.jsx` вАФ different file, different cause, shipped the same day), nor B341 (chrome hardcoded-color/token regressions), nor the Markup `toolbarContent` relocation.

### B380 вАФ Intermittent render crash on Schedule load ("Cannot read properties of undefined"), caught by the workspace ErrorBoundary `[Scheduler]` (bug)  *(arrived as cross-chat diagnosis brief "NEW-1" 2026-06-22; minted **B380** вАФ highest B# across both files was B379; net-new, deduped vs B221/B239 stale-chunk + B315 undo-race)*
`[x]` **Filed AND fixed + headless-verified (V105) the SAME session per STANDING RULE #1 (branch `claude/relaxed-dijkstra-sokq4a`).** Opening the Schedule module would intermittently show the workspace ErrorBoundary's **non-chunk "Try again / Reload page"** fallback with a `<pre>` of the "Cannot read properties of undefined (reading 'вА¶')" form; **Try again** (a state reset, not a reload) recovered cleanly. Confirmed NOT the stale-chunk family (B221/B239) вАФ the boundary took the genuine-render-crash path and a pure re-render fixed it.
- **Root cause вАФ reproduced, not guessed.** The Schedule shell embeds the standalone Gantt in an iframe (`/sequence/`) and bridges that app's project list to the shared Row-1 breadcrumb over postMessage (`planar:nav-state`). The shell derives the breadcrumb's current project with `projects.find((p) => p.id === activeId)` (the brief's #1 candidate, `Scheduler.jsx`). The embedded app builds its list as `Object.values(data.projects).map(p => ({id, name}))`; while ITS own data is still loading it can transiently emit a **sparse / not-yet-resolved** list containing an `undefined`/null entry. One such entry makes `p.id` throw **inside the Scheduler's render** вЖТ caught by the workspace boundary. A pure re-render recovers because the steady-state list is well-formed, which is exactly why it presents as intermittent. The brief's other candidates (`AppHeader`/`ProjectBreadcrumb` `p.id`/`p.name`, `useProfile/displayName` in `Shell.jsx`) were each verified **already null-safe** (signed-in + real-iframe headless repro, 0 crashes); the deref that actually throws is the Scheduler's `.find`.
- **Fix вАФ guard at the source (not optional-chaining at every call site).** New pure, unit-tested `src/workspaces/scheduler/lib/navState.js` (matches the B315 pure-module precedent): `parseNavState(message)` validates source/type and routes through `sanitizeProjects(list)`, which coerces the inbound list to an array of plain `{id, name}` objects вАФ **dropping the null/undefined/primitive entries that are the only values that throw on a later `p.id`/`p.name` read**; `deriveCurrentProject(projects, activeId, section)` never throws and never returns `undefined` (Dashboard/reports вЖТ null; a stale activeId not in the list вЖТ null, the empty/loader state). `Scheduler.jsx` routes both the inbound message and the current-project derivation through these. One **data-entry guard** in the shared `ProjectBreadcrumb` (`(controlled ? controlledProjects : internalProjects).filter(Boolean)`) hardens its own `p.id`/`p.name` map for any controlled caller. The race is **removed** so the (now-rare) genuine crash still stays visible вАФ NOT widened `isChunkLoadError`, NOT a blanket ErrorBoundary auto-retry (per the brief).
- **Behaviour preserved.** For the real embedded app's well-formed `{id,name}` payload the output is identical to the previous inline logic вАФ only the not-ready/malformed shapes are made safe.
- **Tests/verify:** +12 unit (`test/schedulerNavState.test.js`) вАФ sanitize drops the throwing entries / keeps real objects, parse validates + sanitizes, derive is null-safe on the race/Dashboard/stale-id paths. Full suite **1198 green**, lint **0 errors**, build green, `Scheduler` lazy chunk intact. Headless **V105** (`ui-audit/verify-scheduler-no-crash.mjs`, 9/9) вАФ the first-render race shows the loader/empty (no boundary), a deliberately malformed nav-state doesn't crash the header and the good projects still render, signed-in-with-late-profile doesn't crash; **proven to FAIL (boundary + page error) with the guard off**, so it's a real regression net. Existing `verify-schedule-picker.mjs` still **8/8** (no regression to the bridge/switch/dashboard).

### B378 вАФ Sheet labels are garbage on text-dense (general-notes / specs) sheets `[Doc Review / Markup]` (bug)  *(arrived as cross-chat "NEW-1" 2026-06-22; minted **B378** вАФ highest B# across both files was B373, so B378 is the real next free ID; extends/hardens B266 + the shared `sheetMeta` reader, deduped against B266/B348)*
`[x]` **Filed AND fixed + headless-verified the SAME session per STANDING RULE #1 (branch `claude/ecstatic-maxwell-6y8aq1`).** A structural general-notes set labelled "atrociously": body boilerplate shown AS the sheet title ("вА¶reproduced or used withoutвА¶", "CJ DENOTESвА¶"), the same cross-referenced number on several rows ("Structural ¬Ј S202" √Ч4), and a mix of those with plain "Sheet N." Root cause: every read was tuned for a normal drawing (sparse plan + one dense title-block strip); a notes sheet (wall-to-wall text, no drawing area) violates all of those assumptions at once. Fixed at the shared reader so BOTH the Markup sidebar and the Stitcher benefit:
- **Title scorer was backwards (`readSheetTitle`, `sheetMeta.js`).** It scored `lineHeight √Ч letterCount`, which *rewards* long sentences вАФ so the copyright block and a legend row outscored the real short title. Re-weighted to **prefer font height, with a small word/letter cap** (a title is a few words, not a sentence): candidates over 7 words / 48 letters are dropped, height dominates the score, letters only break ties. Added a **boilerplate filter** (`property of` / `reproduced` / `copyright` / `denotes` / `continued` / "may not be вА¶") to the existing skip list. Net: "GENERAL NOTES" wins over the boilerplate it used to lose to.
- **The "band-first" guarantee was fictional for the number (`readSheetMeta`).** `parseSheetNumber` ran over the whole-page joined string, and its `(?:no\.?|#)?` is optional, so a body cross-reference ("SEE DWG S202") was grabbed as THIS sheet's number вАФ identical on every sheet that referenced it. Made the number read **title-block-zone-scoped**: from the detected band, or вАФ when a dense notes sheet defeats the density-based band detector вАФ from the right/bottom edge **strip** where title blocks live; only a non-dense sheet may fall back to the whole-page read. So the sheet's OWN number ("S-001") is read and the body cross-ref ("S202") is excluded.
- **`reconstructLines` merged across the full page width.** Two items sharing a baseline but ~900 pt apart (a title-block label and a far-left body note) were joined into one "line", which then failed the title filter as "too wordy" вАФ losing the title entirely on a notes sheet. Now **splits a row on a large horizontal gap** (generous threshold вАФ far bigger than any intra-phrase word gap, so "MATCH LINE вА¶ SEE SHEET C-6" still joins), so a title-block title can't bleed into a body line.
- **Sidebar gate too weak (`DocReview.jsx`).** The old `hasReal = sheetNumber || titleBlock` let a bare band authorize a title-derived label. Replaced with a `trustedTitle` gate: a title is surfaced only when it came from a real band, OR is corroborated by a zone-read number, OR the sheet is a recognized text page (general notes/specs) вАФ else it falls back cleanly to the discipline item, then the number, then "Sheet N." Singles now show the real title ("GENERAL NOTES ¬Ј S-001") instead of a generic discipline label.
- **Identical adjacent numbers = a misread вЖТ drop it.** New pure `markAdjacentDuplicateNumbers` (`sheetGroups.js`) clears a sheet number that repeats on an adjacent page (a real set never prints the same # twice in a row) and lowers confidence, so the no-band fallback can't produce a run of identical wrong rows. Applied in both the Markup consumer (`DocReview` `orderedMeta`) and the Stitcher path (`readSheets`).
- **Tests:** +9 unit (`sheetMeta`/`sheetGroups`/`sheetRead`): the title scorer ignores boilerplate, the number is zone-scoped (reads S-001 not the S202 cross-ref), `textDense` is flagged, the dedup clears adjacent duplicates. Full suite **1153 green**, lint 0 errors, build green, `DocReview` lazy chunk intact. Verified **V104**.

### B379 вАФ False auto-calibration ("¬ЈвЙИ") on general-notes / specs sheets `[Doc Review / Markup]` (bug)  *(arrived as cross-chat "NEW-2" 2026-06-22; minted **B379** вАФ next free ID after B378; relates to B267 `statedCalibration`, deduped against it)*
`[x]` **Filed AND fixed + headless-verified the SAME session per STANDING RULE #1 (branch `claude/ecstatic-maxwell-6y8aq1`).** On the same structural set, pure-text notes sheets (S00x) showed "¬ЈвЙИ" (auto-calibrated) even though they carry no plan scale, while sheet 1 correctly read "NOT TO SCALE." Root cause: `parseSheetScale` matches a scale-looking string **anywhere** in the dense notes text, and `statedCalibration` only gated on a standard plot size вАФ so a 36√Ч24 general-notes sheet with a stray "1\"=20'" in its body auto-calibrated. Auto-calibrating a non-drawing sheet silently mis-scales it (crash-severity per "never auto-guess" вАФ a wrong calibration poisons every downstream takeoff).
- **Fix вАФ classify the sheet, then gate.** `readSheetMeta` now computes a **`textDense`** flag (a general-notes / specifications / legend sheet): true when the title is a notes/specs/legend/index title, or the drawing area is saturated with sentence-like prose (вЙ•10 lines of вЙ•6 words вАФ plans carry only short labels). `statedCalibration` **returns 0 when `textDense`**, so such a sheet is left uncalibrated ("not present" вЙ† "couldn't parse", per B267) rather than silently scaled. A real plan sheet (sparse drawing-area text, a stated scale in its title block) still auto-calibrates exactly as before.
- **Tests:** +1 unit (`sheetRead`: a textDense sheet with a stated scale on a standard plot вЖТ 0) plus the `textDense` true/false assertions under B378. Verified **V104** (the same harness asserts the notes sheet shows no "¬ЈвЙИ" while the plan sheet still does).

### B374 вАФ Area measurements can't be selected by their filled interior (dead-centre hit target) `[Doc Review / Markup]` (bug)  *(owner-reported from chat 2026-06-22 вАФ "no easy way to delete this little triangle вА¶ insane"; minted **B374** вАФ highest B# across both files was B373; batch B374вАУB377)*
`[x]` **Filed AND fixed + headless-verified + shipped the SAME session per STANDING RULE #1 (branch `claude/youthful-mccarthy-xjcotz`).** Michael's "triangle" was an **uncalibrated Area measurement** вАФ its value label falls back to the literal string **"set scale"** when a sheet has no feet-per-page-unit (`measureLabel`, `lib/takeoff.js`). Clicking the triangle's body to select it (the natural first step to delete it) did nothing.
- **Root cause:** in `DocReview.jsx` `hitTest`, **rect/cloud** got a point-in-bbox interior test (B33) but **area fell through to the generic measures branch вАФ nearest vertex/segment only**. The Area polygon renders FILLED (`fill="#0e749022"`), so it reads as a solid clickable object while its **interior was a dead hit target**; only a click on the thin edge/a vertex registered, and at low zoom (e.g. 26%) that band is nearly impossible to hit вЖТ the measurement felt undeletable.
- **Fix:** added an `m.kind === "area"` branch to `hitTest` вАФ `pointInPoly(p, pts)` returns d=0 for a click anywhere inside the polygon. `pointInPoly` is now **EXPORTED** from `lib/takeoff.js` (the same ray-cast already behind `centroidOf`, not a 2nd copy; handles concave outlines). A <3-pt / degenerate area still selects by its edge or vertex via the fallback (now incl. the **closing edge**, which the old branch skipped вАФ also applied to perimeter). Added a **smaller-shape-wins tie-break** on interior (d===0) hits so a small markup sitting on a big filled area isn't swallowed by the area underneath.
- **Verified (V104):** new `ui-audit/verify-delete-markup.mjs` **10/10** (chromium-1228, 0 page errors) вАФ draws an uncalibrated "set scale" Area, then: a **centroid click selects it** (stroke 2вЖТ3), a click **outside does NOT** select (hit test stays specific), and Delete removes it. No regression: V72 viewer **13/13**, B300вАУB302 green. lint 0 ¬Ј 1144 tests ¬Ј build green.

### B375 вАФ No on-canvas delete control for a selected markup (deletion was keyboard-only) `[Doc Review / Markup]` (feature) вАФ pairs with B374
`[x]` **Same session/branch.** Even once a markup is selected, removing it was **Delete/Backspace only**, plus a "Delete selected" button buried in the (collapsible) Takeoff panel вАФ nothing on the canvas where the user is looking, so deletion wasn't discoverable. Added a clear **√Ч button anchored to the selected markup's top-right**, rendered OUTSIDE the `pointerEvents:none` overlay (like the inline text/calibrate editors) so it takes its own click; `stopPropagation` on pointer-down keeps that click from starting a pan/draw underneath. Runs the same one-undo-frame path as the Delete key (`pushHistory` вЖТ filter out the id вЖТ `setSel(null)`). Hidden while editing text / calibrating. Theme tokens only (`--danger-text` fill + `--on-accent` glyph вАФ AA in both themes; no raw hex). Verified in V104 (√Ч appears on the selection and deletes the markup).

### B376 вАФ Per-item delete in the Takeoff list (all markups) + a deletable measure list in the Stitcher `[Doc Review / Markup + Stitch]` (feature)
`[x]` **Same session/branch.** The hit-test-independent removal path, so anything can always be taken off вАФ even on a dense sheet or when not in Select mode.

Full on-canvas select-on-stitch is deliberately **not** built (it never existed there; the list closes the gap without that larger refactor).

### B377 вАФ Scanned-sheet OCR worker threw "logger is not a function" on every page (error storm) `[Doc Review / Stitch + OCR]` (bug)  *(found while headless-verifying B374вАУB376; minted **B377**)*
`[x]` **Same session/branch.** Surfaced by the Stitcher harness runs: a page with no text layer triggers the B352 Tesseract OCR fallback, and the worker threw **`TypeError: logger is not a function`** repeatedly (13√Ч in one B300вАУB302 run). **Root cause:** `defaultMakeWorker` (`lib/ocr.js`) passed `logger` вАФ always `undefined`, since no caller supplies one вАФ straight into `createWorker({ вА¶, logger })`. Tesseract invokes `logger` on the **main thread** for every progress packet the worker posts back, and an explicit `logger: undefined` **clobbers Tesseract's own default no-op**, so each message threw. **Fix:** default `logger = () => {}` (still injectable for a real progress UI later). Confirmed gone in the unminified dev build (0 `PAGEERROR`) and across all Stitcher harnesses вАФ **B300вАУB302 uncaught JS errors 13 вЖТ 0**. OCR unit tests unaffected (they inject the recognizer, bypassing the default worker). NB the WASM core + English model still load from the jsDelivr CDN at runtime; only the logger crash was in scope.

### B373 вАФ Restore the compact, app-wide cloud-sync indicator in AppHeader Row 1 `[App Shell / all workspaces]` (feature)  *(arrived as cross-chat "NEW-1" 2026-06-22 вАФ a provisional label colliding with the older NEW-1 open-file intent + the B365/B372 NEW-1 markers/delete items; first filed **B366**, renumbered **B373** вАФ a concurrent `main` (PRs #277/#278) took B366вАУB372 (GIS Site Analysis resilience + source registry, delete-persistence) while this was in flight, so B373 is the real next free ID)*
`[x]` **Filed AND shipped + headless-verified the SAME session per STANDING RULE #1 (branch `claude/vibrant-dijkstra-i3ddzg`).** The small save-status indicator the owner expected in the header had drifted away: the Site Planner showed a **text** chip ("Synced вЬУ"), Document Review had moved its chip out of Row 1 down to the Row-2 Reviews control (B358), and the Stitcher carried its own вАФ so there was no single, compact, app-wide indicator, and the owner's design intent (a **cloud glyph + check, no "Saved" text**) had been lost. Worse, the failure mode that made it "disappear" was a silent drop-to-blank on error. Restored as **one shared component, app-wide, that goes LOUD on a failed write and never silently vanishes.**
- **New shared `src/shared/ui/CloudSyncBadge.jsx`** вАФ a compact cloud glyph (no text label) driven by the **normalized `saveState` every workspace already computes** (so it reflects the REAL cloud write, never an optimistic always-green). Pure exported `cloudBadgeView(state)` is the whole truth-table вЖТ glyph + color + loud/actionable flags. States, each visually distinct (not text-dependent): **synced** = quiet green cloud-check (the resting default); **saving** = amber cloud-up, pulsing; **offline** = amber cloud-pause (saved on device, will sync); **error** = **LOUD** red cloud-slash + a red ring, click вЖТ popover with what-failed + **Retry now**; **local** = muted "device" glyph (signed out); **null** = nothing (no project/doc loaded вАФ legitimately empty, not a hidden error).
- **The crash-severity guardrail in code (the headline ask):** the badge wraps itself in a small error boundary (`CloudBadgeBoundary`) that, if the badge ever throws while rendering, shows the **loud error glyph instead of returning null** вАФ the exact "silent unmount" that made the old indicator vanish. Keyed on `state` so a transient throw clears once inputs change, and so it tracks live state across module/project switches without going stale.
- **`AppHeader` renders it once, in Row 1, from `saveState`** вАФ so it's genuinely shared across Site / Schedule / Markup. New optional `onRetrySave` + `saveDetail` props let a workspace supply the retry action and a tailored popover message (e.g. "reload to merge" for a conflict, where a blind retry is wrong).
- **Site Planner:** retired the text `plannerSaveSlot` chip (the compact badge replaces it); wires `onRetrySave={retryCloudSave}` (suppressed for a conflict, which needs a reload) + a conflict `saveDetail`. The loud failure **banners** (cloudSaveFailed / cloudConflict) stay as the can't-miss interrupt; the badge is the always-present at-a-glance state.
- **Document Review + Stitcher:** new pure exported `docSaveState(status, signedIn, idle)` (in `usePersistence.js`) maps the doc-review raw status onto the normalized vocabulary вАФ **a failed/conflicting write вЖТ "error" (LOUD)**, idle (nothing loaded) вЖТ null (no cry-wolf at rest), signed-in вЖТ synced, signed-out-with-content вЖТ local. DR feeds it to AppHeader; the **Stitcher has its own chrome (no AppHeader), so it renders its own `CloudSyncBadge`** in its toolbar вАФ same glyph, same loudness, everywhere.
- **Retired the now-redundant Row-2 ReviewsBar save chip** (its `chipFor` + `SaveIcon`) so a module never shows two competing save indicators вАФ the app-wide Row-1 badge is the single source. ReviewsBar is now purely the filing control. Removed the obsolete `test/reviewsBadge.test.js`; its "failed-write-is-loud / no-cry-wolf" contract migrated to the new badge test.
- **Tests:** new `test/cloudSyncBadge.test.js` (13) locks the contract вАФ **a failed save is never visually identical to "all good"** (distinct glyph + color + loud flag), null shows nothing, the crashed fallback is loud, and the doc rawвЖТnormalized mapping keeps failures loud. Full suite green post-merge (lint 0 errors, build green; `SitePlannerApp`/`DocReview` lazy chunks intact).
- **Verified (V103):** two headless harnesses (chromium-1194, 0 page errors). `ui-audit/verify-new1-cloud-badge.mjs` **20/20** вАФ every state present and visually distinct, error is loud + click-to-Retry fires the handler, null renders nothing, and **a crashed badge falls back to the loud glyph (does NOT vanish)**. `ui-audit/verify-new1-header-integration.mjs` **5/5** вАФ the badge is wired into the **live** Row-1 header with a project open, shows the honest on-device state logged-out (not a fake green "synced"), and **survives switching modules** (Site вЖТ Markup hides it when nothing's loaded вЖТ back to Site restores it). Screenshots in `ui-audit/screens/new1-*.png`.

### B372 вАФ A deleted site reappears (delete not persisting) `[Site Planner]` (bug)  *(owner-reported 2026-06-22 from chat as "NEW-1"; first filed B366, renumbered **B372** вАФ a concurrent `main` (PR #277) took B366вАУB371 (GIS Site Analysis resilience + source registry) while this was in flight, so B372 is the real next free ID)*
`[x]` **Filed AND fixed + headless-verified + pushed the SAME session per STANDING RULE #1 (branch `claude/cool-ride-pm0m2l`).** Deleting the HOLLISTER site brought it back вАФ on a hard reload (path A) **and** mid-session with no reload (path B). Crash-severity per the silent-failure principle: a delete that looks successful in the UI but doesn't stick is silent data divergence.
- **ONE root cause for both paths (so kept as one item вАФ the owner said split only if path B were independent).** The site you delete from the map is, in the common case, the one you had **open**: opening it sets `activeSiteId`, and "Back to map" only flips the view вАФ the `SitePlanner` stays **mounted (hidden)**, keyed to that `activeSiteId`. Deleting it calls `deleteSiteGroup` вЖТ `setActiveSiteId(null)`, which **unmounts** that planner; its unmount cleanup `persistOrDrop()` (and the `beforeunload`/visibility flush + any queued debounced autosave) then ran `saveSite()` for the just-deleted id, **re-writing the row**. (a) The existing in-planner `deletedSelfRef` guard only covered the *single-plan* delete from inside the planner, NOT the map's whole-site delete. (b) **Path B:** the resurrected record sits in the local store and re-surfaces on the next `refreshSites()` (any mapвЖФplan nav). (c) **Path A:** on reload, `pullCloud`'s heal-the-split sees a local-only row the cloud is missing and **re-pushes it to the cloud**, making the resurrection permanent. This also explains "maybe it's just that project" вАФ it was the one he had open; sites never opened this session had no mounted planner to resurrect them.
- **Fix 1 вАФ kill the resurrection at the one chokepoint (`lib/storage.js`).** A per-tab session tombstone `recentlyDeleted` (Set): `deleteSite` adds the id; `saveSite` refuses to **re-create a deleted, currently-absent row** (`if (!existing && recentlyDeleted.has(id)) return false`). EVERY resurrection path (unmount persist, beforeunload/visibility flush, debounced autosave, a cross-tab storage echo) funnels through `saveSite`, so this closes all of them вАФ not just the one the bug surfaced. A normal edit-save (record still present) and a brand-new site (id never deleted) are untouched; `stageLegacySite`/`importOneSiteToCloud` lift the tombstone so a deliberate same-id re-import still works; it's per-tab and clears on reload (by then the delete has settled).
- **Fix 2 вАФ make a real cloud-delete failure LOUD (never a phantom success).** `cloudDelete` now uses `.delete(вА¶).select("id")` so a 0-row no-op (already gone, or an ownership/RLS mismatch) is distinguishable from a real removal, and a thrown/4xx error returns `{ok:false}`. `deleteSite` **returns** that promise; `deleteSiteGroup`/`deletePlan` AWAIT it, and on a genuine error show a red **"Couldn't delete вА¶ from the cloud вАФ it may reappear when you reload"** banner and **re-pull** so the list reflects the honest truth instead of a fake success. (Decision: a 0-row delete is treated as success, not an alarm вАФ a local-only site never pushed to the cloud legitimately removes 0 rows, so alarming on 0-row would cry wolf; RLS also means a row a user can *see* is a row they *can* delete. We alarm only on an actual error, which is the silent case that mattered. This refines the owner's literal "0 rows = failure" into the safer rule that won't false-alarm.)
- **Why the ownership-mismatch theory didn't pan out as the cause (checked first, as asked):** RLS `select` is `auth.uid() = user_id`, so a row visible in the list is owned by the current user вАФ a foreign-owned row would never appear to be deleted in the first place, and wouldn't return from `cloudList` on reload either. The real mechanism was the mounted-planner resurrection above. `cloudDelete` is still hardened to surface a true permission/network error loudly.
- **Verified (V102):** new `ui-audit/verify-b372-delete-durable.mjs` вАФ boots into the planner for HOLLISTER, returns to the map (planner stays mounted), deletes it, and asserts on the **store source-of-truth** + the rendered list: **6/6** (Chromium, logged-out, 0 page errors), incl. not-resurrected immediately, no mid-session reappearance after a list refresh, and still-gone after reload (Schiel preserved). **Proven to have teeth вАФ with the guard disabled the harness FAILS exactly as reported (`store ids = [s2,s1]`, card returns, survives reload).** Plus **9 new unit tests** (`test/deletePersistence.test.js`: `interpretDelete` row-count/error matrix + the end-to-end resurrection guard). **lint 0 ¬Ј build green ¬Ј `SitePlannerApp`/`DocReview` lazy chunks intact** (full suite re-run green post-merge).
- **Note for the signed-in tail:** the loud-banner path on a *genuine cloud-delete error* can't be driven logged-out (the sandbox CORS-blocks Supabase auth); its logic is unit-locked (`interpretDelete`) and the local resurrection (the actual bug) is fully headless-verified. A one-line signed-in confirm is noted in VERIFICATION V102, not owed from Michael.

Unit-locked in `test/siteAnalysis.test.js` + `test/gisSources.test.js`. lint 0 ¬Ј 1129 tests ¬Ј build green.

### B366 вАФ Screening resilience + honest error taxonomy (a 503 is not "CORS") `[Site Planner / Analysis]` (bug)  *(arrived as coworker-brief "NEW-1" 2026-06-21; minted **B366**)*
`[x]` **Fixed + verified 2026-06-22 (branch `claude/nice-cori-ghm37q`).** The screen fired ~8вАУ10 ArcGIS `/query` calls **all at once**; under that burst hosts (even Esri-hosted ones) returned transient **HTTP 503**, with **no retry** (one blip вЖТ permanent UNKNOWN) and **every** failure mislabeled "Couldn't reach the GIS server (network or CORS)" though CORS is fine on every endpoint. (A 503 whose error response lacks the CORS header surfaces to `fetch` as an opaque "Failed to fetch" вАФ which is exactly why the catch-all blamed CORS.)
- **New shared `lib/gisFetch.js`:** `fetchArcgisJson` = one resilient fetch вАФ **AbortController timeout** + **jittered exponential-backoff retry** (3 attempts) on a transient 5xx/429/network/timeout + automatic **GETвЖТPOST** when a dense-polygon URL gets over-long. `classifyGisError` вЖТ an honest `{kind, message, retryable}` taxonomy: `http-5xx`/`http-4xx`/`arcgis`/`timeout`/`network`/`offline` вАФ **never** a blind "CORS" (a bare "Failed to fetch" reads "couldn't reach / temporarily unavailable", since in-browser a header-less 503 is indistinguishable from a real CORS block and a retry usually clears it). `pLimit` concurrency limiter.
- **`runSiteAnalysis` now throttles the WHOLE fan-out** (environmental + jurisdiction + road) through ONE pool of **3** вАФ the burst that provoked the 503s is gone.
- **State machine:** new **`unavailable`** finding status (retryable; amber; a per-source **вЖї Retry** control), **visually + semantically distinct from `absent`/"None found"** вАФ a failure is NEVER read as clear (the silent-error guard). The honest reason (e.g. "HTTP 503 вАФ temporarily unavailable") is surfaced; jurisdiction/road use the same shared classifier.
- **Tests:** `test/gisFetch.test.js` (15 вАФ retry-then-succeed, give-up-after-budget, no-retry-4xx, arcgis-200-error-body, POST-for-long-URL, pool max-in-flight, honest-not-CORS). Live headless `gis-verify/site-analysis-resilience-verify.mjs` **11/11** (V101): forced-503 вЖТ honest "503", Retry present, 0 "network or CORS", 0 page errors. lint 0 ¬Ј build green.

### B367 вАФ GIS screening cache: keep last-good on a failed refresh + data age (stale-while-revalidate) `[Site Planner / Analysis]` (feature)  *(arrived as coworker-brief "NEW-2" 2026-06-21 вАФ the existing roadmap "GIS layer caching" item; minted **B367**. Phase 2 = B371, Later.)*
`[x]` **Phase 1 done + verified 2026-06-22 (branch `claude/nice-cori-ghm37q`).** Folds the long-standing roadmap "#1 GIS layer caching" detail into the screen and builds on the existing SWR cache (B96). A transient source outage must never **blank** a layer.
- **Behavior:** `analyzeSource` now KEEPS the last-good copy when a refresh fails вАФ the finding stays `present`/`absent` (its real last value) flagged **`stale` + `refreshError`**, and the panel shows "**вЯ≥ Showing the last good result (as of <date>) вАФ couldn't refresh: <reason>**" rather than downgrading to UNAVAILABLE or blanking. Only a failure with **no** cached copy is a hard UNAVAILABLE. Every result already carries its data-age + a screening-only caveat (generalized from the Floodplain "last-good" UI to all rows).
- **Tests:** `test/siteAnalysis.test.js` "a failed REFRESH keeps the last-good copy (stale, not blanked)"; headless V101 ages the cache past TTL then forces a 503 вЖТ flood/wetlands show last-good + "couldn't refresh", uncached RRC rows show honest 503. lint 0 ¬Ј build green.
- **Phase 2 (deferred вЖТ B371, Later):** a regional Houston-metro snapshot/offline pre-cache so a never-seen parcel resolves offline. Heavier (storage + refresh job); gated behind this Phase 1 per the brief.

### B369 вАФ GIS Source Registry + verification harness (stop shipping test / non-authoritative endpoints) `[Site Planner / Platform]` (feature / infra)  *(arrived as coworker-brief "NEW-4" 2026-06-21; minted **B369**. Map-display-layer migration tail = B370, Open.)*
`[x]` **Done + verified 2026-06-22 (branch `claude/nice-cori-ghm37q`).** Answers the owner's "why do we keep mapping to test / non-final places?" вАФ two failure modes now have a machine guard: **(1)** we mis-wire it (NWI on `/Test/`, Wells/Pipelines on a Harris republication) and **(2)** agencies move/rename/retire services.
- **Registry** `src/shared/gis/sources.js` вАФ ONE versioned source of truth: per row `key, label, provider, serviceUrl, layerId, geometryType, fields, coverage, tier, lastVerified, fixtures`. The screen (`siteAnalysis.js`) + jurisdiction identify (`jurisdiction.js`) now read EVERY endpoint from here вАФ **zero inline service URLs** in the analysis path.
- **Tier/lint guard (CI вАФ blocks merge):** `ui-audit/gis-source-audit.mjs` + `test/gisSources.test.js` fail the build on a `/Test/`,`/staging/`,`geogimstest`,вА¶ URL that isn't an acknowledged **`monitored-exception`** (the only one is Wetlands, locked down), or if an endpoint is re-inlined in the analysis connectors. Wired as a named step in `build.yml`.
- **Coverage / authority fixtures (the centerpiece вАФ what catches 14-vs-8,014):** each row carries known-truth assertions (Chambers wells вЙ• 1000, Mont Belvieu well вЙ• 1, вА¶); `gis-verify/gis-source-coverage-verify.mjs` checks reachability + that every `outField` still exists on the live layer (schema-drift catch) + the coverage minimums. **Verified in-sandbox** against FEMA/NWI/TxGIO/TxDOT (all pass); RRC rows run in CI (host not on the sandbox allow-list).
- **Drift detection + alerting:** `.github/workflows/gis-drift.yml` re-runs the live verify **weekly**; on any regression it opens/bumps a single **@claude** GitHub issue with the report (auto-closes when green).
- **Runtime fallback chain (#6):** a row may carry `fallbacks`; `analyzeSource` tries the mirror before failing, then the SWR cache (B367) вАФ degrading honestly (B366 taxonomy). Tests: `test/gisSources.test.js` (10) + `test/gisFetch.test.js`. lint 0 ¬Ј 1129 tests ¬Ј build green.

### B365 вАФ Redesign project-status map markers for correct visual hierarchy `[Site Planner]` (feature)  *(arrived as cross-chat "NEW-1" 2026-06-21; first filed **B362**, renumbered **B365** вАФ a concurrent `main` took B362вАУB364 (bump-out resize, bonded-child rotation, scanned/DWG reading) while this was in flight, so B365 is the real next free ID)*
`[x]` **Filed AND shipped + headless-verified the SAME session per STANDING RULE #1 (branch `claude/trusting-cori-rkn2x3`).** The status markers inverted the hierarchy вАФ Pursuit (most important) was a thin **dashed cool-blue hollow outline** that vanished into the aerial, while settled Complete shouted. Fixed so salience now tracks importance: **Pursuit = eye-magnet, Complete = recessive.**
- **One source of truth (already existed вАФ extended, not duplicated).** `src/shared/ui/statusTokens.js` (`STATUS_TOKENS`/`statusToken`, the B234 set shared by map pins, list rows, filter chips, group headers, and the status menu) is the single map the item asked for. ### B364 вАФ Mobile: pinch-zoom crash ("null is not an object вА¶ .mid") + multi-tab banner falsely nagging logged-out users `[App Shell / Site Planner / Doc Review]` (bug)  *(owner-reported 2026-06-21 from a mobile screenshot: opened on phone, "moved around for a sec" вЖТ Site Planner error boundary fired; **separately** a "open in another tab" banner appeared though he wasn't signed in and shouldn't carry cross-session state.)*
`[x]` **Fixed + verified 2026-06-21 (branch `claude/mobile-session-state-bug-omeec4`).**
- **Crash root cause:** the two-finger pinch handler (`applyPinch`, B331) read `pinchRef.current.mid` *inside* the `setView` updater. On mobile a finger can lift between scheduling the update and React running the updater вАФ `reseedPinch` nulls `pinchRef.current` вАФ so the deferred updater dereferenced null (`null is not an object (evaluating 'вА¶вАЛ.current.mid')`) and the workspace's error boundary showed "Site Planner hit an error and couldn't load." **Fix:** snapshot `pinchRef.current` into a local before `setView` in **both** `SitePlanner.jsx` and `doc-review/DocReview.jsx`, so the updater uses the captured baseline and can't hit null.
- **Multi-tab banner root cause / scope:** the B313 same-project-in-another-tab warning fired for **logged-out** sessions too, where it's just a false mobile nag (the banner exists to protect saved *cloud* work, not anonymous device-only browsing). **Fix:** gated to signed-in accounts only вАФ new `accountActive` prop on `AppHeader` (defaults off) plumbed `Shell (!!user) вЖТ SitePlannerApp/SitePlanner/DocReview/Scheduler вЖТ AppHeader`; presence is fed a null project and the banner is suppressed when logged out. Logged-out = fresh, quiet.
- **Tests:** `test/multiTab.test.js` (10) still green (pure protocol unchanged); `ui-audit/verify-multitab.mjs` rewritten to assert the new behavior (two logged-out tabs on the same project вЖТ **no** banner in either) вАФ **3/3 (V99)**. build green.

### B362 вАФ Bump-out (dog-ear) resize doesn't persist; reverts to the 55вА≤√Ч60вА≤ default on any host refit `[Site Planner]` (bug)  *(arrived as coworker-chat "NEW-1" 2026-06-21, confirmed live on project **Jacintoport** вАФ cloud site `smqdxst8pf3g`, bump-outs `e8986`/`e8987` both stuck at default 60√Ч55. First filed **B357**; renumbered **B362** вАФ a concurrent `main` (#268/#269) took B357вАУB361 (Markup header de-clutter + Scheduler) while this was in flight, so this is the real next free ID. **Folds in** the long-deferred triage item "building bump-outs aren't clamped when the host shrinks" вАФ now closed here.)*
`[x]` **Fixed + verified 2026-06-21 (branch `claude/festive-newton-90t0zh`, PR #271).**
- **Repro:** select a building bump-out, resize it, then resize/edge-drag/numerically-resize the host вЖТ the bump snapped back to 55вА≤√Ч60вА≤. **Root cause:** a dog-ear stored no size of its own вАФ `dogEarGeom` always recomputed w/h from the constants `DOGEAR_W`/`DOGEAR_D`, and `refitChildren`вЖТ`fitDogEar`вЖТ`dogEarGeom` ran for every dog-ear on each host resize, discarding the user's dimensions.
- **Fix:** extracted the bump geometry to a pure, unit-tested **`lib/dogEar.js`** (`dogEarGeom`/`dogEarSize` + the defaults). A resized bump now **records its span along the dock wall + its projection** (`along`/`proj`) on its `dogEar` tag (captured in `refitChildren` the moment the bump is the resized element); `fitDogEar` re-anchors **position + host angle only**, preserving the stored size. The along-span is **CLAMPED to the wall вАФ never reset** вАФ when the host shrinks past the corner (closes the deferred "not clamped" item), and **springs back** when the host grows again. Knock-on correctness: the **dock-door layout** now avoids a bump by its actual span (not a flat 55вА≤), and the **yield panel** says "N bump-outs ¬Ј sizes vary" instead of falsely claiming "55вА≤√Ч60вА≤" once a bump is resized.
- **Schema:** `SITE_MODEL_VERSION` 6вЖТ7; the new `along`/`proj` fields ride inside `els`, lossless/idempotent through `createSiteModel` (absent вЗТ the 55вА≤√Ч60вА≤ default, so every existing bump is unaffected).
- **Tests:** new `test/dogEar.test.js` (5) вАФ default 55√Ч60 + flush-at-corner, the `dogEarSize` inverse, **the exact repro (resize bump вЖТ resize host вЖТ size preserved)**, clamp-then-spring-back on host shrink, host-rotation carry. Coordinated with B363 (resize re-syncs angle *without* resetting size). **lint 0 ¬Ј 1066 tests ¬Ј build green ¬Ј `SitePlannerApp` lazy chunk intact.** Live: `ui-audit/verify-b362-b363.mjs` 6/6 (V98).

### B363 вАФ Bonded children (bump-outs, court, sidewalk) keep a stale rotation when the host is re-angled `[Site Planner]` (bug)  *(arrived as coworker-chat "NEW-2" 2026-06-21, confirmed live on **Jacintoport** вАФ host `e8984` at rot 0¬∞ but all four bonded children (`e8985` court, `e8986`/`e8987` bump-outs, `e8988` sidewalk) at 359.035¬∞, the whole assembly ~1¬∞ off the building. First filed **B358**; renumbered **B363** вАФ `main` #268/#269 took B357вАУB361 in flight.)*
`[x]` **Fixed + verified 2026-06-21 (branch `claude/festive-newton-90t0zh`, PR #271).**
- **Root cause:** a bonded child's rotation was only copied from the host at create/refit time (`dogEarGeom`/`makeStrip`/`oppTrailerGeom` set `rot: host.rot`); the only thing that re-copied it was `refitChildren`, which runs on host **resize only**. So any state where child rot вЙ† host rot вАФ a host placed at a parcel-bearing angle, children added, the host later straightened by a path that didn't carry them вАФ was left visibly off-angle until the next resize.
- **Fix (1) вАФ derived invariant, re-applied on ANY host geometry change.** A bonded box child's angle is now a derived value: `host.rot` + its fixed quarter-turn offset (0/90/180/270 вАФ sidewalks/courts/bump-outs share the host angle; side-parking/wall-trailers sit at a +90/180/270 turn). A shared pure `bondedChildRot`/`quarterOffset` (`siteModel.js`) + a `resyncBondedRot` pass is now folded into **every** host-geometry path вАФ resize (`refitChildren`) **and** rotate (`rotateAssemblyTo` *and* the rotate-handle drag) вАФ so a child can no longer be stranded off-angle (previously only resize re-synced, and only some child types).
- **Fix (2) вАФ one-time repair in migrate.** `normalizeBondedRotations` runs inside `createSiteModel` (the migrate path вЖТ fires on every load), re-anchoring a drifted child to the host's **current** frame: its angle snaps to `host.rot + offset` **and** its centre is rotated about the host centre by the stale delta (a host straightened without its children leaves their *positions* stale too, not just the angle value). **Idempotent + identity-preserving** for already-correct data; safe because a bonded box child is only ever at a quarter turn, so any other angle is drift, not intent (points-based children skipped). This **repairs Jacintoport and any other already-diverged project the moment it's opened**, and persists on the next save.
- **Coordinated with B362:** `refitChildren` captures the bump size **before** the rotation resync, and resync only touches `rot` вАФ so re-syncing a child's angle never resets a resized bump.
- **Schema:** `SITE_MODEL_VERSION` 6вЖТ7 (shared with B362).
- **Tests:** new `test/bondedRotation.test.js` (6) вАФ the quarter-turn offset math, **the full Jacintoport repair (rot AND position re-anchored)**, idempotency + identity-preservation on correct data, points-children skipped, version-bump guard. **lint 0 ¬Ј 1066 tests ¬Ј build green.** Live: `ui-audit/verify-b362-b363.mjs` 6/6 (V98) вАФ drifted assembly straightens on load, user-sized bump keeps 80√Ч70 across a save/load round-trip.

### B358 вАФ Truthful save "cloud" chip вАФ kill the "Not saved" cry-wolf `[Doc Review / Markup]` (bug)  *(parallel-branch handoff "NEW-2" 2026-06-21; minted **B358**)*
`[x]` **Fixed + verified 2026-06-21 (branch `claude/hopeful-dirac-aqjlqb`).** The owner's "the cloud for files is fucked up" was the save badge in **`ReviewsBar`** (the handoff guessed `ProjectBreadcrumb` вАФ the breadcrumb only ever shows an at-risk вЪ†; the actual badge is in ReviewsBar, confirmed against the tree). It rendered **"Not saved" with nothing open / nothing to save** вАФ a flag that cries wolf trains the eye to ignore the one state that matters; it also had no `conflict` state (B314 conflicts fell through to "Not saved"). Replaced with a **truthful little cloud chip** driven by one pure `chipFor(status, signedIn, idle)`: **idle (nothing to save) вЖТ no chip at all**; **saving** вЖТ cloud-вЖС + "SavingвА¶" (pulsing amber); **unsaved** вЖТ cloud-вЖС "Unsaved"; **conflict** вЖТ cloud-вЬХ "Sync conflict" (loud red, never silent); **saved OR signed-in** (cloud-backed, mirroring the Site Planner's "Synced вЬУ") вЖТ calm green cloud-вЬУ "Saved"; **signed-out with content** вЖТ honest "On this device" (a monitor glyph вАФ saved here, can't sync), not a false "Not saved". Colors are theme tokens (legible in light/dark per B341). Headless (logged-out): empty Markup shows **no** save chip; once a PDF is open it reads "On this device". The signed-in "Saved"/`saving`/`conflict` states (sandbox blocks sign-in) are locked by `test/reviewsBadge.test.js` (7 truth-table tests). `components/ReviewsBar.jsx`. **NB:** the separate **"Cloud off"** pill (Shell `authControl`) is a *different* indicator вАФ it only appears when Supabase isn't configured for the build (so it shows in the sandbox preview); on a cloud-configured planyr.io it's the account/Sign-in pill. Left as-is per the handoff's "don't conflate"; if it's visible in production, the cloud env vars aren't wired into that deploy (a config item, not this code).

### B360 вАФ Move "Reviews" out of Row 1 into the Markup tools row `[Doc Review / Markup]` (task)  *(parallel-branch handoff "NEW-4" 2026-06-21; minted **B360**)*
`[x]` **Done + verified 2026-06-21 (branch `claude/hopeful-dirac-aqjlqb`).** `ReviewsBar` was mounted in `AppHeader`'s Row-1 `saveSlot` (only DocReview fills it вАФ it was never cross-module). Moved `<ReviewsBar>` into Row 2's `toolbarContent`, beside Open PDF / Stitch; its (now truthful, B358) save chip rides with it. DocReview's `saveSlot` is now empty вАФ correct, not a regression. Wiring (status/signedIn/meta/onMeta/onOpen/onNew, + new `idle={isEmpty()}`) unchanged. Markup-scoped (Site/Schedule untouched). Headless: the "Reviews" button now resolves inside Row 2 (index 1), not Row 1.
### B356 вАФ Invisible site-name in the header + a whole-app sweep so it can't happen elsewhere `[App / Theming]` (bug)  *(owner-reported 2026-06-21: "I can't see the project name here вА¶ it's gray text on their gray background вА¶ go through the entire site and check the rest so this doesn't happen"; filed **B355** but renumbered **B356** вАФ a concurrent `main` (#265, lettered plan concepts) took B355 while this was in flight, so this is the real next free ID)*
`[x]` **Fixed + headless-verified BOTH themes 2026-06-21 (branch `claude/gallant-mccarthy-k6sqmr`).** Root cause was the B341 theme-flip trap again: the Site Planner **site-name button hardcoded white text** вАФ `hdrTab(12.5, "#fff", 600)` вАФ on chrome that now themes light, so white-on-near-white was invisible. `contrast-audit.mjs` couldn't catch it because it only checks the **token pairs defined in `index.css`**, and this colour was a literal passed into a style helper (invisible to a `color:` grep, too).
- **Headline fix:** site-name вЖТ `PAL.chromeInk` (theme-aware). The same trap also hit the **signed-out "Sign in" avatar** (white "вАЇ" on the light pill вЖТ `var(--chrome-text)` on `var(--chrome-bg)`) and the **"current" marker** in the site/plan switcher menus (plain accent on the soft-accent fill = 3.8:1 вЖТ a new theme-aware `accentStrong`, 7.3:1 light / bright in dark). Also made `ModuleLoader` theme-aware (was `#6b7280` on a hardcoded `#f6f8fa`, 4.26:1).
- **Whole-app sweep (the owner's real ask):** new `ui-audit/contrast-sweep.mjs` walks the **rendered DOM** of every workspace in **both themes**, reading each text node's computed colour vs its effective (first opaque ancestor) background, compositing alpha, applying the AA floor by size/weight. Catches colours set ANY way (helpers, inheritance) вАФ which static analysis cannot. It found exactly the avatar + "current" issues; all now green.
- **Dark-theme hardening:** the sweep + a contrast calc showed **every hardcoded semantic colour** (`#b45309` amber, `#b3361b`/`#b91c1c` red, `#15803d` green, `#0e7490` teal, `#7c3aed` purple, `#1d4ed8` blue) fails AA on a **dark panel** (2.2вАУ3.4:1) while passing on a light one. Added theme-aware **`--success-text` / `--danger-text` / `--info-text`** tokens (+ palette.js mirror; `--warn-text` already existed) and rerouted the semantic TEXT that sits on **themed** panels (SitePlanner inspector, DocReview takeoff + drop-zone, LayerPanel, SiteAnalysis findings, MapFinder status menu) to them. **Left untouched (correct):** fixed-light-banner text, **fixed-`#fff` panels** (Stitcher + Project Files/Library drawers вАФ self-consistent + readable; their not-theming-to-dark is a separate cosmetic item), and SVG/map data-colour tables. **SiteReviewModal** (a fixed-dark modal) had its own too-dim subtitles (`#4a6080` 2.5:1) lightened to AA on its dark bg.
- **Guards:** the 3 new tokens are registered in `contrast-audit.mjs` (8 new pairs, all PASS both themes) so a palette edit can't silently re-introduce a low-contrast pair; `contrast-sweep.mjs` is the runtime net for the helper/inheritance class the static audit can't see.
- **Verified (V96):** `contrast-sweep.mjs` вЖТ **0 low-contrast elements** in planner / site-menu / Markup / Schedule, **light AND dark**; `contrast-audit.mjs` all pairs PASS; **1041 unit tests**; lint **0 errors**; build green; screenshots show "Katy Logistics Park" clearly visible in both themes.

### B354 вАФ Markup yield panel miscounts redline annotations as "uncalibrated measurements" `[Doc Review / Markup]` (bug)  *(owner chat 2026-06-21 "keep going" вАФ Markup-tool stress test; minted **B354** вАФ next free after B353)*
`[x]` **Fixed + verified 2026-06-21 (branch `claude/stitch-tool-stress-test-1tvw5b`).** Stress-testing the Markup yield panel turned up a real miscount. The panel warns **"N measurement(s) on uncalibrated sheets are excluded"** from `rollup(markups, calByPage)` вАФ but `rollup` was handed the WHOLE markup list (measurements **and** redline annotations: rect / cloud / line / arrow / text), and any non-measurement kind on an *uncalibrated* sheet fell into `measureValue`'s generic branch (`calibrated:false`) and incremented `uncal`. So drawing a redline cloud or adding a text note on an uncalibrated sheet made the panel falsely warn "1 measurement(s) вА¶ excluded" when **zero** measurements were made (and could mislead a reviewer into thinking a real takeoff was dropped). `rollup` now tallies **only** the measurement kinds (`distance/perimeter/area/count`, derived from the existing `MIN_MEASURE_PTS` so there's one source of truth) and skips everything else (and null entries) outright. Totals were already correct (redlines never matched the area/perimeter/distance branches); only the `uncal` warning was wrong. `lib/takeoff.js`. **New `test/markupRollupStress.test.js` вАФ 6 adversarial tests** (redlines don't inflate `uncal`; redlines on a calibrated sheet aren't summed; a true uncalibrated measurement still counts; all four measure kinds total correctly; null/unknown-kind entries don't crash; a non-finite page calibration excludes the measure). Existing 16 takeoff tests still green; full suite **994 tests**, lint 0 errors, build clean. Pure-logic fix вАФ no live-browser verification needed.
