### B350 вАФ Stitcher: aggregated notes/legend across the set + Bluebeam-style detail-callout "cloud" `[Doc Review / Stitch]` (feature)  *(owner chat 2026-06-21 "make it great on all the other stuff"; minted **B350**)*
`[x]` **Built + headless-verified 2026-06-21.** Two upgrades to the stitch tool, both backed by pure shared readers so they're unit-tested away from pdf.js:
- **Notes/legend, captured across the whole set (never lost to the crop).** The auto-stitch crop (B338) hides each sheet's title-block band вАФ where the **general notes / legend** usually live. A new pure reader `src/shared/files/sheetNotes.js` (`parseNotes` finds each `GENERAL/GRADING/KEYED NOTES`, `LEGEND`, `ABBREVIATIONS` block; `aggregateNotes` merges every placed sheet's blocks, **dedupes** repeated boilerplate, and **flags a note that didn't appear on every sheet** with the sheet(s) it came from вАФ so a note that **changes page to page** is surfaced, not buried). Wired into `readSheetMeta` (each page now carries `notes`) and shown in the pinned **Composite key** as an expandable "Notes & legend ¬Ј N" section.
- **Click a detail reference вЖТ the detail pops up as a "cloud" (Bluebeam-style).** A new pure reader `src/shared/files/detailRefs.js` reads detail-callout **bubbles** (a detail id stacked over a sheet code вАФ "5 / A-3" вАФ plus inline `5/A-3` and `SEE DETAIL 5 ON SHEET A-3` forms; conservative вАФ a plain fraction can't match) and where details are **defined** (`DETAIL 5`, `SECTION A-A`). Each callout renders as a clickable hotspot ring on the placed sheet; clicking it **pulls up that detail in a floating cloud popup** that renders the referenced sheet (reused from a placed sheet, or rendered on demand from a loaded PDF), **centered on the named detail** when the target sheet labels it вАФ pan/zoomable, so you never leave the current drawing. Honest fallback: a target that isn't in the set yet says so. New toolbar **Details** toggle; hotspots only grab clicks in Pan mode (measure/align/calibrate pass through).
- **Persistence:** placed sheets now carry `sheetNumber`/`detailRefs`/`detailAnchors`/`notes` through save/load. **Scope:** all inside the doc-review workspace; lazy chunk split intact. **Tests:** 14 new unit tests (`test/detailRefs.test.js` 8, `test/sheetNotes.test.js` 6); full suite green (1029 with main folded in); lint 0 errors; build green. **Headless:** `ui-audit/verify-b350.mjs` 11/11 (notes aggregated + the C-5-only note flagged; the "5/A-3" hotspot opens a "Detail 5 ¬Ј Sheet A-3" cloud rendering the A-3 sheet) + `verify-b335-b339.mjs` 13/13 no-regression.
### B352 вАФ Scanned-sheet OCR: read image-only drawings into the auto-assembly pipeline `[Doc Review / Stitch]` (feature)  *(owner-requested 2026-06-21 right after B335вАУB339: "Add ocr capabilities if I don't have that"; minted **B352** вАФ was B340's OCR tail; a very hot `main` (B341вАУB351 + V88вАУV92) consumed every earlier number this session)*
`[x]` **Shipped + verified 2026-06-21 (branch `claude/loving-newton-t7gzpq`).** Fills the dormant OCR seam B336/B337 left wired, so a **scanned / image-only** drawing (no text layer) now reads, groups, stitches, crops, and auto-calibrates through the SAME pipeline as a vector PDF.
- **How:** `doc-review/lib/ocr.js` renders a no-text page to a canvas (`renderPageToOcrCanvas`, pdf.js, density-capped вЙ§24 MP) and runs **Tesseract.js** (WASM, in its own worker) to recover the text **with per-word bounding boxes**, then `wordsToItems` converts those boxes into the exact `{ str, x, y, w, h }` page-unit items `sheetMeta.readSheetMeta` (B336) already consumes вАФ so OCR'd pages feed the title-block/scale/match-line reader identically. Low-confidence words are dropped (consistent with "never auto-guess").
- **Lazy + cheap on the common path:** `createOcrRunner` only spins up the worker when a no-text page is actually hit (a normal vector set pays nothing); the Tesseract orchestrator is a separate ~16 KB chunk and the WASM core + English model load from a pinned CDN (jsDelivr вАФ reachable from Cloudflare Pages) only on first use, then browser-cached. The drawing's pixels never leave the browser. The Stitcher shows a "Reading scanned sheet (OCR)вА¶" status while it runs.
- **Verified:** **7 unit tests** (`test/ocr.test.js` вАФ the bboxвЖТpage-unit conversion, lazy single-worker reuse + dispose, fail-soft, and a scanned title block flowing through `readSheetMeta` to the right sheet number / title / scale / match-line) **+ a LIVE headless run** (`ui-audit/verify-b352-ocr.mjs`, **V93**): the real Tesseract engine loads from jsDelivr in Chromium and reads a "scanned" title block + match line вАФ "GRADING PLAN / SHEET NO. C-5 / SCALE: 1\"=40' / MATCH LINE - SEE SHEET C-6" вАФ recovering C-5, the title, the 40-scale, and the C-6 target. lint 0 ¬Ј full suite green ¬Ј build green; DocReview lazy chunk intact, Tesseract split into its own on-demand chunk. **OCR-path stress-hardened the same session вАФ see the B352 stress addendum below.**
> **Dedup:** this is B340's OCR tail, pulled forward on owner request; B340 keeps the 3 remaining computer-vision tails (graphic scale-bar, geometric edge-match, legend symbol-union). Distinct + complementary to main's stitch-engine stress-tests and Stitcher-component bug sweeps (this session) вАФ those predate OCR and never touch `ocr.js`.

**Stress addendum (owner: "stress test it") вАФ B352.** Adversarial pass over the OCR layer (the stitch-engine stress tests predate OCR and didn't cover it). It turned up + fixed one real **non-finite poison** (the same class the engine stress-test fixed in `stitchGeom`): a **non-finite bbox coordinate** (NaN/¬±Infinity вАФ which a noisy scan can emit) slipped past `wordsToItems`' `x1 <= x0` guard (`NaN <= NaN` is `false`), pushing a NaN item that would poison the whole reader (title-block density вЖТ NaN, line sort вЖТ undefined). `wordsToItems` now requires all four box coords **finite** + the box non-inverted, guards a 0/NaN/negative/Infinity render scale and non-finite page dims, and coerces non-string OCR text. New `test/ocrStress.test.js` вАФ **15 tests** across malformed boxes, broken Tesseract shapes (`extractWords`), every orchestration failure (render/recognize/worker-creation throw вЖТ null; all-low-confidence вЖТ graceful no-text record), the OCRвЖТ`readSheetMeta`вЖТgrouping integration (a garbage scan stays standalone; an unreadable number isn't force-merged; clean scans group through NaN noise), and a **300-iteration randomized fuzz** asserting no non-finite item ever leaks and `readSheetMeta` always returns a finite [0,1] confidence. **LIVE stress** (`ui-audit/verify-b352-ocr.mjs`, 9/9): the real engine reads a clean scan AND вАФ the dangerous case вАФ emits **0 words on a blank page and on pure noise (no hallucinated sheet number/title)**, and a small-font degraded render doesn't throw. Full suite **959 tests**, lint 0, build clean.

### B351 вАФ Auto-filing matcher: close two browser-path MISFILE vectors `[Doc Review / Auto-file]` (bug)  *(owner chat 2026-06-21 "keep going" вАФ stress-testing adjacent to the stitch tool; minted **B351** вАФ next free after B350)*
`[x]` **Fixed + verified 2026-06-21 (branch `claude/stitch-tool-stress-test-1tvw5b`).** Continuing the "stress-test / look up how to break things" pass into the auto-filing project matcher (same risk class as the stitcher: **a misfile is worse than an unfiled file**). The browser matcher (`matchProject.js` `scoreProjectInText`) searches the sheet's raw text, so it had two false-positive vectors the server twin (`server/filing/matcher.js`, which compares *extracted fields* with exact equality) avoids by construction вАФ both could **auto-route a drawing onto the wrong project**:
- **Short IDs matched as a substring of the separator-stripped whole document** вАФ `normId(wholeText).includes(id)` matched a 4-digit job / 6-digit parcel number as a coincidental substring spanning unrelated words (e.g. job `"1045"` inside `"вА¶210455вА¶"`, or a parcel inside a longer run). Now matched by **boundary-aligned equality** against `idWindows` (the normId of each run of вЙ§5 *adjacent* tokens), so a real id split by punctuation/space (`1234567-000-001`, `1234567 000 001`, `KG-2025`) still matches but a coincidental digit run can't manufacture a confident match.
- **Scattered name words scored 0.8 (auto-filed)** вАФ a 2-word common name like *Katy Grand* whose words merely appear *somewhere* on an unrelated Katy-area / Grand-Parkway sheet auto-routed there. A full-**phrase** hit still scores 0.9 (auto-files), but a scattered all-words hit now scores **0.55 вАФ below the 0.6 auto-file floor**, so it can corroborate another signal via noisy-or but never auto-route by itself ("never auto-guess").
- Also hardened `scoreProjectInText` to tolerate a `null` entry in the projects list (the `= {}` default only caught `undefined`).
- **Untouched:** the shared `decide()` thresholds (`minConfidence 0.6` / `minMargin 0.15`) вАФ only the client-specific text-search *scoring method* changed, so the decision contract stays in parity with the server matcher. **New `test/matchProjectStress.test.js` вАФ 11 adversarial tests** (substring-id rejection + real split-id recall, scattered-name-no-autofile + phrase recall + corroborated match, empty/junk/ambiguous/huge-blob/malformed-input). Existing 8 matcher tests still green; full suite **968 tests**, lint 0 errors, build clean. (Auto-filing is gated dormant behind `VITE_AUTOFILE_ENABLED`, so this is precision hardening on a not-yet-lit path вАФ no production behavior change.)

     fixed + headless-verified (`ui-audit/verify-stitch-bugs.mjs` now 14/14, incl. these two). -->

### B348 вАФ Inline Calibrate box detaches from its line on wheel-zoom `[Doc Review / Stitch]` (bug)  *(owner chat 2026-06-21 "look for more"; minted **B348**)*
`[x]` **Fixed + verified 2026-06-21.** The Calibrate entry box stored its screen position **once** (computed at open time). `onDown` blocks pan while it's open, but `onWheel` is NOT blocked вАФ so zooming to read the drawing while typing the known length left the box stranded away from its two-point line. The box now derives its screen position from the stored **world** points via the live pan/zoom each render (`calPos`), so it tracks the line under any zoom. `Stitcher.jsx` (`doCalibrate` stores points only; render computes `calPos`). Headless confirmed the box follows a wheel-zoom.

### B349 вАФ Composite key shows a meaningless "N units/ft" instead of the drawing scale `[Doc Review / Stitch]` (bug, minor)  *(owner chat 2026-06-21 "look for more"; minted **B349**)*
`[x]` **Fixed + verified 2026-06-21.** The pinned composite key read `Scale set ¬Ј {round(1/ftPerUnit)} units/ft` вАФ i.e. **page-points per foot** (~2 for a 1"=40' sheet), which reads as nonsense to a reviewer. Since the world frame is always identity-scale (world unit = page point), `ftPerUnit √Ч 72` is the real **feet per paper inch**, so the key now reads `Scale set ¬Ј 1" вЙИ 40'` вАФ the engineer's scale the reviewer recognises. `Stitcher.jsx` composite-key readout. Headless confirmed `1" вЙИ 40'` for the auto-calibrated set and that `units/ft` is gone.

### B343 вАФ Stitcher tray hides a file whose grouping failed (its pages become unreachable) `[Doc Review / Stitch]` (bug)  *(owner chat 2026-06-21; first filed B341, renumbered **B343** вАФ main #244 took B341/B342)*
`[x]` **Fixed + verified 2026-06-21.** The background readвЖТgroup (B335) sets a file's `groups` to `[]` on any read exception. The tray's grouped view rendered `p.groups.map(...)` вЖТ **zero entries**, so a file that failed to group showed nothing and the user had no way to add its pages (the "all pages" toggle was their only escape, with no hint it was needed). Now a file is shown in grouped mode only when its read produced **вЙ•1 logical sheet** (`hasGroups`); an empty/failed group result falls back to the raw per-page list for that file (groupSheets always yields вЙ•1 run for a readable page, so empty == failure). `Stitcher.jsx` `trayItems`/`anyGroups`.

### B344 вАФ Removing the world-frame (index-0) stitch sheet strands a leftover un-aligned sheet `[Doc Review / Stitch]` (bug)  *(owner chat 2026-06-21; first filed B342, renumbered **B344** вАФ main #244 took B341/B342)*
`[x]` **Fixed + verified 2026-06-21.** The first placed sheet is the world frame (`aligned:true`); the Align button + "Not aligned" chip are gated on `i > 0`. Removing the frame promoted a still-`aligned:false` sheet to index 0, where it **lost its Align button yet stayed measurement-blocked** (`measureOverUnaligned`) вАФ an unrecoverable stuck state (measuring errored "Align that sheetвА¶" with no Align affordance). New `removeSheet` helper promotes the new first sheet to the frame (`aligned:true`) on removal, restoring the "index-0 is the frame" invariant. Also guarded `onDown`'s align path against a sheet removed mid-align (was a `sheet.M` null deref). Headless: add frame + un-aligned sheet вЖТ remove frame вЖТ survivor is framed, no stranded "Not aligned".

### B345 вАФ Stitcher ¬± zoom buttons anchor on the world origin, not the viewport centre `[Doc Review / Stitch]` (bug, minor)  *(owner chat 2026-06-21; first filed B343, renumbered **B345**)*
`[x]` **Fixed + verified 2026-06-21.** The wheel zoom is cursor-anchored (shared `zoomAround`, B329) but the ¬± buttons just scaled `view.zoom` with pan untouched, so content slid toward the top-left corner on every click (cf. the single-sheet B290). New `zoomBtn(factor)` routes the ¬± buttons through `zoomAround` about the **viewport centre**. Headless confirmed a fixed point's offset from centre scales ~1.2√Ч per click.

### B346 вАФ Stitcher distance read-outs round to whole feet (inconsistent with area's 2-dp acres) `[Doc Review / Stitch]` (bug, minor)  *(owner chat 2026-06-21; first filed B344, renumbered **B346** вАФ the stitch counterpart of B296)*
`[x]` **Fixed + verified 2026-06-21.** B296 gave the single-sheet tool one-decimal linear feet, but the Stitcher's on-canvas distance label and the "Distance" takeoff total still used whole-foot `f0` (a 150.6 ft line read "151 ft"). Added `f1` and used it for both. Headless confirmed a decimal-foot read-out.

### B347 вАФ Seeded auto-stitch fallback gives no endpoint-order cue (reverse clicks flip the sheet 180¬∞) `[Doc Review / Stitch]` (bug)  *(owner chat 2026-06-21; first filed B345, renumbered **B347**)*
`[x]` **Fixed + verified 2026-06-21.** When auto-stitch (B337) can't place a sheet but knows its seam side, manual Align is **pre-seeded** with the moving sheet's two seam endpoints (`detectedEndpointsFor`) and the user clicks the two matching points on a placed sheet. Nothing showed WHICH seed was "first" vs "second", so clicking the matching points in reverse order silently rotated the sheet 180¬∞ via `solveM`. The seeded flow now draws **numbered markers (1, 2)** at the moving sheet's seed endpoints (its current position), so the click order is unambiguous. Additive render only; no geometry change.

from its title block (e.g. "C-5 вАФ GRADING PLAN", "COVER SHEET"), not generic "Sheet N". Built on #242's
shared reader (`sheetMeta.readSheetMeta` вАФ which locates the title-block band first, so a "SEE SHEET X"
cross-ref or a detail/grid ref can't masquerade as the sheet number, the crux this item called out).

label). OCR for scanned sheets stays the shared remaining slice (tracked under B267 + #242's dormant OCR

### B341 вАФ Stress-test the drawing stitch tool: harden the auto-stitch against bad PDF sets `[Doc Review / Stitch]` (task)  *(owner chat 2026-06-21: "stress test the stitch tool, look up how to break things and implement strategies to do so"; minted **B341** вАФ next free after B340)*
### B350 вАФ Stress-test the drawing stitch tool: harden the auto-stitch against bad PDF sets `[Doc Review / Stitch]` (task)  *(owner chat 2026-06-21: "stress test the stitch tool, look up how to break things and implement strategies to do so"; **renumbered twice in a very hot number space** вАФ first shipped as B341 (PR #248), bumped to B348 when a concurrent `main` kept B341 for theming-contrast (PR #244), then bumped again to **B350** when THREE more sessions collided on B348 (PR #255 calibrate-box, a Markup-sidebar feature, and this). B350 was the next free after B349 at this push; the other two B348 entries belong to other already-merged sessions and are left as-is. Code comments + tests + harness all carry B350.)*
`[x]` **Shipped + verified 2026-06-21 (branch `claude/stitch-tool-stress-test-1tvw5b`).** Adversarial pass over the stitch core (`stitchGeom.js`, `autoStitch.js`, `sheetGroups.js`, `sheetMeta.js`) вАФ drove each engine with the inputs a messy real-world PDF set throws at it and fixed four ways it could **fail silently** (the worst kind here: a bad transform flings a sheet off-canvas, or вАФ worse вАФ butts two drawings together at the wrong size/place and the takeoff reads a confident wrong number). All four follow the owner rule **"a wrong stitch is worse than an un-stitched one"**: when a signal is unreliable the sheet is left **unplaced вЖТ manual-Align safety net**, never auto-guessed.
- **Non-finite endpoints (NaN/Infinity) used to slip past the degenerate-baseline guard** вАФ `Math.hypot(NaN) < 1` is `NaN < 1` вЖТ `false`, so a NaN coordinate (bad read / mis-built drawing area) reached `solveM`, produced a NaN matrix, and poisoned the sheet transform **and** the whole composite's bbox (every `Math.min/max` over it вЖТ NaN). `alignBaselinesDegenerate` now rejects any non-finite point. (`stitchGeom.js`)
- **Contradictory match-line labels produced a wrong (overlapping/mirrored) stitch** вАФ if both sheets claimed the seam on their "right", `buildAdjacency` trusted it. It now treats the **geometric opposite** as the source of truth and **drops the edge** when a sheet's own label contradicts it (вЖТ manual Align). (`autoStitch.js`)
- **Mismatched page sizes were silently rescaled** вАФ a similarity fit from two endpoints will shrink/blow up a half-size detail page to make the seam meet. `autoPlaceGroup` now rejects a placement whose implied scale strays past **`MAX_STITCH_SCALE` (¬±25%)** and leaves the sheet for manual Align. (`autoStitch.js`)
- **Grouping chained across a major rollover** вАФ the packed `ordinal` (major¬Ј100+minor) made `C-1.99 вЖТ C-2.00` look consecutive (and could collide two codes onto one ordinal). `consecutiveCodes` now compares the parsed major/minor by numbering level, so a rollover starts a new logical sheet. (`sheetGroups.js`)
- **New `test/stitchStress.test.js` вАФ 29 adversarial tests** across 8 break-strategy groups (non-finite/degenerate coords, contradictory seams, size mismatch, cycles/duplicates/self-refs/missing targets, sheet-code edge cases, reader junk/empty/huge input, a **300-iteration randomized fuzz** asserting the partition + finiteness + scale-band invariants, and the measure-over-unaligned guard). Full suite green (**879 tests**, lint 0 errors, build clean). Pure-engine + DI hardening, so no live-browser verification needed; the manual-Align safety net and text-layer path are unchanged. **(Round 1 вАФ PR #248, merged 2026-06-21.)**

**Round 2 вАФ reader / grouping / calibration path (follow-up, same B350).** After round 1 hardened the placement geometry, a second adversarial pass over the text reads and takeoff math turned up one real functional gap and locked in the rest:
- **A set numbered past sheet 99 was invisible to grouping AND auto-stitch** вАФ `parseSheetNumber` capped the major at `\d{1,2}`, so `C-100` read as `""`, while `parseSheetCode` (sheetGroups) and the match-line `SHEET_REF` (sheetMeta) both already accepted 3 digits. A sheet with no readable number can't be chained by contiguity or found in the seam graph's by-number index, so a `C-100вА¶C-110` plan set never grouped or stitched. Bumped the **label-anchored** read to `\d{1,3}` (still requires a "SHEET NO." label, so the `A195` grid-ref guard is intact). (`titleBlockParse.js`)
- **New `test/stitchReaderStress.test.js` вАФ 13 tests**: 3-digit sheets now read + group + auto-stitch end-to-end (incl. through the wired `readSheetMeta`); date reading rejects impossible months/days/years and picks the newest under a huge-blob load; takeoff math (`dist`/`polyArea`/`pathLength`/`centroidOf`/`measureValue`/`measureLabel`) degrades on too-few / collinear / concave / coincident / non-finite input and **never fabricates a number** вАФ a non-finite calibration reads a safe sentinel ("set scale" / "вАФ"), never a plausible-looking figure. Full suite green (**892 tests**, lint 0 errors, build clean).

**Round 3 вАФ LIVE interactive stress (headless browser).** Rounds 1вАУ2 fuzzed the pure engines; round 3 attacks the one surface they can't reach вАФ the real React interaction layer вАФ with a new headless harness **`ui-audit/verify-stitch-stress.mjs`** (V92, **14/14 checks, 0 page errors**) driving a synthetic 4-page civil set: **(S1)** a degenerate manual Align (two coincident reference clicks) is refused and the sheet is **not flung**; **(S2)** measuring over a not-yet-aligned sheet is **blocked** and commits nothing; **(S3)** an interrupted pan (window `blur` mid-drag) doesn't crash or stick; **(S4)** ¬± zoom-button spam **clamps** at 5%/800%; **(S5)** a 45-click random fuzz across all tools never crashes the Stitcher. The hypothesized "remove a sheet mid-Align вЖТ deref `undefined.M`" crash was found **already guarded** (the sibling session's B344 fix, `if (!sheet) { setAlign(null); вА¶ }` in `onDown`) вАФ so this round adds a permanent interaction regression net rather than a new fix. No source change; harness + V-log only.

### B336 вАФ Sheet-metadata reader: title block, scale, match-line labels `[Doc Review]` (feature)  *(owner chat 2026-06-21; arrived as "NEW-2"; minted **B336**)*
`[x]` **Shipped + verified 2026-06-21 (branch `claude/loving-newton-t7gzpq`).** The shared positional reader the whole batch consumes. New `extractPageItems` (pdf.js) keeps each text run's x/y; pure `src/shared/files/sheetMeta.js` finds the **title-block band** (text-density on the right/bottom edge), the **sheet title** (largest wordy line in the band, label/data rows skipped), the **stated scale** (reuses B267 `parseSheetScale`), and every **MATCH-LINE label** with its position + orientation (page-edge вЖТ vertical/horizontal cut). Reuses B312's `titleBlockParse` for discipline/number/revision/date вАФ no second/parallel reader; surfaces a `confidence` instead of guessing. `doc-review/lib/sheetRead.js` glues pdf.js вЖТ reader вЖТ grouping with a **dormant injectable OCR seam** for scanned pages (вЖТ B340). **12 + 6 unit tests** (`test/sheetMeta.test.js`, `test/sheetRead.test.js`).
> **Dedup:** folded the CLAUDE.md roadmap "read its title block" (auto-filing) вАФ extends the shipped filing readers with the positional layer they lacked, doesn't duplicate them.

### B335 вАФ Drop a whole set вЖТ auto-group pages into logical sheets (collapsed list) `[Doc Review / Stitch]` (feature)  *(owner chat 2026-06-21; arrived as "NEW-1"; minted **B335**)*
`[x]` **Shipped + verified 2026-06-21.** Pure `src/shared/files/sheetGroups.js` collapses consecutive pages that share a plan type (discipline + `item`) AND a contiguous sheet-number run into logical sheets ("Grading Plan ¬Ј C-5вАУC-7 ¬Ј 3 sheets"); cover/general-notes stay standalone; conservative (under-groups rather than mis-merges). The Stitcher tray now shows **logical sheets** (read+grouped in the background after a drop), with an **"all pages"** safety-net toggle and a "Reading sheetsвА¶" state. Clicking a grouped plan adds every page at once (auto-stitched, B337). **7 unit tests** (`test/sheetGroups.test.js`); headless V87 confirmed a 4-page set вЖТ 2 logical entries.

### B337 вАФ Automatic match-line stitching `[Doc Review / Stitch]` (feature)  *(owner chat 2026-06-21; arrived as "NEW-3"; minted **B337**)*
`[x]` **Shipped + verified 2026-06-21.** Pure `doc-review/lib/autoStitch.js` builds the seam graph from B336's match-line labels and places each sheet by feeding the shared seam's two endpoints into the **existing `solveM()`** similarity fit (`stitchGeom.js`, B300) вАФ BFS from the most-connected anchor, the whole group then slotted to the right of existing content. A label-less sheet stays **unplaced** and drops to the 2-point manual Align **pre-seeded** with its detected seam endpoints (half the clicks); manual Align remains the safety net. **5 unit tests** (`test/autoStitch.test.js`); headless V87 confirmed 3 sheets auto-stitch with **coincident seams** (ќФx вЙИ 0.78¬Јwidth, not the old +40 gap).
> **Dedup:** this WAS the roadmap's "automatic match-line detection later," now specified вАФ folded, built on `solveM`. The geometric edge-line middle-fallback (when labels are missing) is deferred вЖТ B340.

The graphical legend **symbol-union** is deferred вЖТ B340.

### B321 вАФ `deleteReview` orphans the Drive copy when the cloud record can't be read `[Doc Review / Files]` (bug)  *(arrived as coworker-chat "NEW-1" 2026-06-21; minted **B321**)*
`[x]` **Fixed + verified 2026-06-21 (branch `claude/bold-bohr-hohz2x`).** Deleting a review no longer leaves source bytes orphaned in Google Drive (or Supabase Storage) when the cloud record read misses.
- **Already shipped (B207 Drive wiring):** the brief's primary point вАФ "there is no Drive delete anywhere in the code" вАФ was already addressed: `deleteReview` removes every `sources[].driveKey` through `deleteFromDrive` (a `DELETE /api/files?key=вА¶`) alongside the Supabase `BUCKET.remove(keys)`.
- **Residual fix (this session):** if `loadReview(id)` returns `null` (a transient network miss), `sources` was `[]`, so **neither** the Supabase objects **nor** the Drive objects were removed. `deleteReview` now falls back to the synchronous **local mirror** (`readDraft(uid, id)`, which carries the same `sources[]` incl. `storageKey` + `driveKey`) to recover the file list, so cleanup still runs. Best-effort and in parallel; it never blocks the row delete, and the legacy `<uid>/<id>/` folder sweep is unchanged.
- **Verified вАФ lint 0 ¬Ј 788 tests ¬Ј build green** (8 new in `test/docPersistence.test.js`); doc-review lazy chunk intact. The storage path is auth-gated (cloud + Drive), so the unit tests assert the graceful-degrade contract; a signed-in delete-with-Drive is the live check (logged in VERIFICATION).
> **Dedup:** primary already done under B207; this is the loadReview-null residual. Distinct from B38(a) (upsert re-file orphaning).

### B322 вАФ "Open PDFвА¶" and every Stitcher sheet upload to Supabase only, never Drive `[Doc Review / Stitch + Files]` (bug)  *(arrived as coworker-chat "NEW-2" 2026-06-21; minted **B322**)*
`[x]` **Fixed + verified 2026-06-21 (branch `claude/bold-bohr-hohz2x`).** Interactively-opened single sheets and **all** stitched sheets now go through the **same Drive-first / Supabase-fallback path** as filing, instead of Supabase-only.
- **One shared storage policy:** added `reviewStore.storeSource(srcId, blob, { projectId, discipline, fileName })` вАФ push to Google Drive (the primary home); only if Drive doesn't take it, fall back to Supabase Storage. `fileNewReview` was refactored to call it too, so there's a single source of truth for "where a source's bytes live" (no more two slightly-different copies of the policy).
- **Call sites:** `DocReview.openFile` and `Stitcher.openFiles` now call `storeSource` (were `uploadSource` вЖТ Supabase only) and persist `driveKey`; both `buildSnapshot`s carry `driveKey`; `Stitcher.loadStitch` reads back Drive-first then Supabase (`DocReview.fetchSourceBytes` already did). 
- **Why it matters:** (a) these files now live in Drive like filed ones (the "Drive is the primary file home" direction); (b) they **bypass Supabase's 50 MB per-file cap on the happy path** вАФ an E-size sheet or a large multi-sheet set that used to silently flag `oversize` ("re-drop on load") now stores in Drive; (c) stitched sheets carry a `driveKey`, so a stitched set can read its sheets back from Drive.
- **Verified вАФ lint 0 ¬Ј 788 tests ¬Ј build green** (`storeSource` degrade-path test); doc-review lazy chunk intact. The full Drive round-trip needs the (not-yet-deployed) Drive backend + sign-in, so it's the live check; the fallback to Supabase keeps today's behaviour until Drive is on.
> **Dedup:** net-new; the viewer (B288вАУB296) and stitch-guard (B300вАУB302) batches never touched the storage backend choice. Pairs with B321 (Drive delete) and B323 (keyless-source window).

### B323 вАФ A source saved with a null key during the upload window becomes unfetchable on a quick reload `[Doc Review]` (bug)  *(arrived as coworker-chat "NEW-3" 2026-06-21; minted **B323**)*
`[x]` **Fixed + verified 2026-06-21 (branch `claude/bold-bohr-hohz2x`).** A file opened and then reloaded **before its upload resolved** no longer strands the backdrop with a pointer the loader can't fetch.
- **Cause:** `openFile`/`openFiles` set the source into state immediately with `storageKey:null` (and no `driveKey`), which made it an autosave dep; the debounce + the synchronous local mirror could capture that **keyless** source before the upload's `.then(setSource w/ key)` ran. A reload in that window saved a record pointing at a source with no key вЖТ `fetchSourceBytes` couldn't fetch it вЖТ a permanent "re-open it to view", even though the bytes may have landed.
- **Fix:** `buildSnapshot` now persists a source only when it's actually stored вАФ `isStoredSource(s) = !!(s.storageKey || s.driveKey || s.oversize)`. While a just-opened/added file is still uploading (keyless), it's **omitted** from the saved `sources`, so a mid-upload reload can't save a broken pointer; the markups still save, and once the upload resolves the source is persisted normally (its key change re-triggers autosave). Applied to both the single-sheet and the per-sheet Stitcher snapshots. (`oversize` still counts as "stored" вЖТ the existing graceful "re-drop on load" path is unchanged.)
- **Verified вАФ lint 0 ¬Ј 788 tests ¬Ј build green** (`isStoredSource` unit tests: keyed/drive/oversize вЗТ persistable; keyless/absent вЗТ not); doc-review lazy chunk intact.
> **Dedup:** net-new; shares the `isStoredSource` predicate with B322's snapshots. Backdrop-only loss (markups were always safe).

### B324 вАФ A genuine edit made within the post-open suspend window isn't flagged dirty вЖТ never reaches the cloud `[Doc Review]` (bug)  *(arrived as coworker-chat "NEW-4" 2026-06-21; minted **B324**)*
`[x]` **Fixed + verified 2026-06-21 (branch `claude/bold-bohr-hohz2x`).** An edit made right after opening/resuming a review (inside the ~1.5 s programmatic-load window) is now mirrored, flagged dirty, and reaches the cloud.
- **Cause:** the autosave effect early-returned for the whole suspend window (B19), skipping **both** the local mirror **and** `dirtyRef=true`. The unmount/hide flush gates its cloud upsert on `dirtyRef`, so an edit in that window never reached the cloud (lost cross-device, or entirely on a tab crash before flush). The window is armed at load-start, so it usually elapsed harmlessly during a large PDF's fetch вАФ it bit on small/cached PDFs.
- **Fix:** the per-tick decision is now a pure, unit-tested `lib/autosavePlan.js вЖТ planAutosave({enabled, empty, loadEcho, suspended})`. The programmatic-load **echo** is identified precisely by a `loadEchoRef` flag (armed by `suspendSave`, consumed on the echo tick) rather than by the blunt time window, so it's still skipped вАФ but a **genuine edit**, even inside the window, now **mirrors + flags dirty** (so it's recoverable on-device AND flushes to the cloud); only its **debounced cloud re-save** stays suppressed while suspended, preserving B19's "don't re-stamp the just-loaded snapshot" intent (and B44's "no re-upsert of unchanged data on a mode toggle").
- **Verified вАФ lint 0 ¬Ј 788 tests ¬Ј build green** (`planAutosave` unit tests cover: load echo вЗТ consume only; edit-in-window вЗТ mirror+dirty, no debounce-save; edit-out-of-window вЗТ mirror+dirty+save; blank/disabled вЗТ nothing).
> **Dedup:** net-new; interacts with B19 (suspendSave) + B44 (dirty-gated flush), both preserved. Not covered by any open item.

### B325 вАФ Stitcher pan crash: "Cannot read properties of null (reading 'panX')" when a pan is interrupted `[Doc Review / Stitch]` (bug)  *(owner-reported 2026-06-21: "its broken, i was on the stitcher and it broke"; minted **B325** вАФ a hot `main` had reached B324)*
`[x]` **Fixed + shipped 2026-06-21 (branch `claude/awesome-feynman-i7wypf`).** The pan handler's `setView` updater read `drag.current` **inside** the deferred updater. That updater runs in React's render phase, which for a continuous `pointermove` can be deferred a tick; a discrete event in between вАФ `pointerup`, `pointercancel`, or the **B270** blur/visibility gesture-abort вАФ nulls `drag.current` first. Reading the ref then dereferenced null and threw in the render phase вЖТ the Document Review **error boundary** caught it ("hit an error and couldn't load") and the whole stitcher went down. A real user hits this by tab-switching / losing focus / a pointer-cancel mid-pan. **Fix:** capture the drag origin into a local and close over it via a pure `panTo()` helper in `lib/stitchGeom.js`, so an aborted gesture can't crash the deferred updater. **Verified:** 4 unit tests (`test/stitchGeom.test.js` вАФ math, null-ref-survival, + a teeth test that the OLD ref-reading pattern throws `/panX/`) and a headless harness (`ui-audit/verify-b325-pan.mjs`: a normal pan moves the world; 12 mid-pan aborts вЖТ no error boundary, 0 `panX` errors; pan still works after). lint 0 ¬Ј build green. VERIFICATION **V84**.

### B341 вАФ Contrast regression from the scheme change; full-app audit `[Site / shared / theming]` (bug)  *(owner-dropped 2026-06-21 "Backlog mode"; arrived as "NEW-1"; first filed B321, renumbered **B341** вАФ concurrent `main` consumed B321вАУB340)*
`[x]` **Fixed + audited + verified this session (branch `claude/dreamy-fermi-qqyt9j`).** After the
B316вАУB320 scheme change, several chrome elements rendered too light to read. **Root cause:** B318 flipped
the chrome from always-dark to **themes-with-the-app** (light theme вЖТ light chrome), and migrated
`index.css` + `AppHeader` + `palette.js` + the per-file `PAL` *objects* to tokens вАФ but a set of
**chrome-region components kept inline hardcoded old-dark-chrome hexes** (`#ece7db` cream text,
`#fff` active text, `#9b9482`/`#8a8473` warm grays, `#2e2a23` borders, `rgba(255,255,255,0.0x)` fills,
a hardcoded-dark status-bar bg, and pale dark-chrome badge colors `#86efac`/`#fbbf24`). On the new
**light** chrome those became cream/white-on-white; one (the planner status bar) was dark-text-on-a-
still-hardcoded-dark-bg. The two reported cases вАФ the **user-name pill** and the **Dashboard/Map
toggle** вАФ were exactly this class, so the fix audited the **whole tree**, not just the three reported spots.
- **Audit method (as briefed):** diffed the scheme commit (`32a1b8a`) to see which tokens changed,
  then grepped every consumer of the retired hexes; built a **programmatic WCAG checker over every
  defined token pair** in both themes (`ui-audit/contrast-audit.mjs`, parses the real `index.css`) +
  a **live headless probe** that reads the computed text/bg of the actual chrome elements
  (`ui-audit/verify-b341-contrast.mjs`).
- **Token system itself was sound** вАФ every actionable pair clears AA in both themes; the only WARNs
  are documented exceptions (locked Site/Schedule brand fills, only ever used as вЙ•3:1 underline +
  unused `--on-accent-*` text tokens; the amber Markup underline whose state is also carried by its
  passing text; owner-exempt subtle borders). So the regression was purely the unmigrated components.
- **Fixes (repointed to tokens):** `Shell.jsx` (account pill + dropdown), `ProjectBreadcrumb.jsx`
  (crumbs + dropdown; **AppHeader now passes the `-text` accent token**, never the fill, for the
  "current"/"New project" labels вАФ fill-as-text was 3.4:1), `SitePlanner.jsx` (status bar bg, Files
  button, left-rail + tool-rail + snap/parcel active text, hdrTab chips, save-slot warn color),
  `DocReview.jsx` (header title + Files + chrome buttons), `Stitcher.jsx` (toolbar dividers/buttons),
  `ReviewsBar.jsx` (badge colors + dropdown), `LayerPanel.jsx` (warm grays вЖТ tokens; it rides the
  themed surface-overlay so it was dark-on-dark in dark mode), and the reusable `Field` label.
- **Two new tokens** (both themes, AA-checked): **`--on-accent`** (text ON the global accent fill вАФ
  white in light, near-black in dark because the B319 dark accent `#F26B3A` is too light for white at
  only 3.0:1) and **`--warn-text`** (legible amber for saving/unsaved/offline badges, replacing the
  dark-chrome `#fbbf24`).
- **Before вЖТ after (reported + key siblings), contrast on the light chrome:**

  | Element | before | after (light / dark) |
  |---|---|---|
  | User-name / Sign-in pill text | `#ece7db` on `#FFF` вЙИ **1.2:1** | **16.66 / 15.11** |
  | Dashboard¬ЈMap crumb (active) | `#fff` on `#FFF` = **1.0:1** | **16.66 / 15.11** |
  | Dashboard¬ЈMap crumb (idle) | `#9b9482` вЙИ **3.0:1** | **11.2 / 10.4** |
  | Planner status bar text | dark-on-dark вЙИ **1.3:1** | **9.6вАУ14.3 / 8.2вАУ16** |
  | Markup "Saved вЬУ" badge | `#86efac` вЙИ **1.4:1** | **5.3 / 11** |
  | Active module tab + inactive tabs | (ok) | 5.3вАУ6.9 / 8вАУ10.3 |

- **Deliverables:** `ui-audit/contrast-audit.mjs` (token-pair report, exits non-zero on any actionable

### B316 вАФ Light / dark / system theme with cool-gray light palette `[AppHeader / theming]` (feature) вАФ foundation-scale  *(owner-dropped 2026-06-20; arrived as "NEW-3"; minted **B316** вАФ next free after B272)*
`[x]` Add a theme selector with three modes вАФ **Light**, **Dark**, **System** (`prefers-color-scheme`). App is currently hard-locked to one look; this adds the switch. **Both modes are net-new full surface palettes** (owner decision 2026-06-20, see below): Light = cool gray-white surfaces; Dark = a genuine dark-*surface* mode (dark content panels), **retiring** today's warm cream/paper work area.
> **вЬУ DECISION (owner, 2026-06-20) вАФ "build a true dark mode":** the app today is **not all-dark** вАФ content surfaces are a warm **cream/paper** ("drafting") palette (`body #efeadf`, panels `#f6f3ec`, ink `#26231e`) under **dark graphite chrome** (top bars + rail, `#14110e`/`#191613`). Asked whether "keep the existing dark unchanged" meant preserve today's cream-content + dark-chrome look, or build a real dark-*surface* mode, the owner chose the latter: build a **genuine dark-surface** Dark mode (dark content panels) and **retire the cream**, alongside the cool-gray Light. **Consequence for scope:** *both* themes are net-new surface palettes вАФ the only "existing dark" that survives is the dark **chrome** (bars/rail); the dark **content-surface** values (dark equivalents of surface-page / surface-raised / borders / text) **don't exist yet and must be designed**, and every one of the ~886 color spots needs a proper two-way (lightвЖФdark) mapping, not a one-way "add light." This increases effort vs. preserving the current look and reinforces the multi-pass-foundation plan below.

> **рЯФБ UPDATE 2026-06-21 вАФ design RESOLVED + decomposed into B317вАУB320 (building this session).** The owner ran the theming design through a ChatGPT visual pass; the returned spec settles every open question here. Implemented as four sibling children of this umbrella: **B317** (infrastructure), **B318** (full palette + theme-aware chrome), **B319** (work-surface canvas/sheet), **B320** (contrast + status). B316 stays as the umbrella/record. **Canonical visual reference: `planyr-theming-mockup.html`** вАФ match its *rendered* result, not just raw hexes. вЪ† Owner named that file as the reference but it is **not in the repo** as of this update вАФ request a copy to keep in-repo + diff against. **Two assumptions in THIS item are now reversed/resolved:** (1) ~~"the dark chrome survives unchanged in both themes"~~ вЖТ **chrome now themes WITH the app** (light theme = light chrome, dark theme = dark chrome); a permanently-dark bar in an otherwise-white app forces constant pupil readjustment вАФ worst case for eye strain (see B318). (2) the net-new dark surface palette **and** the two-value accent-text question are now **fully specified** in B318. Retire the warm cream, the old always-dark warm chrome (`#14110e`/`#191613`), and the ember accent (`#e8590c`).

**Mechanics (from the owner's spec):**
- Drive theming off `data-theme="light|dark"` on `<html>`. All colors as CSS variables, both themes fully defined.
- **System** resolves via `prefers-color-scheme` and must update **live mid-session** вАФ attach a `matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)')` change listener.
- Persist the choice (light/dark/system) in **localStorage as source-of-truth on load**; mirror to the `profiles` row (NEW-1) for cross-device. localStorage wins on first paint to avoid a network round-trip.
- **FOUC gotcha (do this FIRST):** an inline script in `index.html <head>` that reads the stored choice (or system pref) and sets `data-theme` **before React mounts** вАФ otherwise every load flashes the wrong theme. ("FOUC" = flash of un-themed content.)
- Theme control lives in the **account dropdown (NEW-2)** or **Settings** вАФ consolidate, don't duplicate.
- Files likely touched: `index.html` (inline pre-paint script), a `ThemeProvider`/context, the token stylesheet (`src/index.css`), the account dropdown (NEW-2), the `profiles` mirror via the NEW-1 hook.

**Light-mode surface tokens (cool gray-white вАФ owner-verified legible):**

| Token | Light value | Dark value |
|---|---|---|
| surface-page | `#F3F5F8` | existing locked dark |
| surface-raised (cards) | `#FFFFFF` | existing locked dark |
| border-default | `#E1E5EB` | existing |
| border-strong (hover) | `#CDD3DC` | existing |
| text-primary | `#1B1E26` | existing |
| text-secondary (muted) | `#565E6E` | existing |
| text-tertiary (hints) | `#8B92A1` | existing |

> вЪ† **Per the decision above, "Dark value = existing" for the *surface* rows is now a net-new true-dark surface palette to be designed** (dark page / dark cards / dark borders / light-on-dark text), NOT the current cream. Only the dark **chrome** (bars/rail) pre-exists. The owner's Light column is fixed; the Dark surface column needs its cool-neutral dark equivalents specced as part of the build.

**Accent pair model:** each module accent is **two tokens** вАФ a **fill/brand** value (unchanged, locked hexes вАФ these already live in `src/shared/ui/moduleAccent.js` as `MODULE_ACCENT`) and an **on-light text** value (tuned, AA-passing as foreground). The `-text` token is theme-dependent.

| Module | fill (both modes) | text вАФ light mode | text вАФ dark mode |
|---|---|---|---|
| Site | `#1D9E75` | `#0F6E56` | `#5DCAA5` |
| Schedule | `#7F77DD` | `#534AB7` | `#AFA9EC` |
| Markup | `#EF9F27` | `#8A5410` | `#EF9F27` |

- **On-fill text rule (both modes):** text/icons **on** an accent fill вАФ Site & Schedule fills carry **white** (`#FFFFFF`); **Markup (amber) fill carries dark text** (`#412402`). White-on-amber is unreadable; enforce wherever a status/tab chip uses the amber fill.
- **Usage rule:** accent-as-**fill** (tab band, active indicator, status-chip bg) вЖТ **fill** token. Accent-as-**foreground** (colored text, thin icons, links) вЖТ **`-text`** token, never the fill token.
- **Edge case вАФ status palette:** the locked status tokens (Pursuit / Active / On Hold / Complete / Dead) need the same discipline. For each status color used as text/icon on a light surface, **derive programmatically** the nearest variant that clears **AA вЙ• 4.5** as foreground on `#FFFFFF`/`#F3F5F8`; keep originals as fills with the same on-fill rule. **Flag any status color whose foreground variant can't reach 4.5** for review (don't hand-pick).
- **Constraint (unchanged):** module accents stay confined to the **top tab row only** вАФ light mode doesn't change that.

> **Build plan / scope (grounds the "foundation-scale" tag) вАФ REUSE, don't rebuild:**
> The app has **no central theming layer today**: ~**886 hardcoded hex literals across ~30 files**, **9 local `PAL` objects** (`SitePlanner.jsx`, `MapFinder.jsx`, `AuthPanel.jsx`, `ParcelDrawing.jsx`, `DocReview.jsx`, `Stitcher.jsx`, `ProjectLibrary.jsx`, `ProjectFilesDrawer.jsx`, `ReviewsBar.jsx`), inline styles throughout, plus literals inside `src/index.css`. `MODULE_ACCENT` (`moduleAccent.js`) is already the single source for the **fill** colors вЖТ extend it with the `-text` counterparts rather than re-listing hexes. `BrandMark` already takes a `surface="dark|light"` prop (theme-aware) вЖТ just feed it the active theme. The Scheduler is an **iframe** (`public/sequence/index.html`) with its **own** colors вЖТ needs its own token sheet or a postMessage theme bridge (separate surface).
> Recommended sequence: **(1)** define the full token set for both themes in `:root` / `[data-theme]`; **(2)** FOUC inline script; **(3)** `ThemeProvider` + `matchMedia` live listener + localStorage persistence; **(4)** migrate the 9 PALs + inline literals + `index.css` literals to consume tokens (the bulk вАФ do it per-workspace, verifying each surface); **(5)** AA-derive the status palette; **(6)** theme the Scheduler iframe; **(7)** wire the control into NEW-2/Settings + the NEW-1 cross-device mirror. A shell-only/partial theme that leaves the canvas/map/doc-review hardcoded would be a **misleading half** (per the "finish the job" rule) вАФ so this ships as a deliberate multi-pass foundation, ideally after NEW-1 + NEW-2 land.

     against at verification. "Ship together" вАФ all four merge as one chain this session. -->

### B317 вАФ Light / Dark / System theme infrastructure `[Global / theming]` (feature) вАФ child of B316; build FIRST  *(owner-dropped 2026-06-21 via ChatGPT spec; arrived as "NEW-1"; minted **B317**)*
`[x]` Build the theming foundation every module inherits. **Ships together with B318вАУB320; build B317 first (they depend on it).**
- **Token system:** CSS custom properties driven by `data-theme="light|dark"` on `<html>`. Components reference **tokens only**, never raw hex. **Extend** the existing locked token set (`:root` vars in `src/index.css` + the per-file `PAL` objects) rather than starting fresh вАФ repoint them at tokens.
- **Three modes:** Light, Dark, System. **System** follows the OS via `window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)')` and must **live-update** when the OS flips вАФ attach a `change` listener, don't read once at load.
- **Persistence:** store the choice in `localStorage['planyr.theme']`; **default System** on first run.
- **No theme flash (FOUC):** apply the resolved theme in a tiny inline `<head>` script **before first paint**, so the page never flashes the wrong colors before React boots.
- **Switch UI:** three-way control in Settings and/or the **row-1 settings menu in `AppHeader`**.
- Files: new `ThemeProvider`/context, the global token stylesheet (`src/index.css`), `AppHeader`, `index.html` (pre-paint script).
> Lineage: the **infrastructure half of B316**. Finalizes B316's FOUC/ThemeProvider/matchMedia/localStorage mechanics. localStorage is source-of-truth on load; the `profiles` cross-device mirror stays a later additive follow-on, not a prerequisite.

### B318 вАФ Full theme palette + theme-aware chrome `[Global / AppHeader]` (feature) вАФ depends on B317; child of B316  *(owner-dropped 2026-06-21 via ChatGPT spec; arrived as "NEW-2"; minted **B318**)*
`[x]` Replace the retired warm-cream work surface **and** the old always-dark chrome. **Chrome now themes WITH the app** вАФ this deliberately **reverses** B316's "dark chrome in both themes" assumption: a dark bar in an otherwise-white app (bright office) forces constant pupil readjustment, the worst case for eye strain. **Light theme вЖТ light chrome; Dark theme вЖТ dark chrome.** Depends on B317.

- **Module fills (fixed, both themes):** Site `#1D9E75`, Schedule `#7F77DD`, Markup `#EF9F27`. **On-fill text:** white for Site/Schedule; **dark `#412402` for Markup** вАФ never white on amber.

NB `src/index.css :root` hardcodes `--chrome/--chrome-line/--chrome-ink/--chrome-muted/--accent` to warm/ember + a `rgba(232,89,12,вА¶)` focus ring, and `Shell.jsx`/`AppHeader.jsx` hardcode `#14110e`/`#2e2a23`/`#c9c3b4` вАФ all move to per-theme tokens.

### B319 вАФ Work-surface theme behaviors: canvas + Markup sheet `[Site, Markup]` (feature) вАФ depends on B317/B318; child of B316  *(owner-dropped 2026-06-21 via ChatGPT spec; arrived as "NEW-3"; minted **B319**)*
`[x]` The drafting canvas and the document viewer need their own dark behavior, distinct from panel surfaces. Depends on B317/B318.
- **Site canvas dark tokens:** `canvas-bg #0E1014`, `grid-minor rgba(232,235,240,0.05)`, `grid-major rgba(232,235,240,0.10)`; lift **parcel stroke to `#2FBE90`** on dark.
- **Drafting/selection accent dark variant:** the selected-element + dimension-line **red-orange is a work-surface color, NOT a module accent** вАФ the "accents don't change" rule doesn't apply: light `#C2410C` вЖТ dark **`#F26B3A`** (`#C2410C` too dim on the dark canvas).
- **Markup in Dark:** the **mat** (around the drawing, `#cfc8ba` today at `DocReview.jsx:539` + `Stitcher.jsx:343`) darkens to **`#0E1014`**; the **drawing sheet stays white** вАФ it's the **immutable backdrop**, and inverting a construction sheet misrepresents it. Direct application of the standing immutable-backdrop principle, not a one-off.
- Files: Site Planner canvas renderer (`SitePlanner.jsx`); Markup viewer mat/sheet container (`DocReview.jsx`, `Stitcher.jsx`).

### B320 вАФ Contrast + text-hierarchy pass `[Global / theming]` (task) вАФ depends on B317/B318; child of B316  *(owner-dropped 2026-06-21 via ChatGPT spec; arrived as "NEW-4"; minted **B320**)*
`[x]` Apply the dark text ramp (B318) and lock the rule behind it. Depends on B317/B318.
- **Standing rule (also added to `CLAUDE.md`):** build text hierarchy through **weight, size, and uppercase letter-spacing вАФ never by fading text toward the background.** Low-contrast gray body/label text is an eye-strain problem in bright offices and is **disallowed**. Subtle grays stay correct **only** for borders, the drafting grid, and the semantic "Complete" status badge.
- **Status badges need dark-surface variants.** The canonical `STATUS_TOKENS` (`src/shared/ui/statusTokens.js`: pursuit `#378ADD`, active `#639922`, onhold `#BA7517`, complete `#888780`, dead `#E24B4A`) are tuned for white cards; saturated values go muddy on `#1D2027`. Add a lighter dark-mode variant per status (mockup direction: Active вЖТ `#2FBE90`, Complete вЖТ `#8B92A1`). NB a drifted duplicate `STATUS_COLOR` lives in `ProjectLibrary.jsx:13` вАФ reconcile while here.
- **Verify all body text clears WCAG AA (вЙ• 4.5:1)** against its surface in **both** themes; flag any accent/status that fails and propose the fix rather than shipping it silent.

### B312 вАФ Auto-filing reads the title block with plain code first; AI only as a fallback `[Document Review / Files]` (feature) вАФ owner direction on B299  *(owner 2026-06-20: "a ton of this could be done without an LLMвА¶ is this gonna cost tokens?"; minted **B312** вАФ concurrent `main` consumed B300вАУB311)*
`[x]` **Built + tested + shipped this session.** Re-architected auto-filing (B299) to **"plain code first, AI only as fallback"** so the common case is **free, instant, and needs no cloud or API key** вАФ exactly the owner's point that reading a title block, picking the latest date, and recognizing "ALTA survey" is ordinary code, not an LLM job.
- **Tier 1 вАФ deterministic, in the browser, $0 (the default now):** for any PDF with an embedded text layer (most CAD-exported vector drawings), read the text with the existing `extractPageText` (pdf.js, the same reader B267 uses) and parse the filing fields with pure code:
  - `src/shared/files/titleBlockParse.js` (pure, **17 unit tests**): `classifyDiscipline` (a keyword table вАФ **ALTA** вЖТ Survey/ALTA Survey, boundary/topo вЖТ Survey, grading/paving/drainage вЖТ Civil, fire sprinkler, landscape, environmental, geotechвА¶; sheet-number prefix as the tie-break), `findDates`/`latestDate` ("search all dates, pick the newest" = the issue date, across MM/DD/YYYY, YYYY-MM-DD, "June 30, 2025", "30 June 2025"), `parseSheetNumber` (labelled-first, conservative вАФ returns "" rather than grab a grid ref), `parseRevision`, `readTitleBlockText`.
  - `src/shared/files/matchProject.js` (pure, **8 unit tests**): `matchProjectInText` **searches the sheet text for each named project's identifiers** (name phrase, or exact parcel/account/job number) and reuses the B299 "never auto-guess" decision (confident single вЖТ matched; none/ambiguous вЖТ needs-filing tray). Mirrors `server/filing/matcher.js`'s thresholds.
  - `src/workspaces/doc-review/lib/localRead.js` glues them to pdf.js (lazy-imported) вЖТ a decision in the SAME shape the server returns.
- **Tier 2 вАФ AI fallback, only when Tier 1 finds NO text** (a scanned/image-only sheet) **and** the backend is enabled. So tokens are spent only on the hard minority, not every file. `autofile` (`lib/autofiling.js`) is now local-first with an injectable `localRead`; `capturePlacementFacts` uses a new `forceServer` flag (placement is genuinely an AI/CV step).
- **On by default, safely:** the provider now exposes `autofileReady = true` (Tier 1 always works in the browser вАФ no key, no deploy), so the drawer auto-files dropped drawings out of the box. A **confident match auto-routes**; **anything else falls back to today's behavior** (the active project, or the holding tray) вАФ so the only behavior change is that confident matches now file themselves, and a wrong confident match is still re-filable from the row. `backendReady` stays gated on `VITE_AUTOFILE_ENABLED` (the honest "AI can also read scanned sheets / capture placement" signal).
- **Verified вАФ lint 0 ¬Ј 743 tests (53 new: titleBlockParse 17 + matchProject 8 + autofiling tiering) ¬Ј build green; doc-review lazy-chunk split intact.** Headless on the built app (`ui-audit/verify-b299-autofiling.mjs`): the Files drawer opens, the new modules (parser, matcher, lazy-pdf localRead) evaluate in a real browser, **0 page/console errors**. **Real-sheet accuracy** (the keyword table + name match against the owner's actual KG B1 / Jacintoport drawings) is the live acceptance check вАФ logged as **VERIFICATION V79** (needs a signed-in drop of a real construction sheet; the deterministic logic itself is exhaustively unit-tested).
> **Dedup:** does NOT replace the B299 AI reader (`server/filing/`) вАФ it puts a free deterministic front-end on it and demotes it to a fallback. Reuses `extractPageText` (B267) for text, the B299 matcher logic/thresholds, the B299 file-facts index + drawer wiring. The AI path stays the answer for scanned sheets + placement-fact capture.

     canvas. Headless-verified together as **VERIFICATION V78**. -->

### B310 вАФ Accidental parcel selection while panning the planner canvas `[Site Planner]` (bug)  *(arrived as "NEW-1" 2026-06-20; first filed B300, renumbered **B310** вАФ concurrent `main` consumed B300вАУB309)*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-20 (branch `claude/blissful-mccarthy-dkozi0`).** With parcels rendered, grabbing the planner canvas to pan kept registering as a parcel select вАФ `startMoveParcel` (`SitePlanner.jsx`) fired `setSel` on pointer-**down** and `e.stopPropagation()` blocked the background pan, so a press anywhere on a lot selected it whether the gesture was a click or the start of a drag. Navigating across lots felt like constantly clicking into them.
- **Fix вАФ click-vs-drag discrimination on the parcel layer.** A press on a **locked** parcel (the default every county-pulled / drawn lot carries вАФ created `locked:true` in all six creation paths) now starts a **PAN** (`drag.current.mode:"pan"`) tagged with the parcel id + the press origin (`tapParcel`, `downX/downY/downT`), instead of selecting. On pointer-**up** (`onUp`) it counts as a deliberate **click вЖТ select** only if travel вЙ§ `PARCEL_CLICK_SLOP_PX` (**5px**, measured in SCREEN px so it's zoom-independent) **and** the press was < `PARCEL_CLICK_MS` (**400ms**); any larger/longer movement panned and leaves the selection untouched. Uses Pointer Events + `setPointerCapture` (already the canvas's model) so the up fires even if the pointer left the polygon, and the gesture joins the existing `abortGesture` recovery (`capturePidRef`) so an interrupted parcel-pan can't strand the grab cursor (B271-class).
- **Preserved:** a deliberately **unlocked** parcel still grabs-to-move on press (you unlocked it to reshape/move it вАФ matches elements); the full-polygon hit area is unchanged (we gate on gesture *intent*, never shrink the target); Shift-click-to-merge and align-edge picking still work. Space / the Pan tool remain the always-on pan escape hatches.
- **Verified вАФ lint 0 ¬Ј 712 tests ¬Ј build green; `SitePlannerApp` lazy chunk intact.** Headless on the built app (`ui-audit/verify-b310-b311.mjs`, logged-out, seeded one locked parcel): a deselectedвЖТ**click selects** (strokeвЖТ#c2410c / width 3); a **drag of 95px pans and does NOT select** (stroke stays #5b6650 / width 2, the parcel's on-screen box shifted +95px), **0 page JS errors**. Logged as **VERIFICATION V78**.

### B311 вАФ "Select parcels" mode toggle (non-hijacking default) `[Site Planner]` (feature) вАФ layered on B310  *(arrived as "NEW-2" 2026-06-20; first filed B301, renumbered **B311**)*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-20 (branch `claude/blissful-mccarthy-dkozi0`).** A **Row-2 toolbar toggle** ("Select parcels", next to Snap, shown only when the plan has parcels) as a hard-off fallback for pure browse/measure workflows where zero accidental selection is wanted. **Non-hijacking default = ON:** click a lot to select it, dragging always pans (normal selection works out of the box thanks to B310, so the toggle isn't the primary gate). **OFF:** a press on a parcel is click-through вАФ `startMoveParcel` returns *without* `stopPropagation`, so the event falls through to the background pan exactly as if it landed on empty canvas; a click never selects. Turning it OFF also drops any current parcel selection so browse mode is clean.
- **Persistence:** stored as `settings.parcelSelect` (default `true` in `DEFAULT_SETTINGS`), so it rides the existing per-project Site Model `settings` save/restore path вАФ saved per project, restored on reopen. No new store, no localStorage key.
- **Verified вАФ same harness (`ui-audit/verify-b310-b311.mjs`):** default reads **ON** (`aria-pressed=true`); flipping it **OFF** вЖТ a click no longer selects (parcel stays unselected); flipping it back **ON** вЖТ a click selects again; **OFF persists across a full page reload** (per-project). lint 0 ¬Ј 712 tests ¬Ј build green. Logged as **VERIFICATION V78**.

### B315 вАФ Undo (Ctrl+Z) unreliable after moving a building `[Site Planner]` (bug)  *(arrived as coworker-chat "NEW-1" 2026-06-21; renumbered B310вЖТB313вЖТ**B315** as a very hot `main` twice consumed the number вАФ B310/B311 parcel click-vs-drag + B312 auto-filing, then B313/B314 multi-tab + optimistic-concurrency)*
`[x]` **Fixed + headless-verified 2026-06-21 (branch `claude/ecstatic-ritchie-ihzkym`).** Moving a building then pressing Ctrl+Z now reverts the **entire** move in one step, every time (was: sometimes nothing, sometimes a partial revert).
- **Root cause (confirmed by reading, NOT guessed вАФ the brief's hypothesis #2, the race):** the drag-move transaction boundary was already correct вАФ `startMove`/`startMoveParcel`/`startGroupMove` push history **once** at drag-start, nothing during the drag, nothing on pointer-up (so hypothesis #1, per-frame pushes, did **not** apply). The defect was that `stateRef` вАФ the single source both for the snapshot pushed onto the undo stack AND for the baseline `undo()` compares against (the B32 no-op dedup `histKey(stateRef.current)` check) вАФ was updated in a **passive `useEffect` (no deps)**. A ref written in a passive effect lags the committed render by a paint, so a quick undoвЖФdrag sequence could snapshot/compare a **stale** state вЖТ revert to the wrong frame (partial) or skip the frame in the dedup loop (does nothing). Timing-dependent вЗТ intermittent, matching the fuzzy repro.
- **Fix:** (1) `stateRef.current` is now assigned **during render** instead of in a passive effect, so `pushHistory`/`undo`/`redo` always read the TRUE current state вАФ the race window is gone. (2) Extracted the stack + dedup into a **pure, unit-tested** module `lib/history.js` (`createHistoryStack({ keyOf })` вЖТ push/undo/redo/drop/canUndo/canRedo), matching the `stitchGeom.js` precedent; `undo`/`redo` take the live state **explicitly**, so the stale-ref class of bug can't recur. (3) **Interrupted-drag edge case** (brief's list): Esc / lost-focus / pointer-cancel **mid-move** now reverts to the pre-drag snapshot stashed on `drag.current` and drops the dangling frame (`cancelActiveMove` in `abortGesture`), so a cancelled drag leaves no half-recorded command.
- **Edge cases covered + verified:** one drag = one undo (full revert); redo restores; two moves = two undos (one each); multi-select/group move = one push = one undo (geometry-agnostic stack); independent transactions don't clobber each other (a move-undo doesn't touch an unrelated vertex edit); Esc-mid-drag cancels cleanly.
- **Verified:** lint 0 ¬Ј **full suite green** (11 new in `test/history.test.js`, incl. a deterministic repro of the stale-baseline failure mode) ¬Ј build green. Headless on the built app (`ui-audit/verify-b315.mjs`, chromium-1194, logged-out): drag a building 300px вЖТ **one Ctrl+Z snaps it fully back, ќФ=0.0px** (not partial); redo; two-moves-two-undos; Esc-mid-drag revert; **0 JS errors**.
> **Dedup:** net-new. **Related but distinct from B32 (done)** вАФ B32 stopped no-op edits from polluting the stack (the *dedup* the `while`-loop does); B315 is the *stale-baseline race* that made even a clean move-frame revert wrong/skipped. NOT a duplicate of any open item; no open item covered undo-after-move. Kept as ONE item (the brief said split only if the diagnosis turned out to be redo- or multi-select-specific вАФ it wasn't; the race affects all undo, redo + multi-select already work as separate transactions).

### B308 вАФ Server-side Mapillary token proxy so the street-level layer works for all users `[Site Planner / functions]` (feature)  *(coworker-chat "NEW-1" 2026-06-20; first filed B303 then renumbered **B308** вАФ concurrent `main` landed a Doc Review batch on B303вАУB307, so both can't share the number)*
`[x]` **Built + shipped 2026-06-21 (branch `claude/busy-allen-ofgy9l`).** The "Poles & hydrants from street imagery" layer now works for **every visitor with no per-user token**, and the Mapillary access token never reaches the public bundle or any client request URL вАФ it lives only as an encrypted Cloudflare Pages Secret the owner set (`MAPILLARY_TOKEN`, Production). Resolves the audit's *token-in-bundle* + *token-in-URL* LOW findings; honours the KEY DECISION "Mapillary token is a secret."
- **Pages Function** `functions/api/mapillary/[[path]].js` reads the token from the runtime binding `context.env.MAPILLARY_TOKEN` (NOT `import.meta.env`/a `VITE_*` var) and forwards to the Graph API. **Guardrails** (pure helpers in `functions/api/mapillary/_proxy.js`, unit-tested): allow-list ONLY `map_features` + fields `id,object_value,geometry`; **Origin check** (same-origin / `*.planyr.io` / `*.planyr.pages.dev`, foreign Origin вЖТ 403); bbox/limit validation; short edge-cache (`max-age=300`) to cut quota. **Dormant-graceful:** no token (e.g. a Preview deploy, which doesn't have the secret) вЖТ 503 + empty `data`, the client shows "not available here", never a hard error.
- **Client:** new leaflet-free `lib/mapillaryClient.js` (`mapillaryRequestUrl`/`pickDetections`); `evidenceLayers.fetchMapillary` calls the same-origin `/api/mapillary/map_features` with **NO `access_token`** by default (a pasted token = an optional power-user override straight to Mapillary). Removed the no-token gate in `mapillaryLayer` + `syncOverlayLayers` and the `needsSetup` flag on the layer; the LayerPanel box is now "Works automatically вАФ (Advanced) use your own token". `.env.example` + README document the secret-lives-in-Cloudflare rule.
- **Verified:** lint 0 ¬Ј **722 tests** (10 new, `test/mapillaryProxy.test.js`: allow-list, Origin, limit-clamp, and the client default carrying no token) ¬Ј build green; **0 `MLY|` token literals + 0 `VITE_MAPILLARY_TOKEN` in `dist/`**. Headless on the built app (`gis-verify/mapillary-proxy-verify.mjs`): toggling the layer with no token вЖТ it loads via **same-origin `/api/mapillary/map_features`**, **0 token leaks** in any request URL, **no** direct `graph.mapillary.com` call, graceful degrade in preview, **0 JS errors**.
- **вП≥ LIVE confirm (the one piece the sandbox can't do вАФ a Pages Function needs the Cloudflare runtime):** on planyr.io Production after the next deploy, zoom вЙ• 16 over a covered area вЖТ pole/hydrant dots render via `/api/mapillary/вА¶`, token nowhere in page source/bundle/URLs. Logged in VERIFICATION. (The owner already set the secret, so this is just the deploy + a coworker eyeball.)
> **Dedup:** net-new; builds on B285/B286 (Mapillary rename + gating). The cleanup half (drop the dead `VITE_MAPILLARY_TOKEN` read) stays as **B309** `[~]`, held until this is confirmed live.

### B303 вАФ Undo / redo for Document Review markups + calibration `[Doc Review / Markup]` (feature)  *(arrived as "NEW-1" 2026-06-20 owner chat; provisionally B283, renumbered **B303** вАФ concurrent `main` consumed B283вАУB302; batch B303вАУB307)*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-20 (branch `claude/stoic-faraday-th9mp8`).** Repro: place/delete/move a markup or measurement, press Ctrl/вМШ-Z вЖТ nothing happened; the workspace had no history at all, so a mis-edit was unrecoverable. **Fix:** **Ctrl/вМШ-Z undo, Ctrl/вМШ-Shift-Z + Ctrl-Y redo** in BOTH `DocReview.jsx` (single sheet) and `Stitcher.jsx` (stitched set), plus on-canvas **вЖґ / вЖЈ** buttons (disabled when there's nothing to undo/redo).
- **Pattern reused, not reinvented:** mirrors the Site Planner's `pushHistory` вАФ `pastRef`/`futureRef` of editable-state snapshots taken **by reference** (DocReview `{markups, calByPage, calInfo}`; Stitcher `{measures, ftPerUnit}`), with a `histKey` signature so `undo` **skips frames identical to the current state** вАФ the **B32/B105 lesson** that a stray push can't make Ctrl-Z look like a no-op. `pushHistory()` fires only on a REAL mutation; the background stated-scale auto-scan (B267) deliberately does NOT push. History resets when the document context changes (open new PDF / load / new review).
- **Covers `main`'s viewer edits too:** a markup **move** (B293, committed on pointer-up) and a **text create/edit/delete** (B293 inline editor) each push one frame, so the new editing affordances are undoable as well as plain draws.
- **Poly-vertex placement:** mid-draw, Ctrl-Z (and Backspace/Delete) step back the **last placed vertex** of a polygon/area/count draft before falling through to full undo / delete-selection.
- **Verified headless** (`ui-audit/verify-b303-b307.mjs`): draw a rect вЖТ Ctrl-Z removes it вЖТ Ctrl-Shift-Z and Ctrl-Y each restore it; undo disabled before any edit; same proven in the Stitcher.

### B304 вАФ Manual Calibrate validates input (no more silent mis-calibration) `[Doc Review / Markup]` (bug)  *(arrived as "NEW-2" 2026-06-20 owner chat; provisionally B284, renumbered **B304**; batch B303вАУB307)*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-20 (branch `claude/stoic-faraday-th9mp8`).** Repro: Calibrate вЖТ click two points вЖТ at the length prompt type a non-decimal form (e.g. **"1/8"** or **"1:240"**) вЖТ `parseFloat` returned **1** and the sheet calibrated to a wrong scale with NO warning, silently poisoning every downstream measurement; gibberish ("abc") silently did nothing. **Root cause:** `parseFloat(window.prompt(...))` stops at the first non-numeric char, and the invalid branch `return`ed with no feedback.
- **Fix:** replaced `window.prompt` with an **inline on-canvas entry box** (honoring the owner "no dialog boxes" rule, like `main`'s B293 text editor) backed by a new tested parser **`parseFeet`** (`lib/parseLength.js`). It validates the WHOLE string: accepts plain feet (`120`, `120.5`, `120'`), **feet-and-inches** (`38'-7 3/4"`), and explicit fractional feet (`12 1/2 ft`); **rejects** scale ratios (`1:240`), bare ambiguous fractions (`1/8`), non-numeric junk, and zero/negative вАФ each with a clear inline message. A bad entry keeps the box open to fix; a blank cancels. Applied in BOTH `DocReview.jsx` and `Stitcher.jsx`.
- **Dedup:** distinct from **B267/B268** (auto-calibrate / scale cross-check) вАФ the **manual-entry** path they don't cover. Clears the **calibration** half of the B155/B156 "no dialog boxes" note; `main`'s B293 already converted the **text** prompt, so only ParcelDrawing's calibrate prompt remains under B155.
- **Verified:** unit вАФ `test/parseLength.test.js` (7 cases incl. the exact "1/8" / "1:240" / "abc" bugs). Headless вАФ the inline box opens (no prompt), **rejects "1/8" and stays uncalibrated**, rejects "1:240" as a ratio, and **accepts "100" вЖТ sheet calibrated** (single sheet + Stitcher).

### B305 вАФ Markup toolbar overcrowds; header buttons wrap into uneven multi-line labels `[Doc Review / Markup]` (bug)  *(arrived as "NEW-3" 2026-06-20 owner chat; provisionally B285, renumbered **B305**; batch B303вАУB307)*

- **Verified headless:** the Open / Stitch / Library buttons compute `white-space:nowrap` and render as a **single 25px line** (вЙ§34px) at 1440px вАФ no wrapping. Screenshot `screens/b303-b307.png`.

### B306 вАФ Sheet paging: Prev/Next buttons + keyboard `[Doc Review / Markup]` (feature)  *(arrived as "NEW-4" 2026-06-20 owner chat; provisionally B286, renumbered **B306**; batch B303вАУB307)*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-20 (branch `claude/stoic-faraday-th9mp8`).** Repro: on a 32-sheet set the only way to change sheets was clicking each entry in the left list вАФ no Prev/Next, and arrow / PageUp / PageDown didn't flip sheets. **Fix** (`DocReview.jsx`): a **вАє N / total вАЇ** pager above the sheet list, plus **вЖР / вЖТ and PageUp/PageDown** keyboard paging (gated so they don't fire mid-draw or mid-calibrate-entry), and the sheet list **auto-scrolls to keep the current sheet in view** (`scrollIntoView`). A shared `goToPage` keeps the current zoom (matching `main`'s viewer behaviour) and drops any in-progress draft/selection.
