### B307 вАФ Measurement labels sit at the path midpoint / true centroid `[Doc Review / Markup]` (bug)  *(arrived as "NEW-5" 2026-06-20 owner chat; provisionally B287, renumbered **B307**; batch B303вАУB307)*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-20 (branch `claude/stoic-faraday-th9mp8`).** Repro: a Distance label rendered on the first endpoint (`pts[Math.floor((len-1)/2)]` resolves to `pts[0]` for a 2-point line); an Area label sat at the vertex average, which can fall outside a concave (L-shaped) region. **Fix** (new pure helpers in `lib/takeoff.js`): **`midOfPath(pts, closed)`** anchors distance/perimeter labels at the true **arc-length midpoint**; **`centroidOf(pts)`** anchors area labels at the **area-weighted centroid**, and when that lands outside a concave shape it drops to the midpoint of the widest interior scanline span so the label stays **inside**. Wired into `DocReview.jsx` (distance/perimeter/area) and `Stitcher.jsx` (area). Coexists with `main`'s B296 (the label's 1-dp numeric format) вАФ B307 is the label's POSITION.
- **Verified:** unit вАФ `test/takeoff.test.js` (midpoint of a 2-pt line + an L; closed wrap-around; square centroid; concave-L centroid proven interior by ray-cast). Headless вАФ a horizontal distance label renders at **xвЙИ454** (midpoint вЙИ450), not вЙИ250 (pts[0]).
### B300 вАФ Stitcher alignment has no degenerate-baseline guard; coincident clicks fling the sheet with a garbage transform `[Doc Review / Stitch]` (bug)  *(arrived as "NEW-1" 2026-06-20 owner chat; first filed B288 then renumbered **B300** вАФ concurrent `main` consumed B288вАУB299; batch B300вАУB302)*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-20 (branch `claude/admiring-hypatia-xjv8a1`).** Repro (numerically verified): in Stitch, aligning a sheet means clicking two matching points; if the two clicks on the moving sheet (or the two reference points) land on ~the same spot, `solveM`'s `lb = Math.hypot(vb) || 1` **masked the zero baseline** and returned an extreme similarity transform (e.g. `solveM(b1==b2, A1, A2 100 apart)` вЖТ √Ч100 scale, e/f вЙИ вИТ500), throwing the sheet far off-canvas at huge scale вАФ silently, and Stitch has no undo. **Fix:** extracted the pure stitch geometry (`fwd`/`inv`/`solveM`/`sheetBBox`) out of `Stitcher.jsx` into a unit-testable **`lib/stitchGeom.js`**, and added **`alignBaselinesDegenerate(b1,b2,A1,A2)`** + `MIN_ALIGN_BASE`, which rejects an alignment whose moving-sheet baseline `|b2вИТb1|` **OR** reference baseline `|A2вИТA1|` is below a small threshold (mirrors DocReview's Calibrate "line too short" guard). The align commit checks it **before** `solveM`: on a degenerate baseline it shows the banner ("Those two points are too close together вАФ pick two points farther apartвА¶") and restarts the alignment at step 0, leaving the sheet **untouched**; only a healthy baseline applies the transform (and now also stamps the sheet `aligned:true`, see B301).
- **Verified:** 8 unit tests (`test/stitchGeom.test.js`, incl. the runaway-scale case the guard blocks + `solveM` scale/rotation recovery + `fwd`/`inv` round-trip) and **headless on the built app** (`ui-audit/verify-b300-b302.mjs`, chromium-1228): a degenerate Align shows the banner and the sheet's `<g transform>` is **unchanged** (not flung); a real Align still succeeds. lint 0 ¬Ј build green; DocReview lazy chunk still splits (stitchGeom rides inside it).
> **Dedup (batch B300вАУB302):** net-new вАФ no existing item covers the stitch alignment math. NOT main's single-sheet-viewer **B288вАУB296** (zoom/pan/markup-edit) nor its auto-filing **B299** (server-side title-block read), all different surfaces; distinct from **B181/B182/B183** (the *map* placement cascade) and **B130/B131** (parking). Shares `lib/stitchGeom.js` with B301.

### B301 вАФ Measuring over a not-yet-aligned sheet silently uses the composite scale вЖТ wrong quantities `[Doc Review / Stitch]` (bug)  *(arrived as "NEW-2" 2026-06-20 owner chat; first filed B289 then renumbered **B301**; batch B300вАУB302)*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-20 (branch `claude/admiring-hypatia-xjv8a1`).** Repro: add a second sheet (it drops at identity scale, offset to the right) and draw a Distance/Area over it **before** pressing Align вАФ the measurement applied the single composite calibration (ft per world unit, defined by sheet 1), so if that sheet's real scale differed the reading was **silently wrong** (and even at a shared scale its position/rotation could be off). **Fix:** each placed sheet now carries an **`aligned`** flag вАФ the first sheet *is* the world frame (auto-aligned `true`); every later sheet starts `false` and flips to `true` only when its Align completes (B300's commit path). Unaligned sheets are **flagged visually** вАФ an amber dashed "вЪ† Not aligned вАФ click Align" overlay on the canvas, plus a "вЪ† Not aligned вАФ measurements may be off" chip + amber-emphasized Align button in the Placed-sheets list. Committing a Distance/Area whose points fall over an unaligned sheet (**`measureOverUnaligned`** / `sheetContains` in `lib/stitchGeom.js`) raises a **warning banner** ("Heads up: that measurement is over a sheet that isn't aligned yet вАФ Align it firstвА¶"). **Warn, not block** (the app's "surface it loudly, let the user decide" principle). The flag is persisted in the stitch snapshot and restored on load вАФ older saves default their non-base sheets to aligned, so nothing already-saved is falsely flagged.
- **Verified:** unit tests for `sheetContains` + `measureOverUnaligned` (warns only over an `aligned:false` sheet; never over the base or with no sheets) and **headless**: a fresh 2nd sheet shows the canvas overlay + the panel chip, a measurement over it shows the warning, and a successful Align clears both. lint 0 ¬Ј build green.
- **вЖС Superseded by B316 (2026-06-21, owner call "don't let it measure on uncalibrated things"):** the **warn** became a **hard block** вАФ a Distance/Area point over an un-aligned sheet is now refused at click time (`blockedOverUnaligned`, nothing commits), and the chip reads "Not aligned вАФ Align before measuring." `measureOverUnaligned`/`aligned`-state unchanged. See B316 / V83.

### B302 вАФ Degenerate 2-point Area (0 sf) and 2-point Perimeter (single segment) are committable `[Doc Review / Markup]` (bug)  *(arrived as "NEW-3" 2026-06-20 owner chat; first filed B290 then renumbered **B302**; batch B300вАУB302)*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-20 (branch `claude/admiring-hypatia-xjv8a1`).** Repro (numerically verified): `finishDraft` committed Area/Perimeter at вЙ•2 points, but a real polygon needs вЙ•3 вАФ a 2-point Area saved as **0 sf** (shoelace) and a 2-point Perimeter drew closed yet measured only the single segment (10 ft for a 10-unit span at 1 ft/u, not the 20 ft a closed loop implies), leaving meaningless zero/half entries in the takeoff list. **Fix:** added **`MIN_MEASURE_PTS` + `canCommitMeasure(kind,n)`** to `lib/takeoff.js` (area/perimeter вЙ•3, distance 2, count 1 вАФ matching what `polyArea`/`pathLength` actually need) and gated **both** finish paths on it вАФ Enter/`finishDraft` and (after merging main's B291 phantom-point fix) double-click/`onDbl` вАФ so a 2-point Area/Perimeter is a no-op (the draft is cleared) whichever way you finish, consistent with the existing count min-point guard. Other kinds (distance/rect/cloud/calibrate) are unaffected.
- **Verified:** unit tests for `canCommitMeasure` (the вЙ•3 / 2 / 1 contract) + the degenerate-geometry rationale (2-pt area = 0; a 2-pt "closed" path = one 10-unit segment, not 20; a real 3-pt loop closes 3+4+5=12) and **headless**: a 2-point Area finished by Enter or double-click commits nothing and the takeoff stays "No measurements yet", while a 3-point Area commits one polygon. lint 0 ¬Ј build green.
> **Dedup:** minor severity (clutter, not corrupted totals вАФ a 0-sf area contributes 0 to the rollup), filed with B300/B301 but a separate surface (`takeoff.js` / single-sheet Markup). Complements main's **B291** (which stripped the double-click's phantom points) by also enforcing the вЙ•3 minimum on that finish path.

### B299 вАФ Auto-filing: drop a drawing вЖТ it reads the title block вЖТ matches a project вЖТ files itself `[Document Review / Server + Files]` (feature)  *(owner HANDOFF 2026-06-20; first built as B270, renumbered through a very hot `main` that consumed B270вАУB298 вАФ incl. a different **B270** (Project Files drop-zone queue) and a different **B297** (account profiles) вАФ so it landed at the real next free ID **B299** at merge time)*
`[x]` **Built + wired + tested this session (branch `claude/sleepy-archimedes-gts4wa`).** The auto-filing **backend tranche**: drop a PDF вЖТ a server-side title-block read вЖТ match to one of the named projects вЖТ auto-route + auto-name, with a "needs filing" tray for anything it can't confidently match. Server-side because the read uses an **API key that must never reach the browser** (KEY DECISIONS) вАФ it lives in the `/server` compute layer (Cloud Run), distinct from Supabase. Status mirrors the convert (B238) / Drive (B207) backends: **code complete, fully unit-tested, wired through the UI, gated dormant** until the owner provisions Cloud Run + `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY` + `DOC_FILING_URL`.
- **Title-block reader** `server/filing/titleBlockReader.js` вАФ mirrors the client `titleReader.js` request shape (model `claude-opus-4-8`, adaptive thinking, a `json_schema` output, the PDF as a base64 `document` block) but runs **server-side** and calls the Messages API over **raw `fetch` with an injectable `fetchImpl`** (like `server/convert/aps.js`), so the Cloud Run image stays dependency-free and the read is unit-testable without a key. **One read, two payoffs:** the same pass captures the FILING fields (project / number / address / parcel / discipline / sheet # / title / revision / date) AND the PLACEMENT-readiness facts (scale callout + bar, north arrow, drawn boundary, stated coord system, labeled dimensions) in the shape of `src/shared/placement/placementFacts.js`. Pixel-geometry (scale-bar length in px, dimension endpoints) is deliberately left to the later CV step (B268/B183) вАФ the read captures presence + printed values, never guessed geometry. `parseStatedScaleFeetPerInch` handles engineer's (`1"=40'`) + architectural (`1/4"=1'-0"`) scales, NTSвЖТnull.
- **Matcher** `server/filing/matcher.js` (pure) вАФ scores each project on parcel/account (exact) вЖТ job number (exact) вЖТ address (token overlap) вЖТ name (token overlap), combined noisy-or; **never auto-guesses** (a misfiled drawing is worse than an unfiled one). A confident SINGLE project вЖТ `matched`; **no / multiple / low-confidence** вЖТ `needsFiling` with a reason (`no-readable-identifiers` / `no-match` / `ambiguous` / `low-confidence`). Thresholds tunable via env. `scoreProject` is transparent (lists the signal it matched on). Auto-name `server/filing/naming.js` mirrors the canonical `reviewStore.composeTitle` "<Project> - <Item> - YYYY.MM.DD".
- **Service + HTTP** `server/filing/filingService.js` (read вЖТ match вЖТ decision + the index row) + `server/filing/server.js` (`POST /file` body = PDF bytes, `X-Planyr-Projects` header = base64 JSON; `GET /health`) вАФ honest status codes (200 real decision / 400 / 413 / 422 unreadable / 503 not-configured), **never a 200 with a junk decision**. `Dockerfile` (no native binary, no npm install вАФ built-ins only) + `README.md`. The reader/service/server are injectable end-to-end (mirrors `dwgConvert.test.js`).
- **File-facts index (Supabase Postgres, NOT /server)** вАФ `src/workspaces/doc-review/db/file_facts.sql`: `public.file_facts` (one small row per filed drawing: project / discipline / sheet / revision / date / match confidence / needs-filing / placement jsonb), RLS private-by-default identical in shape to `doc_reviews`, indexed `(user_id, project_id, discipline, doc_date desc)` for the north-star "map вЖТ project вЖТ discipline вЖТ latest set" without re-reading the PDF. Client I/O `reviewStore.upsertFileFacts/listFileFacts` (degrade gracefully if unmigrated) + pure helpers `lib/fileIndex.js` (`toFactsRow`, `mergeFactsIntoReviews` вАФ surfaces captured placement on the drawer's review rows).
- **capturePlacementFacts wired (deliverable #4)** вАФ `src/workspaces/doc-review/lib/autofiling.js` is the real `createIndexProvider`: `capturePlacementFacts` + `autofile` ride the SAME server read. `backendReady` reflects `VITE_AUTOFILE_ENABLED` honestly (false by default вЖТ UI never claims "auto-detected" while dormant). Same-origin proxy `functions/api/file.js` (verifies the Supabase session, forwards to Cloud Run `DOC_FILING_URL`; 503 until set). The drawer drop handler auto-files when `backendReady`, else the **exact** prior manual path (a 404/503 is a graceful SKIP, like the Drive path) вАФ **no regression**.
- **Verified вАФ lint 0 ¬Ј 602 tests (52 new: `test/docFiling.test.js` 37, `test/autofiling.test.js` 15) ¬Ј build green; doc-review lazy-chunk split intact.** Headless on the built app (`ui-audit/verify-b299-autofiling.mjs`): the Project Files drawer opens, the new `autofilingProvider`/`fileIndex` imports evaluate in a real browser, **0 page/console errors**, auto-filing dormant by default (no spurious "it files itself" behavior). The signed-in dropвЖТreadвЖТfile round-trip + the live read are the deploy-gated checks (sandbox blocks sign-in + no key) вАФ logged as **VERIFICATION V74**.
- **Dedup:** this is the backend that fills the `createIndexProvider.capturePlacementFacts` seam B180/B181 stubbed and the auto-filing roadmap item; it WRITES THROUGH the Drive substrate (B207) and feeds the placement cascade (B182/B183). Distinct from B266/B267/B268 (the in-Markup sheet-label/scale siblings of the read pass) вАФ those share the title-block read principle but run browser-side on the open sheet; this is the filing index. **Owner to-do (deploy, when ready):** `gcloud run deploy` `server/filing/` + set `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY` (server-side) + point `DOC_FILING_URL` at it + set `VITE_AUTOFILE_ENABLED=1` + run `db/file_facts.sql` once.

### B297 вАФ First/last name capture at signup + a real `profiles` table `[Auth / Backend]` (feature)  *(arrived as "NEW-1"; first labeled B271, renumbered **B297** вАФ concurrent `main` consumed B271вАУB296)*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-20 (branch `claude/eloquent-edison-6anmlb`).** Names are now persisted in a queryable **`public.profiles`** table (one row per `auth.uid()`), not just in auth `user_metadata` вАФ the scalable foundation for the B2B direction (org/role/prefs later). The signup form already collected First/Last/Org; that path is unchanged (still seeds `signUp({ options: { data } })`), but a DB **trigger** now copies those into the table so there's one queryable source of truth for display.
- **Migration (idempotent, run once in the Supabase SQL editor):** `src/workspaces/site-planner/db/profiles.sql` вАФ the `profiles` table (`id uuid pk вЖТ auth.users on delete cascade`, `first_name`, `last_name`, `org`, `updated_at`); **RLS private-by-default** (the same select/insert/update own-row shape as `public.sites`/`public.doc_reviews`, `auth.uid() = id`, no cross-user reads, no delete вАФ the row lives/dies with the user); a `handle_new_user()` **SECURITY DEFINER trigger** on `auth.users insert` that inserts the matching row from `raw_user_meta_data` (the trigger route avoids the client-side follow-up-insert race вАФ the row always exists before the user can read it); and a **backfill** that seeds rows for all existing users (null names are fine вАФ the UI falls back, see B298). `on conflict (id) do nothing` throughout so re-running is safe.
- **Client I/O + hook (additive, reuses the existing anon client + session вАФ no new keys):** `src/workspaces/site-planner/lib/profile.js` (`loadProfile`/`saveProfile`, mirrors `cloudSync.js` shape; throws on a real fetch error so "no row" вЙ† "offline"; `saveProfile` also best-effort syncs the name into auth `user_metadata` so the table and the auth record never disagree and the offline fallback stays fresh) and `src/shared/profile/useProfile.js` вАФ the `useProfile(user)` hook returning `{ profile, loading, displayName, firstName, org, initial, reload, save }`, with a stale-fetch guard (a slow load can't show the previous user's profile) and an optimistic local update on save so the pill refreshes instantly.
- **Verified вАФ lint 0 ¬Ј 572 tests (562 + 10 new) ¬Ј build green.** The never-blank display chain is pure-extracted (`displayNameFor`/`firstNameFor`/`orgFor`/`initialFor`) and unit-tested in `test/profileDisplay.test.js` (profile wins over metadata; First Last вЖТ first вЖТ last вЖТ metadata вЖТ email; whitespace-only trims to email; empty only when there's no user). The actual cloud round-trip (real profiles table read/write while signed in) needs a signed-in click-through вАФ the sandbox proxy CORS-blocks auth вАФ logged as **VERIFICATION V73**.
> **Dedup:** builds on the existing email/password auth (Supabase Phases 2вАУ4) and the `AuthPanel` signup form (which already had the name fields). Distinct from the Site Model `status` reuse (B14) вАФ this is per-*user* identity, not per-*project* lifecycle. The deferred `planarfit:* вЖТ planyr:*` localStorage rename is untouched (separate item).

### B282 вАФ Opening a file from the global Project Files panel no-ops on the first click when launched from another workspace `[Doc Review]` (bug)  *(owner-reported 2026-06-20, repro'd in the signed-in session; arrived as "NEW-1"; first filed B270 then renumbered **B282** вАФ concurrent `main` consumed B270вАУB281 (incl. a different B270, the Project Files drop-zone queue) while this was in flight, so B282 is the real next free ID. "NEW-1" is only a scratch label вАФ B180/B206/B266/B270 also "arrived as NEW-1".)*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-20 (branch `claude/wonderful-galileo-abbbus`).** From the Site side, opening the global **рЯЧВ Files** panel (with a project like Jacintoport open) and clicking a filed document (e.g. the MEP set) switched to the **Markup** tab but landed on the empty **"Open or drop a construction PDF"** placeholder вАФ the document did **not** open; it stayed empty even after a multi-second wait, with **no console errors** (silent). The breadcrumb also reset to "Select a project". Clicking the **same file a second time** (now that Document Review was mounted) opened it correctly. 
- **Root cause (confirmed via the repro).** Document Review is a **lazy-loaded workspace** вАФ the Shell renders only the active workspace (`React.lazy`/`Suspense`), so DR's code doesn't mount until you first enter the tab. The **global** Project Files drawer lives in the Site Planner (`SitePlanner.jsx`), and its open handler was `onOpenReview={() => onShellSwitch?.("doc-review")}` вАФ it **switched workspaces but threw away the clicked review row entirely**. So in the same tick the app switched to DR *and* dropped the open request; DR mounted fresh and booted to its default/resume state, never opening the clicked file. The second click worked because DR was by then already mounted and its **own** in-workspace drawer wires `onOpenReview={openReview}` (the real handler). (The in-workspace path was never broken вАФ only the cross-workspace one.)
- **Fix вАФ persist the open-intent across the mount, mirroring the existing `navIntent` pattern.** New **`docIntent`** channel in `Shell.jsx`: `openReviewInDocReview(row)` stashes a **token-stamped** `{ kind:"open-review", row }` and *then* switches to `doc-review`; the Shell passes `docIntent` + `onOpenReviewInDocReview` to every workspace (parallel to the `navIntent`/Dashboard plumbing). The Site Planner's global drawer now calls `onOpenReview={(row) => onOpenReviewInDocReview?.(row)}` (threaded `SitePlannerApp` вЖТ `SitePlanner`), handing the **whole review row** up. `DocReview` consumes the pending intent in a mount/update effect (`openReview(row)`), guarded by a **module-scoped `lastConsumedDocToken`** (same technique as `SitePlannerApp`'s `lastConsumedNavToken`) so a plain tab switch-back never re-fires the last open.
- **No race with resume.** DR's boot effect (resume-the-last-review) now **stands down** when a fresh open-intent is present at mount (captured once via `bootDocIntentRef`), so the two async loads can't fight and silently land the wrong file.
- **Breadcrumb carries through.** `markupProject` is **seeded from the fresh intent** at mount (handling both a `listReviews` row's `project_id` and a loaded record's `projectId`), and `openReview` re-confirms it after load вАФ so the project context no longer flashes to "Select a project".
- **Can't fail silently again.** `openReview` is hardened: it wraps `loadReview` in try/catch and, when the row can't be loaded (removed row / cloud unreachable), shows a **visible dismissible error banner** ("Couldn't open вА¶") with a **Browse FilesвА¶** retry, instead of the previous bare `if (!rec) return`.
- **Verified вАФ lint 0 ¬Ј 550 tests ¬Ј build green; the DocReview / SitePlannerApp / ProjectFilesDrawer lazy chunks all still split (workspace isolation intact).** Headless smoke on the **built** app (`ui-audit/verify-new1.mjs`): Document Review **mounts and remounts cleanly** with the new `docIntent` prop + ref capture + intent effect + hardened `openReview` + error banner вАФ **zero JS errors** on a fresh mount AND after an unmount/remount. The signed-in **first-click open** itself (global Files вЖТ click a real filed set вЖТ DR opens it on the *first* click, breadcrumb shows the project) is **auth-gated** вАФ the sandbox proxy blocks sign-in and this build has no Supabase creds, so the panel can't list real files headless вАФ logged for a live signed-in confirm on planyr.io as **VERIFICATION V70**.
> **Dedup:** net-new вАФ the only cross-workspace "open a file into Document Review" handler is the global `ProjectFilesDrawer` rendered by `SitePlanner` (the in-workspace DR drawer + `ReviewsBar` + `ProjectLibrary` already call `openReview` directly and were unaffected). Distinct from **B180** (the Files tagged-index/saved-views feature this rides on) and from the silent-no-op family (**B82** calibrate, **B32** undo, the map-click open in B66) вАФ those are unrelated surfaces. Reuses the **B191вАУB193** `navIntent` cross-workspace pattern rather than inventing a new mechanism. Distinct from the concurrently-landed **B270** (Project Files drop-zone + processing queue) вАФ same `ProjectFilesDrawer` file, unrelated concern (file ingestion vs. cross-workspace open).

### B283 вАФ Coverage detection engine + honest per-layer status states `[Site Planner / GIS]` (feature)  *(arrived as "NEW-1" 2026-06-20; minted **B283** вАФ highest B# across both files was B273)*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-20 (branch `claude/busy-allen-ofgy9l`).** New **`lib/coverage.js`** engine answers, per layer, whether its DATA reaches the current view вАФ so a layer that loads green but paints blank outside its region reads as "no data here," not "broken" (the COH water/sewer/storm root cause). Each layer is tagged **national | statewide | regional** (`LAYER_SCOPE`). For a **regional** layer the engine reads the service's own **`fullExtent` from the existing `?f=json` health probe** (`probeService` now captures it вАФ **no extra request**), reprojects it to lat/lon, buffers it by the nearby radius (NEW-2/B284), and intersects it with the viewport вЖТ **`in` / `out` / `unknown`**. The three honest states (`displayCoverage`): **data-in-view**, **covers-region-but-empty-here**, **out-of-coverage**. National/statewide are **always in-coverage** (their empty/painted state still comes from the in-view query). **Fails open everywhere** вАФ missing extent or errored probe вЖТ treated as available, never hidden.
- **Real reprojection (the crux):** services publish their extent in mixed SRs вАФ verified live 2026-06-20 that **HCFCD/City-of-Houston use EPSG:2278 (Texas State-Plane, US ft)** while AGOL layers use **Web Mercator (3857)**. So the shared `src/shared/coordinates/index.js` stub's reserved **`projectToGrid`/`gridToProject`** are now **implemented** (Lambert Conformal Conic 2SP per EPSG GN 7-2), **validated against pyproj to <1e-4¬∞**; `coverage.js` dispatches 4326 / Web-Mercator / 2278 and reprojects all 4 extent corners to safely enclose the conic footprint. This is a read-only screening use вАФ the planner keeps its own per-site feet frame.
- **HARD RULE honoured + unit-tested:** coverage is a **picker-only** signal and **never** alters a layer's request bbox/where/extent. The request-spec builders live in a leaflet-free **`lib/layerRequest.js`** that takes **no coverage input by construction**; `test/coverage.test.js` asserts the COH request always carries its **full pinned sublayer set [0,1] and no where/bbox**, coverage-independent.
- **Wired** into the map finder + planner (recompute coverage on map move / view change, debounced, + when the nearby-range pref changes; regional extents prefetched once via the health probe and cached). **Tests:** `coverage.test.js` (27) + projection assertions in `coordinates.test.js` + `layerRequest.test.js` вАФ **609 tests green**, lint 0, build green, lazy chunks intact. **Verified live headless** (`gis-verify/coverage-picker-verify.mjs`, V71): panning north out of Houston flipped **HCFCD (State-Plane path) + H-GAC ETJ (Web-Mercator path)** to "No data in this area," 0 JS errors.

### B284 вАФ Coverage-aware layer picker: relevance modes + nearby range `[Site Planner / GIS]` (feature) вАФ depends on B283  *(arrived as "NEW-2" 2026-06-20; minted **B284**)*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-20 (branch `claude/busy-allen-ofgy9l`).** The Layers panel (`components/LayerPanel.jsx`) now consumes B283's coverage. A **"Relevance"** control вАФ **Show all / Dim / Hide** (**Dim** is the default) вАФ plus an adjustable **"nearby range"** slider (default **2.5 mi**, the buffer fed back into B283) decide how out-of-coverage layers are presented:
- **Dim:** out-of-coverage layers sink to the bottom of their group, grayed, with a **"No data in this area"** caption вАФ still one-click toggleable.
- **Hide:** they collapse behind a **"Show N layers with no local data here"** toggle (reveal shows them dimmed).
- A layer that is currently **ON is never demoted** (you always see what you've enabled). The mode + radius are **shared across both the map-finder and planner panels and persisted** (`coverage.js` prefs with pub/sub, `planarfit:relevance:v1`), so a change in one panel reflects in the other live.
- **List ordering/visibility ONLY вАФ never the rendered map** (the map is driven by `overlays` + `syncOverlayLayers`, untouched). `normalizeMode`/`normalizeRadius` clamp + default; unit-tested. **Verified live** (V71): the control + slider render, Dim is default, and the dim/"No data in this area" treatment fires on a real pan out of region.

### B285 вАФ Rename "Street-level detections (Mapillary)" to plain language `[Site Planner / GIS]` (task)  *(arrived as "NEW-3" 2026-06-20; minted **B285**)*

### B286 вАФ Mapillary layer was inert вАФ gated clearly as "needs setup" + excluded from the default set `[Site Planner / GIS]` (bug)  *(arrived as "NEW-4" 2026-06-20; minted **B286**)*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-20 (branch `claude/busy-allen-ofgy9l`).** The layer fired zero requests + showed a red "failed"-style "Add a Mapillary token" message as shipped вАФ it never worked. **Chose option (b): keep it, but gate it honestly** (not (a) bake a token вАФ that violates the secrets rule and ships a shared rate-limited key; not (c) remove вАФ its detections can be richer/fresher than OSM later, and the owner can have it gone with one word). A new **`needsSetup` flag** marks it as **not part of the default working set** (the relevance picker sorts a tokenless instance to the bottom as "Needs setup"), and the no-token state now reads **"Not configured вАФ add a free access token to enable this layer"** via a distinct **`unconfigured`** status (a gray "needs setup" dot, **not** the alarming red "failed") in `syncOverlayLayers` + `evidenceLayers.mapillaryLayer` вАФ and **no error toast** fires. **Note:** poles already come from OSM and hydrants from OSM + City-of-Houston, so this layer is redundant-but-optional today; say the word and it's removed entirely. **Verified live** (V71): toggling it (no token) reads "Not configured", no red failure.

### B287 вАФ Retry/backoff for transient 5xx on jurisdiction VECTOR services (City ETJ, County boundaries) `[Site Planner / GIS]` (bug)  *(arrived as "NEW-5" 2026-06-20; minted **B287**)*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-20 (branch `claude/busy-allen-ofgy9l`).** Live 2026-06-20 the City ETJ (H-GAC FeatureServer) and County-boundaries (TxDOT/AGOL) layers threw intermittent **503s on their geojson queries**. **Deduped against the existing retry/backoff** and found the gap: raster tiles already retry via `withTileRetry` and the `?f=json` metadata probe via `fetchWithRetry`, but **esri-leaflet's FeatureLayer issues its own GeoJSON query with no retry** вАФ so one transient blip dropped the whole vector layer to "failed." New **`attachFeatureRetry`** (`layers.js`) wires a pure **`featureRetryDecision`** policy (`layerRequest.js`) onto every `esriFeature` layer: on a `requesterror` it re-issues via `refresh()` with **exponential backoff** (400вЖТ800вЖТ1600 ms), holds the dot at "loading" while retrying, reports "failed" **only after `max` retries**, and resets on a successful `load`; a **hard 4xx is permanent** (no retry). The transient set (`429, 500, 502, 503, 504`) is now **one shared constant** (`TRANSIENT_STATUS`) across raster/metadata/vector. **9 unit tests** (`layerRequest.test.js`); lint 0 ¬Ј 609 tests ¬Ј build green.

### B279 вАФ Production error telemetry вЖТ Supabase table `[Infra / Telemetry]` (feature)  *(arrived as "NEW-2" 2026-06-20 owner chat; filed **B279** in the B278вАУB281 Infra tranche вАФ jumped past B271вАУB277 consumed by concurrent `main` + PR #217; batch comment lives in BACKLOG.md)*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-20 (branch `claude/trusting-hawking-1c4d6g`).** The app now self-reports runtime errors so silent production failures stop being invisible until someone stumbles on them. New **`src/shared/telemetry/clientErrors.js`**: three global sources вАФ window `error`, window `unhandledrejection`, and Vite's `vite:preloadError` вАФ plus the React **ErrorBoundary** (`componentDidCatch`) all funnel into one fire-and-forget sink that inserts a row into a new **`public.client_errors`** table via the EXISTING anon Supabase client (the "Supabase table, not Sentry" decision вАФ no new vendor, no new keys). Installed in `main.jsx` before render; the Shell tags each row with the active workspace (`setTelemetryModule`).
- **Session-optional + no read hole (RLS):** `src/shared/telemetry/client_errors.sql` makes the table **INSERT-only** for `anon` + `authenticated` (no SELECT/UPDATE/DELETE policy), so an error **during login вАФ before any session exists вАФ still records**, and clients can write but can never read the table back (admins read via the dashboard / service role). `user_id` defaults to `auth.uid()` (null when anonymous); `WITH CHECK (user_id is null or user_id = auth.uid())` blocks forging another user's id. **Run the SQL once in the Supabase SQL editor** (idempotent; same pattern as `doc_reviews.sql`).
- **Fail-safe + storm guard:** every path swallows its own errors and never rethrows into the app (telemetry that throws is worse than none). `decideReport` (pure, unit-tested) suppresses an exact-duplicate signature within 10 s and caps sends to 20/min, so a render-loop error storm becomes a handful of rows, not thousands. Messages/stacks truncated (2 k / 8 k). NOT capture-phase, so blocked tiles / broken images don't spam it.
- **Build provenance:** `vite.config.js` bakes the short git SHA into the bundle (`__BUILD_ID__` define, read via a typeof guard вЖТ "dev" under dev/test) and stamps it on every row, so a report traces back to the exact deploy.
- **Dedup (the filing's own correction held):** the `vite:preloadError` listener it "pairs with" already existed and shipped (**B221** `installChunkReloadGuard`, `src/app/chunkReload.js`); this **adds** a telemetry write for that event through its OWN listener (chunkReload.js left untouched + pure). NET-NEW otherwise вАФ no prior telemetry / Sentry item in either file.
- **Verification:** lint **0 errors** (only the pre-existing `SitePlanner.jsx`/`MapFinder.jsx` warnings); **587 tests** (12 new in `test/clientErrors.test.js` вАФ storm-guard dup/rate/window, row shaping, message/stack extraction + truncation, signature); `npm run build` green, all three workspace lazy chunks intact, `__BUILD_ID__` fully replaced (no leftover token). **Self-verified headless** (`ui-audit/verify-telemetry.mjs`, **6/6** on the built bundle via `vite preview`, re-run clean after merging the latest `main`): all three global sources captured with the correct `source` tag, a duplicate suppressed, build id baked in, and the page stays alive after firing synthetic errors (fail-safe). The live **cloud insert** (signed-in, after the one-time SQL) is the one auth-only path the sandbox can't exercise logged-out вЖТ logged in **VERIFICATION V69**.
> Independent of the B278 (Playwright) ID-collision concern; built + shipped this same session per the owner's "ship ship and then build whatever you need to." B278 / B280 / B281 stay Open (CI/secret-bound вАФ see their `вЫФ Verify-blocker` notes).

### B277 вАФ Overlay visibility toggle (hide without deleting) `[Document Review / Site Planner]` (feature)  *(arrived as "NEW-4" 2026-06-20; minted **B277** вАФ concurrent `main` consumed B270вАУB273 while this was in flight; batch B274вАУB277)*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-20 (branch `claude/peaceful-ride-k41y6e`).** Added a per-overlay eye / eye-slash toggle to the Site-plan overlay panel (`SitePlanner.jsx`) so a placed overlay can be switched OFF the map without deleting it вАФ the standard layers-UI affordance (Bluebeam/ArcGIS/Photoshop). Distinct from B272's delete (hide вЙ† delete): a hidden overlay stays in the panel, listed + recoverable.
- **Render:** the canvas overlay map skips an overlay with `visible === false` (returns null) вАФ off the map, still in the panel with the eye-slash to bring it back. **Persistence:** `visible` rides in the overlay record (saved + cloud-slimmed + content-merged like every other overlay field), so a hidden overlay stays hidden across reload (and, signed in, across devices); it's also folded into the undo/redo signature so a hide/show is undoable.
- **Data shape was already reserved (B131):** `isOverlayPrintable = o.src && o.visible !== false` was shipped "forward-compatible with a future per-overlay hide," so hiding an overlay **also drops it from Print/PNG export automatically** (WYSIWYG) вАФ no extra wiring. Inline `EyeIcon`/`EyeOffIcon` SVGs render crisply everywhere.
- **Verified headless** (`ui-audit/verify-overlay-delete-hide.mjs`, the built app, logged-out): hide removes the overlay from the map but KEEPS it listed; the hidden state PERSISTS across reload (the record carries `visible:false`); show brings it back. lint 0 ¬Ј 549 tests ¬Ј build green; `SitePlannerApp`/`DocReview` lazy chunks intact.
> **Dedup:** B131 (print-overlay master toggle) reserved the `visible` semantics; this implements the per-overlay UI toggle it anticipated. Pairs with B276 (delete persistence) вАФ same overlay surface, shipped together. (B314/B313, the data-integrity pair from the same batch, shipped this session too.)

### B276 вАФ Overlay delete doesn't persist across reload `[Document Review / Site Planner]` (bug)  *(owner-reported 2026-06-20, "Jacinto Port"; arrived as "NEW-3"; minted **B276** вАФ concurrent `main` consumed B270вАУB273; batch B274вАУB277)*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-20 (branch `claude/peaceful-ride-k41y6e`).** Deleting a placed overlay (the owner's "Jacinto Port" sheet) made it vanish, but it RETURNED on reload. **Root cause (as the backlog predicted):** the cross-copy reconciler `mergeSiteContent` (`siteModel.js`) **unions `sheetOverlays` by id**, so when the post-delete local copy (overlay gone) is merged with a copy that still has it вАФ the cloud copy on the next `pullCloud`/`mergePulledSites`, or another tab via the `storage` fold вАФ the deleted overlay is **resurrected**. Exactly the documented B126 union-merge trade-off ("a delete in only one copy can reappear once вАФ per-item tombstones are the fully-correct future hardening"); `removeOverlay` only dropped it from local state, nothing recorded that the deletion was deliberate.
- **Fix вАФ per-item tombstones (`deletedIds`), the B126 hardening, now built:** an additive Site Model field (`SITE_MODEL_VERSION` 5вЖТ6) holding ids the user deliberately deleted. `mergeSiteContent` unions the `deletedIds` from BOTH copies and **drops any tombstoned id from every unioned collection**, so a deletion wins over presence in either copy вАФ across reload, tab-sync, and device-sync. `removeOverlay` records the tombstone; it's threaded through the save effect, the live/undo refs, the cross-tab `storage` fold, `applySnapshot`, and version-restore so it persists and undo correctly resurrects (the tombstone rolls back with the overlay). Bounded + deduped (вЙ§5000 ids).
- **General but scoped:** the mechanism works for any collection (a tombstoned building stays deleted too) but is wired only at the overlay delete site for now; other delete handlers can adopt `setDeletedIds` trivially. **No regression:** collections not yet recording a tombstone keep the existing recoverable union behavior; `slimForCloud`/`slimForHistory` pass `deletedIds` through untouched (only inline rasters are stripped). **Composes with B297** (optimistic concurrency, shipped this session): a delete already rides the normal save, so it'll advance B297's version like any edit.
- **Verified:** unit вАФ `test/storage.test.js` (6 new B276 cases: tombstone in either copy wins, set-union, no-regression on non-tombstoned items, generalizes to a building, end-to-end through `mergePulledSites`). Headless вАФ `ui-audit/verify-overlay-delete-hide.mjs` (built app, logged-out): delete persists across reload and the record carries the `deletedIds` tombstone. lint 0 ¬Ј **549 tests** ¬Ј build green; lazy chunks intact.
> **Dedup:** net-new bug; the fix is the per-item tombstone B126 explicitly deferred. Distinct from B260 (overlay *scale* misread, done). Pairs with B277 (visibility), shipped together.
### B313 вАФ Multi-tab open warning (same project open in another browser tab) `[App Shell]` (feature)  *(arrived as "NEW-2" 2026-06-20; minted **B313** вАФ renumbered B275вЖТB298вЖТB313 as a very hot `main` reached B311; pairs with B314 + the already-live B276/B277)*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-20 (branch `claude/peaceful-ride-k41y6e`).** A non-blocking header banner now warns when the SAME project is open in another tab of the same browser вАФ "This project is open in another tab. Editing it in more than one tab can conflict вАФ work in a single tab to be safe." вАФ so a two-tab clash isn't a surprise. Same-browser only; cross-DEVICE conflicts are B314's server guard.
- **How:** `src/shared/presence/multiTab.js` вАФ a BroadcastChannel (same-origin cross-tab bus) presence tracker. Each tab announces its open project (`hello`/`here`/`update`/`bye` + a heartbeat); a pure `summarizePresence` reduces the live peer set into the banner state (conflict only when another tab is on the *same* project; stale peers pruned by TTL). Wired into the shared `AppHeader` via a `useMultiTab(projectId)` hook (BOTH workspaces get it); the banner clears the moment the other tab closes/navigates (its `bye`, or the TTL). Degrades to a silent no-op where BroadcastChannel is unavailable.
- **Verified headless** (`ui-audit/verify-multitab.mjs`, 4/4, the built app, two real tabs in one browser context): Tab A alone shows nothing; opening Tab B on the same project raises the banner in BOTH; closing Tab B clears A's banner. Plus **10 unit tests** (`test/multiTab.test.js`) incl. a real two-instance BroadcastChannel round-trip (same-project вЖТ conflict; different project вЖТ present-but-no-conflict; clears on leave). lint 0 ¬Ј build green; lazy chunks intact.
> **Dedup:** the VISIBLE companion to B127 (which made two same-browser tabs silently *converge*) вАФ surfaces the situation, doesn't replace the merge. **Optional, deliberately not built:** the Web Locks single-active-editor *lock* (non-leader tabs go read-only) вАФ the spec marked it optional; the banner is the required warning, the read-only lockout is an invasive follow-up. Pairs with B314 (the cross-device half).

### B314 вАФ Reject stale saves (optimistic concurrency on the save path) `[Platform / Persistence]` (bug)  *(arrived as "NEW-1" 2026-06-20; minted **B314** вАФ renumbered B274вЖТB297вЖТB314 as a very hot `main` reached B311; pairs with B313)*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-20 (branch `claude/peaceful-ride-k41y6e`); migration RUN by owner 2026-06-20 вЖТ goes ACTIVE on deploy.** Two sessions editing the same project no longer silently last-write-wins: a save carries the `version` it last synced, and the DB applies it ONLY if the stored version still matches (a single atomic conditional UPDATE), bumping it. A stale write (another session advanced the row) is **REJECTED as a conflict**, not applied вАФ the Site Planner shows a loud blue "this project was changed in another session вАФ reload before saving" banner with a **Reload** button. No silent clobber; work is never lost (the edit is saved on-device, and the reload union-merges it via mergeSiteContent, then re-pushes the combined result).
- **Reusable primitive (foundation for the deferred multi-user feature):** `src/shared/cloud/optimisticUpsert.js` вАФ a pure `casUpsert` compare-and-swap over `(user_id, id, version)`, used by BOTH `public.sites` (cloudSync.js) and `public.doc_reviews` (reviewStore.js). Version tokens are tracked per-tab in the cloud layer (populated on list/load, advanced on each write, cleared on delete / user-switch), so a conflict propagates back as a typed `{ conflict:true }` the UI turns into the reload prompt. Doc Review surfaces it on its save badge (the persistence hook gains a `conflict` state).
- **Graceful degradation = merge-safe:** before the migration ran, the conditional write returned "column version does not exist" and the client fell back to a plain upsert (today's EXACT behaviour) вАФ so saving never regressed; the guard was simply dormant. (The detector requires the error name the *version* column, so doc_reviews' optional library columns can't be mistaken for it and wrongly disable the guard.)
- **Verified:** **16 unit tests** (`test/cloudConcurrency.test.js`) cover the whole matrix вАФ conflict (0 rows), success (+version), degrade (un-migrated), brand-new insert, unique-violationвЖТconflict, never-throws, and the not-the-version-column guard. The live cloud conflict path needs sign-in (the sandbox blocks auth logged-out), so it's logged for a signed-in click-through (VERIFICATION V79). lint 0 ¬Ј build green; lazy chunks intact.
> **вЬЕ MIGRATION RUN (owner, 2026-06-20):** `src/workspaces/site-planner/db/optimistic_concurrency.sql` was run in the Supabase SQL editor (added the `version` column to `sites` + `doc_reviews`). The guard goes ACTIVE on this deploy. Composes with B276's tombstones (a delete advances the version like any write).

### B271 вАФ Canvas could get stuck unclickable behind a frozen grab/hand cursor when a pointer gesture was interrupted `[Core / Site Planner + Doc Review]` (bug)  *(owner-reported 2026-06-20 via chat, with a screenshot of the "Claude is debugging this browser" banner; arrived as "NEW-1"; minted **B271** вАФ real next free ID after concurrent `main` consumed B270)*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-20 (branch `claude/gifted-lamport-miamoc`).** Owner hit a state where the whole app went unclickable вАФ a hand cursor over everything, clicks doing nothing вАФ while every other website kept working. It coincided with a browser devtools/remote-debugger session attaching to the tab (the on-screen "Claude is debugging this browser" banner), but the fragility is **ours**: Planyr was the only page that locked up, so a latent bug in our pointer handling is the real cause (the attachment merely exposed it).
- **Root cause.** The planner canvas (`SitePlanner.jsx`) starts a pan/drag by capturing the pointer (`setPointerCapture`) and setting `panning` + `drag.current`, and relied **only** on `onPointerUp` (`onUp`) to release capture and clear that state. But the browser fires **`pointercancel`** (not `pointerup`) when a gesture is interrupted вАФ a devtools/remote-debugger session attaching, an OS gesture takeover, or the window losing focus mid-drag вАФ and the canvas had **no `onPointerCancel` handler and no blur/visibility recovery**. So the cleanup never ran: `panning` stayed `true` (cursor stuck on the select-mode grab/grabbing hand) with pointer-capture still held вЖТ the canvas swallowed every click. Other sites don't hold global pan/drag state, which is exactly why only Planyr broke. The same capture-pan pattern (same latent lockup) existed in the Doc Review **Stitcher** and the **ParcelDrawing** canvas.
- **Fix вАФ four independent recovery paths where there were zero** (`SitePlanner.jsx`, `doc-review/Stitcher.jsx`, `site-planner/components/ParcelDrawing.jsx`):
  1. **`onPointerCancel` on each canvas** вЖТ an `abortGesture()` that releases pointer-capture (via `e.pointerId`) and clears `drag.current` / `panning` / the in-progress marquee + draw drafts (it **aborts**, never commits a half-finished gesture).
  2. **Window `blur` + `visibilitychange`(hidden) recovery** вЖТ same teardown, **plus** it drops the Space hold-to-pan flag (`spaceRef`/`spacePan`) so a missed Space key-up can't leave the hand cursor on. Mirrors the existing Shift-reset-on-blur effect.
  3. **Escape** now also tears the gesture down (release capture + clear `drag`/`panning`/`spacePan`) вАФ a manual safety hatch on top of the draft/menu reset it already did.
  4. **`onBgDown`/`onUp` bookkeeping** вАФ record the captured pointer id (`capturePidRef`) so blur/Escape can release a capture they didn't see start, cleared on normal release.
- **Verified вАФ lint 0 ¬Ј 543 tests ¬Ј build green; lazy chunks (`SitePlannerApp`/`DocReview`) intact.** New headless test `ui-audit/verify-pointer-recover.mjs` drives a **real** pointer on the **built** app: a pan shows `grabbing`; **window blur** mid-pan recovers the cursor to `grab`; a **`pointercancel`** mid-pan recovers to `grab`; the canvas is still interactive afterward (a fresh pan re-engages); no uncaught errors. Before the fix, both interruptions left `grabbing` stuck (the lockup).
- **Dedup:** folds into the established pointer-capture discipline already in `onUp` (`setPointerCapture`/`releasePointerCapture`), not a parallel mechanism. The "ghost portal overlay" hypothesis was investigated and **disproved** as the cause: the full-canvas inline-editor catchers (`numEdit`/`editCallout`) already commit-and-clear on pointerdown and are bounded by their own state вАФ the stuck pointer-capture / stuck-pan path is what produced the lockout. Secondary "main-thread stall" hypothesis tracked separately as **B272** (investigated; no actionable bug; low priority).

### B270 вАФ Project Files: persistent drop-zone + processing queue (multi-file ingestion + persistent upload tray) `[Site Planner / Document Review вАФ Project Files]` (feature)  *(arrived as "NEW-1" from a parallel chat вАФ only Amendments A & B reached this session; minted **B270**, the real next free ID after concurrent `main` consumed B246вАУB269)*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-20 (branch `claude/quirky-bardeen-xje4nv`).** Turned the Project Files drop zone (the shared `ProjectFilesDrawer`, opened from Row 1 across workspaces) from a one-file-at-a-time loop that reported errors through a `window.alert` (a KEY-DECISION violation) into a **persistent processing queue with an upload tray**. Pure, browser-free model + derived view in **`src/shared/files/uploadQueue.js`** (`QUEUE_STATUS`, `makeQueueItem`/`makeQueueItems`, `splitQueue` (the derived two-group view), `hasPendingDemote`, `runPool` (concurrency pool), `isAcceptedFile`; **12 unit tests**, `test/uploadQueue.test.js`). UI wiring in `ProjectFilesDrawer.jsx` (`UploadTray` + `QueueRow` + the ingest/pipeline/demote logic); demote slide/fade in `index.css`.
- **Folded spec вАФ Amendment A (multi-file ingestion is first-class).** Drop, the native file picker (`multiple`), AND clipboard paste all funnel through one `ingest()` that iterates the file list and creates **one independent queue item per file**, each with its own `uploadId`, run through a small **concurrency pool** (3 at a time) вАФ so dropping 8 files yields **8 independent concurrent rows**, not one batch row and not a serialized chain. **Mixed types in one action:** PDFs enter the pipeline; unsupported types get a clear **per-file rejection row** (`rejected`, with a Dismiss √Ч) вАФ never silently discarded.
- **Folded spec вАФ Amendment B (persistent tray, not a vanishing toast).** Filed items do not disappear from under the user. On success a row goes to a calm muted **`done`** state (green check, reduced weight); after a ~3s confirmation beat it **demotes** from the active **PROCESSING** group into a collapsible **"Recently filed ¬Ј N"** group via a subtle slide/fade вАФ never an abrupt removal. The trail **collapses by default once it has more than ~3 entries** and has a **Clear** affordance. `needs_filing` (filed but unrouted вАФ a **Triage** button jumps to the holding area's one-click confirm) and `failed` (a **Retry** button) **never auto-dismiss** вАФ they stay in the active group until the user acts. **Net:** active group = in-flight + exceptions (live to-do); recently-filed = an auditable, clearable trail. The two groups are a **derived view over one queue array** (filter by status + a `filedAt` timestamp), not two lists вАФ the demote is a status/timestamp transition, exactly as the implementation note specified.
- **Graceful degrade kept:** an oversize (>50 MB) or upload-failed file still files the work layer and the row carries a non-fatal "re-drop on open to view" warn (it is `done`, not `failed`); a Drive-copy failure is a soft warn too. "Drive not enabled yet" stays silent (B207 best-effort).
- **Verification:** lint clean on the changed files (the 13 repo warnings are all pre-existing in `SitePlanner.jsx`); **549 tests** (537 + 12) green; `npm run build` green; the doc-review/`ProjectFilesDrawer` lazy chunk split still holds (28 kB chunk). Real-browser headless: (a) the existing `verify-files-refile.mjs` still PASSes (drawer mounts, **0 JS errors** вАФ the new imports/components load), and (b) drove a **mixed 3-file pick** through the real component вЖТ **"PROCESSING ¬Ј 3"**, two PDF rows + one **"Not a PDF" rejection row** with Dismiss, Retry buttons, **no `window.alert`** (screenshot captured). The `done`вЖТRecently-filed demote / >3 collapse / Clear need a *successful* cloud filing (= sign-in, which the sandbox blocks logged-out) вАФ that path is unit-tested (`splitQueue`/`hasPendingDemote`/`RECENT_COLLAPSE_AT`) and logged for a signed-in click-through in VERIFICATION (**V66**).
> **Dedup вАФ build on what's shipped, don't fork:** this upgrades **B180**'s drop zone (the saved-views drawer) and reuses **B217**'s "needs filing" holding area + one-click confirm (Triage routes there вАФ no second filing UI). **Auto-file-by-title-block** (read title block вЖТ match a project вЖТ auto-route/auto-name; low-confidence вЖТ holding area) is **NOT** this item вАФ it stays the **backend tranche** (B180 вП≥ + the auto-filing roadmap item), stubbed behind `createIndexProvider`; B270 is the browser-only ingestion/queue surface it will feed. Filing still files under the active project (or the holding area) until that lands.

### B265 вАФ Doc Review (Markup) PDF render is blurry вАФ honour devicePixelRatio `[Doc Review / Markup]` (bug)  *(arrived as "NEW-2" 2026-06-20; renumbered **B265** as concurrent `main` consumed B246вАУB264; batch B265вАУB269, the other four filed Open: B266/B267/B268/B269)*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-20 (branch `claude/friendly-euler-hw8v1t`, PR #205).** Sheets in Markup rendered soft/illegible вАФ note text unreadable at fit-to-page, only marginally better zoomed вАФ because `renderPageToCanvas` (`src/workspaces/doc-review/lib/pdf.js`) sized the canvas backing store to `(scale √Ч base)` with **no devicePixelRatio factor** and gave the canvas no explicit CSS size, so on a HiDPI/Retina display the browser **upscaled a 1√Ч-density bitmap** to fill 2√Ч physical pixels = blur. (Same HiDPI class as the Site Planner's B169/B170 basemap fix вАФ different surface: the PDF.js canvas, not Leaflet tiles.)
- **Fix:** the page now renders the backing store at `scale √Ч dpr` (`dpr = min(window.devicePixelRatio, 2)`) while the canvas's **on-screen (CSS) size stays at the logical `scale√Ч` size** (`canvas.style.width/height`), so the dense bitmap is sampled down вЖТ crisp text. A new `backingScale()` caps the backing store to a **~24 MP budget** (drops dpr toward 1√Ч on a huge E-size sheet at deep zoom) so the denser render can't OOM, and **never goes below 1√Ч** (never worse than before). Zoom already re-renders at the new scale (true re-rasterization); this makes every render dpr-aware.
- **Overlay geometry unchanged by construction:** `renderPageToCanvas` still returns `dims.w/h = floor(base √Ч scale)` вАФ byte-identical to before вАФ and that's what both the wrapper box and the markup SVG overlay bind to, so measurements/markups land exactly where they did.
- **Verified headless** (`ui-audit/verify-new2-dpr.mjs`, the REAL built viewer driven at two pixel densities with a generated 1-page PDF): at **deviceScaleFactor 2** the backing store is **2.000√Ч** the CSS size (1054вЖТ2108 px) = crisp; at **deviceScaleFactor 1** it's **1.000√Ч** (unchanged); the **on-screen size is identical across both densities** (1054√Ч1364) вЖТ overlay geometry provably unaffected. lint 0 ¬Ј 543 tests ¬Ј build green; DocReview + pdf lazy chunks intact. The crispness *gain* only manifests on real HiDPI hardware (headless DPR-forcing proves the 2√Ч mechanism); logged for a live retina eyeball as **VERIFICATION V65**.
> **Dedup:** net-new for the Doc Review canvas вАФ **B169/B170** (basemap HiDPI/retina) and the map-finder over-zoom fixes are the *Site Planner basemap-tile* siblings of the same principle, not this surface. The Stitcher's `renderPageToImage` is a separate path (fixed 2√Ч + a placed-image transform), intentionally left as-is. Filed alongside **B266/B267/B268/B269** (sheet labels, auto-calibrate, scale cross-check, sample-fixture cleanup) which stay Open вАФ this was the cleanly-fixable, verifiable one of the batch.

### B260 вАФ Dropped site-plan overlay placed 10вАУ30√Ч too large when its printed scale is misread вЖТ the drawing's title block blankets the map ("file name all over the map") `[Site Planner / overlay]` (bug)  *(owner-reported 2026-06-20 with a screenshot of "Jacinto"; arrived as "NEW-1"; minted **B260** вАФ concurrent `main` took B246 (dock-zone build-out, PR #204) and B247вАУB259 (Scheduler backlog) while this was in flight, so B260 is the real next free ID after B259)*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-20 (branch `claude/sweet-wozniak-txzr3e`).** Owner dropped a landscape drawing onto the planner and a huge rotated string вАФ the sheet's title block, ~`BV-255-2024-LD1 вА¶ ARCH ASSET FOR вА¶` вАФ covered nearly the whole aerial; only the parcel (`26.33 ac`) looked right.
- **Diagnosis (corrected the hand-off's guess).** It is **NOT** a world-scaled *text label*: every label path in the planner is screen-space or px-capped вАФ element labels `11¬Јls`, parcel acreage chip `12¬Јls`, callouts are boxed + capped at their own `size`, all markup/measure labels are fixed px, and the overlay's name **placeholder** is a hard-coded `fontSize={13}` (confirmed in a headless seed: the placeholder text stays 13 px even when its dashed rect is huge). The giant string is the rasterized overlay **IMAGE** itself. `addOverlayFile` auto-applied a scale note read off the sheet (the B73 `trueScale` path вЖТ `ftPerPointForScale(detectedScale)`) with **no sanity check on the resulting size**. A landscape sheet commonly prints a **vicinity / key-map scale** (e.g. 1вА≥=600вА≤) next to the plan scale (e.g. 1вА≥=30вА≤), and `parseScaleNote` returns the **first in-range match**, so the vicinity scale can win вЖТ `ftPerPx` 10вАУ30√Ч too big вЖТ `imgW¬ЈftPerPx¬Јppf` renders the sheet (and its title block) enormous, spilling far past the viewport. (The drawing's white paper is knocked to transparent, so on a dark aerial the only thing that reads is the dark title-block text вАФ which is why it looks like "just the file name, splattered.") **Reproduced headless:** a seeded overlay at the misread 1вА≥=600вА≤ rendered **14279√Ч9519 px** on a 1440√Ч900 view.
- **Fix 1 вАФ guard the auto-scale (root cause).** New pure, browser-free `chooseOverlayScale()` in `lib/overlayScale.js`: trust the read scale **only** when it lands the sheet at a sane on-screen size (**вЙ§4√Ч / вЙ•0.04√Ч the viewport width**); otherwise fall back to the existing "size to fit" (~60% of the view) and report a `too-big`/`too-small` reason. The read scale is **still stored** on the overlay, so the panel's "Read from sheet: 1вА≥=XвА≤ **[Apply]**" still offers it as a one-click when the user wants it. `addOverlayFile` now routes through it and, on a rejected scale, flashes an **honest, actionable** note ("вА¶its printed scale would place it far too large вАФ sized it to fit instead; set the exact scale or 'Trace a length' in the Site-plan overlay panel"). No silent mis-place.
- **Fix 2 вАФ one-click rescue.** New **"Size to view"** button in the Site-plan overlay panel: resizes the selected overlay to ~60% of the current view and recenters it вАФ recovery for an already-splattered overlay (the owner's existing "Jacinto" file) or any manual scale slip. Distinct from "Fit view" (which zooms the canvas), with tooltips on both to disambiguate.
- **Verified вАФ lint 0 ¬Ј 538 tests ¬Ј build green; lazy-chunk split intact.** `chooseOverlayScale` has **7 new unit tests** (`test/overlayScale.test.js`: trusts a correct 1вА≥=30вА≤, rejects a misread 1вА≥=600вА≤ as too-big, rejects a deep-zoom tiny render as too-small, falls back with no/non-standard scale, the fit fallback вЙИ 60% of the view, NaN/zero-divide defense). Headless on the **built** app (`ui-audit/verify-overlay-fix.mjs`): **(A)** dropping an image runs the real import path вЖТ overlay lands **535 px** wide on a 1440 px view (sane, not splattered); **(B)** a seeded splattered overlay (**14279 px**) shrinks to **535 px** with one "Size to view" click (before/after screenshots). **Honest gap:** PDF rasterization can't run in the sandbox Chromium (pdf.js `getOrInsertComputed` is unsupported there), so the PDF scale-read path is covered by the unit tests + the image-path E2E rather than an end-to-end PDF drop вАФ logged for a real-browser confirm as **VERIFICATION V63**.
- **Dedup:** distinct from **B148** (oversized world-space *summary banner* вАФ a genuine screen-vs-world text bug) and builds on **B73** (the overlay scale tooling this hardens). The hand-off's "world-scaled label, scaled to the geometry's bounding box" hypothesis was investigated and **disproved** вАФ no label path produces it; the cause is overlay-image scaling. The "Place on map" cascade (`shared/placement/placeOnMap.js`, B182) remains a stub (`onPlaceOnMap` only closes the drawer) and emits no label, so there is **no** second "auto-place emits a bogus label" item.

### B247 вАФ Scheduler Export modal: Header/Cover fields drop focus after every keystroke `[Scheduler / UI]` (bug)  *(orig "B3/M4" in the owner's Planar backlog; provisionally B246, renumbered **B247** вАФ concurrent `main` took B246 (dock-zone build-out, PR #204) while this was in flight, so B247 is the real next free ID after B246)*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-20 (branch `claude/zen-bohr-7xgk6q`).** In Export вЖТ "Header / Cover", typing in Exhibit / Title / Prep. by / Prep. for / Date / Conf. tag dropped focus after each character (one keystroke at a time). **Cause:** `Field` (and `Toggle`/`SegBtn`/`Row`) were defined *inside* `PDFExportModal`, so every render minted a new component identity вЖТ React unmounted the live `<input>` and mounted a fresh one, taking focus with it. **Fix:** hoisted `Field`/`Toggle`/`SegBtn`/`Row` to module scope (all props-only вАФ no closure over modal state) above `PDFExportModal`; their JSX usages are unchanged (now resolve to the stable module-scope identity). `SHdr` was deliberately left inside the modal вАФ it closes over `setSecOpen`/`secIsOpen`, so hoisting it would need prop-threading for zero user benefit (perf-only). **Verified headless** (`ui-audit/verify-scheduler-bugfixes.mjs`, V62): typed "ALTA & Topo Survey вАФ Phase 2" character-by-character into the Title field вАФ full value intact, focus retained, 0 console errors.

### B248 вАФ Scheduler "Export Report" (HTML) doesn't escape user strings `[Scheduler / export]` (bug)  *(orig "B6¬љ")*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-20 (branch `claude/zen-bohr-7xgk6q`).** The older `exportHTML` path still did raw template interpolation, so a task named "ALTA & Topo Survey" or "Budget > $1M" (or any `<`/`>`/`&` in name/owner) corrupted the downloaded HTML report. `buildPDFHtml`/`buildGanttSVG` already used the module `escapeHtml` helper; this was the last raw path. **Fix:** wrapped every interpolated user string in `exportHTML` вАФ project name, task id, task name, start/end dates, the status label, and owner вАФ in `escapeHtml(...)`. Numbers (duration, %) left as-is.

### B249 вАФ Deleting a custom status crashes views that still reference it `[Scheduler / status]` (bug)  *(orig "B1")*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-20 (branch `claude/zen-bohr-7xgk6q`).** Create a custom status вЖТ apply to tasks вЖТ delete it, and several views went blank (the % Done cell, the HTML export) because the deleted key was dereferenced as `HEALTH[t.health].dot` with no fallback. **Fix, two halves:** **(a) Reassign on delete** вАФ `removeOption` now walks every project's tasks and sets `health: "gray"` ("Not Started") on any task still carrying the deleted key *before* filtering the status out (same `setData`), so no task is ever left pointing at a missing key. **(b) Defensive lookups** вАФ guarded the two genuinely-unguarded sites with `(HEALTH[вА¶] || HEALTH.gray)` (the `exportHTML` row and the % Done cell), matching the `|| HEALTH.gray` pattern already used in ~10 spots. The project-header lookup (`HEALTH[projHealth(cur)]`) was already safe вАФ `projHealth` only ever returns base keys.

### B250 вАФ JSON import skips the normalization/migration pipeline `[Scheduler / import]` (bug)  *(orig "B4")*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-20 (branch `claude/zen-bohr-7xgk6q`).** `importJSON` did `setData(parsed)` raw, skipping the migration the cloud/seed **load** path runs вАФ so an old or partial backup could load with predecessors in the old shape, missing settings, and un-cascaded dates. **Fix:** route the import through the *same* pipeline as load: `ensureContacts(normalizeIds(ensureHolidays(normalizeToV6(parsed))))`, then rebuild `HOLIDAY_SET` and run `cascadeDates вЖТ rollupParentDates` per project (mirrors the seed-load branch exactly). The pre-import `pre-import` snapshot is preserved. A current backup re-imports byte-identically (the migrations are idempotent); an old/partial one loads cleanly with defaults filled in.

### B251 вАФ New/renamed custom status renders one beat late `[Scheduler / status]` (bug)  *(orig "B5/M3")*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-20 (branch `claude/zen-bohr-7xgk6q`).** Adding or renaming a custom status often didn't show in pickers until you clicked around. **Cause:** `HEALTH`/`HK`/`HDARK` are module-level mutable globals rebuilt by `rebuildHEALTH(...)` inside the `[data]` effect; the rebuild mutates the globals but doesn't itself re-render, so the render that processed the change read stale values. **Fix (the low-risk option A):** track a `prevHealthKey` ref of the serialized `customHealth`+`healthLabelOverrides`; after `rebuildHEALTH`, when that key actually changes, bump a small `setHealthTick` once to force a re-render that re-reads the fresh globals. Keyed so it fires only on real status-config changes, and loop-safe (the tick isn't a `[data]` dependency, so it can't re-trigger the effect) вАФ mirrors the existing holiday-recascade guard in the same effect. **Verified headless** (V62): boots clean, no "Maximum update depth" loop, 0 console errors.

### B252 вАФ Undo history holds 50 full board snapshots `[Scheduler / perf]` (task)  *(orig "P3")*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-20 (branch `claude/zen-bohr-7xgk6q`).** Every edit pushed a full deep copy of `data` onto the undo stack, capped at 50 (~50√Ч the board's JSON held in memory). **Fix:** lowered the cap to 20 (`slice(-19)`) вАФ undo still works through many steps, memory footprint cut ~60%. (The bigger "snapshot only the active project / store inverse diffs" options stay deferred under B256/roadmap; not needed yet.)

### B253 вАФ "Today" stays fresh across midnight / tab-left-open `[Scheduler / dates]` (bug) вАФ already resolved  *(orig "B7")*
`[x]` **Already done in current code; verified 2026-06-20, no change needed.** The owner's doc predated the fix. `NOW` is now a live module value refreshed on `focus`, `visibilitychange`, and a 60s `setInterval`, each bumping a `todayTick` that forces the re-render that re-reads it; `computeDisplayHealth` (overdue/due-soon) and the Gantt "today" line read `NOW`; `NotesModal` stamps `toShortDate(NOW)` / `parseFlexDate(dateStr) || NOW` at open time. So the today line, overdue colouring, and new-note date all roll over without a reload. Filed for the record so the old finding is closed.

### B254 вАФ Split-view Snap/Free chip lingers ~5s after releasing the divider `[Scheduler / UI]` (bug?) вАФ resolved as won't-change  *(orig "B9"; minted **B254**)*
`[x]` **Resolved 2026-06-20 (no code change вАФ owner decision).** The owner's doc suspected the `setTimeout(() => setDragging(false), 5000)` (public/sequence/index.html) was a 500ms typo. **Inspected first:** the chip is an *interactive* Snap/Free toggle (fixed portal, top-right); the ~5s keeps it clickable after a drag so you can flip snap mode for the next drag without re-grabbing the divider вАФ i.e. the delay serves a real purpose, not an obvious typo. Raised it to Michael; he said **"don't worry about the chip thing"** вЖТ leave the 5s as-is. Closed so it isn't re-raised. No change shipped.

### B261 вАФ Add an explicit "Group" tool (Bluebeam-style, no content lock) `[Site Planner]` (feature)  *(arrived as "NEW-1" 2026-06-20; minted **B261** вАФ highest B# across both files was B246, so B261вАУB264 are the real next free IDs)*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-20 (branch `claude/eager-keller-1ueisx`).** A deliberate Group replaces the old implicit drag-to-bond. A persistent group = a shared **`groupId`** on вЙ•2 els/markups (additive Site-Model field; rides `els`/`markups` losslessly, no migration). It is DISTINCT from the temporary multi-selection (marquee / Shift-click; evaporates on the next click) AND from the building-host **`attachedTo`** assembly (a rigid childвЖТhost bind with resize-refit).
- **Commands:** select вЙ•2 вЖТ **Group** (toolbar **вКЮ Group**, the element context menu's "Group selection (N)", or **Ctrl+G**) stamps a fresh `groupId`. **Ungroup** via toolbar **вКЯ**, context menu, or **Ctrl+вЗІG**. **Duplicate group** (Ctrl+D on a group, or context "Duplicate group") clones every member + each member's attached children with remapped ids and a fresh shared `groupId`; a LONE paste/duplicate strips `groupId` (added to `ORPHAN_TAGS`) so a single copy starts standalone.
- **Grouping means "they stay together," nothing more** (owner clarification 2026-06-20): a single click on any member selects the WHOLE group, and move / copy / delete / arrow-nudge then act on all of them вАФ basically how a building + its attached features already travel together, extended to arbitrary peers (e.g. a road + an easement). A dashed enclosing box labelled "вКЮ Group" marks it as one unit. **There is deliberately NO whole-group resize** вАФ scaling everything at once "isn't how you plan buildings" (site elements are real feet). To resize a piece, drill into it (below). (An earlier build added uniform group-resize handles; removed per the owner вАФ `startGroupResize`/`scaleMarkup` deleted, the box is now a pure indicator.)
- **No content lock:** double-click a member to "drill in" (`drillId`) and edit it in place (resize / retype / restyle) WITHOUT ungrouping; right-click still opens the actions menu; members keep their own properties. Grouping happens ONLY from the explicit command вАФ never from a plain drag or click.
> **Self-verified headless** (`ui-audit/verify-b261-b264.mjs`): group two elements вЖТ "вКЮ Group" box renders with **no resize handles** вЖТ dragging one member moves **both** (108px each) вЖТ Ungroup removes the box вЖТ members move independently again; **0 page errors**. lint **0 errors** ¬Ј **537 tests** ¬Ј build green; `SitePlannerApp` lazy chunk intact. Logged **VERIFICATION V64**.
> **Dedup:** no prior open Group item. Supersedes the *bonding* half of the B114 snap/bond work (the Shift-dragвЖТ`attachedTo` bond is removed вАФ see **B262**). The owner-mentioned "earlier split-snap item" was the B114 family (already done), not a separate open item; the still-open **B115** (keyboard-shortcuts pass, owner-gated) listed the now-removed вЗІ-drag bond gesture вАФ its shortcut table is updated here.

### B262 вАФ Keep snap as pure alignment only (no relationship) `[Site Planner]` (feature)  *(arrived as "NEW-2" 2026-06-20; minted **B262**)*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-20 (branch `claude/eager-keller-1ueisx`).** Removed the implicit drag-to-bond entirely: the Shift-drag вЖТ `alignSnap` вЖТ `attachedTo` path, the green "+" attach hint, and the bond-on-drop in `onUp` are gone, and the now-unused `alignSnap` / `flushContact` / `isAxisRect` helpers + `canAttach` / `bondTarget` / `bondRot` were deleted (net вИТ2 lint warnings). Dragging an element now only MOVES it; with snap on, the ambient flush-snap (`edgeSnapCenter`) only ALIGNS position (grid + flush against neighbours, AutoCAD-style) and never creates a group or attachment. The building-host `attachedTo` assembly (docks / parking / sidewalks) and the explicit "Attach toвА¶" command are unchanged.
> **Self-verified headless** (V64): with snap ON, dragging a building flush against a parking field then away leaves the parking untouched (ќФ=0px вАФ no bond).
> **Dedup:** pairs with **B261** (grouping moved to the explicit Group tool); narrows **B114** (the snap toggle + Alt-bypass stay; only the bond half is removed).

### B263 вАФ Snap pref is silently global & sticky across sessions/projects `[Site Planner]` (bug)  *(arrived as "NEW-3" 2026-06-20; minted **B263**)*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-20 (branch `claude/eager-keller-1ueisx`).** Snap was persisted in `localStorage` (`planarfit:snap`) and re-applied on every load, so it could be ON without the user enabling it this session ("I never clicked snap"). It's now a **per-SESSION** pref: it defaults **OFF** every time the app opens, is remembered only within the current browser-tab session (`sessionStorage` вАФ survives plan/project switches this session, resets on a fresh tab/session), and `loadSnapPref` retires the old global `localStorage` key on read. The toolbar pill makes state explicit (**"Snap off"** / **"Snap 10вА≤ on"** with a green dot) and its tooltip clarifies snap only aligns position вАФ it never groups or bonds (so with **B262** no group/bond-type move can fire from this flag).
> **Self-verified headless** (V64): a fresh session вЖТ button reads "Snap off" and no global `localStorage` key exists; toggling on writes `sessionStorage` only.

### B264 вАФ No way to delete a single plan; only "delete site + all plans" `[Site Planner]` (feature)  *(arrived as "NEW-4" 2026-06-20; minted **B264**)*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-20 (branch `claude/eager-keller-1ueisx`).** Added a per-plan delete to the **Plan вЦЊ** menu: each plan row carries a **вЬХ** that arms an inline **"Delete '<name>'? Delete / Cancel"** confirm (no `window.confirm` вАФ honours the no-dialog-edits rule). The **last** plan in a site never shows a вЬХ (removing the whole site stays the map/finder's job). App-side `deletePlan` removes just that plan; if it was the plan currently open it switches to a sibling. A new `deletedSelfRef` suppresses EVERY save path for the plan being deleted (the debounced autosave, the leave/unmount `persistOrDrop`, the `beforeunload`/visibility flush, and `flushSite`) so the unmounting planner can't immediately re-write the row we just deleted.
> **Self-verified headless** (V64): a 2-plan site вЖТ вЬХ shows the inline confirm вЖТ Delete removes one plan (the **current** plan was deleted вЖТ it switched to the sibling and did NOT resurrect) вЖТ the lone remaining plan has no вЬХ; **0 page errors**.

### B246 вАФ Employee/non-dock side build-out: "пЉЛ" adds sidewalk вЖТ parking rows (mimics the dock stack) + restore the lost sidewalk `[Site Planner]` (bug/feature)  *(owner-reported, chat вАФ "still missing the option to addвА¶ rows of parking. Filed provisionally as B243, renumbered **B246** вАФ concurrent `main` took B243вАУB245.)*
