Wired to **both** the on-canvas non-dock "пЉЛ/вИТ" pair (per side, with a live title: "Add a 5вА≤ sidewalk" вЖТ "Add a parking row" вЖТ "Add another parking row") **and** the panel **Car parking** row (applies to every non-dock side). So car parking now grows unlimited rows like the dockside zones, and the sidewalk is back as the first step. (Non-dock side = the short ends, plus the long side opposite single-load docks.)
> **Self-verified headless** (`ui-audit/verify-dock-zones.mjs`, rebased on latest `main`): on a non-dock side the 1st "пЉЛ" restores the **sidewalk**, the 2nd adds the **first parking row**, the 3rd **deepens the field by another row** (27px вЖТ 38px on screen); the panel + on-canvas dock-stack and per-zone flows all still pass; **0 page errors** (`dock-zones-parking.png`). lint **0 errors** ¬Ј **532 tests** ¬Ј build green; `SitePlannerApp` lazy chunk intact. Logged **VERIFICATION V55** (updated).
> **Dedup:** extends B242 (on-building controls); reuses the existing `addSidewalkSide` / `addParkingRowSide` / `growParking` so the employee side stays consistent with the row-stepping used by the Car Parking element elsewhere.

### B244 вАФ Resilient county parcel fetch with TxGIO statewide fallback `[Site Planner / parcels]` (feature)  *(arrived as "NEW-1" 2026-06-20; minted **B244** вАФ concurrent `main` took B239вАУB243 (Schedule stale-chunk hardening, brand icons, dock-zone fixes, PDF download) while this was in flight, so B244/B245 are the real next free IDs after B243)*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-20 (branch `claude/focused-darwin-8gkesb`).** When a county's own appraisal-district endpoint is down, parcel selection now degrades gracefully instead of hanging. Trigger was the 2026-06-19 FBCAD outage: `gis.fbcad.org/serverarcgis2` returned 503 then **total timeouts on every path** (layer, `/rest/services`, `/rest/info` вАФ the whole ArcGIS server unresponsive), so a Fort Bend click **froze the tab ~45s** with no answerer. What shipped:
- **Hard timeout (the freeze fix).** `fetchJson` in `lib/arcgis.js` now wraps every county GIS request in an **`AbortController` with an 8 s cap** (`PARCEL_FETCH_TIMEOUT_MS`) вАФ an indefinite hang becomes a prompt, typed `timeout` failure so the fallback can take over. Covers **every** parcel surface automatically (map click-select, address-search select, in-planner identify) since they all route through `fetchJson`/`queryAtPoint`.
- **Per-source circuit breaker.** New `lib/sourceHealth.js` (pure, injectable clock, **7 tests**): after **3 consecutive failures** a source's breaker **opens for a 5 min cooldown** (`recordSourceResult`/`isSourceOpen`/`sourceCooldownMs`), then auto-resumes (half-open) so a recovered server is picked back up without a reload. `filterHealthyCandidates` drops an open primary from the click's candidate list **but never the statewide source** вАФ so we stop re-hammering a dead host while coverage always survives. A success resets the streak (a blip never trips it). Wired into `MapFinder.handleClick` + `selectParcelAt`: candidates are health-filtered before the query and `identifyParcelDetailed`'s new per-source outcomes feed the breaker.
- **Fallback chain (primary вЖТ TxGIO statewide).** B137 already appended the statewide TxGIO layer (`feature.geographic.texas.gov/.../stratmap_land_parcels_48_most_recent`) as a universal click candidate; this makes the chain *robust* (timeout + breaker above) and adds the **search-side** fallback: `lib/parcelQuery.js` `lookupParcels` tries the county's own CAD and, on a typed outage, retries the TxGIO layer **scoped to that one county**.
- **County-scoped statewide search.** `lib/counties.js` `statewideFallbackFor(county)` returns the TxGIO layer + `county='<NAME>'` scope (HARRIS / FORT BEND; Chambers already rides TxGIO so it has no separate backup). The shared, injection-safe `buildParcelWhere` (`parcelQuery.js`, **10 tests**, ports the B47 identifier guard) ANDs the scope **only when the layer actually has a `county` field** (self-healing for a pasted single-county URL) so an ID/address search can never match a like-named parcel in another county. Click-to-select is a point query and needs no scope.
- **Honest source labeling.** When a hit comes from the statewide layer while a real CAD existed for that spot, MapFinder now shows an amber **"Statewide backup source вАФ <County> county's own parcel server is unavailable; вА¶ may lag county updates"** notice (a click banner + a badge in the address-search info card). The county name is read from the parcel's own `county` attribute (`findAttr(attrs, /^county$/i)`), title-cased.
- **Field mapping / normalization.** `lib/appraisal.js` `APPR_FIELDS` extended to cover TxGIO's column names (`legal_area`/`gis_area` вЖТ Acreage, `mkt_value` вЖТ Total value, `stat_land_use` вЖТ Land use, `year_built` вЖТ Year built) so a backup parcel surfaces the **same curated rows** as one from its home county (`test/appraisal.test.js`, **6 tests**). FBCAD's *native* field names can't be captured/mapped yet вАФ its server is down вАФ so that mapping is the one explicitly-deferred sliver (the generic detectors already read TxGIO's `prop_id`/`situs_addr`/`owner_name` fine).
- **Verified вАФ lint 0 ¬Ј 532 tests ¬Ј build green; lazy-chunk split intact.** **Live headless run (`gis-verify/fbcad-outage-fallback-verify.mjs`):** with `gis.fbcad.org` intercepted as 503 (the real outage), a Sugar Land / Fort Bend click **selected the real TxGIO lot (prop_id 40594, county "FORT BEND") in 1.2 s** вАФ HCAD answered empty, FBCAD's 503 never froze the click вАФ and the **"Statewide backup source" notice rendered** (`gis-verify/fbcad-outage-fallback-verified.png`). Logged **VERIFICATION V61**; no owner action.
> **Dedup vs B137:** B137 made TxGIO a *queryable candidate* so a Fort Bend lot *can* be answered (coverage). B244 is the **resilience layer on top** вАФ the timeout that stops the hang, the breaker that stops re-hammering, the honest backup labeling, the search-side county-scoped fallback, and the TxGIO field normalization. Also distinct from **B233** (which added the "source unavailable вЙ† no-parcel-here" split вАФ B244 *feeds* that split with typed failures, see B245) and **B36e** (AbortControllers on *evidence* fetches, a different, busy-gated path). **Note (honest):** the search-side fallback lives in the canonical `runLookup` seam, which the in-planner lookup panel doesn't currently mount (the live search is the map address box, a point query that's inherently single-parcel) вАФ the mechanism is built + unit-tested at the seam so it's correct if/when that panel returns.

### B245 вАФ Validate the ArcGIS response BODY, not just the HTTP status `[Site Planner / parcels]` (bug) вАФ prereq for B244  *(arrived as "NEW-2" 2026-06-20; minted **B245** вАФ next free ID after B244)*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-20 (branch `claude/focused-darwin-8gkesb`).** ArcGIS routinely returns **HTTP 200 with a JSON `{error:вА¶}` body** (e.g. 499 Token Required) for a failed query; the old `fetchJson` did already throw on `j.error`, but it threw a *generic* `Error`, so a caller couldn't tell a **server failure** from a healthy **"no parcel at this point."** Now `lib/arcgis.js` throws a typed **`ParcelFetchError { kind, status, unavailable:true }`** classifying every failure вАФ `timeout` (aborted), `http` (non-OK status), `arcgis` (200 + error body), `network` (fetch/CORS throw) вАФ while a **healthy empty feature list still returns `null`, never an error** (no-parcel-here is a valid answer, not a failure). `identifyParcelDetailed` already separated `responded` vs `errors` for the B233 "unavailable vs none" card; it now also returns **per-source outcomes** (`sources:[{county, ok, hit, error}]`) so the B244 circuit breaker can mark exactly which source failed. `humanizeError` gives each `kind` its own plain wording. This is the prereq that makes B244's fallback trigger reliably (a 200-with-error-body now *counts* as a failure, not a masked success). **Tests:** `test/arcgis.test.js` extended (+7: emptyвЖТnull, 200+errorвЖТ`arcgis`/499, 503вЖТ`http`, networkвЖТ`network`, the timeout-abort path via fake timers, per-source split, humanized wording). lint 0 ¬Ј 532 tests ¬Ј build green.
> **Dedup:** extends **B233** (typed "couldn't reach any service" vs "no parcel here") from the address-search card down into the fetch layer, and reuses the same body-parse principle the layer **`probeService`** (`lib/layers.js`) already applies (HTTP 200 + `.error` = failed) вАФ now applied to the parcel **query** path and surfaced as a typed error. Folded into the B244 ship (one branch); kept as its own item because it's the reusable classification primitive every parcel surface now leans on.

### B243 вАФ Replace browser print with a Planyr-composed PDF download (no print dialog, white background, exact page size) `[Site Planner]` (bug)  *(arrived as "NEW-1"; minted B228, renumbered **B243** вАФ concurrent `main` took B228вАУB242 (dock-zone stack, DWG service, map-finder search, brand icons, вА¶) while this was in flight, so B243 is the real next free ID after B242)*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-20 (branch `claude/eloquent-mendel-jioa4q`).** Owner reported (3 screenshots) that **Print** opened a blank `about:blank` window and the output carried a browser date/time header (top-left), an `about:blank` URL (bottom-left), a `1/1` page number (bottom-right), a cream page background, and Letter-sized content floating in a corner of a Tabloid sheet. **Inspected first (as asked):** the path ALREADY did the hard part вАФ `printPDF` composed the WHOLE sheet (title block + plan + B197 buildings table + metrics) as ONE SVG at the exact declared page size (B200) вАФ and the ONLY defect was the final DELIVERY: `window.open("","_blank")` + `win.print()` handed that sheet to the **browser's** print dialog, which injects the header / `about:blank` / page number (none strippable by CSS or code), and the cream was `PAL.paper` (`#f4f1ea`, the on-screen page colour) bleeding into the sheet fill **and** the plan-clone background rect.
- **Fix = keep the composition, replace the delivery with a real PDF we build ourselves.** New pure, dependency-free writer `src/workspaces/site-planner/lib/imagePdf.js` (`jpegToPdf`): assembles a one-page PDF (catalog вЖТ pages вЖТ page вЖТ image XObject вЖТ content stream вЖТ Info) at an **exact physical size** (`MediaBox = inches √Ч 72 pt`), embeds the page raster with `/DCTDecode` (the JPEG bytes verbatim, no re-encode), with a **byte-accurate xref** and binary-safe assembly (builds a `Uint8Array`; the JPEG never passes through a UTF-16 JS string). No jsPDF/pdf-lib вАФ zero bundle weight, matching the `printSheet.js` pure-lib pattern; unit-tested in `test/imagePdf.test.js` (10 tests: xref offsets land on each object, MediaBox in points, DCTDecode dims, paren/backslash title escaping, bad-input guards).
- **`printPDF` вЖТ `exportPDF`** in `SitePlanner.jsx`: the old `window.open`/`win.print()` machinery is **gone**. It now forces **white** paper (new `paper` arg to `buildExportSvg` for the plan-clone bg + `pal:{вА¶PAL,paper:'#ffffff'}` for the sheet вАФ the two cream sources), inlines the aerial with `dropOnFail=true` so a CORS-blocked image can't taint the canvas (the vector plan still exports), rasterizes the composed sheet at **300 DPI** (`PDF_DPI`, capped by `PDF_MAX_PX = 22M` px вАФ Tabloid@300 вЙИ 16.8M, under the cap), fills the canvas white first (JPEG has no alpha), JPEG-encodes at q0.92, wraps with `jpegToPdf`, and **downloads** `"<date> <project> - <plan>.pdf"` (B201 naming). Generating the PDF ourselves is the mechanism that removes the injected chrome; the declared page size kills the Letter-on-Tabloid float. Raster (vs a vector SVGвЖТPDF converter) is deliberate: the plan uses `feDropShadow` filters, which the browser renders faithfully into the raster but most SVGвЖТPDF converters drop вАФ full WYSIWYG fidelity over crisp-vector-text, and 300 DPI keeps text crisp for print anyway.
- **UI:** File вЦЊ item вЖТ **"Download PDF / pick frameвА¶"**; the print-frame toolbar action вЖТ **"Download PDF"** (+ tooltip); a **"Preparing PDFвА¶"** pill (new `exportingPDF` state + a `spin` keyframe in `index.css`) replaces the old blank "Preparing printвА¶" window. The two `exportPNG` alerts that said "use Print to PDF" now say "Download PDF". Paper/orientation (Letter/Tabloid √Ч landscape/portrait) and the **B131** overlay toggle are unchanged.
> **Self-verified headless** (**V60**, logged-out, against the built `dist/`): **(1)** real app вАФ `ui-audit/verify-pdf-download.mjs` drove File вЦЊ вЖТ Download PDF / pick frameвА¶ вЖТ Download PDF and captured the ACTUAL file: `2026.06.20 Mesa Logistics - Plan 1.pdf`, a valid `%PDF`, **numPages 1**, page **exactly 792√Ч612 pt**, **ZERO pop-up windows**, **0** errors. **(2)** pipeline вАФ `ui-audit/verify-pdf-export.mjs` ran the exact rasterвЖТJPEGвЖТ`jpegToPdf` path for Letter (792√Ч612) and Tabloid (1224√Ч792), each a valid 1-page PDF that paints an image; all four paper corners white, **no cream field** (вЙ§1 stray warm pixel = JPEG chroma-edge artifact), the **building drop-shadow + aerial `<image>` survive** the raster, table/metrics crisp at 300 DPI (`live-download-page.jpg`, `pdf-export-letter.jpg`). lint **0** ¬Ј **496 tests** ¬Ј build green (re-verified after merging the latest `main`); existing `verify-print-live.mjs` still passes with the renamed menu item; `SitePlannerApp` lazy chunk intact.
> **Dedup:** NO existing open item covered this. **B131** (overlay-in-print toggle вАФ done) is PRESERVED (the `printOverlay` checkbox still gates the placed overlay in the export). **B50** (export/print robustness) is partly SUPERSEDED for the print path: its "don't strand a blank PreparingвА¶ window on a serialization throw" guard is moot now that there's no window; PNG export keeps its own try/catch + alerts, untouched. **B159/B160** are the *Scheduler* Gantt PDF/Print export (a different module/app), not this Site Planner path. The single-SVG sheet composition (**B200**) + buildings table (**B197**) + filename (**B201**) are reused unchanged вАФ only the final delivery step changed.

### B239 вАФ Schedule module still dead-ends after a deploy: harden stale-chunk recovery (cache-busting reload + chunk-aware ErrorBoundary) `[App Shell / Deploy]` (bug) вАФ follow-up to B221  *(owner-reported 2026-06-20, chat: "my scheduling module not workingвА¶ this is obviously a huge deal"; minted B228, renumbered **B239** вАФ concurrent `main` took B228вАУB238 (dock-zone stack, Bluebeam vertex editing, map-finder batch, two-backend doc note) while this was in flight, so this is the real next free ID after B238)*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-20 (branch `claude/optimistic-brahmagupta-ubw407`).** The owner still hit the Sequence/Schedule module on the workspace error screen with `Failed to fetch dynamically imported module: вА¶/Scheduler-<hash>.js` **even though B221 had shipped** the stale-chunk auto-reload. **Confirmed the module itself is NOT broken** (headless `ui-audit/diagnose-scheduler.mjs` scenario A: the embedded Gantt renders **44 task rows** the moment its chunk loads вАФ the earlier "blank iframe" reading was just measured before the in-browser Babel transpile of the ~692 KB `/sequence/` doc finished). The residual failure was two gaps in B221's *recovery path*, both fixed here:
- **The recovery reload wasn't guaranteed-fresh.** B221's auto-reload (and the boundary's manual reload) used a plain `location.reload()`, which the browser can satisfy from its OWN cached copy of the stale `index.html` вАФ so the reload lands right back on the previous build's deleted chunk вЖТ second `vite:preloadError` вЖТ cooldown вЖТ dead-end. The no-cache `public/_headers` can't retro-fix an `index.html` a long-lived/returning tab already hard-cached. **Fix:** new `reloadFresh()` in `src/app/chunkReload.js` navigates to the same path with a throwaway `?_r=<ts>` query вАФ a **distinct cache key** the browser MUST fetch from the server вАФ via `location.replace` (no back-button trap), so it always pulls a fresh `index.html` and the current chunk names; `stripReloadParam()` tidies the param off the address bar on the recovered load (called at guard install). The `vite:preloadError` guard now calls `reloadFresh` (loop-guard/cooldown unchanged).
- **The ErrorBoundary's PRIMARY button was a no-op for this error.** "Try again" just `reset()`s вЖТ re-renders the same lazy import вЖТ re-requests the same dead chunk вЖТ fails identically (the dead-end the owner kept hitting). **Fix:** `ErrorBoundary.jsx` is now chunk-aware via a shared `isChunkLoadError()` (matches the dynamic-import failure phrasings across Chrome/Firefox/Safari + the SPA-fallback "expected JS, got text/html" MIME error). For a chunk error it reframes the screen as **"A new version of Planyr is ready"** with a single PRIMARY **"Reload to update"** (cache-busting) button вАФ your work is saved. Genuine render crashes keep the Try again / Reload page pair (both reloads now cache-busting too).
- **`public/_headers` unchanged** вАФ already correct from B221 (no-cache HTML, immutable hashed `/assets/*`); it's the *forward* guarantee, while `reloadFresh` is the *escape hatch* for tabs that cached the old HTML before it took effect.
- **Verified:** lint **0 errors** ¬Ј **443 tests** (`test/chunkReload.test.js` 4вЖТ11: `isChunkLoadError` cross-browser matrix, `reloadFresh` cache-key/replace, `stripReloadParam`) ¬Ј build green; `dist/_headers` still lands at the deploy root and all three lazy chunks emit hashed under `/assets/`. **Self-verified headless** (`ui-audit/diagnose-scheduler.mjs` + `ui-audit/verify-chunk-reload.mjs`, **all green** on the built bundle via `vite preview`): **(A)** a normal Schedule click mounts the iframe and renders 44 task rows; **(B)** a chunk that 404s once then recovers вЖТ the guard cache-busting-reloads and lands in the module; **(C)** a permanently-missing chunk surfaces the **"A new version of Planyr is ready"** screen (no reload loop), and clicking **"Reload to update"** performs a real cache-busting reload вАФ captured nav trail `"/" вЖТ "/?_r=<ts>" вЖТ "/"` (the param added, then stripped). `verify-chunk-reload.mjs` still **3/3** (reload-once, cooldown holds, re-arms).
> **Owner note:** nothing to configure вАФ the fix ships with the next deploy. Because `reloadFresh` cache-busts, even a browser still holding the *old* `index.html` escapes on the first recovery instead of dead-ending. Logged **VERIFICATION V58**.
> **Dedup:** a hardening of **B221** (same stale-chunk-after-deploy family вАФ NOT a new bug class, and explicitly NOT a Scheduler/iframe logic bug, which was ruled out by the 44-row render). Distinct from the render-crash path the ErrorBoundary already handled (B205-era). No change to the lazy-chunk split or the iframe app.

### B238 вАФ Scaffold the DWGвЖТDXF conversion service in /server (LibreDWG primary, APS fallback dormant) `[server]` (feature)  *(arrived as "NEW-2"; provisionally B228, renumbered **B238** вАФ concurrent `main` took B227вАУB236 while this was in flight, so this is the real next free ID after B237)*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-20 (branch `claude/kind-johnson-oqzqco`).** Stood up the conversion **compute** service as a new `server/convert/` workspace alongside the existing /server storage/oauth scaffold вАФ a tiny, dependency-free Node HTTP service that turns a **DWG** into a **DXF**, targeting **Google Cloud Run** (scale-to-zero). Endpoints: `POST /convert` (body = DWG bytes вЖТ DXF bytes, `X-Convert-Engine` header) and `GET /health`. Engine policy (`convertService.js`): **LibreDWG primary** (`libredwg.js` вАФ spawns `dwg2dxf`, treats LibreDWG's error *bitmask* correctly: a non-empty DXF + non-critical code is success-with-warning, a critical code or no output is failure) вЖТ **Autodesk APS Model Derivative fallback** (`aps.js`) only when **`APS_ENABLED`** is on. **APS is DORMANT by default** (account not provisioned): real 2-legged auth is implemented + the full Model-Derivative pipeline is documented inline as a provisioning fill-in, but every dormant/unconfigured path returns a clear `{ok:false}` вАФ never a throw, never a false success. **When LibreDWG fails and APS is off, the HTTP layer returns an explicit error (422), never a 200 with a junk body** вАФ the same no-silent-failure contract as the storage adapter (it **reuses `server/storage/result.js`**, no parallel result type). Status map: 200 (DXF) ¬Ј 400 (no/empty body) ¬Ј 413 (over `MAX_UPLOAD_BYTES`) ¬Ј 422 (unreadable drawing) ¬Ј 503 (engine binary missing). All config via **server-side env only** (`config.js`: `PORT`, `LIBREDWG_BIN`, `CONVERT_TIMEOUT_MS`, `MAX_UPLOAD_BYTES`, `APS_ENABLED`, `APS_CLIENT_ID/SECRET`) вАФ never a `VITE_` var, never committed. **Dockerfile** is a production-correct multi-stage build: stage 1 compiles **LibreDWG 0.13.4 from source** (it isn't in the Debian/Ubuntu repos), static-linked so stage 2 (`node:22-bookworm-slim`, non-root `node` user) carries just the ~MB `dwg2dxf` binary; no npm install (Node built-ins only).
> **Verified this session вАФ built the image and ran the container for real.** `GET /health` вЖТ 200 `{ok,service:"dwg-convert",engine:"libredwg",apsFallback:false}`. `POST /convert` with two **real** sample drawings: **example_2000.dwg** (582 KB) вЖТ **200**, a valid `AutoCAD Drawing Exchange Format, version 2000` DXF (1.27 MB), `X-Convert-Engine: libredwg`; **example_2013.dwg** вЖТ **200**, valid DXF. **Failure path (the important one):** garbage (non-DWG) bytes with APS off вЖТ **422** `{"ok":false,"error":"DWGвЖТDXF conversion failed in LibreDWG and the APS fallback is disabled (APS_ENABLED is off): вА¶"}` вАФ explicit, never a silent success; empty body вЖТ **400**; `GET /convert` вЖТ **405**. **+26 unit tests** (`test/dwgConvert.test.js`: config/APS-dormant parsing, LibreDWG success/warning/critical/spawn-fail/no-output, the engine-policy matrix incl. "APS never consulted when off", APS guard + auth shape, and the live HTTP server's status codes). lint **0 errors** ¬Ј **462 tests** ¬Ј `vite build` green; **isolation confirmed вАФ `grep` of `dist/` finds zero conversion-service code** (the public bundle never imports `/server`).
> **Follow-on (NOT this item):** actual `gcloud run deploy` waits on the GCP project being provisioned in the Google Cloud Console; the service + Dockerfile are proven locally now. The Dockerfile's `CURL_INSECURE` build-arg exists ONLY to build behind this repo's sandbox TLS-inspecting proxy (CLAUDE.md); production/Cloud Build omits it вЖТ full TLS verification.
> **Dedup / inspect-first:** checked before writing вАФ `/server` already held the B206вАУB209 Drive storage adapter + the B207 Google OAuth helper, so this is **additive** (`server/convert/` only); no existing /server code changed. The browser/Supabase side calls this over the network in the backend tranche (distinct from the Supabase user-data backend).

### B237 вАФ Record the two-backend architecture in CLAUDE.md `[infra]` (task)  *(arrived as "NEW-1"; provisionally B227, renumbered **B237** вАФ concurrent `main` took B227вАУB236 while this was in flight, so this is the real next free ID after B236)*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-20 (branch `claude/kind-johnson-oqzqco`).** Reconciled the existing **"Two backends вАФ don't conflate"** section of `CLAUDE.md` **in place** (no duplicate section) so the data layer and the compute layer can never be confused: **(1) Supabase вАФ the data/auth/storage layer (BUILT):** cloud Postgres, email/password auth, RLS, cloud save/load; the frontend talks to it **directly with the anon key**, which is safe in the browser **because RLS protects it** (a request only ever sees the signed-in user's own rows); the permanent home for user data. **(2) `/server` on Google Cloud Run вАФ the compute layer (built in-repo, not yet deployed):** scale-to-zero containers running **DWGвЖТDXF conversion** (LibreDWG primary вЖТ APS Model Derivative fallback, dormant behind `APS_ENABLED`) and **Google Drive auto-filing + bytes I/O** (the file-facts index itself lives in Supabase Postgres; the one-time OAuth *consent* callback is a thin same-origin Cloudflare Pages Function, the heavy compute is Cloud Run). Documented that **all third-party secrets (APS key, Google credentials, Supabase service-role key) stay server-side only, walled off from the public Cloudflare Pages deploy**; the only Supabase key that reaches the frontend is the RLS-protected **anon** key. The two layers talk **over the network** вАФ Supabase the permanent data home, `/server` additive compute added in the backend tranche.
> **Also fixed a stale contradiction** surfaced while reconciling: the Workflow section still said *"Deploy = GitHub Pages (production)"* and *"Cloudflare Pages is optional and deferred"* вАФ both false since the Pages-pipeline retirement (already recorded as DONE near the end of CLAUDE.md). Updated to **Cloudflare Pages = production (planyr.io)**, with per-branch previews noted as the separate optional Cloudflare concern, so the doc no longer contradicts itself about where the public deploy (the thing `/server` is walled off from) actually lives.
> **Dedup:** the section already existed вАФ this **enriched it in place** (Cloud Run / scale-to-zero / LibreDWGвЖТAPS detail + the Cloudflare-Pages walling), it did not add a second copy. Doc-only change: lint 0 ¬Ј 462 tests ¬Ј build green (unaffected).

### B236 вАФ Per-layer GIS data-age / source-vintage stamp `[Site Planner / GIS]` (feature)  *(arrived as "NEW-5"; minted **B236** вАФ concurrent `main` took B225вАУB231 while this was in flight, so B232вАУB236 are the real next free IDs)*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-20 (branch `claude/tender-goldberg-ax4n5w`).** Each GIS layer now shows a low-visual-weight **"as of: &lt;source vintage&gt;"** line in `components/LayerPanel.jsx` (rendered when the layer is on), kept **deliberately distinct** from the existing **"refreshed Xm ago"** cache-age stamp by the layer name вАФ the two are never conflated. The vintage is the source's **own** effective/publication date or maintenance cadence, from a curated, central `LAYER_VINTAGE` map + `layerVintage(id, cfg)` in `lib/layers.js` (a per-config `vintage` override wins; else the map; else `null`). **Honest by rule:** per-panel / per-area datasets say what actually varies ("Effective date varies by FIRM panel", "Survey date varies by NWI project area", "LiDAR collection varies by county (USGS 3DEP)"); continuously-maintained registries say "continuously updated / current edition"; **any layer with no entry renders "vintage unknown" (italic) вАФ never a fabricated date** (same family as "source unavailable вЙ† not present"). **Scope:** source-vintage only; the "last refreshed" half rides the planned GIS-cache SWR work and is NOT built here.
> **Dedup:** the **standalone, ship-now** version of the data-age surfacing already specced inside **B96** (GIS layer cache, stale-while-revalidate) вАФ when caching lands, fold the vintage stamp + the refreshed-age stamp into one surface rather than duplicating. **Self-verified headless** (**V57**, `ui-audit/verify-b232-b236.mjs`): toggling FEMA on shows "as of: Effective date varies by FIRM panel". lint 0 ¬Ј 448 tests ¬Ј build green; lazy chunk split intact.

### B235 вАФ Rework "Your Sites" left rail: chips as filters, type-to-filter, collapsible status groups `[Site Planner / UI]` (feature)  *(arrived as "NEW-4"; minted **B235** вАФ next free ID after B234; depends on B234)*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-20 (branch `claude/tender-goldberg-ax4n5w`).** The status chips are now **positive multi-select filters** (`statusFilter` set): tap one to show only that state, multi-select; none selected = show everything. The filter drives **both** the list **and** the map pins, so "show only Active" focuses both at once (replaces the old hide-on-map `hidden` set). Added a **type-to-filter** text box (`nameFilter`, case-insensitive substring on the site/plan name) at the top of the list. The list is grouped under **collapsible status section headers** (`groupCollapsed`, persisted to `planarfit:sitesGroups:v1`): **Active / Pursuit / On Hold expanded, Complete / Dead collapsed by default** вАФ settled projects become expand-on-demand instead of rows you scroll past. An active name filter **force-expands** matching sections so a match in a collapsed (settled) group is never hidden. Section headers + chips render from the **B234 tokens**; the panel header count shows `shown/total` when a filter is active. One shared `siteRow()` renderer feeds every section.

### B232 вАФ Address search doesn't recenter the map on "Go" `[Site Planner / map]` (bug)  *(arrived as "NEW-1"; minted **B232** вАФ concurrent `main` (PRs #188/#189/#190/#191) took B225вАУB231 (building feature-buttons / Yield donut / dock-zone stack / Bluebeam vertex editing) while this was in flight, so B232вАУB236 are the real next free IDs)*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-20 (branch `claude/tender-goldberg-ax4n5w`).** Confirmed the impl note first: the geocode handler (`goAddress` in MapFinder.jsx) **already** flew the camera, so the bug was the **geocoder itself**, not unwired plumbing. The old code called OSM Nominatim with only `countrycodes=us` and **no viewport bias**, which routinely returns nothing for a bare house-number street address ("19630 Crossbranch") вАФ so the map silently stayed put. Replaced with `geocodeAddress(q, center)`: tries the **Esri World Geocoding Service** `findAddressCandidates` first (keyless single lookup, the same ArcGIS family the app already uses for imagery/parcels, far better at exact US street addresses) **biased to the current map center** via `&location=`; falls back to **Nominatim biased to a ~0.6¬∞ viewbox** around the center. On a hit, `flyTo([lat,lon], 18)` вАФ parcel-level zoom. Failure stays honest (the "couldn't find that address" toast).
> **Dedup / scope:** a separate failure path from B233 вАФ this is the **geocodeвЖТcamera** half; B233 is the parcel identify/select/info half. **Self-verified headless** (**V57**): "19630 Crossbranch Dr, Katy, TX" вЖТ Go recenters the map on the parcel (not a no-op).

### B230 вАФ Replace always-visible "+" midpoint handles with Shift-click / right-click vertex insertion (Bluebeam-style) `[Site Planner]` (feature)  *(arrived as "NEW-1"; provisionally B221, renumbered **B230** вАФ concurrent `main` (PRs #184/#186/#188/#189/#191) took B221вАУB229 (lazy-chunk recovery, Schedule fixes, building-button gating, Yield-panel redesign, dock-zone stack) while this was in flight, so this is the real next free ID after B229; the implementing commit + the PR still say "B221")*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-20 (branch `claude/funny-franklin-hrk815`).** The permanent "+" midpoint handle that every editable edge used to carry is **gone in every state** (selected, moving, all of them); editing now follows the Bluebeam model. Built **once in a shared vertex-editing layer** so all editable geometry inherits it вАФ **detention ponds, parcels, polygon elements, measurement polygons/lines, markup poly/line, and easement paths** вАФ not per element type.
- **Shared core (new):** `editablePath()` resolves the current selection to a uniform `{ layer, id, pts, closed, min }`; `hitEditPath()` returns the nearest vertex / nearest edge within a **screen-pixel** tolerance (9px vert / 11px edge вЖТ zoom-independent grab radius); `insertVtx()` and `deleteVtx()` are single dispatchers keyed by `layer` (parcel/el/measure/markup/ease), each using functional `setState` so they always act on current state. Wired through **three capture-phase handlers** on the canvas `<svg>` (`onPointerDownCapture` / `onContextMenuCapture` / `onPointerMoveCapture`) so the same interaction reaches every layer **before** its own handlers, **without overlaying any new hit target** вАФ a normal click/drag/select is untouched.
- **Add a vertex:** **Shift+click an edge** (away from a corner) drops a control point exactly at the click point on that segment; **right-click an edge** вЖТ portal "Add control point". **Delete a vertex:** **right-click a vertex** вЖТ portal "Delete control point"; **Delete/Backspace** removes the active control point. Deletion is blocked below the geometry minimum (**3 for a polygon**), and the menu item reads "(min reached)" + disables there.
- **Discoverability:** a faint **candidate-insertion dot** snaps to the nearest point on the edge under the cursor on **edge-hover during edit**, and brightens while **Shift** arms the insert вАФ replacing exactly what the permanent "+" advertised, without the clutter. The **active control point** (the Delete target) renders inverted.
- **Kept:** the square corner handles (the real vertices) вАФ shown only when selected, drag behavior unchanged. The five `add*Vertex` "+" handlers and the per-handle Shift-click-delete branches were removed (superseded). **Tie-break rule:** a **corner always wins over its adjacent edges** (`hitEditPath` returns both at a corner; a vertex right-click deletes, never adds), mirroring the insert rule `edge && !vertex` вАФ this was the one real bug found in headless testing and fixed before merge.
- **Portal menu:** the Add/Delete-control-point menu is `createPortal`-mounted at `document.body` (z 6000/6001) so it can never be clipped or trapped behind the canvas / tool-rail stacking contexts; it reuses the app's existing `menu`/`menuPanel`/`menuItem` styling.
> **Self-verified headless** (`ui-audit/verify-b221-b222.mjs`, logged-out, live Harris aerial, a polygon detention pond in a parcel): after selecting the pond вАФ **0** "+" midpoint handles, **4** square vertex handles; **Shift+click an edge вЖТ 4вЖТ5** vertices with the candidate dot shown while Shift held; **edge-hover (no shift) shows the dot**; **right-click a vertex вЖТ portal "Delete control point" вЖТ 5вЖТ4**; **Delete key вЖТ 4вЖТ3**; repeated deletes **stop at 3** (polygon min guard). **0 console errors.** Screenshots `ui-audit/screens/b221-pond-selected.png` + `b221-after-edits.png` eyeballed (squares only, no plus marks). Logged **VERIFICATION V56**. lint **0 errors** ¬Ј **436 tests** ¬Ј build green; `SitePlannerApp` lazy chunk intact.
> **Dedup:** AMENDS the now-done Bluebeam-editing items **B141** (editable vertices on the measurement tools) + **B147** (markup/shape vertex-edit for lines/polylines/polygons), which had introduced the "+" midpoint handle, and addresses the clutter **B215** flagged (the "+" stacking at the edge midpoint). Distinct from the open **B155/B156** (whole-shape interior hit-testing + hover highlight) вАФ those select/hover a shape; this inserts/deletes control points on the already-selected shape.

### B231 вАФ Restyle the detention pond to a modern "Cartographic" water-body treatment `[Site Planner]` (feature)  *(arrived as "NEW-2"; provisionally B222, renumbered **B231** вАФ next free ID after B230; concurrent `main` took B221вАУB229; the implementing commit + the PR still say "B222")*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-20 (branch `claude/funny-franklin-hrk815`).** The detention pond no longer reads as dated clip-art. The decorative wavy-line water hatch, the saturated outline (which read as the Markup-accent orange вАФ the wrong signal for water), and the monospace label are all replaced with a modern cartographic water-body style (how Mapbox / ArcGIS Pro render water). Implemented as a **named, reusable style token** so future water/basin features inherit it; **scoped to the pond element type** (never auto-applied to other polygons).
- **Token (`lib/planStyle.js`):** the pond `TYPE` is now `{ fill:"#5B97A5", stroke:"#2C5D6B", weight:2, cartoWater:true }` (replaced the old `water:true` wavy-hatch flag); `elStyle` exposes `cartoWater`. One token, reusable.
- **Fill (`renderElPx`):** a **radial steel-teal gradient** `#grad-water` (added to `<defs>`) that **deepens toward the center** вАФ `#2F6675` at the middle вЖТ `#5B97A5` at the edge вАФ at ~80% opacity, so a pond reads as water *with volume*, not a flat cutout. The old `pat-water` wavy pattern is deleted. Applies to both the polygon and rectangular pond branches.
- **Outline:** `#2C5D6B`, **2px at a constant screen-pixel width** (the canvas is drawn in pixel space, so the stroke never hairlines when zoomed out nor fattens when zoomed in); **3px when selected**. **No orange anywhere on the water body** вАФ selection is signaled by the thicker teal stroke + the (transient, orange) editing handles, not a colour change on the feature itself.
- **Label:** switched monospace вЖТ **Inter** (the app's proportional UI sans), **dark slate `#0E2E36` with a white casing/halo** (always, so it stays legible over busy aerial), two lines kept вАФ name above ("Detention Pond" / "Existing Detention Pond"), area sub-line below ("0.47 ac ¬Ј 20,272 sf") вАФ centered on the centroid (or the existing baseline anchor in expansion mode). Threaded through the shared LOD/label renderer via a per-candidate `carto` flag, so **only the pond label changes**; every other element label stays mono.
- **Map overview:** `MapFinder.jsx` resolves element fills through the same `elStyle`, so the map's pond pins inherit the flat steel-teal fill + teal outline automatically (no wavy, no orange) вАФ no second code path; the expansion baseline ghost stroke was recoloured to match.
> **Self-verified headless** (`ui-audit/verify-b221-b222.mjs`): `#grad-water` exists with stops **`#2F6675` вЖТ `#5B97A5`**; **no `#pat-water`**; the pond fill uses `url(#grad-water)`; the **`#2C5D6B`** outline is present; the label uses **Inter** + fill **`#0E2E36`** reading "Detention Pond / 2.14 ac ¬Ј 93,100 sf". Screenshot `ui-audit/screens/b221-pond-selected.png` eyeballed вАФ steel-teal body with a deeper center, crisp teal edge, haloed sans label, no hatch, no orange. **0 console errors.** lint 0 ¬Ј 414 tests ¬Ј build green.
> **Dedup:** AMENDS the pond rendering from **B132/B139** (expansion baseline + ghost) and **B140/B157** (on-map pond area labels вАФ the two-line name+area is preserved). Distinct from **B219** (cartographic restyle of the map *furniture* вАФ north arrow + scale bar); this is the *water body* itself.

### B228 вАФ Building-anchored dock-zone stack with LIFO +/вИТ `[Site Planner]` (feature)  *(arrived as "NEW-1"; provisionally B221, renumbered **B228** вАФ concurrent `main` took B221вАУB227 (PRs #186 lazy-chunk reload, #188 B225/B226 feature-button visibility, #189 B227 yield panel, #184 B222вАУB224 Schedule) while this was in flight, so this is the real next free ID after B227)*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-20 (branch `claude/practical-faraday-9mmfch`).** The building footprint is now the control hub for the dock-side site elements: a single **"+"** adds the next zone **outward** from the dock face, a single **"вИТ"** peels the **outermost** one off (LIFO). Fixed outward order **truck court вЖТ trailer parking вЖТ buffer**; "+" walks out (court вЖТ trailer вЖТ buffer), "вИТ" walks in (buffer вЖТ trailer вЖТ court).
- **Reused, not duplicated:** the court stays the existing `truckCourt` paving strip and trailer parking the existing far-side `forCourt` striped row вАФ the change unifies their geometry under one pure layout and adds the buffer. **Buffer is the new zone** вАФ a sage `landscape` clear strip (buffer/setback) bonded to its trailer via a new `forTrailer` tag, labelled "<d>вА≤ Buffer".
- **One geometry source:** `src/workspaces/site-planner/lib/dockZones.js` (`DOCK_ZONES`, `zoneDepthDefaults`, `layoutZone`) positions all three zones flush-outward from the building face, full wall length, trailer rotated so its stalls run along the wall. Used by add / remove / inline depth-edit / **building-resize** (the rewritten `refitChildren` re-lays the stack), so depths survive a resize and outer zones always stay flush. **12 unit tests** (`test/dockZones.test.js`): order, configurable defaults, flush-outward stacking (gap-free, no overlap), vertical-side rotation, building rotation.
- **Editable depths inline** (US survey feet, EPSG:2278), defaults **135 / 50 / 15** and **user-configurable** in **Setup вЖТ Dock zones** (`settings.truckCourtD/trailerParkD/bufferD`) вАФ not hardcoded.
- **Creation rerouted through the building "+":** trailer parking + buffer now add from the building panel (and the on-canvas court "+" вЖТ trailer "+" вЖТ buffer "+" chain). **Car parking** is **also** added from the building panel but occupies the **ends (non-dock short sides)** and is tracked as its **own element outside** the LIFO stack, with its own remove. **[assumption flagged for Michael: should car parking instead join the LIFO removal order? вАФ shipped as a separate control.]**
- **Both long sides:** zones **mirror to every dock face with doors** (cross-dock = both); the "+"/"вИТ" operate on the whole dock-zone set as a **unit** (one "+" advances every dock side; "вИТ" peels the outermost off every dock side). **[assumption flagged for Michael вАФ shipped this way.]**
- **Bump-outs are NOT in this stack** вАФ a footprint modifier, behaviour unchanged; only relocated in the panel (B229).
- **Self-verified headless** (`ui-audit/verify-dock-zones.mjs`, logged-out, cross-dock building): "+"√Ч3 вЖТ 2 courts / 2 trailers / 2 buffers, outward order courtвЖТtrailerвЖТbuffer, "+" disabled at full; inline buffer depth 15вЖТ40 grew the band with outer zones staying flush; building resize 600вЖТ760 kept all zones attached, full-width and flush; "вИТ"√Ч3 peeled bufferвЖТtrailerвЖТcourt; car-parking-ends added a field; **0 page errors**. lint **0 errors** ¬Ј **448 tests** ¬Ј build green; the `SitePlannerApp` lazy chunk split still holds. Logged **VERIFICATION V55**.
> **Dedup:** NOT B71 (per-element trailer curb 6вА≥вЖТ12вА≥) or B78 (stall-layout freeze guard); orthogonal to main's B225/B226 (those size-GATE these feature buttons вАФ visibility; this is the zone stack the buttons drive). Reuses the court (`truckCourt`/`makeStrip`), far-side trailer (`forCourt`/`oppTrailerGeom`) and bump-out (`dogEar`/`placeDogEars`) machinery; the orphaned old one-shot helpers (`addTruckCourt`, `addStripSide`, `makeOppTrailer`, `TRUCK_COURT_D`) were removed.

### B227 вАФ Redesign Site Yield panel: composition donut, identity icon, grouped rows, semantic palette `[Site Planner]` (feature)  *(arrived as "NEW-1"; provisionally B225, renumbered **B227** вАФ concurrent `main` (#188) minted B225 + B226 (building feature-edit-button visibility) while this was in flight, so this is the real next free ID after B226)*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-20 (branch `claude/jolly-turing-n8rmzy`).** Presentational reskin of the Site Yield panel вАФ **no engine / data-model / RLS / persistence change** (it stays per-user/private, reading the exact values the planner already computes). New self-contained `YieldPanel` component (+ a scoped `YIELD_PAL` semantic palette) replaces the old generic `<Section title="Site yield">` in `SitePlanner.jsx`; the generic `Section` and every other panel are untouched. Layout topвЖТbottom: **(1)** a header row = a **parcel-with-footprint identity glyph** (terracotta lot outline `#C0532E` + filled footprint + a half-opacity outbuilding) in a 32 px soft `#F6E7DD` tile + the tracked "SITE YIELD" label + a collapse chevron (its own `useState`, mirroring `Section` вАФ collapse/expand preserved). **(2)** the three existing KPI cards (Site ac ¬Ј Building abbreviated "227k" ¬Ј Coverage %), card `#F2ECE1`, tabular-mono. **(3)** a new **composition donut + legend**: how the site partitions into Building / Paving / Open-green / Detention, derived from engine OUTPUTS only вАФ `buildingPct = coverage`, `pavingPct = max(0, impervious% вИТ coverage%)`, `detentionPct = detentionSf/siteSf√Ч100`, `openPct = 100 вИТ the rest (clamp вЙ•0)` вАФ so the four always sum to 100 and the ring closes. SVG (~100 px, 13 px stroke): faint `#ECE3D5` track + four `stroke-dasharray` arcs, group rotated вИТ90¬∞ to start at top, butt caps, contiguous (`dashoffset = вИТќ£ earlier arcs`); center = site acreage over "acres". Out of scope by request: the headroom/limit bars + scheme-compare view (set aside in chat).

### B226 вАФ Show feature-edit buttons only on the selected/hovered building `[Site Planner]` (feature)  *(arrived as "NEW-2"; minted **B226** вАФ next free ID after B225)*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-20 (branch `claude/lucid-heisenberg-mjhpw3`).** **Dedup finding:** the per-building feature-add buttons ALREADY rendered only on the *selected* building (gated on `sel.kind==='el' && el.id===sel.id`), never "on every building in view" вАФ so that half of the arriving ask was already true. Implemented the rest as the requested SINGLE visibility rule: the buttons render for exactly ONE building вАФ `featActiveId =` the selected one, else (in select mode) the one HOVERED вАФ and only when the **B225** footprint-size gate passes. Net rule: **buttons visible iff (footprint large enough on screen) AND (building selected OR hovered).** **Hover** (`SitePlanner.jsx`: new `hoverElId` state + a block in `onMove`) is computed **position-based** (the topmost building whose footprint bbox contains the cursor), NOT via SVG `onPointerEnter/Leave` вАФ because the buttons sit INSIDE the footprint, an enter/leave trigger would flicker the buttons off the instant the cursor moved toward one; the position test keeps the hover alive. It only runs while idle in select mode with **nothing selected** (selection otherwise drives the buttons), so there's no per-frame churn once you've clicked. Hover previews the add-buttons only вАФ resize/rotate grips stay selection-only.
> **Self-verified headless** (`ui-audit/verify-b225-b226.mjs`, logged-out): with nothing selected, the not-hovering baseline = **0** buttons, hovering the building reveals its **8** (`b226-hover.png` shows the add-buttons with NO selection grips вЖТ pure hover), and moving off hides them (**0**). So the buttons appear on the ONE active building only, gated by the same size rule. Logged **VERIFICATION V53**. lint 0 ¬Ј 414 tests ¬Ј build green; `SitePlannerApp` lazy chunk intact.
> **Dedup:** same render condition as **B225** (folded into one rule, per the arriving note "Combine with NEW-1 into one visibility rule"). Sibling of **B156** (hover-highlight the markup under the cursor) вАФ that's the markup-layer version; this is the building-handle case, position-based for the same flicker reason. Distinct from selection hit-testing (**B155**).

### B225 вАФ Hide building feature-edit buttons when the on-screen footprint is too small (anti-cluster) `[Site Planner]` (bug)  *(arrived as "NEW-1"; minted **B225** вАФ highest B# across both files was B220, so this is the real next free ID)*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-20 (branch `claude/lucid-heisenberg-mjhpw3`).** Zooming OUT on a building with feature-add buttons shrank its footprint while the fixed-pixel +/вИТ buttons (truck-dock / sidewalk / bump-out / parking-row вАФ each inset ~22px inside a wall, r=9) stayed full size, so the cluster grew larger than the footprint and spilled past the edges into an unreadable pile (the owner's screenshot). **Fix (`SitePlanner.jsx`):** each feature-add button is now gated on the building's RENDERED on-screen footprint size in PIXELS (`el.w/el.h * view.ppf`) against a tunable module const `FEAT_BTN_MIN_PX = 72` (вЙИ the ~22px inset + 9px radius clearance on each side, plus a small legibility margin вАФ opposite buttons overlap below ~68px). The gate is **per-axis**: a wall's inset +/вИТ needs its PERPENDICULAR on-screen dimension вЙ• 72px (top/bottom gated on height-px, left/right on width-px); the corner bump-outs need BOTH axes. So a long/narrow on-screen footprint keeps its long-side buttons and drops only the cramped short-end ones вАФ the overlap case the arriving note flagged ("also check") is handled inherently, no collapse-menu needed вАФ and a fully-small footprint drops ALL of them (no spill). Applied to all three feature-add node groups (`sideAddNodes`, `courtAddNodes`, `parkingAddNodes`). **Resize/rotate grips are intentionally NOT gated** (still usable on a small building вАФ the spec says "only the editable feature buttons are suppressed"); the map's **Building Pin + Progress Arc live in `MapFinder.jsx`** (a different component) and are **untouched**, so they stay visible at every zoom level, as required.
> **Self-verified headless** (`ui-audit/verify-b225-b226.mjs`, logged-out, 400вА≤√Ч300вА≤ cross-dock building): swept the wheel zoom from large to tiny; at every non-ambiguous step the drawn button count matched the rule predicted from the measured footprint px вАФ **8** while large (494√Ч370 вА¶ 127√Ч95px), **2** (long-side sidewalks only) at **81√Ч60px** (height < 72 вЙ§ width вЖТ per-axis collision handling), **0** once tiny (вЙ§ 64√Ч48px). Screens `b225-zoomed-in.png` / `b225-partial-longside.png` / `b225-zoomed-out.png`. Logged **VERIFICATION V53**. lint 0 ¬Ј 414 tests ¬Ј build green; `SitePlannerApp` lazy chunk intact.
> **Dedup:** distinct from **B149** (LOD tiering вАФ which *dimensions/labels* draw at a given zoom) and **B121** (label-overlap engine) вАФ those govern annotations; this governs the *interactive edit handles*. Combined with **B226** into ONE visibility rule (size-gate AND selected-or-hovered). Reuses the **B30** precedent of pixel-projected (not feet-based) thresholds.

### B224 вАФ "Schedule-assembling" themed loading animation, reusable engine across modules `[Scheduler]` (feature)  *(arrived as "NEW-3"; provisionally B220, renumbered **B224** вАФ concurrent `main` (#183, #185, #187) took B218вАУB221 while this was in flight, so the real next free block was B222вАУB224)*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-20 (branch `claude/awesome-pascal-zlb19p`).** A reusable, per-module themed loader replaces the bare "Loading workspaceвА¶" text. New `src/shared/ui/ModuleLoader.jsx` (one animation engine) + pure, unit-tested theming `src/shared/ui/moduleLoaderTheme.js` (skin + label) over the shared `src/shared/ui/moduleAccent.js` (`MODULE_ACCENT` extracted to a React-free module; `AppHeader` re-exports it for back-compat). **Schedule skin** = a Gantt building itself: zebra row bands fade in topвЖТbottom (the real banding tints), ghost task bars wipe in leftвЖТright staggered (~100 ms/row) in the accent **`#7F77DD`**, milestone diamonds pop at bar ends, and a soft vertical **playhead** sweeps leftвЖТright; the assemble loop fades at its boundary so it repeats seamlessly, then **cross-fades** (not a hard cut) into the real Gantt. **Site Planner skin** = a parcel outline **stroke-drawing itself** + building footprints fading in + a north-arrow, in the Site accent **`#1D9E75`** вАФ same engine, different grammar. **Accessibility:** honors `prefers-reduced-motion` (drops the cascade + sweep for a static skeleton + gentle pulse). **Threshold:** holds invisible for ~250 ms so fast loads never flash it. **Wired** as the Shell `Suspense` fallback (themed by active module вАФ covers the chunk-fetch phase) AND as a cross-fading overlay in `Scheduler.jsx` over the iframe until its first `planar:nav-state` (covers the heavy iframe boot вАФ the actually-slow phase), with a 9 s safety timeout so it can never stick.
> **Self-verified headless** (**V52**, `ui-audit/verify-loader-prefetch.mjs`): on Schedule nav the loader shows (`role="status"`, `aria-label="Assembling scheduleвА¶"`, 12 elements in `#7F77DD`, SVG present вАФ `loader-schedule.png`) then cross-fades to the iframe; with `prefers-reduced-motion` the cascade + playhead are dropped (**0 animated bars, no playhead** вАФ `loader-reduced-motion.png`). +5 tests in `test/moduleLoaderTheme.test.js` (per-module skin/accent, fallback, threshold). **Dedup:** the loader reuses `MODULE_ACCENT`, so it can never drift from the tab/brand colors. **Pairs with B223** (that shrinks the wait; this covers the residual). lint 0 ¬Ј 419 tests ¬Ј build green; lazy chunk split intact.

### B223 вАФ Speed up Schedule module load `[Scheduler]` (task)  *(arrived as "NEW-2"; provisionally B219, renumbered **B223** вАФ concurrent `main` (#183, #185, #187) took B218вАУB221)*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-20 (branch `claude/awesome-pascal-zlb19p`).** Profiled first: the Schedule tab embeds the standalone Gantt app (`public/sequence/index.html`, ~692 KB) in an iframe, so the dominant navigation cost is **doc-fetch** (downloading + parsing that HTML each visit), not the trivial `Scheduler.jsx` chunk, and not layout/paint. **Shipped the prefetch (the measured win):** new `src/app/modulePrefetch.js` вАФ `prefetchModule(id)` warms a workspace's lazy chunk (same dynamic-import specifier Vite already code-splits) **and, for Schedule, injects `<link rel="prefetch" href="/sequence/">`** so the iframe doc is cached before the click. Wired two triggers: **idle** (`prefetchOnIdle(["scheduler","doc-review"])` via `requestIdleCallback` in `Shell.jsx`, after first paint) and **hover-intent** (`ModuleTab`'s `onMouseEnter` in `AppHeader.jsx`). Lazy-loading still gates the first boot вАФ nothing prefetches until idle. **Confirmed already-satisfied (no change needed):** both `GridView` and `GanttView` already **virtualize** (row windowing by scroll, `startIdx`/`endIdx` + slice), `GanttView` already `useMemo`s its dep-line/month/year layout, and the app already paints from an inline `__PLANAR_DATA__` seed before the Supabase sync (so the cloud round-trip is off the critical first paint and the silent-failure save guard is intact).
> **Self-verified headless** (**V52**, `ui-audit/verify-loader-prefetch.mjs`): the `/sequence/` prefetch link is injected after boot-idle; no boot console errors. **Pairs with B224.** lint 0 ¬Ј 419 tests ¬Ј build green; `Scheduler` (1.79 kB) / `DocReview` / `SitePlannerApp` chunks stay separate.

### B222 вАФ Row color fill hides Gantt bars `[Scheduler]` (bug)  *(arrived as "NEW-1"; provisionally B218, renumbered **B222** вАФ concurrent `main` (#183, #185, #187) took B218вАУB221)*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-20 (branch `claude/awesome-pascal-zlb19p`).** Applying a row color fill made the task bars on that row disappear from the Gantt. **Root cause was a color collision (b):** in `GanttView` (`public/sequence/index.html`), `task.rowColor` was overloaded вАФ the same field that paints the row background (`rowBg`) was also the bar fill via `task.rowColor || <neutral>` for **leaf bars, summary brackets, AND milestone diamonds** вАФ so a fill repainted every on-row datum its own color and it vanished into its own background. **Fix:** each datum now keeps its **own identity hue independent of the row fill** вАФ leaf bars + milestone diamonds = neutral gray `#94a3b8`, summary brackets = depth-navy вАФ and carries a **hairline edge** (`#475569`, a slate darker than the fill) so it stays legible on any fill; notably the **solid/complete leaf bar gained a 1px border** (it was borderless and was the one that fully disappeared on a matching fill). The row fill is now pure background decoration. **Paint order verified + documented** (z-index): row fill (row `<div>`, z auto, bottom) вЖТ grid/today/dependency lines (z2вАУ4) вЖТ bars/milestones (z5, data layer) вЖТ bar + name labels (z6вАУ7, top). Holistic: covers bars, diamonds, links, and labels.
> **Self-verified headless** (**V51**, `ui-audit/verify-rowfill-bars.mjs`, logged-out seed): with a leaf task seeded a row fill, the fill paints the row bands (`rowBands:2`) with **zero bar-sized collisions** (`barCollisions:0`); the bar keeps `#94a3b8` + the `#475569` 1px edge (`rowfill-bars-crop.png` shows the marker clearly on the tinted row). **Dedup:** distinct from B210вАУB212 (the prior Gantt tranche вАФ brackets / status-as-fill / columns). The PDF/Print export path (`buildGanttSVG`) already paints bars neutral gray/navy and never reads `rowColor` for bars вАФ no collision there, left untouched. lint **0 errors** ¬Ј **419 tests** ¬Ј build green; lazy chunk split intact.

### B221 вАФ Lazy workspaces fail to load after a deploy: "Failed to fetch dynamically imported module" (stale content-hashed chunk) `[App Shell / Deploy]` (bug)  *(arrived as "NEW-1"; provisionally B218, renumbered **B221** вАФ concurrent `main` (PR #183) took B218 (dead header controls) + B219 (map-furniture restyle) and a parallel session took B220 (map-finder over-zoom) while this was in flight, so B221 is the real next free ID after B220. The branch's first commit + the PR were opened as "B218". Deduped against the PDF.js `import()` items (B72/B67/B180 lazy-load a heavy library on first use вАФ unrelated to the stale-chunk-after-deploy failure here).)*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-20 (branch `claude/cool-ptolemy-2lb1js`).** Root cause confirmed as the standard Vite stale-chunk-after-deploy problem (NOT a logic bug inside DocReview, and NOT a broken/partial build вАФ the build is green and all three workspace chunks emit cleanly under `/assets/`): an already-open tab is holding the *previous* deploy's `index.html`, which references content-hashed filenames like `/assets/DocReview-<oldhash>.js`; once Cloudflare serves the new build those files are gone, so switching into a not-yet-loaded workspace 404s and throws the user onto the workspace error screen. A hard reload fixes it because it re-fetches the current `index.html` (and its new hashes). Fix, applied globally so it covers **every** lazy route (Site Planner, Document Review, Sequence), not just DocReview:
- **Auto-reload-once on dynamic-import failure** вАФ `src/app/chunkReload.js` (`installChunkReloadGuard`, wired in `src/main.jsx` before render) listens for Vite's `vite:preloadError` window event and reloads the page once. **Loop guard:** the time of the last auto-reload is stamped in `sessionStorage` (`planyr:chunkReloadAt`); a second preloadError within a 10 s cooldown does **not** reload вАФ a genuinely-missing chunk (a broken/partial deploy) falls through to the existing `ErrorBoundary` instead of reload-looping. The stamp self-expires so a *later, separate* deploy re-arms a fresh one-time recovery вАФ deliberately more robust than a boolean flag cleared on mount, which would either race the reload (auto-loop if the default workspace's chunk is the missing one) or reload on every click of a truly-broken module (never letting its error show). The pure decision (`shouldReloadAfterPreloadError`) is unit-tested.
- **Cloudflare cache headers** вАФ `public/_headers` (copied verbatim to `dist/_headers` at the deploy root): `/assets/*` (the content-hashed, immutable build files) get `Cache-Control: public, max-age=31536000, immutable`; the HTML entry points (`/`, `/index.html`, `/sequence/`) get `Cache-Control: no-cache` so a new deploy's asset hashes propagate on the next load instead of being pinned behind a hard-cached HTML.
- **Verified:** lint 0 errors ¬Ј **418 tests** (incl. the new `test/chunkReload.test.js`, 4) ¬Ј build green; `dist/_headers` lands at the deploy root and the three lazy chunks (`DocReview-*`, `Scheduler-*`, `SitePlannerApp-*`) emit hashed under `/assets/`. **Self-verified headless** (`ui-audit/verify-chunk-reload.mjs`, **3/3** against the built bundle on `vite preview`): a first `vite:preloadError` reloads the page; a second within the cooldown does NOT (no loop); pushing the stamp past the cooldown reloads again (re-armed).
> **Owner note:** the `_headers` cache rules take effect automatically once Cloudflare redeploys (on merge to `main`); nothing to configure. **Dedup:** distinct from the PDF.js `import()` lazy-loading in B72/B67/B180 (those defer a heavy library until first use вАФ a feature), and from B205-era ErrorBoundary work (that catches *render* crashes; this catches *chunk-fetch* failures and recovers before the boundary is reached).

### B220 вАФ Esri imagery shows "Map data not yet available" placeholder on over-zoom (map finder) `[Site Planner]` (bug)  *(arrived as "NEW-1"; minted B218, renumbered **B220** вАФ concurrent `main` PR #183 took B218 (dead header controls) + B219 (map-furniture restyle) while this was in flight, so this is the real next free ID after B219. The implementing commits on this branch still say "B218".)*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-20 (branch `claude/quirky-mayer-s3n0pm`).** On the Site Planner **map finder**, zooming in past the area's native imagery ceiling with Esri selected filled the whole canvas with gray "Map data not yet available" tiles while street labels still rendered on top. **Root cause (confirmed):** Esri World Imagery serves those placeholder tiles as **HTTP 200** (not errors), so Leaflet's error-tile fallback never fires; on a retina/HiDPI display `detectRetina` (added in B170 for sharpness) fetches one zoom level **higher** than the display zoom (zoomOffset +1), so a plain `maxNativeZoom: 19` let deep zoom request **z20** = the placeholder. **B182 already fixed this exact bug, but only on the planner-canvas backdrop** (`SitePlanner.jsx` GEO_BASEMAP detail layer's `detailMaxNative`); the **map-finder** layer (`MapFinder.jsx`) got `detectRetina` from B170 but **never the matching clamp** вАФ an incomplete original fix across the two call sites, not a refactor revert. **Fix (`MapFinder.jsx`):** the imagery `L.tileLayer` now clamps `maxNativeZoom` to `L.Browser.retina ? bm.maxNative - 1 : bm.maxNative` for **every source in the Imagery dropdown** (Esri 19вЖТ18, USGS 16вЖТ15 on retina), keeping `maxZoom: 21` so Leaflet **upscales** the deepest real tile past native instead of fetching placeholders. The labels/reference overlay (World_Transportation) is capped at `maxNativeZoom: 19` so it can't diverge above the imagery at deep zoom (the "labels float over gray" tell). Durable code comments left at the `BASEMAPS` config + both layer sites so a future restructure can't silently drop them. **Verified headless** (`gis-verify/mapfinder-overzoom-verify.mjs`, the map finder driven deep over a Katy parcel at DSF 1 and DSF 2): max imagery tile zoom requested = **z19 at both densities** (was z20 on retina), max labels zoom = **z19**, **0** placeholder/past-native responses вАФ logged **VERIFICATION V50**. lint **0 errors** ¬Ј **414 tests** ¬Ј build green; lazy chunks intact.
> **Dedup:** RECURRENCE/completion of **B182** (done вАФ planner-canvas placeholder fix) across the second call site; builds on **B170** (detectRetina) + **B169** (blur diagnostic). Distinct from **B171** (gated high-res-source eval вАФ correctly NOT triggered; the imagery source isn't the problem) and **B162** (label zoom gating).

### B219 вАФ Professional cartographic restyle of the map north arrow + scale bar `[Site Planner]` (task)  *(arrived as "NEW-2"; minted **B219** вАФ next free ID after B218)*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-20 (branch `claude/quirky-cannon-ve2ppz`).** The on-screen north indicator and scale bar read as cartoonish (a chunky solid filled arrowhead; a heavy, thick segmented bar). Restyled the **shared furniture primitives** in `lib/sheetFurniture.js` вАФ one source of truth for BOTH the live canvas and the print/PNG export, so both inherit the upgrade with no fork. The **north arrow is now a classic two-tone surveyor's needle**: a slim elongated kite split on its spine, east half filled in a single neutral ink, west half a hairline outline, with a small "N" above in restrained weight вАФ no compass rose, no bright fill, no 3D. The **scale bar is now a thin segmented cartographic bar**: alternating filled/empty quarters, hairline strokes, 0 / mid / max tick numbers centered under their ticks, a muted "FEET" label, units in feet to match the EPSG:2278 (Texas State Plane, US survey feet) spine. Both sit on a **subtle warm semi-opaque backing** (`rgba(249,248,244,0.84)`) so labels stay legible over busy aerial imagery without reading as a hard white box. Sizing + anchoring are unchanged (the B196 always-visible DOM-overlay corners вАФ north bottom-left clear of the calibration pill, scale bottom-right under the zoom stack), so the visibility guarantees are preserved; this is a pure visual pass.
> **Self-verified headless** (`ui-audit/verify-new1to2.mjs`, logged-out, over a live Harris-county aerial): the furniture renders as the needle (**2 `<path>` halves, 0 `<circle>`**) + the segmented bar (6 `<rect>` = plate + 4 segments + north plate), with the FEET + N labels and the new subtle plate fill; corner screenshots confirm the cartographic look, legible over the imagery; **0 console errors**. `test/sheetFurniture.test.js` (18) stays green **unchanged** вАФ the restyle deliberately preserved every invariant the suite asserts (rect/segment count, no compass rose, FEET/N labels, modest ~0.5 in arrow height, north-up-vs-bearing rotation). lint 0 ¬Ј 414 tests ¬Ј build green; the `SitePlannerApp` lazy chunk split still holds.
> **Dedup:** distinct from **B144/B145** (export furniture clipping/sizing) and **B173/B196** (always-visible on-screen placement) вАФ those fixed *visibility / no-clip*; this is the *aesthetic* pass over the same shared `sheetFurniture.js` primitives, so screen and export both get it without a second code path.

### B216 вАФ Harden edge-run setbacks for IRREGULAR parcels: concave inward placement + gentle-curve grouping `[Site Planner]` (bug/task) вАФ follow-up to B214/B215  *(owner-requested edge-case pass 2026-06-19; minted **B216** вАФ highest B# across both files was B215, so this is the real next free ID)*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-19 (branch `claude/sharp-edison-7gdn3y`).** Edge-case testing on irregular parcels (L-shapes, flag lots, curved frontage, dense survey boundaries, triangles) surfaced two issues, both fixed. **(1) Concave inward placement (refines B215):** the setback pill / boundary-dim fan chose the inboard side by stepping *toward the parcel centroid* вАФ but on a concave / L-shaped / flag-lot parcel the centroid can sit in a notch (or outside the polygon), so a pill was thrown to the WRONG side (outside the lot). Replaced with a **point-in-ring test** (a small step that must land INSIDE the boundary) via a new `inwardScreenNormal` helper (computed in feet, mapped to screen), used by the per-side pill, the per-segment pill, AND the run-length dimension вАФ correct on any shape. **(2) Gentle-curve grouping (refines B214):** `edgeRuns` now chains each edge to the **PREVIOUS** edge's bearing (was the run's FIRST edge), so a gently curved frontage (a few degrees per segment) or survey noise on a nominally-straight line groups into **ONE** side (one setback, one pill, one dimension) instead of many; a genuine corner still breaks the run, and a TIGHT curve (each segment turning beyond tolerance) correctly stays per-segment.
> **Tests:** +2 `edgeRuns` unit tests (gentle-curve groups; tight-curve splits вАФ **14** in `test/edgeRuns.test.js`). New headless harness `ui-audit/verify-edge-runs-irregular.mjs` (L-shape, flag lot, tight + gentle curved frontage, dense 12-vertex survey boundary, triangle) вАФ **19/19**: every setback pill lands inside the lot (the concave fix), every run-length dim outside, no NaN, and the shallow arc groups to 4 sides (not 17). lint **0 errors** ¬Ј **411 tests** ¬Ј build green; the original **B213вАУB215 acceptance still 7/7** (the chain change keeps the 3-segment-east-side case at 4 sides). Verified **V48**. **Dedup:** not a new feature вАФ hardens the B214 run-grouping + B215 fan placement for irregular geometry; same canonical `pc.setbacks` model.

### B215 вАФ Stacked/occluded dimension labels at shared parcel-edge anchors (boundary dim + setback pill + "+" all at the edge midpoint) `[Site Planner]` (bug)  *(arrived as "NEW-3"; minted **B215** вАФ next free ID after B214)*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-19 (branch `claude/sharp-edison-7gdn3y`, commit `cc735e9`).** The parcel-edge boundary dimension, the setback value pill, and the add-vertex "+" handle no longer stack at the same edge midpoint. Each logical SIDE now gets **one run-length dimension placed OUTBOARD** of the edge (`parcelEdgeLabels` rewritten over `selRuns` + `runLabelAnchors`), and the **setback value pill is placed INBOARD** (toward the setback line it describes) вАФ fanned ~25 px apart along the edge normal, so neither occludes the other. The add-vertex "+" stays at the segment midpoint (it is the add-vertex handle, not a stack-expander) and now reads clearly once the dims move off it. No setback-line *length* label is ever drawn (the only length label is the boundary/run dimension), so there is nothing redundant to suppress.
> **Dedup / dependency:** built **with B214** вАФ run-grouping collapses the per-segment dimension stack into one label per side; B215 adds the boundary-vs-setback inboard/outboard fan that run-grouping alone does not. Distinct from **B121** (element NAME/area label overlap, `labelLayout.js`) and **B149** (zoom LOD) вАФ those are the centred element-label pool; this is the parcel-edge dimension/setback/handle pool. Self-verified headless (**V47**, `ui-audit/verify-edge-runs.mjs`): 4 run-length dims (one per side), each fanned 25 px from its pill.

### B214 вАФ Edit setback across a multi-segment side in one action (edge "runs") `[Site Planner]` (feature)  *(arrived as "NEW-2"; minted **B214** вАФ next free ID after B213)*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-19 (branch `claude/sharp-edison-7gdn3y`, commit `cc735e9`).** New pure, unit-tested `src/workspaces/site-planner/lib/edgeRuns.js` groups a parcel's **contiguous near-collinear edges** (¬±7¬∞ of the run's first-edge bearing, wrap-around-aware) into **runs** = logical sides, so a side a survey digitized as ~10 segments reads as ONE side. On the selected parcel the on-canvas setback editor shows **one pill per side**; editing it applies the value across **every segment of the run at once** via `setRunSetback`, writing the **canonical per-edge `pc.setbacks` array** (what `setbacksOf`/`constraintsOf`/`developableArea` read вАФ no parallel store) which `offsetPolygon` already miters into one continuous setback line. A **"By side / Per segment" toggle** (shown only when a side has >1 segment) plus **Alt-click a side pill** give the single-edge override for notches/jogs. The run also drives the single run-length dimension (B215). Easement `restrictsBuildings`/`restrictsPaving` flags already feed the same model via `exclusionZonesOf`, so both setbacks and easement exclusions reach the (stubbed) `developableArea` verdict engine вАФ structurally integrated.
> **Dedup:** reuses the contiguous-edge-run idea already shipped for parcel-edge easements (`buildParcelEdgeStrip` + `easeEdges`), here auto-grouped by bearing and applied to setbacks. Distinct from **B146** (interactive ELEMENT dimension callouts). **+12 unit tests** (`test/edgeRuns.test.js`). Self-verified headless (**V47**): selecting a parcel with a 3-segment east side shows **4 pills (S, E-run, N, W), not 6 edges**; "Per segment" вЖТ 6; toggling back вЖТ 4.

### B213 вАФ Inactive parcel still shows its setback line, acreage label, and edge/boundary dimensions (active-state not inherited by anchored elements) `[Site Planner]` (bug)  *(arrived as "NEW-1"; minted **B213** вАФ first filed as B206, then twice renumbered as concurrent `main` (PR #175 then PR #177) took B206вАУB212 in the same window; this Site-Planner trio landed at the next free block **B213вАУB215** to keep IDs unique)*

### B212 вАФ Configurable table columns (show / hide / add / reorder), MS Project / P6 style `[Scheduler / Table]` (feature)  *(arrived as "NEW-3"; minted B196, renumbered **B212** вАФ concurrent `main` took B194вАУB209 (Site Planner trailer-label/scale-bar/print/storage tranches) while this was in flight, so the real next free IDs were B210вАУB212)*

### B211 вАФ Task status as fill treatment (hollow / partial / solid) `[Scheduler / Gantt]` (feature)  *(arrived as "NEW-2"; minted B195, renumbered **B211** вАФ concurrent `main` took B194вАУB209 while this was in flight)*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-19 (branch `claude/sharp-keller-wphsna`).** Task status moved **off the color channel onto a single continuous fill treatment** in both Gantt render paths (on-screen `GanttView` + the PDF/print `buildGanttSVG`). Every task bar keeps **one identity hue** (the existing task **gray `#94a3b8`**, or an explicit per-task `rowColor` override); status reads as **0вЖТ100% complete**: **not started (0%)** = hollow rounded pill (outline in the hue, required else invisible); **in progress** = partial fill (solid portion = `percentComplete`, lighter remainder behind it, thin outline around the whole); **complete (100%)** = solid fill. A **min-width floor** keeps a 0% bar from collapsing to a sliver. Fill fraction derives from `percentComplete` (Complete вЖТ solid regardless). The **red / paused / overdue** signal stays in the **row background + the table** (untouched), so status never collides with the navy hierarchy. Milestone diamonds follow the same monochrome language (gray, filled when complete, hollow otherwise).
> **Self-verified headless** (`ui-audit/verify-sequence.mjs`): DOM probe finds **11 solid + 24 outlined** gray task bars and **0** bars using the old health colors (yellow/red/green); 0 runtime errors. Palette preserved (the one purple `SS` dependency line `#7c3aed` untouched). lint 0 ¬Ј 352 tests ¬Ј build green.

### B210 вАФ Summary bars as depth-stepped brackets `[Scheduler / Gantt]` (feature)  *(arrived as "NEW-1"; minted B194, renumbered **B210** вАФ concurrent `main` took B194вАУB209 while this was in flight, so this is the real next free ID)*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-19 (branch `claude/sharp-keller-wphsna`).** Replaced the heavy solid summary bars (a thick slab + barely-visible triangle endcaps) with a thin **bracket**: a navy horizontal **span** with **straight-down vertical legs** at each end (no triangles), in both render paths (`GanttView` + `buildGanttSVG`). WBS nesting depth is encoded by **three cues that step together, top-of-tree strongest** вАФ **darkness** (navy `#2B3340` вЖТ `#46506A` вЖТ `#6E7790` вЖТ tint), **span thickness** (7/5/4/4 px), and **leg length** (a fraction of row height) вАФ the ramp **stops deepening at ~4 levels** (the table's indented name carries depth from there). The summary **name centers just above the span** in the bar's own level-navy (no thick fill to print white onto); no per-level label indentation (bars are date-positioned). An explicit `rowColor` override still wins.
> **Self-verified headless** (`ui-audit/verify-sequence.mjs`): DOM probe finds **36 navy bracket elements** (вЙИ a dozen brackets √Ч span+2 legs); a detail screenshot confirms the shape вАФ label above a thin span with a straight-down leg, **no triangle**. 0 runtime errors. lint 0 ¬Ј 352 tests ¬Ј build green.

### B203 вАФ Schedule project picker showed Site Planner projects; scheduling projects inaccessible `[Scheduler / Header-Nav]` (bug) вАФ CRITICAL  *(owner-reported 2026-06-19; minted **B203** вАФ concurrent `main` (#169вАУ#172) took B194вАУB202 while this was in flight, so this is the real next free ID after B202)*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-19 (branch `claude/elegant-bohr-16zcag`).** Owner: in the **Schedule** module the Row-1 project picker listed **Site Planner** sites, and his scheduling projects (Goose Creek, Kilgore - Grand Port / "Grandport", Eight South a.k.a. vSAN, Pursuits, Papadopoulos) were unreachable.
> **Diagnosis first (the silent-data-loss rule) вАФ data was NEVER lost.** The Schedule workspace embeds a separate scheduler app in an **iframe** (`public/sequence/index.html`); that app stores ALL projects as one cloud record (`hs-v1`) in its **own** Supabase project (`ksetjztkplttbcehyicv`), cloud-first with the baked `__PLANAR_DATA__` only as a first-run seed. Inside the iframe the scheduler **hides its own header** (`.in-iframe .app-header{display:none}`), which is where its project picker + Dashboard/Projects toggle lived. The B191вАУB193 shared breadcrumb that replaced it reads `listProjects()` вЖТ the **Site Planner** site store and routes every action into the Site Planner вАФ so Schedule showed Site projects and couldn't open scheduler ones. A wiring bug, not a data bug.
> **Fix вАФ make the Row-1 picker module-aware via a postMessage bridge** (no second store, no schema change): the embedded scheduler now emits its OWN nav state (project list + active project + section) to the shell (`planar:nav-state`) and accepts select / dashboard / new-project commands back (`planar:nav-*`), same-origin-targeted. `ProjectBreadcrumb` accepts an optional **controlled `projects`** list (falls back to `listProjects()` when omitted, so Site/Markup are unchanged); `Scheduler.jsx` feeds in the iframe's projects and posts commands to it instead of bouncing into the Site Planner. Opened directly (not in the shell) the scheduler keeps its native header вАФ no regression.
> **Self-verified headless** (`ui-audit/verify-schedule-picker.mjs`, **8/8**, logged-out with the scheduler cloud blocked вЖТ it fell back to its seed, which still flowed through the bridge): Site crumb "Map" lists Site projects; Schedule crumb "Dashboard" lists the SCHEDULER's projects (Goose Creek / Grand Port / Bee Sand) and **not** the seeded Site projects; selecting a project switches it inside the iframe; the Dashboard crumb opens the scheduler's reports view. 381 tests (full suite, post-merge with `main`) ¬Ј lint 0 ¬Ј build green. **NOTE for the owner:** the headless run is offline/logged-out so it showed the scheduler's 3 *seed* projects; the live signed-in/online app will list his real set (the bug never touched that cloud record).
> **Dedup:** direct follow-up to **B191вАУB193** (the shared breadcrumb) вАФ fixes their Site-only assumption for Schedule; reuses the same `AppHeader`/`ProjectBreadcrumb`, adds only the module-aware list + the iframe bridge. Paired with **B204** (module-contextual home label).
