> **Dedup:** distinct from B131 (overlay-in-print toggle); reuses B198's effective-property selector for the values.

### B198 вАФ Auto-assign clear height & slab thickness as building properties by square footage `[Site Planner]` (feature)  *(arrived as "NEW-2"; minted B198)*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-19 (branch `claude/sweet-hypatia-itdlvu`, commit `8e19081`).** `clearHeight` + `slabThickness` are now first-class building properties (available to any module), auto-assigned from the building's footprint sf via an **editable per-plan rule** (`settings.buildingRules`) plus an **optional manual override** stored on the element (`clearHeightOverride` / `slabThicknessOverride`; override wins, auto recomputes on sf change when unset). Upper tier inclusive at each boundary вАФ `<140k вЖТ 32'/6"`, `[140k,600k) вЖТ 36'/7"`, `>=600k вЖТ 40'/7"` вАФ so a 250,000 sf building defaults to 36'/7" with no input (verified). New pure module `lib/buildingProps.js` (12 unit tests); additive el/settings fields (no migration). Surfaced + editable inline on the selected-building inspector and in the print Options flyout (B199).

### B199 вАФ Print options interface: edit global defaults and per-building overrides `[Site Planner]` (feature)  *(arrived as "NEW-3"; minted B199)*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-19 (branch `claude/sweet-hypatia-itdlvu`, commit `8e19081`).** The print-frame toolbar gained an **Options вЦЊ** flyout (portal-mounted `AnchoredMenu`, so it escapes the toolbar's stacking context): (a) edit the **global size rules** from B198 (thresholds + their clear-height/slab values, with Reset to defaults) and (b) **override** clear height + slab per building (name editable too), with **auto vs set** surfaced and a one-click revert-to-auto. Editing globals changes defaults for un-overridden buildings; a per-building override pins that building. Live-smoke verified (`ui-audit/verify-print-live.mjs`, 0 runtime errors).

### B200 вАФ Print zoom: building/site plan doesn't scale with title block, not a cohesive PDF `[Site Planner]` (bug)  *(arrived as "NEW-4"; minted B200)*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-19 (branch `claude/sweet-hypatia-itdlvu`, commit `8e19081`).** Root cause: the plan was a nested SVG but the title block + metrics were HTML flow around it вАФ two layout systems, so the print scale slider could scale the chrome while the plan held a fixed size. Fix: the **whole sheet is now ONE `<svg>`** (`lib/printSheet.js` `buildPrintSheetSvg`) вАФ title block, the plan (nested `<svg>` keeping its own viewBox), the buildings table (B197) and the metrics share one viewBox and **one scaling transform**, so every layer scales together at any zoom and prints as one cohesive page (`@page margin:0` + intrinsic-inch SVG = exactly one page; inset border clears the printer edge). The on-canvas print frame now matches the printed plan box (WYSIWYG). Headless-rendered: one root SVG, nested plan, letter-landscape 11in viewBox. 15 tests.

### B201 вАФ Print filename format `[Site Planner]` (feature)  *(arrived as "NEW-5"; minted B201)*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-19 (branch `claude/sweet-hypatia-itdlvu`, commits `8e19081` + follow-up).** Exported PDF (document title вЖТ Save-as filename) and PNG use **`YYYY.MM.DD {Project} - {Plan Name}`** вАФ e.g. `2026.06.19 Cypress Logistics - Plan 1` (or `вА¶ - Scheme A` once the plan is renamed). Date = today at export, project = the active site name, **trailing piece = the plan's own label** (`planLabel`). Filesystem-illegal characters are stripped from project + plan (the ` - ` separator and date dots preserved); a blank plan name just drops the tail. `lib/printSheet.js` `sheetFileName`/`sanitizeFilename` (tested).
> **Owner decision (2026-06-19):** the trailing identifier is the **plan name**, not an incrementing number вАФ so the filename always tracks whatever the plan is named (today "Plan 1", later e.g. "Scheme A") and won't drift or surprise. (Superseded the initial incrementing-sheet-number default; the per-session counter was removed.)

### B202 вАФ "Preparing print" hangs before producing file `[Site Planner]` (bug)  *(arrived as "NEW-6"; minted B202)*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-19 (branch `claude/sweet-hypatia-itdlvu`, commit `8e19081`).** The stall was the image-inlining step: aerial/overlay `<image>` fetches ran one-by-one with **no timeout**, so any fetch that hung through the TLS-inspection proxy blocked prep for up to ~60s. Fix: each fetch is now **time-boxed** (`AbortController`, 8s) and they run **in parallel**, so worst-case prep is ~8s and a hung image is dropped (PNG) or keeps its remote href (print loads it natively). Added prep **timing instrumentation** (`console.debug` marks for inline + ready) so any future stall is diagnosable rather than a mystery.

### B196 вАФ Scale bar + north arrow as DOM overlays so they're always fully visible (B173 follow-up) `[Site Planner / UI]` (bug)  *(owner re-reported on the live site 2026-06-19 вАФ "scale still not fully shown, nor the north cardinal direction"; minted B196 вАФ highest B# across both files was B195)*
`[x]` Done 2026-06-19 (branch `claude/kind-meitner-uy2qeh`). **B173 pinned the app to the viewport (no page scroll) but left two residual defects** the owner still saw: (a) the on-screen scale bar + north arrow were drawn *inside the canvas SVG*, anchored to its coordinate space (`buildScreenFurnitureSvg` at `vh вИТ 40`), so they rode the canvas and could still clip on a short/odd viewport; (b) the north arrow sat directly under the green **"Scaled ¬Ј county GIS" calibration pill** (a higher-z DOM element at `left:12, bottom:40`) вАФ so only the "N" peeked out, the arrow body hidden (the exact "north not shown" symptom). **Fix:** lifted both into **DOM overlays anchored to the VISIBLE canvas corners** вАФ new `screenFurniturePlates()` in `lib/sheetFurniture.js` returns the scale bar + north arrow as standalone plates; `SitePlanner.jsx` renders them as two absolutely-positioned `<svg>`s at `bottom:40` (`pointerEvents:none`, `zIndex:7`, `data-export="skip"`), immune to canvas size. Relocated the two colliders: calibration pill `left:12 вЖТ 56` (beside the arrow), zoom controls `bottom:78 вЖТ 100` (above the scale bar). Also kept the planner root `minHeight:600 вЖТ 0` (belt-and-suspenders with B173's `index.css` `100dvh`+`overflow:hidden`, so a sub-600px window clips nothing). The **export** furniture path (`buildSheetFurnitureSvg`) is untouched вАФ export parity preserved. **Self-verified headless at 1600√Ч800 AND 1600√Ч540:** page overflow 0; the "FEET" (scale) and "N" (north) labels both `getBoundingClientRect` fully inside the viewport at both heights; corner screenshots show the scale bar clear below the +/вИТ/в§Ґ zoom stack and the north arrow beside (not under) the calibration pill. lint 0 errors ¬Ј 257 tests ¬Ј build green ¬Ј `SitePlannerApp` lazy chunk intact.
> **Reconciliation:** B173 (DONE, stays) fixed the page-scroll via viewport pinning and judged a portal overlay unnecessary; the owner's live re-report proved the furniture *placement* (in-SVG + pill overlap) was the remaining cause. B196 implements exactly the "fixed overlay anchored to the canvas corner" mechanism B173's note had set aside. B172/B174/B175 (tabs / header вИТ20% / parcel checkbox) shipped independently on `main` and this branch's duplicates of them were dropped during the merge in favour of `main`'s versions.

### B195 вАФ Trailer-parking label stays inside its polygon at every zoom level `[Site Planner]` (bug)  *(arrived as "NEW-2"; minted B190, renumbered **B195** вАФ concurrent `main` (#164/#168 + sibling branches) took B189вАУB193 while this was in flight, so this is the real next free ID after B193)*
`[x]` Done 2026-06-19 (branch `claude/cool-babbage-mpc9sd`). Zooming out grew the trailer label *relative to its shrinking strip* until it overflowed: the label was sized in fixed **screen** pixels (floored at `lsвЙ•0.34`), so it stayed roughly constant while the strip got smaller on zoom-out вАФ "fit logic exists but the limits are off." **Fix:** a trailer label is now sized as a **fraction of the strip's real-world extent** (EPSG:2278 feet вЖТ screen px via the current pixels-per-foot, `view.ppf`), so it scales WITH the area and stays contained by construction. The text runs along the strip's **long** side and the line-stack across its **short** side, each with its own fit bound (the smaller governs вАФ this matches `stripLabelRot`, the B186/B188 helper that aligns the label to the long axis). The font is **floored** at a legible minimum (`minPx`, below which a too-small вЙИ2-spot strip takes *controlled overflow* rather than going illegible) and **capped** at the normal label size so it never balloons when zoomed in. The shared label engine `lib/labelLayout.js` gained a **`noLeader`** option: a trailer label that still can't fit overflows **in place** (centred on the strip), instead of being leadered out, and the engine now **prefers dropping a line to fit inside** before accepting that overflow. Per-label font metrics (`fs`/`lh`/`charW`) are threaded through the candidate вЖТ layout вЖТ render path; every non-trailer label keeps the existing global metrics (defaults unchanged). **Self-verified headless** (`ui-audit/verify-trailer-label.mjs`): across five zoom levels the label stays **inside** the strip вАФ shape **397√Ч55px вЖТ 102√Ч14px**, label/shape height ratio **0.50** (capped when the shape is large) **вЖТ 0.96** (floored when small), `inside=true` at every step; `verify-new1to5.mjs` confirms a vertical strip still rotates correctly and other label types are untouched. **2 new `labelLayout` tests** (noLeader overflow-in-place; drop-a-line-to-fit). 354 tests (full suite, post-merge with `main`) ¬Ј lint 0 ¬Ј build green.
> **Dedup:** extends the **B121** shared label LOD + collision engine (`labelLayout.js`) and complements **B149** (zoom-out decluttering) вАФ area-relative sizing is added *on top of* that one engine, not as a parallel renderer. Reuses **B186/B188**'s `stripLabelRot` (label orientation along a strip) rather than re-deriving it. Depended on **B194** for the final two-line label content. Distinct from B188, which fixed label *orientation/consistency*; B195 fixes label *containment under zoom*.

### B194 вАФ Trailer-parking label: stall depth in the title, drop the row-dimension line `[Site Planner]` (feature)  *(arrived as "NEW-1"; minted B189, renumbered **B194** вАФ concurrent `main` (#164/#168 + sibling branches) took B189вАУB193 while this was in flight, so this is the real next free ID after B193)*

The trailer-parking label is now **two lines** instead of three: line 1 = the per-stall trailer length + name (e.g. **"50вА≤ Trailer Parking"**), line 2 = the trailer count (e.g. **"30 trailers"**). The old third line (overall row dimensions, e.g. "360вА≤ √Ч 50вА≤" / "355вА≤ √Ч 50вА≤") is **dropped entirely** вАФ the depth now lives in the title and the overall row length is intentionally gone. The stall depth is read straight off the element's own config (`cfgOf(el).trailerL`, the depth a trailer sits in) вАФ **not** the overall row length and **not** recomputed; the count keeps the existing `trailerStalls`/`estTrailers` math (polygon fields still read "(est)"). > **Dedup:** distinct from **B188** (which fixed label *orientation/consistency* вАФ running the label in-line on a narrow strip via `stripLabelRot`); B194 changes the label *content*. Builds on B188's strip-label work, doesn't duplicate it. Paired with **B195** (containment under zoom), which depends on this item's final two-line dimensions.

### B193 вАФ Persist current project before switching `[Header/Nav]` (task)  *(arrived as "NEW-3"; filed provisionally as B191, renumbered **B193** вАФ concurrent `main` (#168) took B189вАУB190 for the Site Analysis tranche, so this is the real next free ID after B190/B191/B192)*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-19 (branch `claude/awesome-gauss-jlrq5v`).** A breadcrumb switch (to another project or to the Dashboard) flushes the current project first, so a switch can't silently drop unsaved work вАФ it routes through the **existing** data-loss machinery: in the Site Planner, opening another project goes through `handleOpenSite` вЖТ `flushSite()` and the `key`-change unmount `persistOrDrop()`; in Doc Review, the `useReviewPersistence` unmount/visibility flush already guarantees the local write. On top of that, B193 adds the owner-requested **cloud-at-risk surfacing** (the B124/B125 silent-failure rule): each workspace passes a normalized `saveState` to the breadcrumb, and when it's `offline`/`error`, the switcher shows a **passive вЪ† line in the dropdown** AND a **transient "saved on this device вАФ will sync when reconnected" toast** on the switch. The switch is **never blocked** on a successful cloud save, but is **never silent** about an at-risk one.
> **Self-verified headless** (`ui-audit/verify-new1to3.mjs`): project switches complete cleanly; the at-risk surfacing is gated on `offline`/`error` (the sandbox is logged-out вЖТ `local`, no false warning). **Dedup:** no new persistence path вАФ reuses SitePlanner's `flushSite`/`persistOrDrop` + Doc Review's persistence flush; B193 is the routing + surfacing layer over them. 344 tests ¬Ј lint 0 ¬Ј build green.

### B190 вАФ Click a constraint card to toggle its layer on the map `[Site Planner / Site Analysis]` (feature)  *(arrived as "NEW-2"; filed provisionally as B185, renumbered **B190** вАФ concurrent `main` (#164) took B184вАУB188 for unrelated Site Planner items, so this is the real next free ID after B189)*

### B189 вАФ Site Analysis constraint queries failing (UNKNOWN / "Failed to execute query") `[Site Planner / Site Analysis]` (bug)  *(arrived as "NEW-1"; filed provisionally as B184, renumbered **B189** вАФ concurrent `main` (#164) took B184вАУB188 for unrelated Site Planner items, so this is the real next free ID after B188)*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-19 (branch `claude/bold-edison-h8tfkc`).** Filed AND fixed AND verified live the same session. Bug: on Site Analysis, **Wetlands** + **Pipelines** returned "Failed to execute query." вЖТ UNKNOWN, while Floodplain worked. The bug report's instinct to **audit every category, not just the two visible**, paid off: a **third** source (**Oil & gas wells**, below the fold) was 400-ing too.
> **Root cause was a different field bug per source вАФ confirmed live (HTTP 400 with old fields вЖТ HTTP 200 with real features) against a known Katy/Sheldon-Lake parcel before patching:**
> - **Wetlands** вАФ NWI split layers 1/2 are **JOINED** layers (`Wetlands вЛИ NWI_Wetland_Codes`), so every field comes back **table-qualified** (`Wetlands_CONUS_West.WETLAND_TYPE`); asking for the bare names 400'd, and the qualifier **differs per sublayer** (East vs West). Fix: request `outFields:"*"` and **`normalizeAttrs()`** strips the `Table.` prefix so the summarizers read plain names.
> - **Pipelines** вАФ queried `OPERATOR`/`COMMODITY`, which **don't exist** (real: `OPER_NM`, `CMDTY_DESC`, `DIAMETER`).
> - **Oil & gas wells** вАФ queried `LEASE_NAME`, which **doesn't exist** on the Wells layer (real: `SYMNUM`/`API`/`WELLID`/вА¶).
> All three fixed + flipped **`verified:true`**, so a now-working empty query resolves to **None found** (not conservative UNKNOWN) вАФ matching the bug report's "expected." The silent-error guard is intact: a genuine HTTP/network error still classifies **unknown**, never a fabricated "none." Added **diagnostics** вАФ `defaultFetchJson` carries `{httpStatus,url,arcgisCode}` on the Error and `logQueryFailure()` prints the real failure to the console, so an opaque "Failed to execute query." is debuggable instead of silent.
> **Verified live (headless, `ui-audit/verify-analysis.mjs`, real USFWS/FEMA/TxRRC endpoints):** Floodplain **PRESENT (Zone AE)**, Wetlands **PRESENT (Lake, Freshwater Forested/Shrub Wetland)**, Pipelines **NONE FOUND**, Oil & gas **NONE FOUND** вАФ zero "Failed to execute query." 341 tests (siteAnalysis 25вЖТ36, incl. the qualified-field + corrected-field + normalizeAttrs cases), lint 0 errors, build green. **V45.**
> **Dedup:** this is the per-source debug of **B147**'s "рЯФ≤ Remaining (1)." Distinct from **B133/B135** (those fixed the wetlands *map-overlay image* `/export`; this fixed the Site Analysis `/query` connector вАФ a different request path on the same host).

### B188 вАФ Trailer-parking label inconsistent + should run in-line on the strip `[Site Planner]` (bug)  *(arrived as "NEW-5"; filed provisionally as B184, renumbered **B188** вАФ concurrent `main` took B180вАУB183 for unrelated items, so this is the real next free ID.)*
`[x]` Done 2026-06-19 (branch `claude/happy-goldberg-piym6g`). Two trailer-parking instances rendered their labels differently вАФ the wide field kept its 3-line label horizontal, while the narrow wall strip overflowed (the collision engine leadered it OUT of the strip). Root cause: there was no orientation logic, so a label wider than the strip was pulled outside rather than turned to run along it. Fix = the **shared label-orientation helper** built for B186 (`stripLabelRot`, applied to `landscape`/`sidewalk`/`trailer` strips): when a label is wider than the strip is narrow, it runs ALONG the strip's long axis (vertical text on a vertical strip), so both instances now render consistently in-line and neither claims more space than the strip itself. **Self-verified headless** (`ui-audit/verify-new1to5.mjs`): a thin vertical trailer strip shows its label running vertically down the strip; a wide trailer field keeps its label horizontal. 286 tests ¬Ј lint 0 ¬Ј build green.

### B187 вАФ Truck court resize must anchor to the dock wall and push/pull trailer parking `[Site Planner]` (bug) вАФ high severity  *(arrived as "NEW-4"; filed provisionally as B183, renumbered **B187**.)*
`[x]` Done 2026-06-19 (branch `claude/happy-goldberg-piym6g`). Changing a truck court's **Depth** field (e.g. 135вЖТ140) resized it from the **centre** вАФ losing depth on both sides, detaching the paving from both the dock wall and the trailer parking (a silently-wrong geometry state). **Two root causes fixed:** (1) `resizeSelEl` (the numeric Width/Depth editor) kept `cx/cy` fixed, so it grew/shrank symmetrically вАФ it now applies the same **`hostClampOf`/`clampToHost`** host-edge pin the resize grips already use, so an attached strip/court stays flush against the dock wall and only the FAR edge moves; (2) `refitChildren` never moved the court's back-side trailer when the court itself was the resized element (it only handled trailers when the *building* resized) вАФ it now registers a resized truck court in `courtBox`, so the `forCourt` trailer follows the moved far edge (pushed out on grow, pulled in on shrink, spacing preserved). Covers both the numeric field and the resize grips. **Self-verified headless** (`ui-audit/verify-new4b.mjs`, the owner's exact path вАФ Depth 135вЖТ170): the building/dock-wall label moved **0 px** (court stays anchored) while the trailer label moved **+54 px** out (pushed flush) вАФ court вЖТ court paving вЖТ trailer stay connected, nothing detaches. 286 tests ¬Ј lint 0 ¬Ј build green.

### B186 вАФ Buffer-strip width labels run along the strip's long axis `[Site Planner]` (feature)  *(arrived as "NEW-2"; filed provisionally as B182, renumbered **B186**; shares its helper with B188/NEW-5)*
`[x]` Done 2026-06-19 (branch `claude/happy-goldberg-piym6g`). A "5вА≤ Landscape" / "5вА≤ Sidewalk" label rendered horizontally even on a thin vertical strip, eating canvas across the strip. Added one shared, holistic helper вАФ **`stripLabelRot(el, lines, charW, ppf)`** (covers `landscape`, `sidewalk` AND `trailer`, no per-type duplication) вАФ that returns a rotation when the label is wider than the strip is narrow: the label then runs ALONG the strip's long axis (vertical text on a vertical strip, horizontal on a horizontal one). The shared `labelLayout` collision engine was extended to test the label's **rotated** on-screen footprint, so a vertical label is fitted against the strip's tall height and narrow width (and so it lands INSIDE the strip instead of being leadered out). New unit test in `test/labelLayout.test.js`. **Self-verified headless** (`ui-audit/verify-new1to5.mjs`): vertical landscape/sidewalk/trailer strips show vertical labels; horizontal strips and wide fields stay horizontal. 286 tests ¬Ј lint 0 ¬Ј build green.

### B185 вАФ Site acreage chip is draggable + persisted `[Site Planner]` (feature)  *(arrived as "NEW-3"; filed provisionally as B181, renumbered **B185**.)*
`[x]` Done 2026-06-19 (branch `claude/happy-goldberg-piym6g`). The parcel acreage chip ("32.51 ac") was pinned at the parcel centroid and obstructed the layout. It's now **click-and-drag** (in Select), to anywhere вАФ including outside the parcel boundary вАФ storing a `labelOffset` (parcel-local feet) on the parcel so it survives geometry edits. New `startAcChip` + an `acChip` drag-move case mirror the B146 dimension-callout drag pattern; the offset persists via the existing Site Model save path (additive field on `parcels[]`, mirrors to Supabase when signed in). **Self-verified headless** (`ui-audit/verify-new3.mjs`): the chip dragged 182 px and `parcels[0].labelOffset` was written to the saved store. 286 tests ¬Ј lint 0 ¬Ј build green.

### B184 вАФ 24вА≤ road-width dimension drifts left of centre `[Site Planner]` (bug)  *(arrived as "NEW-1"; filed provisionally as B180, renumbered **B184** вАФ concurrent `main` took B180вАУB183.)*
`[x]` Done 2026-06-19 (branch `claude/happy-goldberg-piym6g`). The road-width dimension ("24вА≤") rendered shifted toward the left edge of the road instead of centred on the span. Cause: the dimension line/label were placed at **18 %** along the element's long axis (a sensible default for a building's depth tick, but wrong for a road, where the width tick should sit on the centreline of the length). Fix: roads now place the width dimension at the **midpoint (50 %)** of the length (`posF = el.type === "road" ? 0.5 : 0.18`); the measured value and the perpendicular span anchor were already correct (the label sits at the midpoint of the measured width), so this is a position-only fix вАФ no measurement-accuracy change. **Self-verified headless** (`ui-audit/verify-new1to5.mjs`): the "24вА≤" label sits centred along the road. 286 tests ¬Ј lint 0 ¬Ј build green.

### B183 вАФ Editable layers decouple from backdrop during pan while loading `[Site Planner]` (bug)  *(arrived as "NEW-1"; filed provisionally as B177, renumbered **B183** вАФ concurrent `main` took B176вАУB181, so this is the real next free ID after B181/B182.)*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-19 (branch `claude/nice-heisenberg-r6lmf1`).** On a freshly-loaded site, grabbing and panning before load settled made the drawn layers (massing/parcels/markup) visibly offset from the aerial for a frame or two, then snap back. **Root cause (confirmed, not the pasted race-condition theory):** in Planyr the SVG *is* the source of truth and the basemap follows it, so the layers can't reproject against a stale transform вАФ the decoupler was **B65's own ghost snapshot**. A `commit` clones the basemap into a frozen overlay held until the fresh tiles `load`; while loading, that `load` is delayed so the snapshot lingered, and a pan moved the live SVG while the **frozen** snapshot stayed put вЖТ the aerial lagged the drawn layers until the snapshot expired (hence "only early on, then snaps back"). **Fix:** drop any lingering snapshot the instant a new gesture starts (`dropGhost()` at the top of the transform path), so a pan is tracked by the live CSS transform (welded to the SVG) and the backfill covers any reveal; a fresh snapshot is taken only at the next commit. **Verified headless** (`ui-audit/diagnose-decouple.mjs`, retina + throttled, pan immediately after load): **0 %** of pan frames have a snapshot on top (idle baseline has one, correctly dropped on the first pan). lint 0 ¬Ј 257 tests ¬Ј build green.

### B182 вАФ Basemap tiles missing at high zoom ("Map data not yet available") `[Site Planner]` (bug)  *(arrived as "NEW-1"; filed provisionally as B176, renumbered **B182** вАФ concurrent `main` took B176вАУB181 (jurisdictions/tax + cost takeoff), so this is the real next free ID.)*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-19 (branch `claude/nice-heisenberg-r6lmf1`).** Zooming in deep showed gray "Map data not yet available" placeholder tiles instead of imagery. **Root cause (measured, `ui-audit/diagnose-zoomdepth.mjs`):** Esri World Imagery is native to **z19**; `detectRetina` (added in B170 for sharpness) fetches **one zoom level higher** than the display zoom, so at deep zoom on a retina display the detail layer requested **z20** (168 requests), which Esri answers with the placeholder image. `maxNativeZoom:19` didn't account for the retina offset. **Fix:** drop the detail layer's `maxNativeZoom` by 1 on retina (`L.Browser.retina ? maxNative-1 : maxNative`), so the highest native fetch is z19 and beyond that it **upscales the deepest real imagery** instead of fetching nonexistent tiles вАФ exactly the requested "clamp to deepest available zoom, scale the last good tiles up; never put placeholders over the plan." **Verified:** max tile zoom requested now **19** at both retina (DSF 2) and non-retina (DSF 1), **0** placeholder/empty responses (was 168). The coarse backfill (`maxNativeZoom:13`) was already clamping correctly. lint 0 ¬Ј 257 tests ¬Ј build green.
> **Follow-up вЖТ B218 (2026-06-20):** this fix was applied only to the **planner-canvas** backdrop (`SitePlanner.jsx` GEO_BASEMAP). The **map-finder** imagery layer (`MapFinder.jsx`) had the same `detectRetina` (from B170) but never got this retina clamp, so the placeholder still showed there on a retina display. B218 brought the identical clamp to the map finder (every dropdown source) + capped the labels overlay. Both call sites now clamp.

### B180 вАФ Verify paving area excludes curb footprint `[Cost]` (bug)  *(arrived as "NEW-1"; minted **B180** вАФ highest B# across both files was B179, so this is the real next free ID. Prerequisite for B181's paving-area trim.)*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-19 (branch `claude/determined-feynman-l7c61b`). Investigated вЖТ confirmed correct by construction, and locked it in.** There was no pre-existing *cost* paving figure to fold curb into вАФ the only paving area the app derived was the **impervious/SF** metric, where including the curb band is *correct* (curb is impervious surface), so that stays untouched. The new cost takeoff (B181) derives paving from the road's **face-of-curb-to-face-of-curb travel width** (`roadTravelWidth` = `min(w,h) вИТ 2¬Јcurb`), which **excludes** the curb by definition: a 30вА≤ FC-FC road yields 30вА≤ of paving, never 31вА≤. So the defect the brief warned about (folding the 6вА≥ curb each side into paving) cannot occur вАФ the cost math reads travel width, not the full element rectangle.
> **Locked against regression:** `roadQuantities` (in `lib/costTakeoff.js`) takes the FC-FC width explicitly and a unit test asserts a 30вА≤ FC-FC √Ч 1000вА≤ barrier-curb road = exactly **30,000 SF (3,333.33 SY)** of paving with curb **outside** that width вАФ so a future change that folded curb back in would fail the suite. **Live-confirmed in-browser:** a seeded 26вА≤-cross road (FC-FC travel 25вА≤) reads **1,611 SY** in the Yield panel (25 √Ч 580 √Ј 9); had curb been folded in (26вА≤) it would read 1,675 SY вАФ the 1,611 proves the exclusion. 300 tests green, lint 0 errors, build green.

### B181 вАФ Curb as a separate linear quantity type with curb-type attribute `[Cost]` (feature)  *(arrived as "NEW-2"; minted **B181** вАФ next free ID after B180.)*
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-19 (branch `claude/determined-feynman-l7c61b`).** A road segment now derives **two independent, separately-priced quantities**:
> - **Paving** вАФ an AREA item, **square yards (SY; 1 SY = 9 SF)** = length √Ч FC-FC paving width √Ј 9. Width is stored/derived as **face-of-curb to face-of-curb** (the drivable surface), so a back-of-curb dimension can't silently inflate it.
> - **Curb** вАФ a LINEAR item, **linear feet (LF)** = length √Ч curbed-side count. **Both sides counted** (a 1,000вА≤ road curbed both sides = 2,000 LF).
>
> **Curb carries a `curbType` attribute that selects its unit price:** `none` / **`barrier`** (vertical ~6вА≥ lip, no gutter pan) / **`curb-gutter`** (curb + flat concrete gutter pan, typ. 18вАУ24вА≥). For **curb-and-gutter**, the gutter pan rides with the curb LF item, so **paving trims by the pan width on each curbed side** (`paving = FC-FC вИТ panWidth √Ч sides`); pan width is a property of the curb-and-gutter type (default 2.0вА≤/24вА≥, editable). Curb LF is split **barrier vs curb-and-gutter** in the rollup so each rides its own price.
> **Implementation:** new pure library `src/workspaces/site-planner/lib/costTakeoff.js` (`roadQuantities`, `costRollup`, curb-type readers) вАФ no React, fully unit-tested (`test/costTakeoff.test.js`, 15 cases). Road-element fields are additive/optional (`curbType`, `curbedSides`, `panWidth`) and persist losslessly through the Site Model (els pass through untouched; no `SITE_MODEL_VERSION` bump). UI: a **"Curb & paving (cost)"** group in the road inspector (curb-type dropdown, curbed-sides Both/One, gutter-pan width, live per-segment SY/LF readout вАФ inline editors only, no dialogs) and a collapsible **"Road cost (screening)"** section in the **Yield** panel (site-wide Paving SY + Curb LF by type, **user-supplied** unit-price inputs вАФ blank by default, never a hardcoded $/LF вАФ and a priced subtotal).
> **Hook left for later (not built):** `roadQuantities` tags each curb run `curbCategory: "linear"` so a future **radius/corner curb** category (often a higher unit price) can be broken out as its own priced line without reworking the rollup.
> **Verified:** 300 tests green (15 new), lint 0 errors, build green, lazy-chunk split intact. **Live headless (logged-out preview):** Yield вЖТ "Road cost (screening)" renders **Paving 1,611 SY ¬Ј Curb ¬Ј barrier 1,160 LF** with the FC-FC caveat and unit-price inputs, **zero page errors** (`ui-audit/verify-cost.mjs`).

### B176 вАФ Jurisdictions overlay `[Site Planner]` (feature)  *(arrived as "NEW-1"; filed provisionally as B167, renumbered **B176** вАФ concurrent `main` took B167вАУB175, so this is the real next free ID after B175.)*
`[x]` Toggleable boundary overlays so you can see, on the map, which districts a site sits in вАФ county, city limits, city ETJ, and MUD/water districts. "See which sites are in a MUD around me." No school (per spec). Screening-grade, with a hard "boundary = has jurisdiction, NOT physically served/connected" caveat on every layer.

A `dynamic` image export renders via a CORS-exempt `<img>` even if the probe can't reach the host.

If HARC ever proves unreliable in prod, alternates: City of Houston cohgis MUDs, or `services.twdb.texas.gov` water districts вАФ a one-line URL swap in `JURISDICTIONS.jur_mud`.

### B65 вАФ White flashing on zoom/pan and general redraw `[Site Planner / map]` (bug)
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-19 (branch `claude/nice-heisenberg-r6lmf1`).** Zooming/panning a located site flashed (originally white) as the aerial blanked between redraws. **Root cause, measured not guessed** (headless probe `ui-audit/diagnose-flash.mjs`): the basemap view-lock effect called `map.setView(center, z, {animate:false})` on *every* planner `view` change; Leaflet's `setView`вЖТ`_resetView` fires `viewreset`, whose GridLayer handler `_resetAll` **wipes and reloads all tiles**, so each wheel step blanked the aerial for a frame (loaded tiles collapsed **22 вЖТ 2**), exposing the backdrop.
> **Fix shipped (two parts):**
> 1. **Mitigation (commit `cf26912`):** the basemap container backdrop was `PAL.paper` (`#f4f1ea`, near-white) вЖТ any gap read as a *bright* flash. Changed to a neutral mid-dark gray (`#3f3f3f`) **only while the aerial is on** (stays `PAL.paper` with the aerial off so the SVG-off background still matches). Bright flash вЖТ dim blink.
> 2. **Real fix вАФ seamless transform-based zoom (commit `af10d1c`):** stop re-`setView`-ing on every frame. Hold Leaflet at a committed center/zoom and, for the small deltas of a live gesture, CSS-`transform` (translate+scale) the whole map container so the already-loaded tiles (and the shared FEMA/NWI overlay layers, which live on the same map) scale to track the gesture вАФ no tile reload, no wipe, no flash. A debounced (180 ms) `setView` re-renders crisp once the gesture settles. First paint / resize / >1.5-zoom-level jumps commit immediately so the aerial is never scaled into a blurry mess. Transform math: `scale = getZoomScale(z, committed)`; translate so the desired center maps to the container centre (matches the SVG, which renders at true scale every frame), `transform-origin:0 0`. Container CSS transforms don't affect Leaflet's coordinate math (it uses cached `_size`/pixel-origin, and `clientWidth` is layout-box, unaffected by transform), so alignment is preserved.
> **Tested + rejected on the way:** flipping the map to `zoomAnimation/fadeAnimation:true` made it *worse* (gap frames 1вЖТ4, min loaded still 2) and reintroduces SVG-desync risk вАФ not used.
> **Verified headless:** `diagnose-flash.mjs` now reports **0 gap frames** (min loaded 8, was 2); `ui-audit/verify-zoom-align.mjs` confirms the drawn building/parcel stay locked to the aerial through the transform and after the crisp commit (no jump). lint 0 errors ¬Ј 257 tests ¬Ј build green. **Live confirmation on planyr.io still nice-to-have** (a one-frame flash can't be captured headless), but the mechanism + alignment are proven. **Note:** Document Review's PDF viewer uses a different (canvas raster) renderer, not Leaflet вАФ if zoom-flashing shows there too it's a separate fix, tracked if/when reported.
> **Follow-up 2026-06-19 (same branch) вАФ kill the blank-backdrop reveal during the gesture.** After the flash fix shipped, the owner saw (screenshot) large flat cream patches while panning/zooming a project. Cause: the CSS-transformed basemap container (`geoWrapRef`) slid/scaled and exposed the canvas's `PAL.paper` (`wrapRef`) behind it. Fix (no new dependency): wrap the basemap in a **static clip box** (`inset:0`, `overflow:hidden`, dark `#3f3f3f` bg, never transformed) holding an **oversized inner map div** (`inset:-GEO_OVERSCAN`, `GEO_OVERSCAN = 320` px). The map now overhangs the viewport by 320 px on every side with `keepBuffer` tiles already loaded, so a normal pan/zoom transform reveals **real imagery**; anything beyond the overhang shows the **static dark backdrop**, never the cream page. The transform math is unchanged (it already uses `map.getSize()/2`, which adapts to the larger container, so basemapвЖФSVG alignment is preserved). Verified headless: `ui-audit/pan-reveal.mjs` (a hard mid-pan drag) now shows imagery edge-to-edge with no cream; `verify-zoom-align.mjs` still shows the geometry locked to the aerial through the transform + crisp commit. lint 0 errors ¬Ј 257 tests ¬Ј build green.
> **Follow-up 2 2026-06-19 (same branch) вАФ kill the whole-screen "flash to black" on zoom-out.** Owner: zooming out from a building flashed the entire screen dark, even parts already loaded. Cause: the crisp re-render (`commit`) calls `map.setView`, whose Leaflet `viewreset`вЖТ`_resetAll` **removes ALL tiles and reloads them**, so for one frame the dark backdrop showed everywhere. Fix = **ghost-buffer the commit**: before the `setView`, clone the current basemap container (with its live CSS transform baked in) into a frozen overlay (`geoGhostRef`) pinned on top; the fresh tiles load underneath; on the tile layer's `load` event (or a 1.4 s fallback) the ghost is removed вАФ so the old picture stays visible until the new one is ready and the wipe is never seen. Also dropped the old non-buffered ">1.5 levels вЖТ hard commit" branch; the crisp re-render now fires on settle (160 ms) OR once accumulated zoom drift passes ~0.75 levels, both **ghost-buffered** so a mid-gesture re-base no longer flashes. Verified headless (`ui-audit/zoomout-frames.mjs`, samples a continuous wheel zoom-out and measures the fraction of dark-backdrop pixels per frame): worst-case dark coverage **1.6 %** (UI edges only) вАФ no full-screen black at any frame (was a brief whole-screen wipe). Alignment + crisp settle unchanged (`verify-zoom-align.mjs`). lint 0 errors ¬Ј 257 tests ¬Ј build green.
> **Follow-up 3 2026-06-19 (same branch) вАФ fix the slow gray initial load (regression).** Owner: after the above, a freshly-opened site sat on the gray backdrop for ~10 s before the aerial appeared. Cause: the overscan (2.5√Ч viewport) **√Ч** detectRetina (2√Ч density) вЙИ **4√Ч the tile bytes** on first paint, so on a real connection the detail tiles took ~10 s to cover (the sandbox is too fast to feel it вАФ reproduced with Playwright CDP network throttling at ~1.2 Mbps: time-to-coverage **9.1 s**). Fix = a **coarse "instant" backfill layer**: a second `L.tileLayer` under the detail layer capped at `maxNativeZoom: 13` (a handful of large-area tiles, no detectRetina) that loads near-instantly and blankets the view with blurry imagery, then the heavy detail layer is added **only after the backfill paints** (`bf.once("load", addDetail)` + a 600 ms fallback) so its many retina tiles don't flood the connection and starve the coarse ones. Result (same 1.2 Mbps throttle): time-to-coverage **9.1 s вЖТ ~3 s** (blurry), detail then sharpens on top to the full 45 tiles; on a normal connection the coarse coverage is ~instant. No regression to the interactive fixes (zoom-out flash still 1.6 %, pan still full-imagery). `addDetail` guards against the aerial being toggled off mid-wait. lint 0 errors ¬Ј 257 tests ¬Ј build green. Harness: `ui-audit/initial-load.mjs` (optional `THROTTLE=1`).

This item added the **literal checkbox affordance** the owner asked for (the prior control was a `вЬУ Active / вЧѓ Inactive` chip on the *selected* parcel only; now every row carries a checkbox, and the row + label dim with a "¬Ј inactive" tag) and **closed the merge-candidacy gap**: `toggleMerge` now refuses to add an inactive parcel to the combine set, and `mergeParcels` filters inactive parcels out of the chosen group вАФ so an inactive parcel is excluded from yield **and** from the working merge, matching B100's intent. `SitePlanner.jsx` only; reuses the existing `toggleParcelActive` (pushes history + autosaves). **Self-verified headless (Chromium, logged-out preview):** two-parcel site вЖТ both checkboxes checked вЖТ unchecking parcel A dims its row + canvas polygon and stamps "¬Ј inactive"; the other parcel stays active. 257 tests green, lint 0 errors, build green.

### B173 вАФ App pinned to the viewport; map scale bar always visible `[Site Planner / UI + Shell]` (bug)  *(arrived as "NEW-2"; filed provisionally as B168, renumbered **B173** вАФ #152 + #153 collisions; next free after B171.)*
`[x]` Done 2026-06-19 (branch `claude/optimistic-wozniak-4iltkx`). Root cause: nothing guaranteed the app couldn't grow taller than the window, so the page itself could scroll and push the bottom-of-canvas scale bar below the fold (and the header off the top). Fix is structural, not a scale-bar move: `index.css` now sets `overflow:hidden` on `html, body, #root` and pins them to `100dvh` (dynamic viewport height вАФ handles mobile browser chrome) via `@supports`; `Shell.jsx` adds a defensive `overflow:hidden` on the shell column. The in-canvas measurement-grade scale bar (bottom-right, `lib/sheetFurniture.js`, shared with print/export) sits a fixed 40 px above the canvas bottom, so once the page can't scroll it is **always** visible вАФ no need to fork a second portal-mounted overlay (kept export parity; the owner's "bottom-left fixed overlay" was the suggested mechanism, the real need was "always visible," now met). **Self-verified headless at 1440√Ч900 AND 1280√Ч600:** `document.scrollHeight === innerHeight` (no page overflow) at both sizes, and the scale bar + north arrow render at the canvas bottom with both header rows visible simultaneously.

### B172 вАФ Module tabs read as inactive, not disabled `[global UI / Shell]` (bug)  *(arrived as "NEW-1"; filed provisionally as B167, renumbered **B172** вАФ concurrent `main` took B167/B168 (#152, map items) and B169вАУB171 (#153, basemap-blur trio), so this is the real next free ID after B171.)*

### B170 вАФ Fix retina/HiDPI tile requests so the aerial basemap renders sharp `[Site Planner]` (bug)  *(arrived as "NEW-2"; filed provisionally as B168, renumbered **B170** вАФ concurrent `main` (`claude/brave-galileo-wm8gti`) took B167 + B168 for unrelated map items, so this is the real next free ID; was gated on B169)*
`[x]` Gated on B169 (the diagnostic), which confirmed the dominant blur causes were **(a) HiDPI tiles never requested** and **(b) the planner's fractional zoom** вАФ so the source-swap fix path (B171/NEW-3) was correctly NOT triggered, since the imagery source isn't the problem.
> вЬЕ **Done 2026-06-19** (branch `claude/awesome-darwin-7ui0qm`). Added **`detectRetina: true`** to **both** Esri World Imagery tile layers вАФ the map finder (`MapFinder.jsx`, `L.tileLayer(bm.tiles, вА¶)`) and the planner backdrop (`SitePlanner.jsx`, `GEO_BASEMAP`). On a HiDPI display (`devicePixelRatio > 1`) Leaflet now requests **one-zoom-higher native tiles and renders them at half size** (downsampled = crisp) instead of upscaling 1√Ч tiles (= soft). This also sharpens the planner's *fractional* zoom (`zoomSnap:0`, driven by `ppfToZoom`) because it prefers downsampling a higher-zoom tile over upscaling a lower one. **Kept the Esri source** (per the NEW-2 constraint) and **did NOT touch the planner map's `zoomSnap:0`** вАФ snapping that map to integer zoom would desync the aerial from the feet-space SVG (the deliberate ppfвЖТzoom scale lock); `detectRetina` only changes which tiles are fetched + their display size, never the map's CRS zoom, so the lock is untouched. **Self-verified in a real headless browser** (`gis-verify/retina-basemap-verify.mjs`, simulating `deviceScaleFactor` 1 vs 2 over a Katy parcel): at standard density the map requests **z11** tiles; at retina density it requests **z12** (one level higher = 2√Ч pixel density), with **0 failed/gray tiles** at either density (no coverage regression) вАФ logged **VERIFICATION V43**. lint **0 errors** ¬Ј **257 tests** ¬Ј build green; `SitePlannerApp` lazy chunk intact. (The sharpness gain is invisible at the sandbox's `devicePixelRatio = 1`, so the *visible* improvement is best confirmed on Michael's own retina/4K display вАФ but the higher-density tile request is proven engaged.)

### B169 вАФ Diagnose basemap blur: retina/DPR vs. fractional zoom vs. source resolution `[Site Planner]` (task)  *(arrived as "NEW-1"; filed provisionally as B167, renumbered **B169** вАФ concurrent `main` (`claude/brave-galileo-wm8gti`) took B167 + B168 for unrelated map items, so this is the real next free ID)*
`[x]` Diagnostic only вАФ instrument + report the root cause of soft aerial imagery **before** any provider change (the fix paths are B170 + B171).
> вЬЕ **Done 2026-06-19** (branch `claude/awesome-darwin-7ui0qm`). Root cause established from the two tile-layer call sites (both the **Esri World Imagery** source, `server.arcgisonline.com/.../World_Imagery/MapServer/tile/{z}/{y}/{x}`) plus a live headless instrumentation:
> - **(a) Retina/HiDPI NOT requested вАФ CONFIRMED, primary.** Neither `L.tileLayer` set `detectRetina` (nor any `@2x` / `tileSize:512`): the map finder (`MapFinder.jsx:291`) and the planner backdrop (`SitePlanner.jsx:1043`) both fetched **1√Ч tiles**, which the browser then **upscales** on any `devicePixelRatio > 1` display (most modern laptops / 4K monitors) вЖТ soft. This is the most likely "it looks blurry on my screen" cause.
> - **(b) Fractional zoom вАФ CONFIRMED for the planner backdrop.** The planner map runs **`zoomSnap: 0`** (`SitePlanner.jsx:1031`) and its zoom is driven **continuously** from `ppfToZoom(view.ppf, lat)`, so the raster is almost always displayed at a **fractional** zoom = interpolated = blurred (independent of DPR). The map finder uses Leaflet's default integer zoom, so it's not affected by (b) вАФ only (a).
> - **(c) Genuinely low-res source вАФ RULED OUT as primary.** Esri World Imagery is **native to z19** (`maxNativeZoom: 19`, ~0.3 m/px) with good Houston-metro coverage; both layers merely *display* past native (21/24), so the only "source" softness is upscaling past z19 at very tight zoom вАФ not a stale/low-res source. Verified live (Katy parcel): tiles return **HTTP 200** with no gray/missing tiles at the working zooms.
> - **Live instrumentation:** `gis-verify/retina-basemap-verify.mjs` drove the headless map at `deviceScaleFactor` 1 vs 2 and recorded the **zoom level of every World_Imagery tile actually requested** + load status. Confirmed the pre-fix behavior (1√Ч tiles, no DPR awareness) and gave the before/after baseline for B170.
> **Outcome вЖТ fix routing:** causes (a)+(b) are real and fixable **without** changing the imagery source вЖТ **B170** (add `detectRetina`, keep Esri, don't snap the planner's locked zoom). Cause (c) is not the issue, so **B171** (license-clean high-res source evaluation) stays **gated** вАФ only revisit if B170 proves insufficient by eye on a real retina display. lint 0 errors ¬Ј 257 tests ¬Ј build green (no app-code change in this diagnostic item beyond the verify harness).

`[x]` Done 2026-06-19 (branch `claude/brave-galileo-wm8gti`). ### B166 вАФ Geometry check reads wrong county acreage (homesite carve-out, not total) `[Site Planner]` (bug)  *(arrived as "NEW-3"; minted B166)*
`[x]` **Repro (owner-reported):** parcel `0440110000065` вАФ Appraisal panel + drawn boundary agree (17.00 AC vs 17.06 ac) but the geometry check screamed **"county 0.50 ac vs 17.06 ac (3,312% off)."** The 0.50 ac was the **HOMESITE carve-out** (Legal: "PT TR 4D (HOMESITE)"), not the total tract.
> вЬЕ **Done 2026-06-19** (branch `claude/busy-carson-1zuiuq`). Confirmed root cause against the **live HCAD parcels layer** field list: the record carries **both** `Acreage` (total) **and** `acreage_1` (a sub-acreage) вАФ both match the acres regex, and `countyAcres()` used `keys.find(...)` which returned whichever came first (the homesite ~0.50). Fix in `SitePlanner.jsx` `countyAcres()`: collect **all** acreage-named fields, drop any whose name marks it a sub-acreage (`home_site|homestead|hs_|hmst|exempt|imprv|improv`), and take the **MAX** of what remains вАФ the total tract is always the largest, so a homesite/ag/exemption carve-out can never win. County-agnostic (fixes the statewide carve-out pattern, not just this parcel). Distinct root cause from B75 (that was a m¬≤-vs-acres unit misread; the TxGIO unit handling is untouched). lint 0 errors ¬Ј 257 tests ¬Ј build green.

### B157 вАФ Added-detention area label seats on the NEW ground, not the whole-pond centre `[Site Planner]` (feature)  *(arrived 2026-06-18 in chat вАФ owner: when expanding an existing pond, show the added surface area + acreage at the centre of mass of the NEW area, because the whole-pond centroid often stays inside the existing basin. Refinement of B139/B140; filed provisionally as B151, renumbered **B157** вАФ concurrent `main` took B150вАУB156 (easement tool, multipart-parcel + Delete-key bugs, markup hit-testing), so this is the real next free ID.)*
`[x]` Done 2026-06-18 (branch `claude/brave-noether-rwzkqk`). B140 stacked the "+added" increment as a third line on the pond's single centred label, so on a one-sided (or uniform) expansion the added figure floated over the EXISTING basin вАФ the exact case the owner flagged, where the whole-pond centroid stays inside the old pond. Now the added detention area gets its OWN on-map label, seated on the **thickest part of the new ground**:
- **New `lib/pondGeom.js` (`addedAreaLabelPoint`, unit-tested):** the pole-of-inaccessibility of (expanded footprint вИТ baseline footprint) via a coarse grid + local refine вАФ the interior point of the new area farthest from any edge. Handles a one-sided strip (lands mid-strip), a uniform "push banks out" ring (lands in the band, never the centre), and a corner push; returns null on no-expansion / pure shrink / degenerate ring. Pure world-feet geometry (no React/DOM), so it unit-tests without a browser.
- **Label (`SitePlanner.jsx` element-label builder):** in expansion mode the centred label reads **"Existing Detention Pond"** + the existing area, re-anchored over the **existing basin** (baseline centroid); a second label titled **"Additional Detention"** + `"+X.XX ac ¬Ј +Y sf"` is pushed at the added-region point (owner wording, 2026-06-18). A plain (non-expansion) pond label is unchanged ("Detention Pond" + area). The added area is the **footprint / top-down** area (the metric behind the owner's "20вАУ25 % of the site" pond-coverage rule вАФ NOT water-surface). Both ride B121's existing LOD/collision pool via a per-label id (`<id>` / `<id>#add`) вАФ no parallel renderer. A net shrink / sub-`POND_ADD_MIN_SF` (50 sf) change falls back to the inline "+/вИТ" increment so the delta still shows.
- **Verified (self, headless Chromium, logged-out preview build, 2026-06-18):** seeded a one-sided expansion + a concentric expansion; the existing-area label seats over the old basin and the "+added" label seats over the new ground (one-sided: to the right of the basin; concentric: out on the new ring, 183 px off the centre that sits inside the old pond), correct sf/ac, **zero console/page errors**. Re-verified after the owner wording change вАФ labels read **"Existing Detention Pond"** and **"Additional Detention"** with the +ac/sf in place. lint **0 errors** (14 pre-existing warnings) ¬Ј **257 tests** (6 in `test/pondGeom.test.js`) ¬Ј build green ¬Ј `SitePlannerApp` lazy chunk intact. Browser pass вЖТ **VERIFICATION V42**.
> Refines **B140** (stays Done as the acres+sf label); builds on **B139**'s `det.baseline`. No `SITE_MODEL_VERSION` bump вАФ reads the existing persisted baseline, adds no field.
> **Follow-up 2026-06-21 (branch `claude/brave-noether-rwzkqk`) вАФ two-tone color + per-zone controls.** Owner: "make it so there's a slight color difference between the existing and additional and that I can change the settings for both." In expansion mode the **existing basin** keeps the cartographic water gradient (from **B231**) while the **added ring** paints in a lighter solid tint (`POND_ADD_FILL_DEFAULT #A7D3DD`, a lighter shade of the new teal pond), so the two read apart at a glance. Two color pickers вАФ *Existing basin* / *Added area* вАФ in the Expanding panel write `det.existFill` / `det.addFill` (live, saved with the element, both overridable); a normal (non-expanding) pond is unchanged. ### B154 вАФ Delete key intermittently needs two presses to remove a selected element `[Site Planner]` (bug)  *(arrived as "NEW-1"; filed provisionally as B151, renumbered **B154** вАФ concurrent `main` took B150вАУB153 (easement tool) plus a second B151 (multipart parcel), so this is the real next free ID; the implementing commit references the bug as NEW-1)*
`[x]` Repro: click an element to select it, press Delete вАФ sometimes it deletes on the first press, sometimes it takes two ("works when I was already on the canvas; fails when I came from a panel/button first"). **Root cause (confirmed, but NOT the report's first guess):** the keydown handler is **already** `window`-level вАФ so it isn't a focus-scope problem. The real cause is a **stale closure via passive-effect re-binding:** `onKey` is created inside a `useEffect`, and although `sel`/`multi` are in its deps, the effect re-binds the listener **after** the commit/paint. A Delete pressed in the brief window right after a selecting click runs the *previously* bound `onKey`, which closed over the old `sel` (often `null`) вЖТ the guard `(sel || multi.length)` was false вЖТ no-op, no `preventDefault`; the next press (listener now re-bound) works. Under a heavy render (this is a ~6k-line component) the window widens enough to be hit intermittently.
> вЬЕ **Done 2026-06-18** (branch `claude/gallant-lovelace-82konu`). Added live `selRef`/`multiRef` mirrors (synced during render вАФ a passive effect would lag the same window) and made the **Delete/Backspace branch read the refs**, and `deleteSel` read `selRef.current`/`multiRef.current`, so deletion always acts on the *current* selection no matter which listener instance fired вАФ no second press. The handler stayed `window`-level (no scope change). Also **hardened the existing typing guard** вАФ it already bailed when `document.activeElement` is INPUT/SELECT/TEXTAREA (so Delete never nuked canvas elements while editing a field); extended it to **`contentEditable`** too. The lone same-tick `setSel(x); deleteSel()` caller (the element context-menu Delete) is unaffected вАФ the element is already selected when that menu opens, so the ref holds it. lint **0 errors** ¬Ј **230 tests** ¬Ј build green; `SitePlannerApp` lazy chunk intact. **Self-verified in a real headless browser** (built app): (A) select an element вЖТ one Delete removes it (2вЖТ1); (B) touch a tool/panel button, then select an element, then a **single immediate** Delete still removes exactly one вАФ the reported flow, now first-press reliable; zero console errors. Logged as **VERIFICATION V40**.

### B150 вАФ Easement drawing tool (core): first-class Easement object, input modes, attributes, editing, render, persistence `[Site Planner]` (feature)  *(arrived as "NEW-1"; minted B150 вАФ next free ID after B149)*
`[x]` New first-class **Easement** object on the editable layer (immutable-backdrop model preserved): a `markups[]` entry `kind:"easement"` with a stable UUID and a display label derived from type + width (cosmetic, editable override). **Mode A вАФ Centerline + width:** digitize a polyline centerline, enter total width вЖТ strip generated by offsetting the centerline ¬±width/2 with flat end caps; width is editable after creation and re-offsets the strip live. **Mode B вАФ Boundary polygon:** draw a closed ring directly. Attributes panel (Element tab): type (Utility/PUE, Sanitary Sewer, Storm/Drainage, Water, Pipeline, Access/Ingress-Egress, Aerial/Overhead, Temporary Construction, Other), holder/beneficiary, width (auto-filled in mode A), recording reference, exclusive (y/n), status (existing/proposed), restrictsBuildings (default true), restrictsPaving (default false), notes. Editing: draggable centerline/polygon vertices (пЉЛ add, Shift-click delete), move, delete, relabel; reuses the existing snap system + persistent toggle. Rendering: semi-transparent hatched fill color-coded by type, centerline shown for strip easements, proposed rendered dashed; per-easement area readout + total encumbered area in Yield. Persistence: Supabase, editable layer, private by default, RLS-protected.
> вЬЕ **Done (branch `claude/clever-franklin-7ds6kg`).** **Engine:** inspected the codebase first per the gate вАФ an offset/buffer utility already existed (`bufferPolyline` in `lib/metesAndBounds.js`), so **no JSTS added**. Generalized it to be asymmetric-ready (`{leftW,rightW}`, default still symmetric ¬±w/2) so a future asymmetric-strip UI needs no geometry rework, and factored out a shared one-sided `offsetPolyline` primitive. **Domain logic** in new `lib/easements.js` (`EASEMENT_TYPES`, `easementLabel`, per-mode `deriveEasementRing`, `easementArea`). The **type dropdown uses the shared portal `AnchoredMenu`** so it can't render behind the rail/zoom rail. Easement is a markup вЖТ persists through the existing markups[] save path (Supabase, private, RLS) with no schema change. New rail "Easement" section (mode + default width/type via the portal menu). Self-verified in a headless browser (centerline + boundary draw, attributes panel auto-opens, portal type dropdown swaps type + relabels, vertex grips). **246 tests pass** (16 new in `test/easements.test.js`); lint 0 errors; build green.

### B147 вАФ Markup/shape tools: Bluebeam-style editing (rotate + resize boxes, vertex-edit lines/polylines/polygons) `[Site Planner]` (feature)  *(arrived 2026-06-17 in chat: "fix the rectangle and markup tools вА¶ make them more like bluebeam, not being able to rotate a rectangle is wild"; minted B147 вАФ next free after B146)*
`[x]` The neutral markup shapes (drawn with the Line / Rectangle / Ellipse / Polygon / Polyline tools) could only be **moved, restyled, or deleted** вАФ selecting one just recoloured it, with **no handles**. You couldn't rotate or resize a rectangle/ellipse, or reshape a line/polyline/polygon. Meanwhile elements have resize/rotate grips and measures/parcels have vertex editing, so markups were the odd one out. **Owner's headline: "not being able to rotate a rectangle is wild."**
> вЬЕ **Done 2026-06-17** (branch `claude/gallant-lovelace-82konu`). Added Bluebeam-style geometry editing to the markups[] layer, **reusing the existing element/measure transform machinery** (no parallel system):
> - **Rect / ellipse:** on select (Select tool), 4 corner + 4 edge **resize grips** + a **rotate handle** above the top edge вАФ mirrors the element handles. Resize is computed in the shape's own rotated frame (opposite side stays fixed); rotate spins about the centre, snapping to 15¬∞ when Snap is on, free (whole degrees) when off. The `rot` field already existed on rect/ellipse (rendered via `transform=rotate`), so this is purely the missing UI. New `mkResize`/`mkRotate` drag modes + `startMarkupResize`/`startMarkupRotate`.
> - **Line / polyline / polygon:** draggable **vertex dots**; **пЉЛ** on edge midpoints (polyline/polygon) to insert a point; **Shift-click** a dot to delete one (keeps the kind's minimum вАФ 2 for line/polyline, 3 for polygon). New `mkVertex` drag mode + `startMarkupVertex`/`addMarkupVertex`, mirroring the measure-vertex handlers (B141). Shared helpers `mkPts`/`setMkPts` normalise line `{a,b}` вЖФ point arrays.
> - **Properties panel:** rect/ellipse gain numeric **Width / Height** and **Rotation¬∞** fields (precise entry; kept out of `mkStyle` via a separate `setSelMarkupGeom` so new shapes don't inherit a past size/angle), plus a one-line editing hint per shape.
> - **Scope:** only the 5 neutral annotation kinds get grips; **semantic markups stay move-only** (utilRoute / traced / infwater / encumbrance carry derived geometry вАФ corridor/pad/centerline/calls вАФ that hand-editing would desync). Locked markups show no grips.
> lint **0 errors** ¬Ј **225 tests** ¬Ј build green; `SitePlannerApp` lazy chunk intact. **Self-verified in a real headless browser** (drove the built app): drew a rectangle вЖТ corner+edge grips + rotate handle appear вЖТ dragged a corner (300вЖТ410 px) and the rotate handle (rotate(0)вЖТrotate(53)); drew a 3-point polyline вЖТ 3 vertex grips + 2 пЉЛ handles вЖТ dragged the middle vertex and the path updated; zero errors from the change. Logged as **VERIFICATION V38**.

### B143 вАФ Text box edits like Bluebeam: Enter = newline, click away / Esc to finish `[Site Planner]` (bug) вАФ follow-up to B142
`[x]` Done 2026-06-17 (branch `claude/practical-noether-ln1f46`). Owner: starting a text box then clicking out "won't let me" exit. Two causes, both fixed to match Bluebeam's Text Box markup (researched against the Bluebeam Revu docs вАФ "finish by selecting away or pressing Esc"; a text box is multi-line):
- **Click-out was trapped at ANY distance:** the canvas pointerdown `preventDefault`s the textarea blur, so `onBlur`вЖТ`commitEditCallout` never fired and you stayed in the editor even clicking 400 px away. - **Enter committed (single-line behavior):** Enter now inserts a **newline**; you finish by clicking away or Esc (Esc keeps the text). Placeholder updated to "Type; click away or Esc to finish".
- Empty box is still removed when you click away without typing (matches Bluebeam).
- Verified live (headless): Enter вЖТ "Line1\nLine2" (still editing); click away +80 px вЖТ finishes + commits two lines; Esc вЖТ finishes keeping the text; empty box removed on click-away; zero console errors. lint 0 errors ¬Ј build green ¬Ј tests pass. Browser pass вЖТ **VERIFICATION V33**.

### B132 вАФ Detention pond expansion: lock an existing pond as a baseline, then read the storage gained `[Site Planner]` (feature)
`[x]` Done 2026-06-17 (branch `claude/practical-noether-ln1f46`). Owner workflow: trace an existing on-site detention pond, lock it as the baseline, then enlarge it (drag banks out and/or deepen) to read the **added detention** in acre-feet. Built entirely on the existing pond machinery вАФ no parallel store, no new schema bump.
- **Panel** (`SitePlanner.jsx`, pond branch of the selected-element inspector): the **Detention storage** section gains a **"Lock as existing pond"** button. Locking snapshots the current footprint ring (world feet: `selEl.points` or `elCorners`) **plus its own depth/freeboard/slope** into `el.det.baseline`, so the comparison is frozen and apples-to-apples. Once locked, an **"Expansion vs. existing"** box shows **Existing** / **Proposed** storage and a live **"Storage gained +X.XX ac-ft"** (green) вАФ or **"Storage lost"** (red) when shrunk below baseline вАФ plus the cubic-feet delta. **Clear** removes the baseline (keeps depth/freeboard/slope).
- **Increase = `detentionStorage(proposed) вИТ detentionStorage(baseline)`** вАФ the *same* prismoidal/taper function for both sides, so the delta can't drift from a method mismatch. Reflects both footprint growth and any depth/slope change.
- **Canvas ghost** (`renderElPx`): the locked baseline ring draws as a faint **dashed outline** under the pond so the expansion is visible. Handled for both the irregular-polygon branch (drawn in world feet directly) and the rotated-rectangle branch (a counter-rotated `<g>` undoes the element's `rotate(el.rot)` so the world-feet ghost lands true). `pointerEvents:none` so it never interferes with selection/drag.
- **Persistence:** `baseline` rides inside the already-persisted `el.det` (additive, lossless) вАФ survives save/reload, no `SITE_MODEL_VERSION` bump. Honest framing kept: "screening only вАФ confirm with your civil engineer."
- **Scope (owner-chosen):** "just the increase." Deliberately **excluded** for now (offered, declined): a required-vs-provided "is it enough?" check against added impervious, and a solver ("grow this much to hit a target"). Easy follow-ons if wanted.
- **Verified:** lint 0 errors (14 pre-existing warnings, none in new code) ¬Ј **191 tests pass** ¬Ј build green ¬Ј lazy-chunk split intact (`SitePlannerApp` own chunk). Browser click-through logged as **V25** in `VERIFICATION.md`.

### B122 вАФ Auto-number buildings with contiguous renumber-on-delete `[Site Planner]` (feature)
`[x]` Done 2026-06-16 (branch `claude/determined-brown-bf86l7`). Each standalone building now shows a sequential **"Building N"** label, numbered by placement order and contiguous (1вА¶N) at all times. Deliberately **render-derived, not stored**:
- **New selectors** in `lib/siteModel.js`: `isBuilding(el)` (a `type:"building"` element that is NOT an attached dog-ear/bump-out вАФ those carry `dogEar` + `noLabel`) and `buildingNumbers(els)` вЖТ `Map(id вЖТ N)` assigned in `els` (placement) order. The number is recomputed from list position every render, so **deleting a building renumbers the rest 1вА¶N in one pass** with no stored field to migrate; a lone building is "Building 1".
- **Label** (`SitePlanner.jsx` element-label render): a standalone building's first label line is now `Building ${n}` (was the bare type name "Building"); every other element label is unchanged. Dog-ears/bump-outs are excluded (already `noLabel:true`), so the parent's bump-out tally ("вА¶ (+2 bump-outs)") is untouched.
- **Identity unchanged + safe:** the "stable internal ID, separate from the number" requirement was already met вАФ every element has a persisted, collision-seeded `el.id` (`uid()` + `ensureIdAbove` on load), and every cross-reference (`attachedTo` for parking/trailers/dog-ears) already binds to `el.id`, never a display number. So a renumber can't silently re-point anything. No schema change, no migration, no `SITE_MODEL_VERSION` bump.
- **Tested:** `test/siteModel.test.js` adds a `buildingNumbers` case (contiguous 1вА¶N by placement order, dog-ears excluded, renumber-on-delete, singleвЖТ"Building 1", null-safe). lint 0 errors ¬Ј **139 tests pass** ¬Ј build green ¬Ј lazy-chunk split intact. ### B119 вАФ Parking orientation flipped: first bay must sit against the building `[Site Planner]` (bug)  *(arrived as "NEW-1")*
`[x]` Done 2026-06-16 (branch `claude/youthful-heisenberg-9w64n4`). **Root cause:** `addParkingRowSide` created building-attached parking with `cfg:{ flipDepth:true }`. The strip's inner (local `y=0`) edge sits against the wall, and `flipDepth` mirrors `carStalls`'s layout so the **drive aisle** landed on that inner edge вАФ i.e. the aisle hugged the building and stalls were pushed outward (the inverse of the spec). **Fix (one line):** drop `flipDepth` for building-attached parking. `carStalls` now lays the first stall row at the building edge with the drive aisle outboard, and `growParking` already grows on the away-from-host edge вАФ so the field grows **outward, away from the building**, exactly as specced. The per-field "Drive aisle on the far side" toggle (B59) still flips it by choice; existing saved parking keeps its stored `cfg` (only newly-added side parking changes). Lint 0-errors, 152 tests pass, build green. Browser-confirm logged as **V17** in `VERIFICATION.md`.

### B128 вАФ Split tool: correctly cut concave parcels (general multi-piece straight cut) `[Site Planner]` (bug вЖТ enhancement)  *(minted B127 on-branch; renumbered B128 after `main`'s #85 concurrently took B127 for the rail/header dropdown fix вАФ the implementing commit still says "B127")*
`[x]` Done 2026-06-17 (branch `claude/inspiring-gates-qrhziq`). Closes the QA marathon's last "substantive bug still present" hand-off and supersedes the long-deferred **B31**.
- **The data-corruption fear was already mitigated, and that was verified, not assumed.** The hand-off carried an `[S2/HIGH]` "Split corrupts area on concave parcels вАФ saved silently, no error." That premise was **stale** (written against pre-#48 code): `performSplit` already had a concave-cut **backstop guard** (area-conservation + per-piece self-intersection check, from the B74вАУB92 batch) that *refuses* a bad cut with a warning instead of saving corrupted geometry. Confirmed by replicating the live `splitPolygon` + guard and fuzzing **320k random concave cuts** (combs/L/U/stars) against a Monte-Carlo point-membership oracle: **zero** wrong splits slipped past the guard; every 4/6/8/10/12-crossing cut was rejected. So there was no silent `siteSqft`/FAR/coverage corruption to fix.
- **The real remaining gap was capability, not safety.** Because the old `splitPolygon` only paired the two extreme-`t` crossings, a straight cut that crosses a concave lot **4+ times** (which honestly yields **k+1** pieces for `2k` crossings вАФ e.g. 3 for a U cut across both prongs) could only ever produce 2 overlapping/omitting "halves," so the guard always **refused** it. Net user-visible behavior: "the Split tool won't cut an L/U/notched lot through its reentrant part."
- **Fix вАФ a correct general slice.** Extracted the parcel-split geometry out of `SitePlanner.jsx` into a new pure, tested module **`lib/polygonSplit.js`**: `splitPolygonByLine(points,A,B)` classifies each vertex to a binary side (guarantees an even crossing count вАФ no odd-parity tangency bug), inserts a crossing node on every sign-change edge, **pairs ALL crossings evenвАУodd along the cut line** (each pair is an interior chord), and traces every resulting piece (walk a boundary arc вЖТ hop the interior chord to its partner вЖТ continue), dropping zero-area slivers. Returns the natural set of pieces (`>=2`) or `null`. The bent-polyline cut moved over too as `splitPolygonByPath` (unchanged logic). `performSplit` now replaces the one parcel with **N** parcels and keeps the area/self-intersection guard as a backstop, so the result can never be worse than before (a rare near-vertex-grazing degenerate sliver still self-intersects вЖТ still refused).
- **UX change to note:** a straight cut through a notched lot now creates **all** the real pieces (e.g. 3 parcels for a U-shaped lot), instead of declining. Convex and 2-crossing concave cuts are byte-for-byte the same two pieces as before.
- **Validation:** new `test/polygonSplit.test.js` (11 cases: convex halving, L 2-crossing, **U вЖТ 3 pieces with exact areas + membership**, 3-tooth comb вЖТ 4 pieces, line-misses/degenerate вЖТ null, bent-path cut, and a 1,500-cut randomized area+membership property check). Standalone prototype passed the 300k-trial oracle (0 area / 0 membership failures; ~0.003% near-degenerate self-int вЖТ safely refused). Full suite **163 tests** (was 152, +11) ¬Ј lint **0 errors** ¬Ј build green ¬Ј lazy-chunk split intact. Owner approved shipping; merged to `main` via PR.

### B116 вАФ Measurement tools (Length / Polylength / Area) in Site Planner `[Site Planner]` (feature вЖТ already implemented)  *(arrived as "NEW-1"; committed provisionally as B115 вАФ renumbered B116 after main's #72 took B115 for "revisit keyboard shortcuts")*
`[x]` Done 2026-06-16 (branch `claude/youthful-heisenberg-9w64n4`). **Dedupe outcome: already implemented вАФ this is the "the app already had them" case the PHASE E spec and this very task anticipated.** Site Planner's `measure` tool already ships all three calibration-aware modes; nothing was rebuilt. Evidence in `SitePlanner.jsx`:
- **All three modes present + surfaced:** the **Measure** rail button + `вЦЊ` mode menu (Length / Polylength / Area) вАФ `measureMode` state persisted to `localStorage` (`planarfit:measureMode`); two-click **Length**, running-path **Polylength** (accumulate points), closed-polygon **Area** (click the first dot or double-click to close). Click handling, `finishMeasure`, `selectMeasure`, delete, and the in-progress draft preview all exist and work.
- **Area label already matches the spec exactly:** renders `"<sf> sf ¬Ј <ac> ac ¬Ј <perim>вА≤ perim"` (e.g. `12,300 sf ¬Ј 0.28 ac ¬Ј 462вА≤ perim`) вАФ perimeter closes the loop; Length/Polylength label the running feet.
- **Calibration-aware, as specced:** labels read from `calibrationState`; when an underlay is `uncalibrated` they render **amber (`#b45309`) with a `вЪ†`** and the rail shows the **"Underlay isn't calibrated вАФ distances may be wrong"** banner (same behavior as Document Review / PHASE E). A drawn/georef/calibrated plan labels in the normal accent.
- **Own editable layer; export behavior consistent:** measurements live in their own `measures[]` layer (migrated `{a,b}`вЖТ`{mode,pts}`), persisted in the Site Model. They export alongside callouts/markups вАФ consistent with the existing annotation architecture (the only `data-export="skip"` users are transient chrome: grid, basemap, scale bar, north arrow, zoom/layers UI, draft previews). Reuse note: the Document Review takeoff math (`takeoff.js`) and the Site Planner helpers (`polyArea`/`centroid`/`pathLen`) compute the same geometry вАФ doc-review in page-units√Чcalibration, the planner natively in feet (the shared EPSG:2278 spine) вАФ so no port was needed.
- **Finish UX:** double-click **or Enter** commits (shared `finishActiveDrawing`, per B103); **Esc cancels** the draft. The task floated "Esc to end" вАФ deliberately **not** adopted, since Esc-cancels-the-draft is the universal convention used by every other multi-point tool in the app; double-click/Enter already satisfy "click points вЖТ end".
- **Only change made (label alignment):** the mode display names were **Line / Polyline / Area**; renamed to **Length / Polylength / Area** вАФ Bluebeam's own terms (Planyr is "Bluebeam-style") and the names this task uses, which also **disambiguates the measurement from the markup "Polyline" tool** (`mpolyline`, вЗІN) that shared the word. Label-only via a module-level `MEASURE_MODES`/`measureModeLabel`; the internal `measureMode` values (`line`/`polyline`/`area`) are untouched, so `localStorage` and all logic are unaffected. Lint 0-errors, 138 tests pass, build green. Browser click-through logged as **V12** in `VERIFICATION.md`.

### B114 вАФ Snapping always on; can't be suppressed during a drag `[Site Planner]` (bug)  *(arrived as "NEW-1")*
`[x]` Done 2026-06-16 (branch `claude/epic-dirac-3ljl49`). Dragging an element (e.g. a road) near a neighbour flush-snapped it to that neighbour's edge with no per-move escape, so you couldn't drop it at a deliberate offset (a 15-ft buffer behind trailer parking). Root cause: the existing "Alt-drop to place free" only skipped the *bond* at drop (`onUp`'s `!e.altKey` guard); the element had already been moved to the flush-snapped position during `onMove`, so Alt never placed it freely вАФ and there was no keyboard toggle. Fix:
- **Hold-to-suppress (the standard CAD pattern):** a new `altSnapOffRef`, re-armed from `e.altKey` on every `onBgDown`/`onMove`, makes the live snap = `settings.snap && !altSnapOffRef.current`. `snap()`/`snapPt()` read it (so grid snap, draw, vertex, and placement all honour Alt), and a per-frame `snapOn` gates the inline paths the core helper doesn't cover вАФ the ambient neighbour flush-snap (`edgeSnapCenter`), resize/edge-resize-to-grid, and rotate-to-15¬∞. Holding Alt bypasses ALL of them for that one move and re-enables on release. Shift-drag (deliberate align+bond) is unaffected.
- **Toggle + shortcut + default OFF:** the toolbar button stays, plus a new **S** shortcut and the Site-defaults checkbox toggle snap; "off" fully disables every snap path above. Per owner request snap now **defaults OFF (free movement)** and is a **global drafting preference** (a tool mode), not a per-site attribute: it lives in `localStorage` (`planarfit:snap`, default off) via `loadSnapPref`/`saveSnapPref`/`setSnap`, seeded at the settings `useState` and preserved across JSON import, so the per-site saved `snap` is ignored on load (every existing site started free, regardless of its baked-in `snap:true`). Turning it on persists across sites/reloads until turned off. (`settings.snap` is still the field every read site uses вАФ it just mirrors the pref now.)
- **Visible state:** the toolbar pill now reads `Snap 10вА≤` вЖФ `Snap off` (green/grey dot, `aria-pressed`), the Site-defaults checkbox is relabeled "Snap to grid & neighbours (S)", the Select-tool hint says "hold Alt to bypass snap & place freely вАҐ toggle snap with S", and the shortcuts panel gains `S вЖТ Toggle snap` and `Alt drag вЖТ Bypass snap`. Build green; lazy-chunk split intact. **Browser-verify** logged in VERIFICATION.md.

### B6 вАФ Auto-parking returns wrong dimension after sidewalk resize + delete `[Site Planner]` (bug)
`[x]` Repro: place building вЖТ add 30-ft sidewalk вЖТ parking within sidewalk вЖТ expand sidewalk to 30 ft вЖТ delete parking вЖТ click "add parking" вЖТ tool produced a ~135-ft parking field. Fixed depth is the spec, so the bug is that **something overrides the depth constant with a measured value**. > Done 2026-06-14 (PR #10). `addParkingRowSide` now offsets by the sidewalk's true *thickness* (`swThick`, which resolves the correct axis) instead of a raw `w`/`h` read that could pick up the sidewalk's *run* (~wall length); the row depth stays the fixed `stallDepth + aisle` constant and can't be contaminated by adjacent or just-deleted geometry.

### B7 вАФ Project lifecycle status on map markers `[Site Planner / map]` (feature)
`[x]` Right-click a project marker to set its status. Lifecycle: **Pursuit вЖТ Active вЖТ On Hold вЖТ Complete вЖТ Dead** (see B8 for the full state set and visuals). Core of this item:
- Right-click marker вЖТ menu of states, current one checked. Mirror the same control in the project detail panel if one exists.
- **Status is a real field** on the project record in Supabase вАФ persists across devices, stays private per the existing row-level security (each user sees only their own).
- **New projects default to Pursuit.**
- Companion features: **filter by status** (toggle each state on/off вАФ "hide Complete" and "hide Dead" will be the common ones), a **legend**, and **pipeline counts** (e.g., "4 Pursuit ¬Ј 6 Active ¬Ј 2 On Hold ¬Ј 11 Complete ¬Ј 5 Dead").
> Done 2026-06-14 (this PR вАФ B7вАУB12 batch). `status` added to the Site Model (`SITE_MODEL_VERSION` 2вЖТ3; new sites default to "pursuit"; pre-feature records migrate to "active"), exposed via a `statusOf` selector with ordered `STATUSES` + `STATUS_META`. It persists inside the model `data` вАФ i.e. the `sites.data` jsonb in Supabase, so it syncs across devices and stays private under the existing RLS, with **no DB migration / no dedicated column**. Set a site's status by right-clicking its map marker **or** a saved-sites list row (current state checked); applied to the whole site group. Companion legend + per-state show/hide filters + live pipeline counts live in the saved-sites panel.

### B8 вАФ Lifecycle states & marker visuals `[Site Planner / map]` (feature)
`[x]` The five states and how each marker reads. Use two redundant cues вАФ **color + shape/glyph** вАФ so status stays legible for colorblind users and on a busy basemap:
- **Pursuit** вАФ amber, dashed ring (tentative, uncommitted).
- **Active** вАФ green, solid (the live work; should grab the eye).
- **On Hold** вАФ slate/indigo blue, solid ring, pause "вАЦ" glyph (alive but paused; revivable). Lean slate/indigo rather than sky-blue so it doesn't vanish over blue water on the basemap.
- **Complete** вАФ gray, muted, small check вЬУ (done; recedes).
- **Dead** вАФ hollow gray, dimmest, faint вЬХ, no fill (didn't proceed; kept for the record). **Not red** вАФ red reads as urgent/alert; a dead deal is inert.
- Live (green) should pop; both Complete and Dead recede into the background, with shape/glyph telling them apart.
> Done 2026-06-14 (this PR вАФ B7вАУB12 batch). Markers carry two redundant cues exactly per spec: Pursuit amber/dashed-ring, Active green/solid (pops), On Hold slate-indigo/pause-вАЦ, Complete gray/muted-check-вЬУ (recedes), Dead hollow-gray/faint-вЬХ/no-fill (recedes; not red). Glyph distinguishes Complete from Dead.

This replaces the row of flat tabs.
