Global account control unchanged. Note: the shell bar and the planner context bar remain two physical rows вАФ the dedup + switcher are the substance of B10; a single physical row is a later polish.

### B11 вАФ Remove the county pre-selection gate; click anywhere, auto-resolve the county `[Site Planner / map]` (feature)
`[x]` Today the user must pick a county (e.g., Harris vs. Fort Bend) *before* clicking a parcel. Remove that gate вАФ the user should be able to pan/click **anywhere** and select any parcel without choosing a county first; the unnecessary upfront choice just adds friction.
- Parcel geometry is published per **county appraisal district (CAD)** вАФ the county agency that maintains the parcel map and ownership data (Harris County Appraisal District, Fort Bend Central Appraisal District, etc.). So "click anywhere" means the backend must **resolve which county the clicked point falls in** (point-in-county lookup) and route the parcel query to that county's CAD service automatically.
- Handle the **county-boundary case** gracefully (a click near a line, or a multi-parcel selection that straddles two counties вЖТ query both services and merge results).
- This also removes the county dropdown from the header, feeding **B10**.
> Done 2026-06-14 (this PR вАФ B7вАУB12 batch). County gate removed. The map resolves every configured CAD county's parcel layer up front; a click is auto-routed via `candidateCountiesForPoint` (coarse per-county bbox pre-filter, padded so borders overlap вЖТ a straddle click queries both) + `identifyParcelAcross` (parallel point-identify across candidates, first hit wins, a down county is skipped not fatal, no match fails gracefully вАФ no parcel, no crash). The selected parcel's resolved county rides into the planner hand-off so the saved site still records its county. The county dropdown is gone from the map header. **Interim:** the Layers panel defaults to the Harris/Houston jurisdiction (same as the prior app default) so the Houston utility overlays stay available with no county picked вАФ per-area jurisdiction resolution is a future refinement.

### B66 вАФ Top-left Site Planyr dropdown renders behind the lower header row `[global UI]` (bug)
`[x]` Clicking the top-left module (product) switcher opened its dropdown *behind* the planner's context bar / map header, so it couldn't be used. Root cause: the Shell `<header>` (which holds the dropdown) and `<main>` (which holds the workspace) were siblings, neither establishing a stacking context, so the dropdown menu (`zIndex:50`) competed in the **root** stacking context against the planner context bar (`SitePlanner.jsx`, `zIndex:60`) and the map header (`MapFinder.jsx`, `zIndex:1000`) вАФ and lost.
> Done 2026-06-15 (branch `site-planner/b64-b66-runtime-ui-fixes`). Fixed in `src/app/Shell.jsx`: `<main>` now establishes a stacking-context floor (`position:relative; zIndex:0`), capping ALL workspace content (the context bar's 60, the map header's 1000, in-workspace modals) beneath it, and `<header>` is lifted above it (`position:relative; zIndex:1`). The global switcher dropdown now always paints over the workspace regardless of the lower bars' internal z-indexes; the shell-level AuthPanel (`zIndex:5000`) still sits above everything. More robust than just bumping the menu's number (which would depend on the exact stacking tree). Build passes.

### B68 вАФ Opening a project with saved elements renders a blank screen (`cfgOf is not defined`) `[Site Planner]` (bug) вАФ crash, high
`[x]` Opening a project that has saved layout elements (e.g. **"Schiel Road"**) blanked the whole page; the console showed `ReferenceError: cfgOf is not defined`, thrown inside the `els.map` during render вАФ so empty/new projects (iterating over nothing) didn't crash, which is why only populated projects blanked. **Root cause:** `cfgOf` is a component-scoped helper (`SitePlanner.jsx:2449`, it closes over `settings`), but it was *also* called at `SitePlanner.jsx:5237` inside `renderElPx` вАФ a **module-level** function that receives `settings` as a parameter вАФ where the component-scoped `cfgOf` is not in scope. It shipped because it compiles fine; a build-only CI check can't see an unresolved identifier at runtime. This is exactly the "disjoint-but-interdependent concurrent merge" failure mode called out in **B63**: a parking `cfgOf` call site (added with B29/B59 in PR #22) landed in a scope where the helper isn't visible, and the clean merge + green build hid it. (Arrived from a parallel chat as provisional "NEW-1"; minted **B68** here вАФ B67 is reserved by the in-flight PR #23 вАФ and deduped: no prior blank-screen item existed.)
> Done 2026-06-15 (branch `claude/loving-knuth-6n43df`, pending PR). Three parts. **(1) Fix:** `renderElPx` now resolves `cfgOf` locally from its `settings` param (identical semantics to the component's), so the parking branch no longer references an out-of-scope symbol. **(2) Build-time guard (the real prevention):** added a minimal ESLint flat config whose headline rule is `no-undef`, run as a CI step before the build (`npm run lint`) вАФ verified it flags the exact bug (`5237:38 'cfgOf' is not defined`) on the pre-fix file, so this whole class of dangling reference now fails the build instead of shipping a blank page. **(3) Hardening:** each lazy workspace in `Shell.jsx` is wrapped in a React `ErrorBoundary` (keyed by workspace id), so a future render crash shows a legible "couldn't load this view" fallback (Try again / Reload) instead of unmounting to a blank page вАФ the shell, the switcher, and the other workspace keep working. `lint` / `test` (30 pass) / `build` all green.


## Archived 2026-06-21 вАФ completed items swept from BACKLOG.md рЯФ≤ Open

### B355 вАФ Default new-site-plan name to lettered concepts (Concept A, B, вА¶ AA) `[Site Planner]` (feature)  *(arrived as coworker-chat "NEW-1" + "NEW-2" 2026-06-21 вАФ two near-identical drops of the same request; deduped into ONE item, minted **B355** = next free after B354; implemented + verified same session)*
`[x]` **Fixed + verified (2026-06-21), on branch `claude/hopeful-galileo-0xbh0q`.** New site plans now default to **Concept A, Concept B, вА¶** instead of "Plan 1, Plan 2". **Dedup note:** NEW-1 and NEW-2 are the same feature; NEW-1's "scope: per-site, resets per site" and NEW-2's "within project scope" resolve to the **same thing in this codebase** вАФ a "project" *is* a Site Planner site group, and a plan's letter sequence runs within that group (exactly where the old `Plan N` numbering lived). No conflict, so they fold into one. **Design (all points honored):** (a) **per-site** вАФ every site's first concept is "Concept A"; the sequence resets per site group; (b) **continues past the highest existing letter, never reuses a gap** вАФ if "Concept B" exists but "A" was deleted, the next is "Concept C" (so a name a teammate remembers is never silently re-pointed); (c) **past-Z is spreadsheet-style** вАФ Concept Z вЖТ AA вЖТ AB вЖТ вА¶ (bijective base-26, never crashes at the 27th); (d) **stays user-editable** вАФ this only sets the default; (e) **no retroactive rename** вАФ existing "Plan N" names are left untouched (they don't parse as concepts, so a site that already has "Plan 1" simply gets "Concept A" as its *next* new plan; the legacy-group migration in `storage.js` still writes "Plan 1" for old un-grouped records). **Implementation:** pure, unit-tested `src/workspaces/site-planner/lib/conceptName.js` (`numberToConcept`/`conceptLettersToNumber`/`parseConceptIndex`/`nextConceptName`), wired into the three creation paths in `SitePlannerApp.jsx` (`newSiteFromMap` вЖТ "Concept A"; `newPlanSameParcel` вЖТ `nextConceptForGroup`) + the blank-site first-save default in `SitePlanner.jsx` + the `createSiteModel` fallback in `siteModel.js`. **Verified:** new `test/conceptName.test.js` 14/14 (AвАУZ, AA/AB roll-over, round-trip, gap-not-reused, legacy "Plan N" ignored); full suite 1055/1055; lint 0; build green. Eligible to move to BACKLOG-DONE on merge.

### B353 вАФ B331 pinch regression: the new pinch handlers clobbered Site Planner vertex editing `[Site Planner / Markup]` (bug)  *(found by owner-requested stress test of B331, 2026-06-21; fixed + verified same session)*
`[x]` **Fixed + verified (2026-06-21), on branch `claude/gifted-heisenberg-a6zlvt`.** Stress-testing the just-shipped B331 pinch (#245) surfaced a **real, live regression**: on the Site Planner SVG the pinch handlers were added as a *second* `onPointerDownCapture`/`onPointerMoveCapture` on the same element, and **JSX silently keeps only the last duplicate** вАФ so the pre-existing vertex-edit capture handlers (`onCanvasVtxDownCapture`/`onCanvasVtxMoveCapture`) were dropped. Net effect: **selecting a parcel/polygon vertex, shift-click-insert-vertex, and the insert-on-edge hover hint all stopped working** вАФ on mouse *and* touch. The build was green and the minimal lint gate has no react plugin, so nothing caught it. **Fix:** merge the two capture lines into one prop each (pinch first; the vertex handler runs only when a pinch is NOT engaged, `if (!pinchRef.current)`) вАФ mouse + single-touch editing restored, pinch still wins when it engages. **Hardening (same pass):** a shared `reseedPinch` re-baselines the gesture to whatever fingers remain on every add/remove, and a 3rd+ finger is absorbed instead of starting a competing pan/draw вАФ a partial lift or extra finger can no longer jump or corrupt the zoom. **Permanent guard:** `test/noDuplicateJsxProps.test.js` AST-scans every `.jsx` (via the already-present `@babel/parser`) and fails if any element repeats an attribute вАФ kills this build-invisible clobber class for good. **Verified (V94):** new `ui-audit/verify-pinch-stress.mjs` 15/15 (adversarial multitouch: 30-cycle storms, clamp saturation, coincident fingers/no-NaN, 3-finger + partial lift, interrupt recovery, mouse-path survival) + verify-pinch 5/5 + all viewport/rail/viewer regressions green; 1015 unit tests; lint 0; build green. Eligible to move to BACKLOG-DONE on merge.

### B343 вАФ Site-plan overlay "hide" (eye toggle) reportedly doesn't persist across reload `[Site Planner / Overlay]` (bug) вАФ re-report of the already-shipped overlay hide/show fix  *(owner-reported 2026-06-21 as "NEW-1"; first filed **B329**, renumbered **B343** вАФ a very hot `main` consumed B329вАУB342 (markup viewport/rail, theming, auto-assembly) while this was in flight, so this is the real next free ID after B342)*
`[x]` **Reported:** hide a placed site-plan overlay via the eye toggle in the Site-plan Overlay panel вЖТ reload вЖТ it comes back visible; the hide "isn't saved like opacity/rotation/page/position." **Investigated this session (branch `claude/beautiful-hopper-f7i8sa`) and could NOT reproduce вАФ the hide already persists through every path.** The `visible` flag rides in the `sheetOverlays[]` record and is written by `patchOverlay` вЖТ `setSheetOverlays` вЖТ the autosave effect; normalized losslessly by `createSiteModel` (`arr()` keeps the whole object), content-merged by `mergeSiteContent`/`mergePulledSites` (newer-wins union вАФ never resurrects a visible copy), carried in the cloud row's `data` jsonb (`slimForCloud` only nulls the raster `src`), preserved by the Storage-rehydrate spread (`{...overlay, src}`), and the map render returns `null` for `o.visible === false` **before** the src-null placeholder вАФ so a hidden overlay shows nothing even mid-rehydrate. **This is the fix already shipped + LIVE in `main`** (commit `b66774b`, "overlay delete persistence + visibility toggle" вАФ recorded in BACKLOG-DONE as B276/B277; the on-tree commit numbered it B272/B273 amid heavy B# churn). Most likely the report observed the live site just before/around that deploy.
- **Proven 4 ways, all green this session:** (1) the existing logged-out live-browser harness `ui-audit/verify-overlay-delete-hide.mjs` вАФ hide вЖТ reload вЖТ still hidden, record carries `visible:false`; (2) a NEW logged-out harness `ui-audit/verify-overlay-hide-stripped.mjs` for the **signed-in reload shape** (raster stripped, `src:null` + `storageKey`, `visible:false`) вАФ renders nothing (no image, no "LoadingвА¶" placeholder), persists across reload, Show brings it back; (3) **8 NEW unit tests** (`test/storage.test.js`) locking the previously-untested **signed-in cloud round-trip** of `visible` (save/load, `createSiteModel` normalize, `mergeSiteContent` both directions, `mergePulledSites` local-hidden-wins + cloud-already-hidden + re-push, the rehydrate spread); (4) a static trace of every save/merge/cloud/render path. lint **0 errors** ¬Ј **810 tests** ¬Ј build green; lazy chunks intact.

### B329 вАФ Markup canvas pan + zoom parity with the Site map (one shared viewport engine) `[Doc Review / Markup]` (feature)  *(arrived as coworker-chat "NEW-1" 2026-06-21; filed B313 вЖТ B320 вЖТ renumbered **B329** as a hot `main` twice took the number)*
`[x]` **Merging via PR #238 вЖТ `main` (2026-06-21).** One shared viewport engine (`src/shared/viewport/viewportTransform.js`: `worldToScreen`/`screenToWorld`/`zoomAround`/`panBy`/`fitView`/`shouldPan`) now drives the Site map, the Markup canvas, AND the Stitcher. The Markup viewer was re-architected scroll-box вЖТ transform (`view={scale,tx,ty}`): **free pan in any direction** (the old scroll box couldn't slide past a fit-width sheet вАФ the "only scrolls vertically" repro), cursor-anchored zoom, **Bluebeam pan/tool collision** (middle-mouse always pans; Space-hold pans; Select on empty pans, on an object selects/moves; a drawing tool draws), **view-transform-only** (markups stay page-unit, calibration untouched), and a perf path that rescales the existing bitmap during a zoom and re-rasterises crisply (debounced) on settle. The Site map + Stitcher migrated their pan/zoom math to the same engine, **byte-identical** (unit-tested) вАФ verified unchanged. Trackpad pinch (ctrl+wheel) routes through the wheel path; touchscreen two-finger pinch is **B331** (follow-up).
> **Verified (V84):** 43/43 headless вАФ `verify-markup-viewport.mjs` 13/13 (free pan L/R/down, cursor-anchored zoom 0.1px drift, calibrated measurement reads identical feet through zoom+pan + stays calibrated, middle-mouse pans-without-drawing, draw+select-move, sheet-switch keeps zoom), `verify-siteplanner-viewport.mjs` 6/6 (Site map unchanged), `verify-docreview-viewer.mjs` 13/13 (B288вАУB296 still green) + viewportTransform unit tests. Eligible to move to BACKLOG-DONE on merge.

### B331 вАФ Touchscreen two-finger pinch-zoom on the Markup canvas + the Site map `[Doc Review / Markup + Site Planner]` (feature)  *(owner-requested 2026-06-21 right after B329/B330; minted **B331** вАФ next free after B324)*
`[x]` **Built + verified (2026-06-21), on branch `claude/gifted-heisenberg-a6zlvt` вАФ ready to ship.** One shared pinch helper now drives both canvases: `viewportTransform.js` gains `midpoint`/`distance`/`pinchZoom(v, prevMid, currMid, factor)` вАФ the touch counterpart of `zoomAround` (zoom by the finger-distance ratio about the gesture's previous midpoint, then translate so that anchored point follows the fingers to the new midpoint, so a pinch both zooms AND pans). The Markup canvas (`DocReview.jsx`) wires it bubble-phase (its children are `pointerEvents:none`, so the gesture reaches the host); the Site map (`SitePlanner.jsx`) wires it **capture-phase** + `stopPropagation` (touches land on the SVG `<rect>` children which carry their own handlers, so the pinch must intercept first). Both paths are **gated on `pointerType==='touch'` + exactly 2 active pointers**, so the verified mouse/trackpad/wheel (ctrl+wheel) path is byte-for-byte untouched; **view-transform only** вАФ stored geometry/calibration never move. **Verified (V88):** `verify-pinch.mjs` 5/5 (REAL trusted multitouch via CDP `Input.dispatchTouchEvent` on a `hasTouch` context вАФ Site map spread/pinch 1.25вЖТ4.71вЖТ1.53 px/ft, Markup canvas 603вЖТ2009вЖТ670 px, 0 errors) + all mouse-path regressions green on the same build (`verify-markup-viewport` 13/13, `verify-siteplanner-viewport` 6/6, `verify-markup-rail` 11/11, `verify-docreview-viewer` 13/13, the merged Stitcher set `verify-b335-b339` 13/13); +4 unit tests (850 total); lint 0; build green; lazy chunks intact. Eligible to move to BACKLOG-DONE on merge.

### B326 вАФ "CAD" discipline is misclassified as reference, so CAD drawings can't be placed on the map `[Doc Review / Files]` (bug)  *(arrived as coworker-chat "NEW-1" 2026-06-21; minted **B326** вАФ first filed B321, renumbered as concurrent `main` #239 took B321вАУB324 then #241 took B325)*
`[x]` **Repro:** file a drawing under the **CAD** discipline вЖТ in Project Files it gets the "reference" tag, no "Place on map" button, and it lands in "Reference docs" instead of "On-the-map docs". CAD is the most placeable class of all (it's literally the drawings). **Cause:** `shared/files/fileFacts.js` `SPATIAL_DISCIPLINES` omitted "CAD", so it fell through to the `DOC_CLASS.REFERENCE` default (intentional only for genuinely-ambiguous cases like "Other"). **Fixed this session (branch `claude/modest-turing-wixo1y`):** added "CAD" to `SPATIAL_DISCIPLINES` so it classifies spatial (gets the Place-on-map action + the spatial saved-views); "Other" still defaults to reference. New unit test alongside the existing `classifyDocClass` tests. lint 0 ¬Ј 802 tests ¬Ј build green. Shipping via PR #240 вЖТ `main`.

### B327 вАФ Canvas memory budget isn't enforced at high zoom; a large sheet can allocate ~500 MB and OOM the tab `[Doc Review / Markup]` (bug)  *(arrived as coworker-chat "NEW-2" 2026-06-21; minted **B327** вАФ first filed B322, renumbered past main #239's B321вАУB324 + #241's B325)*
`[x]` **Repro (numerically verified + headless-confirmed):** an E-size sheet (2448√Ч1584 pt) at 600% zoom allocated a ~140 MP / ~533 MB RGBA backing store вАФ far past the "вЙ§ ~24 MP" the code claimed. **Cause:** `lib/pdf.js` `backingScale` floored the density at 1√Ч (`Math.max(1, вА¶)`), which DEFEATED the budget once the CSS area (base√Чscale) alone passed ~24 MP вАФ a 1√Ч backing store was already over budget and kept growing with zoom вЖТ out-of-memory tab crash, not graceful degradation. **Fixed this session (branch `claude/modest-turing-wixo1y`):** extracted the budget math to a pure, unit-testable `lib/renderBudget.js` and let the device-pixel density drop BELOW 1√Ч when needed, so total backing pixels stay вЙ§ ~24 MP at ANY zoom (a slightly soft raster on a huge sheet at 600% beats an OOM crash). The CSS box stays exactly base√Чscale, so the markup overlay + zoom-anchor math are untouched (no geometry change). New `test/renderBudget.test.js` proves вЙ§24 MP holds for scales 0.5вАУ6 √Ч dpr 1вАУ3; headless `ui-audit/verify-b322-b40.mjs` reads a real 6090√Ч3940 = 24.0 MP canvas at the 600% max (V85). Builds on B247/B265. lint 0 ¬Ј 802 tests ¬Ј build green. Shipping via PR #240 вЖТ `main`.

### B328 вАФ Project Files "Filed / On-map" badge can never show "On-map" `[Doc Review / Files]` (bug, minor)  *(arrived as coworker-chat "NEW-3" 2026-06-21; minted **B328** вАФ first filed B323, renumbered past main #239's B321вАУB324 + #241's B325)*
`[x]` **Repro:** every file in the drawer showed "вЧЛ filed", never "вЧП on map", even for a placed spatial drawing. **Cause:** `fileState` returns ON_MAP only when `isSpatial(f) && f.placed`, but the lightweight `listReviews` query never selected `placed` (and nothing wrote it), so `f.placed` was always falsy. **Fixed this session (branch `claude/modest-turing-wixo1y`):** (a) `listReviews` now pulls just the flag out of the data jsonb (`placed:data->placed`, not the heavy payload; falls back to the core columns on any error вЖТ degrades to "filed", never regresses); (b) `toFileFact` parses it whether it arrives as a JSON boolean or text; (c) new `reviewStore.markReviewPlaced(id)` is the write half, called from the drawer's "Place on map" confirm so a placed file flips to On-map on reopen; (d) `fileIndex.mergeFactsIntoReviews` now OR-ins `placed` so a facts-index row without `placement.placed` can't silently un-place a placed review. New tests in `fileFacts.test.js` + `test/fileIndex.test.js`. Note: the full auto-placement backend (B182) is still unbuilt вАФ this makes the badge LIVE for the manual placement flow that exists today; B182 will set the same flag at true completion. lint 0 ¬Ј 802 tests ¬Ј build green. Shipping via PR #240 вЖТ `main`.

### B316 вАФ Hard-block (not just warn) measuring over a not-yet-aligned stitch sheet `[Doc Review / Stitch]` (bug)  *(owner chat 2026-06-20: "don't let it measure on uncalibrated things" вАФ tightens the shipped B301; first filed B303, renumbered **B316** вАФ a hot `main` consumed B303вАУB315)*

### B288 вАФ Single-sheet review can't be zoomed by wheel / pinch / Ctrl-scroll (only the ¬± buttons) `[Doc Review / Markup]` (bug)  *(arrived as "NEW-1" 2026-06-20; minted **B288** вАФ renumbered from B273, consumed by concurrent `main`)*
`[x]` **Repro (confirmed live on planyr.io 2026-06-20):** open a PDF in Document Review (single-sheet, not Stitch) вЖТ wheel / pinch / Ctrl+scroll over the drawing вЖТ nothing (stuck at 31%); the only zoom is the toolbar ¬±. **Expected:** wheel / Ctrl-scroll / pinch zoom the drawing, anchored on the cursor. The fix already exists here вАФ the Stitcher's `onWheel` (`Stitcher.jsx` ~L171) does cursor-anchored zoom; port it to the single-sheet view (`DocReview.jsx`). Primary "can't zoom" complaint.
> вЬЕ Shipped (PR #220 вЖТ `main`). A native non-passive `wheel` listener on the scroll viewport вЖТ `zoomAround(factor, cursorX, cursorY)`: changes `scale`, stashes the page-unit point under the cursor, then a `useLayoutEffect` keyed on the re-rendered `dims` nudges `scrollLeft/Top` so that point stays under the cursor. Ctrl/Cmd+wheel and plain wheel both zoom (trackpad pinch arrives as Ctrl+wheel). Shares the anchor path with B290. Headless-verified (V72).

### B289 вАФ No drag-to-pan in single-sheet review `[Doc Review / Markup]` (feature)  *(arrived as "NEW-2" 2026-06-20; minted **B289** вАФ renumbered from B274)*
`[x]` Zoomed in, there's no way to grab-and-drag the drawing to move around вАФ no hand tool, no space-drag вАФ so navigation relies entirely on the scrollbars. (Scrollbars do work and reach the whole sheet, so this is a usability gap, not a blocker.) **Expected:** drag-to-pan (a Pan/hand tool and/or hold-Space to pan), matching the Stitcher, which already pans via pointer-drag (`Stitcher.jsx` ~L158/L168).
> вЬЕ Shipped (PR #220 вЖТ `main`). New **Pan** tool (hand) + **hold-Space** in any tool; pointer-drag adjusts the scroller's `scrollLeft/Top` by the negative pointer delta (pointer-capture so a fast drag doesn't drop). Cursor shows grab/grabbing. Releases capture + clears state on pointerup/pointercancel (so it can't reproduce B271's frozen-cursor lockout). Headless-verified (V72).

### B290 вАФ ¬± zoom isn't cursor-anchored `[Doc Review / Markup]` (bug, minor)  *(arrived as "NEW-3" 2026-06-20; minted **B290** вАФ renumbered from B275)*
`[x]` `zoom()` only changes `scale`; it doesn't hold a focal point, so the detail you were looking at drifts and you re-scroll after each step. **Expected:** zoom toward the cursor (or hold the viewport center fixed), like the Stitcher's cursor-anchored wheel zoom. Pairs with B288.
> вЬЕ Shipped (PR #220 вЖТ `main`). The ¬± buttons now call `zoomAround(factor)` with the viewport centre as the anchor (same scroll-anchor path as B288), so the centre of what you're looking at stays put across a zoom step. Headless-verified centre drift 0.6px (V72).

### B291 вАФ Double-click to finish a Count/Area/Perimeter adds 1вАУ2 phantom points (inflates counts, distorts areas) `[Doc Review / Markup]` (bug) вАФ takeoff correctness, HIGH  *(arrived as "NEW-4" 2026-06-20; minted **B291** вАФ renumbered from B276)*
`[x]` **Repro:** pick Count, click N items, then double-click to finish (as the tool hint instructs) вЖТ the count reads N+2 with two stray dots at the double-click spot; same root cause distorts Area/Perimeter (extra/duplicate vertices at the closing click). Cause: each pointerdown appends a point (`DocReview.jsx` onDown), and a double-click fires TWO pointerdowns before `onDoubleClick`вЖТ`finishDraft` commits. Enter finishes cleanly; only the advertised double-click path is broken. **Expected:** double-click finishes without adding the doubled vertices. The Site Planner already solved this with a shared `finishActiveDrawing()` + `removeLastVertex()` вАФ reuse that approach.
> вЬЕ Shipped (PR #220 вЖТ `main`). `onDbl(e)` strips any trailing draft points coincident (вЙ§ ~6px screen) with the double-click location before committing the poly/count, so the two pointerdowns the browser fires for a double-click can't survive as phantom vertices. Enter path unchanged. Headless-verified: 3 clicks + double-click вЖТ exactly 3 count dots, not 5 (V72).

### B292 вАФ Zoom level resets to fit-width every time you switch sheets `[Doc Review / Markup]` (bug, minor)  *(arrived as "NEW-5" 2026-06-20; minted **B292** вАФ renumbered from B277)*
`[x]` **Repro (confirmed live 2026-06-20):** zoom Sheet 1 to 134%, click Sheet 2 вЖТ it snaps back to 31% (fit-width); zoom is lost on every sheet change. Cause: the sheet button calls `setScale(0)`. **Expected:** keep the current zoom across sheet switches when reviewing a set.
> вЬЕ Shipped (PR #220 вЖТ `main`). The sheet button no longer forces `setScale(0)`; switching sheets re-renders the new page at the current scale. The fit pass still runs on first open and on the explicit Fit / Fit-page buttons. (Merged cleanly with main's B267 per-sheet scale tooltip on the same button.) Headless-verified (V72).

### B293 вАФ Can't move or edit a markup after placing it (Select only allows delete) `[Doc Review / Markup]` (feature)  *(arrived as "NEW-6" 2026-06-20; minted **B293** вАФ renumbered from B278)*
`[x]` Today Select supports delete only вАФ a misplaced redline/measurement/text note has to be deleted and redrawn, and placed text can't be re-edited. Key design points: drag a selected markup to reposition it (commit once on pointer-up, coords stay in page units); double-click a text note to edit it. The ParcelDrawing surface already implements move + edit-text (B67) вАФ mirror it here.
> вЬЕ Shipped (PR #220 вЖТ `main`). Select-mode interior drag translates a markup's page-unit points live and commits once on pointer-up (a sub-3px drag is still a plain click-select; interior drag moves, never pans вАФ per B155's locked rule). Double-click a text note opens an **inline `<input>` overlay** at the note (Enter/blur commit, Esc cancel); text **creation** routes through the same inline editor (opening on pointer-UP so the click's own focus change can't blur+discard it), removing Doc Review's `window.prompt` for text (KEY DECISION "no dialog-box edits" + the B155 note). Calibrate's prompt is left as-is (tracked under B155). Adjacent to B155 + B156, which stay open. Headless-verified move + create + edit (V72).

### B294 вАФ Dropping a PDF only works on the empty screen, not once a document is open `[Doc Review / Markup]` (bug, minor)  *(arrived as "NEW-7" 2026-06-20; minted **B294** вАФ renumbered from B279)*

The drop handler is bound only to the empty-state view; the Stitcher accepts drops anywhere. **Expected:** dropping a PDF over the open document opens it (reuse the existing re-drop/source-binding path).
> вЬЕ Shipped (PR #220 вЖТ `main`). The canvas/viewport now carries the same `onDragOver`/`onDrop` as the empty state, routed through the existing `openFile` (which already re-binds a re-dropped source by name so its markups stay attached). (Verified by code + the proven openFile path; a synthetic file-drop isn't in the headless harness.)

### B295 вАФ "Fit" only fits width; tall/portrait sheets can't be viewed whole `[Doc Review / Markup]` (feature, minor)  *(arrived as "NEW-8" 2026-06-20; minted **B295** вАФ renumbered from B280)*
`[x]` The fit logic computes width-only (`avail / base.width`), so a portrait/tall sheet overflows vertically and can't be seen in one view. Add a fit-to-page option (min of width-fit and height-fit) alongside fit-width.
> вЬЕ Shipped (PR #220 вЖТ `main`). New **Fit page** button next to **Fit**; the fit pass reads a `fitMode` ('width' | 'page') and uses `min(availW/baseW, availH/baseH)` for page-fit. Headless-verified Fit-page fits the whole sheet where Fit-width overflows (V72).

### B296 вАФ Linear measurements round to whole feet, inconsistent with area's 2-decimal acres `[Doc Review / Markup]` (bug, minor)  *(arrived as "NEW-9" 2026-06-20; minted **B296** вАФ renumbered from B281)*

> вЬЕ Shipped (PR #220 вЖТ `main`). `measureLabel` now formats distance/perimeter with one decimal (`f1`); area (acres 2-dp / sf whole) unchanged. Covered by a unit test (`test/takeoff.test.js`).

### B206 вАФ Storage-adapter discipline: confine all backend-specific logic to one module `[Server]` (task)  *(arrived as "NEW-1"; provisionally B203, renumbered **B206** вАФ `main` took B203вАУB205)*
`[x]` Shipped 2026-06-19 (branch `claude/laughing-ritchie-k5narx`). A **single storage-adapter module is the only thing the app talks to for file ops** (save / fetch / list / move / rename / delete / share-link). The app references files **only by Planyr's own stable keys** вАФ never a Google Drive file id, Drive folder path, or Drive sharing handle. The adapter's internal **mapping table is the only place Planyr-key вЖФ backend-id translation exists**; no backend id leaks past it. **NEW-2/3/4 all sit behind this.**
- **What shipped:** `server/storage/adapter.js` (the only entry point вАФ save/fetch/list/move/rename/remove/shareLink, all returning result objects, never throwing), `idMap.js` (the sole Planyr-keyвЖФbackend-id translator; in-memory store now, Supabase-Postgres-backed later), `result.js` (the `{ok}` result + `attempt()` wrapper), and `index.js` (server-side assembly вАФ the one place creds are read). **20 unit tests** (`test/storageAdapter.test.js`) incl. the **acceptance test**: an "app consumer" written only against the adapter behaves identically across two different backends, and a list never exposes a backend id (an unbound backend object is invisible to the app).
> **Dedup:** the adapter is the **bytes** layer; the **index of file facts** (B180's `fileFacts` view-model + the `doc_reviews` table) is the separate catalog layer that records *which* file is *what* вАФ they meet only at the Planyr key. Existing direct Supabase-Storage calls (`reviewStore.uploadSource/downloadSource`, `overlayStorage.js`) are the **adoption targets**: route them through the adapter when the Drive backend goes live (so the swap is verified end-to-end with real creds), not as risky blind surgery now.

### B208 вАФ Share-by-link via a link-provider abstraction (Drive links now, Planyr links later) `[Server]` (feature)  *(arrived as "NEW-3"; provisionally B205, renumbered **B208** вАФ `main` took B203вАУB205)*
`[x]` Shipped 2026-06-19. Sharing emits a link from a **single link-provider interface** (`server/storage/linkProvider.js`). For now it returns the backend's **native Drive share link** (recipients see a familiar Google Drive link вАФ intentional, keeps the owner's company comfortable). **ALL link generation routes through this one interface**, so switching later to Planyr-native signed links (`planyr.io/s/<token>` вЖТ backend mints a temporary signed URL, serves bytes through the adapter) is a **one-place change** (`kind: "planyr"` + a `signer`). No Drive link call is hardcoded in UI/app code. **Tested** both kinds (Drive-native via the backend; Planyr signed via an injected signer; not-configured fails visibly).
> **Non-goal (deferred):** drag-a-file-out-of-the-browser-into-an-email вАФ a desktop sync-client gesture; the owner uses Drive directly for that for now.

### B209 вАФ File operations must surface success/failure; no silent file failures `[Server]` (task)  *(arrived as "NEW-4"; provisionally B206, renumbered **B209** вАФ `main` took B203вАУB205)*
`[x]` Shipped 2026-06-19. Every adapter op (upload, fetch, move, rename, delete, link-generation) returns a **visible success/failure result** (`server/storage/result.js`): the adapter **never throws** and **never reports a half-finished op as success** вАФ a throwing backend, a backend `{ok:false}`, or an unmapped key all surface as `{ ok:false, error }`. **Same severity class as the silent cloud-save failures that caused prior data loss.** Covered by the no-silent-failure tests in `test/storageAdapter.test.js`.
> **Dedup / align:** this **extends** the existing save-status-visibility guarantee (B125 вАФ make cloud save status visible, no silent failures) to **Drive file operations**; it is the storage-layer contract, surfaced in the UI through the same honest-status pattern the persistence layer already uses (don't build a parallel status system вАФ when the adapter is adopted, its `{ok:false}` feeds the existing save badge / banners).

### B162 вАФ Suppress street labels at low map zoom `[Site Planner / map]` (feature)
`[x]` Street labels should be hidden below zoom 14 and visible at zoom 14+. The basemap uses a separate Esri Reference/World_Transportation raster overlay (`LABELS_TILES`) вАФ Case B from the spec. Implementation: zoom-driven `layer.setOpacity()` on `zoomend`, initial opacity set from live map zoom when the layer is created.
> Done 2026-06-18 (branch `claude/charming-fermat-f9ktvp`). Added zoom-driven `useEffect` (`[zoom]` dep) that calls `layer.setOpacity(zoom >= 14 ? 0.4 : 0)` on the `labelsRef.current` tile layer. Initial opacity in the labels `useEffect` reads `map.getZoom()` directly (not the React state) to avoid a one-frame flash. Browser-verified: labels layer opacity transitions from `0` (zoom 11) вЖТ `0.4` (after 8√Ч zoom-in) вЖТ `0` (after 8√Ч zoom-out) correctly.

### B151 вАФ Multipart parcel: clicking the smaller tract selects the wrong piece (only the largest part highlights/imports) `[Site Planner / map]` (bug) вАФ relative of B36c  *(owner-reported 2026-06-18, "Pearland"; minted B151 вАФ `main` concurrently took B147вАУB150, so this is the real next free ID)*
`[x]` Repro (owner): Pearland, account **`0440520000010`** ("TRS 3 & 5 (AG-USE)", 15.5 AC, situs "0 DEL PAPA"). Clicking the **meat** of the parcel registers the account (selection count ticks up) but the clicked piece **does not highlight** вАФ instead the **adjacent piece to the right** lights up. Owner clarification: *"I didn't click on a county line вАФ it just won't let me click the parcel in the meat of the parcel."*
> **Root cause (confirmed by live endpoint probes AND a live headless-browser repro, not assumption).** `0440520000010` is a **HARRIS** parcel (HCAD + the statewide TxGIO layer agree; identical geometry), but it is **MULTIPART** вАФ two physically separate tracts under one account: a **west tract ~6.66 AC** and an **east tract ~8.12 AC**, with a *different* parcel (`0440520000002`) between them. The geometry helpers in `arcgis.js` (`largestRingLngLat`/`featureToParcel`) deliberately returned only the **single largest ring** (the B36c "biggest |area| ring can't be a hole" pick). So a click anywhere in the parcel resolves the right account, but the highlight (`MapFinder` `handleClick`) and the planner import only ever drew/added the **east (largest) tract** вЖТ clicking the **west** tract appeared to select the neighbour, and planning the site silently **dropped ~6.66 AC** (card showed 8.12 AC, not ~15). Disproves the pasted brief's guesses: the parcel is Harris (not Brazoria/"missing county"); click coords round-trip exactly in EPSG:4326 (no SR bug вАФ verified the geometry the app sends matches the click latlng); IDs are present and the highlight is drawn from geometry, not the ID field; the query is a true `esriSpatialRelIntersects` point-in-polygon (no nearest/buffer). The seam *does* exist (the parcel's south edge is the diagonal Harris/Brazoria line; a click just over it selects a Brazoria parcel that lives only in the statewide TxGIO layer) but that was **not** the owner's symptom вАФ multipart was.
> **Fix (minimal + shared; branch `claude/nifty-bohr-mtz70c`).** New `outerRingsLngLat(feature)` in `lib/arcgis.js` returns **every outer-boundary ring** of a (possibly multipart) feature, classifying outers vs. holes by winding **sign** (so a separate small tract is kept even when a hole's |area| exceeds it вАФ the B36c size trap), holes dropped, each ring opened. Wired into **all three** parcel-import paths so it's fixed everywhere, not per-symptom: (1) **map-click select** (`MapFinder.handleClick`) now highlights all parts via Leaflet **multipolygon** nesting (`[[part],[part]]`, not a hole-punch) and stores `rings`/`latlngsList`; `computeAssembly` emits **one planner parcel per part** in the shared frame (full acreage) and the cursor hit-test checks every part; (2) **in-planner identify вЖТ Add to plan** (`SitePlanner.addIdentifiedParcel`) adds every part (`ring` = largest is still kept for the jurisdiction/road straddle tests); (3) **in-planner address/account lookup вЖТ import** (`importFeature`) imports every part on one **shared** anchor so the tracts keep their true relative position. 5 new unit tests (`test/arcgis.test.js`: single ring; both tracts of a 2-part; donut drops the hole; small separate part kept despite a bigger hole; empty вЖТ []). lint **0 errors** ¬Ј **230 tests** ¬Ј build green; `SitePlannerApp` lazy chunk intact.
> **Browser-verified (Claude self-test, logged-out, served from the local `dist/` build).** Clicking the **west tract** now highlights **BOTH** pieces (highlight path = 2 subpaths spanning the full **1326√Ч664 ft** parcel) and the card reads **"1 PARCEL ¬Ј 14.78 AC ¬Ј DEL PAPA"** (was 8.12 AC, east-only) вАФ `gis-verify/pearland-FIXED-clickwest.png` (before: `gis-verify/pearland-mp-clickwest.png`; script `gis-verify/pearland-fix-verify.mjs`). Logged as **VERIFICATION V39**; no owner action.

### B146 вАФ Interactive, decluttered dimension callouts (move + edit) + road-dimension fixes `[Site Planner / UI]` (feature)  *(arrived 2026-06-17; minted B146 вАФ concurrent merges took B141вАУB145, so this is the real next free ID)*
`[x]` вЬЕ Both increments DONE + browser-verified 2026-06-17. Owner ask (2026-06-17): the red edge-dimension callouts overlap the centred name/area labels (see the B121 screenshots вАФ the red "271" prints over "116,327 sf"). They should (1) **auto-move so they don't clutter in the first place**, and (2) be **directly adjustable** вАФ click an element to select it, then click its dimension to grab it: **drag the dimension line to reposition it**, and (for roads) **click the dimension number to edit the width**. Apply the move interaction to **buildings, parking, and roads**. Plus two road fixes: the dimension must **track a resize** (it went stale), and roads should **resize in 1вА≤ increments**.
> **Increment 1 вАФ road-dimension fixes вАФ вЬЕ DONE 2026-06-17 (branch `claude/determined-brown-bf86l7`), browser-verified.** (D) The road dimension callout (and the Element-panel "Travel width" field) now **derive from live geometry** via `roadTravelWidth(w,h,curb)` in `lib/siteModel.js` (unit-tested), replacing the frozen `el.travelW` that went stale after a resize вАФ the resize handlers update w/h, so the callout now tracks. (E) Road resize (corner + edge handles) snaps to **1вА≤ increments** (not the grid step), so a width dials to the exact foot. Self-verified headless: drew a road (dim **170вА≤**), dragged a corner to widen it вЖТ dim updated live to **428вА≤** (it would have stayed frozen before) вАФ logged **V35**. lint 0 ¬Ј 205 tests ¬Ј build green.
> **Increment 2 вАФ the interactive layer вАФ вЬЕ DONE 2026-06-17 (branch `claude/determined-brown-bf86l7`), browser-verified** (owner chose "Full interactive"). (A) **Auto-declutter:** the dimension number now sits OUTBOARD of its line (away from the centred label), so it no longer overprints the sq-ft by default. (B) **Drag-to-move:** when an element is selected its dimension is a grab handle (a fat invisible hit-line along the dim) вАФ drag it anywhere; the offset is stored per element as `el.dimOffset` (local feet, persisted) and a dashed **leader** points back to what it measures. Works for buildings, parking, and roads. (C) **Roads вАФ click the number to edit the width:** clicking the dimension number opens an **inline on-canvas editor** seeded with the current travel width вЖТ `setRoadTravel`, resizing the road (the line still drags to reposition). Implementation: a `dimMove` drag mode + `startDimMove`/`editDimWidth` in `SitePlanner.jsx`, threaded into `renderElPx`; `dimOffset` rides through the Site Model additively (no migration). **No dialog boxes (owner rule, 2026-06-17 вАФ "horrible UI"):** the width editor is a shared inline `numEdit` `<input>` overlay (commit on Enter / click-away, cancel on Esc), and the pre-existing per-edge **setback** and overlay **trace-length** `window.prompt`s were converted to that same inline editor; rule recorded in CLAUDE.md KEY DECISIONS. Self-verified headless: dragged a building's "314вА≤" out with a dashed leader; clicked a road's "199вА≤" вЖТ **inline box on the canvas (no dialog)** вЖТ entered 30 вЖТ road resized to a **30вА≤** travel width вАФ logged **V36 / V37**. lint 0 ¬Ј 225 tests ¬Ј build green.

### B137 вАФ Fort Bend parcels render but aren't clickable (display covers more counties than the click queries) `[Site Planner / map]` (bug) вАФ coupled to B11/B13/B36  *(filed as "B130" in the brief; minted B137 вАФ `main` concurrently took B130вАУB136, so this is the real next free ID)*
`[x]` Repro: Map view вЖТ "вЬУ Selecting вАФ click lots" вЖТ pan to a Fort Bend area (purple parcel outlines visible) вЖТ click directly on a lot вЖТ nothing selects; "No parcel right there вАФ zoom in and click directly on a lot" fires. Harris parcels select fine at the same zoom. Expected: clicking any displayed parcel selects it, regardless of county.
> **Root cause (confirmed by live endpoint probes, not assumption).** The visible outlines and the click-query had different *coverage*. The `chambers` entry in `COUNTIES_MAP` is actually the **statewide TxGIO** parcel layer (one service covering all 254 Texas counties); its display layer (`makeParcelLayer`) has no county filter, so when zoomed in it **paints parcel outlines everywhere вАФ including Fort Bend.** But on click, `candidateCountiesForPoint` only made TxGIO a query candidate inside the narrow *Chambers* bbox. A Fort Bend click therefore queried only **Harris** (returns nothing вАФ verified 0 features at a Sugar Land point) and **FBCAD** вАФ and FBCAD's host (`gis.fbcad.org/serverarcgis2`) is currently **down (HTTP 503 on every path, even the host root; Harris/TxGIO/Esri all return 200 from the same network)**. So the click had no answerer and fell through to the "no parcel" message, even though the TxGIO layer that drew the outline *does* return that exact Fort Bend lot on a point query (verified: `county:'FORT BEND', prop_id 40594`). This is precisely the brief's hypothesis #1 вАФ display covers more than the queried source. (The brief's other guesses вАФ separate selection service, missed reprojection, click tolerance вАФ were ruled out: display and click share the same resolved per-county URL, `queryAtPoint` already sets `inSR:4326`, and Harris selects fine via the identical code path.)
> **Fix (minimal + structural; branch `claude/magical-ramanujan-v1dnuw`).** Marked the TxGIO source `statewide:true` in `COUNTIES_MAP` and made `candidateCountiesForPoint` (`lib/counties.js`) **always append any statewide source as a universal fallback** вАФ so the click can always select an outline it can see. Appended **LAST**, so a county's own CAD still answers first when reachable (more authoritative, richer fields) and the statewide layer only catches clicks the county CAD didn't; the answering county is then corrected to its true CAD key by the existing **B36(a)** `countyAtPoint` relabel (already keyed on a `chambers`-sourced hit, so no extra wiring). This also makes Fort Bend selection **resilient to FBCAD being down** (TxGIO covers it) and keeps `viewCounty`/Layers-panel jurisdiction unchanged (bbox matches still lead). No change needed in `MapFinder` beyond what already existed. 5 new unit tests in `test/counties.test.js` (Fort Bend routes to fortbend + statewide fallback; fallback ordered last; no dup when in-bbox; Harris still leads; out-of-bbox still gets statewide). lint 0 errors ¬Ј **180 tests** ¬Ј build green; lazy chunk split intact.
> **Coupled to B11/B13/B36:** same county-resolution theme. Does NOT close B13-pt1 (true point-in-county polygons vs. the bbox pre-filter) вАФ that's still the deferred, more-accurate routing; this is the resilience/coverage fix that makes "click anywhere selects the parcel you see" hold today. Browser confirmation (real click on a Fort Bend lot) logged as **VERIFICATION V29**; no owner action.

If our app's `<img>` export gets 403'd cross-origin from planyr.io, wetlands STILL won't draw. Public ArcGIS export endpoints usually allow cross-site, so it's *probably* fine вАФ but confirm by eye. (CORS specifically doesn't block the picture: if `fwsprimary` sends no `Access-Control-Allow-Origin`, the esri metadata fetch fails but the image still loads via the CORS-exempt `<img>` вАФ PR #60 resilience вАФ so it should render anyway.)

Like FEMA, NWI may be source-scale-gated, so zoom in.

Wetlands is render-only (no click-identify anywhere), so losing the vector layer's queryable attributes costs nothing today. **Verified in a real headless browser** (esri-leaflet `imageMapLayer` over Sheldon Lake, `gis-verify/wetlands-verify.{html,mjs}`): the `exportImage` request returns **HTTP 200 `image/png`**, the service metadata fetch returns **200 JSON**, and the standard NWI symbology (navy open water = Sheldon Lake, greens = vegetated wetlands) **paints** вАФ screenshot `gis-verify/wetlands-fwsprimary-verified.png`. **B130's flagged cross-site-403 risk is DISPROVEN:** the host **reflects any `Origin`** in `Access-Control-Allow-Origin` (confirmed for `https://planyr.io`, localhost, and an arbitrary origin), so esri-leaflet's `useCors:true` image loads cross-site with no refusal; the earlier out-of-band 403 did not reproduce. lint **0 errors** ¬Ј **197 tests** ¬Ј build green (count after merging the latest `main` in; the change adds no tests вАФ a GIS source swap is verified in-browser, like B129/FEMA) ¬Ј `SitePlannerApp` lazy chunk intact. If `fwsprimary` ever 403s/500s, the honest "service unavailable" path (B129) still applies and the durable fix remains a `/server` proxy through our own origin. **Shipped to `main` via PR #101.** **вЪ†пЄП Correction (see B135):** that raster turned out to be a **100 m-per-pixel** source, so wetlands rendered as coarse **BLOCKS**, not true shapes вАФ B135 switches to the crisp **vector** `Test/Wetlands_gdb_split` MapServer (`layers:[1,2]`), which is the Wetlands-Mapper look.
> **Follow-up (deferred, low priority вАФ captured so it's not lost):** the **unused** future GIS-caching engine `lib/vectorLayers.js` (imported nowhere in the app yet; built for the Track-1 "GIS layer caching" roadmap item) still references the dead `fwspublicservices` host for both its vector `/query` and its `imageFallback`. There is **no drop-in vector replacement on `fwsprimary`** (its `Wetlands/MapServer/0/query` 500s and it exposes no FeatureServer вАФ only the raster renders), so when that engine is eventually wired up, NWI there must either use the raster (no per-polygon `WETLAND_TYPE`) or wait for the `fwspublicservices` vector host to recover. Left as-is for now since it's not live and can't be browser-verified.

### B135 вАФ Wetlands draw as coarse 100 m blocks (raster), not true polygons вАФ switch to the crisp vector MapServer `[Site Planner / GIS]` (bug) вАФ follow-up to B133
`[x]` **Owner-spotted (2026-06-17).** After B133 turned NWI wetlands back on, they painted as chunky ~100 m green/blue **blocks** instead of the true wetland shapes the official USFWS Wetlands Mapper draws. Cause: B133 pointed at `fwsprimary`'s `Wetlands_Raster/ImageServer`, which is a **100-m-per-pixel raster** (`pixelSizeX/Y = 100`) вАФ inherently blocky at any zoom, and carrying no Cowardin class labels.
> вЬЕ **Done 2026-06-17** (branch `claude/fervent-albattani-yyp0qe`). Found and switched to the real **crisp vector** source. Investigation: `fwsprimary`'s production `Wetlands/MapServer` is an empty dynamic shell (export + query both 500); the polygons the Mapper draws live in the **staging** service `вА¶/server/rest/services/Test/Wetlands_gdb_split/MapServer`, where layer 0 ("Wetlands") is empty and the data is split into **layer 1 = Wetlands_CONUS_East** and **layer 2 = Wetlands_CONUS_West** (Texas is in West). **Fix:** `STATEWIDE.wetlands` is now a **`kind:"dynamic"`** esri `dynamicMapLayer` (esri `/export f=image`, like FEMA) at that MapServer with **`layers:[1,2]`** (covers the lower-48). **Verified in a real headless browser** (`gis-verify/wetlands-verify.{html,mjs}`, now the vector variant): the `вА¶/export?вА¶layers=show:1,2&f=image` request returns **HTTP 200 `image/png`** with **true-shape polygons + NWI class labels** (PFO1A / PSS1A / PUBHвА¶) over Sheldon Lake вАФ screenshot `gis-verify/wetlands-fwsprimary-vector-verified.png` вАФ and the host is **CORS-clean** (echoes `Access-Control-Allow-Origin: https://planyr.io`). Source-scale-gated (layer `minScale ~1:250k`) вАФ like FEMA, zoom to about city level to see polygons. **CAVEAT (also in the code comment):** `Test/` is a USFWS **staging** path during their host migration; it may be renamed/removed when the production `Wetlands/MapServer` is repopulated (revisit then, or if `fwspublicservices` recovers) вАФ and the app already degrades to the honest "service unavailable" path (B129) if it disappears. lint **0 errors** ¬Ј **197 tests** ¬Ј build green; `SitePlannerApp` lazy chunk intact. Browser pass logged as **VERIFICATION V27**. How I found it: loaded the live USFWS Mapper in a headless browser to read its real service refs (`gis-verify/mapper-capture.mjs`).

### B117 вАФ Draw-tool palette can't scroll to its bottom on desktop вЖТ SHAPES group unreachable `[Site Planner]` (bug)
`[x]` Repro: open Site Planner on a normal laptop viewport; the dark draw-tool rail (the **Tools / Site elements / Shapes** palette) is taller than the screen but won't scroll to the end вАФ the SHAPES group and anything below it sits past the fold and is unreachable. Expected: the rail scrolls cleanly to its last row at any viewport height, with the full list reachable. **Confirmed cause:** the rail container in `SitePlanner.jsx` sets `overflowY: narrow ? "auto" : "visible"`, so it only scrolls inside the phone/`narrow` overlay (B113); on the desktop path `overflowY:"visible"` + `flex:none` with no height bound lets the content spill off-screen with no scrollbar. Fix: give the rail `overflow-y:auto` on the desktop path too and bound its height to the viewport вАФ it already sits in a flex row, so add `min-height:0` on the column so it can shrink-and-scroll; confirm the last row is fully visible.
> Not a dup of **B107** (that reworked the *mode-tab* column вАФ Yield/Parcel/Element/Aerial/Overlay/Setup вАФ and found it already fits) or **B113** (that added only the *phone* slide-in overlay, with its own `overflow:auto`; the desktop layout was left byte-identical, so this desktop scroll gap is untouched). Michael described it as the "left" rail; in the current build this palette renders on the **right** (dark chrome) вАФ same element, identified here by its Tools/Site-elements/Shapes content. Pairs with **B118** (shorter rows overflow less often), but this is the underlying bug вАФ even a short rail must stay fully reachable.
> вЬЕ **Done 2026-06-16** (branch `claude/eager-brahmagupta-7sagg0`). The rail container (`SitePlanner.jsx`) now uses `overflowY: "auto"` on the desktop path too (was `narrow ? "auto" : "visible"`) plus `minHeight: 0`, so it shrinks inside the height-bounded flex body row and scrolls to its last row at any viewport height вАФ the SHAPES / Measure / Annotate groups below the fold are now reachable. Desktop layout otherwise byte-identical; the phone/`narrow` overlay path is unchanged. lint 0 errors ¬Ј 138 tests ¬Ј build green.

### B127 вАФ Measure-type dropdown (and the other rail/header menus) render behind/clipped by the rail `[Site Planner / UI]` (bug)  *(arrived as "NEW-3"; minted B127 вАФ next after B126)*
`[x]` Repro: in the right tool rail, open the **Measure** tool's mode dropdown (the **вЦЊ** caret next to "Length"). Expected: the menu opens above all adjacent UI вАФ fully visible and clickable. Actual: the flyout was partially/fully hidden вАФ clipped by the rail, painting "behind" the neighbouring rail/zoom rail. **Root cause = the two classic CSS layer traps, both introduced/exposed by B117.** The rail container (`SitePlanner.jsx`) sets `position:relative; zIndex:30` (a **trapped stacking context** вАФ caps every child's z-index against the canvas/map siblings no matter how high) **and** `overflowY:"auto"` (B117 changed this from `narrow ? "auto" : "visible"` to always `"auto"` to fix the desktop scroll-to-bottom). Per the CSS spec, once `overflow-y` is non-visible the `overflow-x:visible` **computes to `auto`** too, so the rail now clips horizontally вАФ and these flyouts open sideways out of the rail (`right: calc(100% + 10px)`), so they got cut off. You cannot have a vertically-scrolling rail that also lets a child overflow sideways, so bumping z-index can't fix it.
> вЬЕ **Done 2026-06-17** (branch `claude/sweet-pasteur-5kd1p4`). Built the **durable, shared fix** the brief asked for: a new reusable **portal** popover layer `src/shared/ui/AnchoredMenu.jsx` (`ReactDOM.createPortal` to `document.body`) вАФ the menu mounts at the document root, escaping **both** any ancestor stacking context **and** any `overflow:auto` clipping at once. It positions itself against its trigger via `getBoundingClientRect` (`position:fixed`, viewport-clamped, repositions on scroll/resize), measures-then-reveals so there's no flash, and keeps the click-away backdrop. z-index 4000/4001 = the app's existing modal layer (matches `ParcelDrawing`'s portal; above the map, below `AuthPanel`'s 5000). **Migrated every instance of the trapped pattern in the workspace** вАФ not just the one menu: the 5 rail flyouts (**Measure**, Boundary, Building dock, Car-Parking rows, Road width) and the 3 header menus (**Site вЦЊ**, **Plan вЦЊ**, **File вЦЊ**). Visuals/placement/widths unchanged. lint 0 errors ¬Ј **152 tests** ¬Ј build green; lazy chunk split intact (`AnchoredMenu` rides in the `SitePlannerApp` chunk). **Follow-up candidate (not done):** the Document Review `ReviewsBar` "Reviews вЦЊ" dropdown is the same class in the other workspace вАФ it opens downward and uses its own styling (not `menuPanel`), so it's left for a focused doc-review pass; the shared component now lives in `src/shared/ui/` so adopting it there is trivial. Browser pass queued as **VERIFICATION V16**. **Not merged to `main` вАФ owner review first.**

### B126 вАФ Data-loss ROOT FIX: sync kept the whole last-saved copy (a thinner one erased a fuller one) + automatic local backups `[Persistence]` (bug) вАФ DATA-LOSS, critical
`[x]` Follow-up to **B124/B125**. The shipped B124 fix stopped whole *sites* from vanishing on pull, but buildings could still disappear *inside* a surviving site: both `saveSite`/the cloud and `mergePulledSites` reconciled two copies by **whole-record newer-`updatedAt`-wins** with **no content merge**, so any copy saved last with fewer buildings (a stale tab, a second device, a partial/mid-load save) silently overwrote the fuller one вАФ and `pullCloud`'s re-push then propagated the thin copy to the cloud. Owner hit this: ~12 projects emptied while the last-edited one (SCHIEL, intact at ~10 buildings / 24 building-elements once bump-outs are counted) survived. Free-tier Supabase вЖТ no PITR, so the emptied sites weren't server-recoverable; owner opted to **fix forward** (quick to recreate) and harden against recurrence.
> **Fixed 2026-06-16 (branch `claude/zen-sagan-9otrll`).** (1) **Content-preserving merge** вАФ `siteModel.js` gains `mergeSiteContent(a,b)`: scalar/meta come from the newer copy, but every drawn collection (els, markups, measures, callouts, parcels, sheetOverlays, parcelDrawings, elevation cross-sections) is **unioned by id**, so a building present in EITHER copy survives; a stripped inline raster is healed from the copy that still has it. `mergePulledSites` now uses it (was whole-record newer-wins) and re-pushes whenever the merge produced more content than the cloud had, so kept work reaches the cloud instead of being stranded. (2) **Automatic local version history** вАФ `storage.js` snapshots the prior version of a site on every `saveSite` into a capped, slimmed (geometry-only), local-only ring (`planarfit:sites:history:v1`); `snapshotVersion`/`listVersions`/`getVersion` back the planner's **Plan вЦЊ вЖТ Version historyвА¶** dialog, which restores any earlier version (the replaced state is itself snapshotted, so a restore is reversible). **Trade-off documented:** a delete made in only one copy can reappear once (recoverable by deleting again) вАФ per-item tombstones are the fully-correct future hardening, and the version history makes any surprise recoverable meanwhile. lint **0 errors** ¬Ј **152 tests** (8 new: union-keeps-all, two-device union, per-id newer-wins, image-heal, end-to-end no-thinning + re-push, history captures/restores/de-dupes) ¬Ј build green. Browser pass queued as **VERIFICATION V15**. **Not merged to `main` вАФ owner verification first.**
> **вШЕ Status corrected 2026-06-17 (this session): MERGED + DEPLOYED** via **PR #83** вАФ confirmed live on planyr.io (the deployed `SitePlannerApp` chunk carries `planarfit:sites:history:v1` + the **Plan вЦЊ вЖТ Version historyвА¶** dialog). The "not merged" note is stale; the Version history restore is available to the owner now (key to **B136** recovery вАФ local/per-device only). Effectively DONE (eligible to move to вЬЕ Done).

### B127 вАФ Two-tab convergence: a stale tab could thin the durable store; open tabs didn't live-sync `[Persistence]` (bug) вАФ follow-up to B126
`[x]` Found by the **V15** cohort run. **No data loss** (B126's automatic backup recovered the fuller copy), but a rough edge: with the SAME site open in two tabs, a stale tab's save/flush **blind-overwrote** the durable store with its thinner copy, so the two tabs could **disagree on reload** until the stale tab closed + one edit healed it.
> **Fixed 2026-06-16 (branch `claude/zen-sagan-9otrll`).** (A) **`storage.js` `saveSite` now folds a stale write into the store** instead of blind-overwriting: a per-TAB `lastSeenAt[id]` (set by `loadSite`/`saveSite`) distinguishes "I'm the current writer" (plain replace вЖТ single-tab deletes still stick) from "another tab advanced the store since I last synced" (content-merge via `mergeSiteContent` вЖТ never thins). So the durable store + every reload now always hold the union. (B) **`SitePlanner.jsx` adds an idle-guarded `storage`-event listener** that folds another tab's save into the open canvas (union вАФ never drops either tab's work; only-if-changed to avoid churn/ping-pong; skipped while mid-drag/draw/typing), so two open tabs converge **live** without a reload. 2 new unit tests (stale-write folds; single-tab delete still sticks). lint 0 err ¬Ј **154 tests** ¬Ј build green. Re-test under **VERIFICATION V15** (two-tab case).
> **вШЕ Status corrected 2026-06-17 (this session): MERGED + DEPLOYED** via **PR #89** вАФ the persistence cluster (content-merge, version history, two-tab fold) is confirmed in the live planyr.io bundle. Effectively DONE (eligible to move to вЬЕ Done).

### B130 вАФ Parking tool: "Split into rows" tiles single-loaded rows вАФ generate double-loaded modules + correct curb logic + rename `[Site Planner]` (bug)  *(arrived as "NEW-1"; minted B130 вАФ next after B129)*
`[x]` **Repro:** draw a car-parking area, click **"Split into rows."** **Current (wrong):** the field is tiled as `[stall row + drive aisle]` repeated down its whole depth вАФ single-loaded throughout, a full aisle against every row (the most pavement-hungry layout; ~40% more depth per row than needed, so fewer rows fit and stall yield comes in low). **Expected:** tile a **double-loaded module** вАФ two stall rows sharing one aisle.
- **Generation logic.** Repeating module = double-loaded: stall row + aisle + stall row. At 90¬∞: 18вА≤ + 24вА≤ + 18вА≤ = **60вА≤ module**; stall width 9вА≤ default. **Single-load only where geometry forces it:** the top row against a building face/sidewalk, a row against a property line, or a final strip too shallow for a full 60вА≤ bay. **Remainder:** if the last band can't fit a full 60вА≤ module, drop a single-loaded row or hand the strip back as leftover/landscape вАФ **never insert another full aisle to fill it.**
- **Orientation:** rows parallel to the building face by default; fall back to the polygon's **longest edge**.
- **Parameters to expose:** stall width (8.5вАУ9.5вА≤, default 9вА≤), stall depth (default 18вА≤), aisle width (default 24вА≤ at 90¬∞), parking angle (90/60/45¬∞), single- vs. double-loaded.
- **Curb logic (6вА≥ curb).** Apply one 6вА≥ curb around the **perimeter** of the paving, wherever pavement meets non-paving (dirt, landscape, building face, property line). **Never at internal seams** вАФ aisle-to-stall-row inside a module, or stall-row-backing-onto-stall-row between stacked modules (that's continuous paving). **No curb across drive-aisle openings** where vehicles pass (entry throat, aisle-to-aisle, aisle-to-street) вАФ there pavement meets pavement, so the meets-non-paving rule already skips it. A **dead-end aisle terminating against landscape DOES get a curb** (terminus, not blockage). Test: vehicles cross the edge вЖТ gap, no curb; vehicles stop at the edge вЖТ curb.
- **Rename:** change the button **"Split into rows" вЖТ "Split rows/aisles"** (it splits the field into stall rows + drive aisles). *(Owner 2026-06-17: explicitly NOT "Generate parking" / "Lay out stalls" вАФ those don't fit; "Split rows/aisles" is the label.)*
- **Out of scope (tracked separately, large lift):** clipping the field to the parcel boundary.
> **Dedupe / reconcile вАФ EXTEND the existing parking + curb code; do NOT build a parallel generator.** A double-loaded parking engine, the depth-stepping model, and a derived-curb system already exist (built in **PR #38** + **PR #86**), so most of NEW-1 is implemented and only specific gaps are genuinely open. Map of exists-vs-open:
> - **Double-loaded field-fill is already built and correct** вАФ not single-loaded. `carStalls(w,h,cfg)` (`SitePlanner.jsx` ~375) tiles `mod = 2¬ЈrowDepth + aisle` (two stall rows per aisle) with a single-loaded trailing remainder only when a full 60вА≤ module won't fit; defaults are already `stallW 9 / stallDepth 18 / aisle 24 / parkAngle 90` (~line 656) with 90/60/45¬∞ + per-element `cfg` overrides surfaced (Setup ~5765, per-element ~5380). So the **un-split** field already matches the spec (**B69**, Done). **The "single-loaded throughout" repro is `splitParkingRows` (~line 3619), not the fill:** clicking "Split into rows" evenly divides the depth into N independent one-row elements, each of which re-renders single-loaded вАФ that is the live bug to fix.

Keep B70's calc/draw/dimension three-way contract and the 6вА≥ default вАФ NEW-1 only tightens *where* the curb lands. Polygon/irregular pads are currently out of scope for the auto-curb (B70 deferred nuance); confirm whether NEW-1's perimeter rule should now cover them.
> **Progress 2026-06-17 (branch `claude/blissful-feynman-0ijfr2`): the core split bug + the rename are SHIPPED; the two enhancements stay open.** Fixed the actual repro вАФ `splitParkingRows` now splits a field into **double-loaded module elements** (two stall rows sharing one drive aisle, 60вА≤ at 90¬∞) plus **at most one trailing single-loaded row** for an odd remainder, instead of one single-loaded `[row + aisle]` per row. **Total depth and stall count are preserved exactly** (the piece depths sum back to the field's `h`), so yield doesn't change вАФ only the split geometry. Extracted the pure math to **`lib/parking.js`** (`parkDepthForRows` / `parkRowsForDepth` / new `splitParkingPieces`) with **`test/parking.test.js`** (10 cases: module split, odd-remainder single row, total-depth preservation, sub-row fold-in, вЙ§1-module no-op, degenerate-config guard). The **un-split** field already double-loaded via `carStalls` (B69), so it's untouched. lint **0 errors** ¬Ј **185 tests** (10 new) ¬Ј build green ¬Ј `SitePlannerApp` lazy chunk intact. Shipped to `main` (owner said push to main). **Browser pass DONE** вАФ self-verified live 2026-06-17 in a headless browser (rename + double-loaded split confirmed on planyr.io / branch preview), logged as **VERIFICATION V24**. **Still OPEN (deliberately deferred this pass):** (2) **free-field longest-edge auto-orientation** вАФ interacts with B119's building-attached orientation + the depth-stepping, wants its own careful pass; (3) the **fuller curb rule** (full perimeter / skip internal seams + vehicle openings / curb a dead-end terminus) вАФ extends `curbEdgesOf`, which feeds yield math, and has the open design Q above (polygon pads + opening detection), so not safe to guess into production yet.

The only remaining piece вАФ clipping the field to the parcel boundary вАФ was always out of scope here and is now filed as its own item **B131**.

### B131 вАФ Print-dialog toggle to include the site-plan overlay in the printed/exported output `[Site Planner]` (feature)  *(arrived as "NEW-1"; filed provisionally as B130, renumbered B131 after `main`'s #95 concurrently took B130 for the parking "Split rows/aisles" fix вАФ the implementing commit + branch still say B130)*
`[x]` Add a checkbox to the print-frame dialog (the Letter/Tabloid + Landscape/Portrait toolbar) that controls whether the placed **site-plan overlay** (B72 вАФ the drag-dropped PDF/image backdrop) is included in the print / PDF / PNG output. **Confirm-before-build resolved:** both the print dialog and the overlay live in **Site Planner** (`SitePlanner.jsx`) вАФ the print-frame toolbar's `printPaper`/`printOrient` and the `sheetOverlays` layer вАФ **not** Document Review, so it was built here (no retag). All design points met: label **"Print overlay"** (a print-action verb, not the screen-toggle "Show"); the control is **only shown when an overlay is actually loaded** (no dead control); it **defaults to the overlay's on-screen visibility** (checked when a rendered overlay is on screen); and it acts as a **master include/exclude** across multiple overlays, forward-compatible with a future per-overlay hide (`visible !== false`).
> вЬЕ **Done 2026-06-17** (branch `claude/adoring-pascal-clrp0k`). **WYSIWYG by construction:** the export path **clones the live SVG**, so an included overlay keeps its exact transform вАФ real-world feetвЖТpixel position (EPSG:2278-anchored origin), scale, rotation, opacity, and page selection (the chosen page is already the rasterized `src`) вАФ composited **above the aerial backdrop** in the same z-order as on screen. New pure helper `lib/overlayPrint.js` (`isOverlayPrintable` / `printableOverlays` / `hasPrintableOverlay`) is the single source of truth for the checkbox's visibility + default and the compositing filter; `buildExportSvg(frame, includeOverlay)` tags each overlay raster `data-overlay-image` (kept or dropped per the toggle) and the on-canvas selection chrome + unsynced placeholder `data-export="skip"` (so neither ever prints). Also fixed a **latent inconsistency**: overlays used to **silently vanish from output whenever an aerial underlay was present** (the underlay pass stripped *all* `<image>`s) вАФ now overlays are honored in both **Print** and **PNG export**. lint 0 errors ¬Ј **181 tests** (6 new in `test/overlayPrint.test.js`) ¬Ј build green; lazy chunk split intact. Browser pass queued as **VERIFICATION V24**. **Shipped to `main` via PR #96** (owner said "ship").

### B113 вАФ Planner is not responsive at mobile width `[Site Planyr / UI]` (feature)  *(branch "B99")*

The planner is effectively desktop-only. Needs a mobile treatment (collapsible/off-canvas rails, a bottom toolbar). Larger effort вАФ roadmap, not a quick fix. (Audit L1; see `ui-audit/screens/planner-mobile.png`.)
> Fix (`SitePlanner.jsx`): a `matchMedia("(max-width: 760px)")` `narrow` flag drives a phone treatment вАФ **every mobile style is `narrow ?`-gated, so the desktop layout is byte-identical**. When narrow: (1) the right 168px tool palette no longer eats width вАФ it **slides in from the right as an overlay** (with a tap-to-dismiss backdrop) summoned by a floating **"вЬО Tools"** button, and auto-closes when you pick a tool so you can draw; (2) the left menu panel (Yield/Parcel/вА¶) **overlays the canvas** (`position:absolute`, capped to `min(320px, 100vw-74px)`) instead of pushing it, its drag-resize handle hidden; (3) the thin 54px left rail stays inline; (4) the header scrolls horizontally instead of wrapping (condensed gap/padding). Net: the canvas keeps full usable width on a phone.
