### B15 вАФ Import JSON drops callouts & markups, and leaves stale ones on the canvas `[Site Planner]` (bug) вАФ DATA-LOSS, high
`[x]` рЯФІ fixed in audit PR. `importJSONFile` (SitePlanner.jsx ~2459) set parcels/els/measures/settings/underlay but **not** `callouts`/`markups`, although `exportJSON` writes them. Result: (a) imported callouts/markups are discarded; (b) the currently-open plan's callouts/markups aren't reset, so they bleed into the imported plan and get persisted on the next autosave. Fix: `setCallouts(d.callouts || [])` + `setMarkups(d.markups || [])` in import (symmetric with export).

### B16 вАФ `isBlankSite` ignores `markups` вЖТ markup/encumbrance-only sites are silently deleted on leave `[Site Planner]` (bug) вАФ DATA-LOSS, high
`[x]` рЯФІ fixed in audit PR. `isBlankSite` (SitePlanner.jsx ~795) omits `markups`, so a site whose only work is drawn markups or a plotted metes-and-bounds **encumbrance** is treated as blank: the autosave guard skips it and `persistOrDrop` *deletes* the un-located record on unmount. Fix: include `markups` in `isBlankSite` and in the autosave guard object.

### B17 вАФ Doc Review local mirror saved without `updatedAt`; `reconcile` compares mismatched fields `[Document Review]` (bug) вАФ DATA-LOSS risk, high
`[x]` рЯФІ fixed in audit PR. `buildSnapshot` (DocReview.jsx/Stitcher.jsx) omits `updatedAt`, so `flushLocal()вЖТwriteDraft` mirrors a record whose `data.updatedAt` is stale/absent; `reconcile` then compares cloud `updatedAt` vs draft `_localAt` (different events/clocks) and can let a stale local draft shadow a newer cloud copy. Fix: stamp `updatedAt: Date.now()` in `buildSnapshot` so the mirror and the cloud `data` carry a consistent timestamp.

### B18 вАФ Last-debounce-window edits flush local-only and are lost when `pullCloud` blind-replaces on next login `[Site Planner]` (bug) вАФ DATA-LOSS, high
`[x]` The beforeunload/visibility/unmount/site-switch flushes call `saveSite` (local cache) but **never** `pushSiteToCloud`; `pullCloud` then *replaces* the per-user cache wholesale on next login, discarding any edit made in the final ~400 ms before close that the debounced cloud push missed. Fix options: make `pullCloud` merge by `updatedAt` (keep the newer side), and/or push on `pagehide` via `fetch(..., {keepalive:true})`/`sendBeacon`. (Bigger change вАФ left for review.)

### B19 вАФ Resume-on-mount re-saves the just-loaded review with a fresh `updatedAt` `[Document Review]` (bug) вАФ correctness, medium
`[x]` рЯФІ fixed 2026-06-15 (branch `doc-review/b19-resume-resave`): `useReviewPersistence` exposes `suspendSave(ms)` which parks a suspend window; the autosave effect early-returns while it's active. `loadSingleReview` arms it once (single commit); `loadStitch` arms it at start and re-arms before its async `setPdfs`/`setPlaced` commits, so a programmatic load never re-stamps just-loaded data with a fresh `updatedAt`. `loadSingleReview`/`loadStitch` set state вЖТ the debounce deps change вЖТ autosave writes the loaded snapshot back with `updatedAt: now`, so a resume can stamp stale data as newest and (multi-tab) clobber a newer cloud edit. Fix: a `suspendSave` ref set during programmatic load, early-returning from the autosave effect for that tick.

### B21 вАФ Down overlay re-probes & repaints the error banner every 45 s forever; background errors share the click-instruction slot `[Site Planner / map]` (bug) вАФ correctness, high
`[x]` рЯФІ fixed in audit PR. `PROBE_TTL` (40 s) < the 45 s re-probe interval, so a genuinely-down enabled layer re-probes and re-fires `onError` every tick, repainting the bottom-left banner indefinitely; that banner is also the only `err` slot, so a background layer hiccup masks the "click a lot" guidance until a user action clears it. Fix: de-duplicate identical error toasts and auto-clear background layer errors after a timeout.

### B22 вАФ Rapid parcel clicks race вЖТ duplicate selection + leaked highlight polygon `[Site Planner / map]` (bug) вАФ correctness, medium
`[x]` рЯФІ fixed 2026-06-15 (branch `site-planner/map-gis-robustness`) вАФ defensive: `handleClick` now removes any pre-existing hilite for a key before overwriting (no orphaned `L.polygon`) and dedupes the `selected` entry by key (no double-counted acreage). NOTE: in the current code the toggle check runs AFTER the `await`, so two clicks resolve sequentially into a correct toggle and the described double-add doesn't actually reproduce вАФ these guards close the theoretical gap without an in-flight ref that would drop a legitimate second-lot click. `handleClick` is async with no sequence guard; two fast clicks on the same lot can both take the "add" branch (the toggle check runs before the first `await` resolves), producing a duplicate `selected` entry (double-counted acreage) and an orphaned `L.polygon` left on the map. Fix: guard with an in-flight ref / request id, and remove any pre-existing hilite for a key before overwriting.

### B23 вАФ `ditchStats` returns `NaN` profile distance for a single elevation sample `[Site Planner]` (bug) вАФ correctness, high
`[x]` рЯФІ fixed in audit PR. elevation.js only guards `length === 0`; with exactly one sample, `i/(n-1) = 0/0 = NaN` flows into the cross-section profile/labels. Fix: treat `< 2` samples as insufficient (`return null`), letting the caller's "no samples" path handle it.

### B24 вАФ `measureLabel` prints `"NaN"` / can crash on degenerate measurement points `[Document Review]` (bug) вАФ correctness, medium
`[x]` рЯФІ fixed in audit PR. takeoff.js `measureLabel`/`measureValue` have no finite/length guard; an empty `distance` markup dereferences `m.pts[0].x` (throws) and short polys can render `"NaN ft/ac"`. Fix: guard missing/short `pts` and non-finite values.

### B25 вАФ Metes-and-bounds: curve calls silently parsed as straight chords; no unreadable-call flagging `[Site Planner]` (bug) вАФ correctness, high
`[x]` `CALL_RE` has no `radius`/`arc`/`delta`/`chord` handling; given a curve call it matches the chord bearing+distance and dead-reckons it as a straight segment, with no `dropped`/`unparsed` signal вАФ so the traverse is silently wrong and the UI can't warn. (Roadmap already wants "parse curves; flag unreadable.") Fix: detect curve calls and either tessellate the arc or return `{unparsed:true, raw}` so callers can flag them.
> Progress 2026-06-15: deferred from the round-2 correctness PR вАФ flagging/tessellating curve calls needs parser + UI work validated against real deed text (risk of breaking the working straight-call parser for Harris/FBCAD); left Open for a focused pass with sample deeds.

### B26 вАФ Metes-and-bounds: parser gaps (dash-DMS unparsed, deg>90 accepted, loose closure floor) `[Site Planner]` (bug) вАФ correctness, medium
`[x]` рЯФІ fixed 2026-06-15 (branch `site-planner/correctness-round2`): (a) `-` added to the degree/minute separator classes so `S 12-15 W` parses; (b) `parseCalls` skips any call with `deg > 90`; (c) the `pathCloses` absolute floor dropped 25 ft вЖТ 5 ft (the 2% relative term kept), so a small lot can't falsely "close" on 25 ft of misclosure. (a) The header advertises `S 12-15 W` but the DMS separator classes exclude `-`, so dash-separated bearings return `[]` (silently dropped). (b) The degrees group `[0-9]{1,3}` accepts a quadrant bearing > 90¬∞ (e.g. `N 145 E`) and plots it. (c) `pathCloses` floors tolerance at `max(25, 2%¬Јperim)` so a small lot can be declared "closed" with a 25-ft misclosure, hiding parse errors. Fix: add `-` to the separator classes; reject/flag `deg>90`; drop/shrink the absolute closure floor and always surface the misclosure.

### B27 вАФ Enter-to-commit power-line trace uses stale `tracePts`/`traceMode` `[Site Planner]` (bug) вАФ correctness, medium
`[x]` рЯФІ fixed in audit PR. The keydown effect closes over `traceMode`/`tracePts` but they're not in its dep array, so pressing Enter to finish a trace reads stale values (often `[]`). Fix: add `traceMode`/`tracePts` to the effect deps (double-click already worked because it's a fresh prop).

### B28 вАФ `mergeRings` collinear-cleanup threshold is area-based (scale-dependent) `[Site Planner]` (bug) вАФ correctness, medium
`[x]` рЯФІ fixed 2026-06-15 (branch `site-planner/correctness-round2`): the corner test now thresholds the perpendicular deviation `|cross|/hypot(cвИТa)` (> 0.1 ft), so it's scale-independent. The corner test `Math.abs(cross) > 1` compares twice-triangle-area in ft¬≤ (scales with edge length), so on long edges a real slight bend can be dropped (or noise kept), distorting a merged parcel boundary/acreage. Fix: threshold the *perpendicular distance* `|cross|/hypot(cвИТa)` against a small foot tolerance.

### B29 вАФ Parking +/вИТ shrink guard ignores per-field `cfg` overrides `[Site Planner]` (bug) вАФ correctness, medium
`[x]` рЯФІ fixed 2026-06-15 (branch `site-planner/b58-b62-planner-correctness`): `parkBand(el)` and `canShrink` now derive the band from `cfgOf(el)`, matching `growParking`. `parkBand()`/`canShrink` use global `settings.stallDepth/aisle`, but `growParking` uses `cfgOf(el)`; for a field with per-element cfg the on-canvas вИТ handle is enabled/disabled against the wrong row size (guard disagrees with the actual op). Fix: compute the band from `cfgOf(el)` in the guard too.

### B30 вАФ Markup/measure minimum size is in feet, not pixels вЖТ silently discarded when zoomed out `[Site Planner]` (bug) вАФ minor, medium
`[x]` рЯФІ fixed 2026-06-15 (branch `site-planner/correctness-round2`): the minimums are now `3 / view.ppf` ft (a ~3px drag), so a deliberate drag isn't silently dropped at any zoom. The `dist(a,b) >= 2` / `w,h >= 2` minimums are world-feet; at low ppf a deliberate multi-pixel drag can be < 2 ft and the markup/measure is dropped with no feedback. Fix: make the minimum pixel-based (scale by view ppf).

### B31 вАФ Two-point Split returns null when both crossings share an edge `[Site Planner]` (bug) вАФ minor, low
`[x]` `if (lo.i === hi.i) return null` uses only the extreme-`t` hits, so a valid straight cut across a concave parcel (whose first/last crossings land on the same edge while valid interior crossings exist) silently no-ops. Fix: when `lo.i === hi.i`, pick the two crossings with distinct edge indices that yield two вЙ•3-vertex rings.
> Progress 2026-06-15: deferred from round-2 вАФ the same-edge multi-crossing case is fiddly concave-polygon geometry (minor/low) that's hard to validate without runtime cases; left Open to avoid shipping a bad split.
> **Superseded 2026-06-17 by B128 (Done):** the whole concave multi-crossing case (not just the same-edge sub-case) is now handled by a correct general slice in `lib/polygonSplit.js` вАФ see B128 for the validated fix.

### B32 вАФ Undo stack polluted by `pushHistory` on no-op edits `[Site Planner]` (bug) вАФ minor, high
`[x]` `beginEditCallout` and the dock/type `onChange` handlers call `pushHistory()` before/without an actual change, so cancelling a callout edit or reselecting the same dropdown value adds an undo frame (first Ctrl+Z appears to do nothing). Fix: push history only when a mutation is actually applied.
> Progress 2026-06-15 (branch `site-planner/correctness-round2`): the **callout** half is fixed вАФ `beginEditCallout` no longer pushes history on open, and `commitEditCallout` pushes only when the text actually changes (cancel or commit-unchanged adds no frame). Re-checked the **dock/type dropdown** half вАФ it's a NON-ISSUE: a native `<select>` `onChange` fires only on an actual value change (re-selecting the already-selected option doesn't fire it), so it never adds a spurious frame. The callout half was the real bug; B32 is resolved.

### B33 вАФ Doc Review redline shapes (rect/cloud/text) are unselectable except at corner points `[Document Review]` (bug) вАФ minor, high
`[x]` рЯФІ fixed 2026-06-15 (branch `doc-review/followup-minors`): `hitTest` is now shape-aware вАФ rect/cloud select across their whole body (point-in-box ¬± tolerance), text selects across its rendered label box, and measures select on nearest vertex OR segment (so a line body selects, not just its endpoints). `hitTest` measures distance only to stored vertices; rect/cloud store two corners and text one point, so clicking an edge or body never selects them (hard to select/delete redlines). Fix: shape-aware hit testing (point-in-rect, distance-to-segment, text bbox).

### B34 вАФ Doc Review single-viewer `render()` calls `setScale` internally вЖТ re-entrant render race `[Document Review]` (bug) вАФ correctness, medium
`[x]` рЯФІ fixed 2026-06-15 (branch `chore/audit-tail-grind`): the fit-to-width scale is computed in its OWN effect (when `scale===0`); `render()` returns early until a concrete scale exists and no longer calls `setScale`, so it's a pure draw and the double-render / `dims` mismatch is gone. In fit-to-width mode `render` calls `setScale(s)` then keeps drawing; the `scale` change re-fires the render effect, so two renders run and `dims`/canvas can briefly mismatch the overlay. Fix: compute fit scale in a separate effect; keep `render` a pure draw at a concrete scale.

### B35 вАФ `listProjects` status display is fragile (newest-row-wins; fallback drops status) `[Document Review]` (bug) вАФ minor, medium
`[x]` рЯФІ fixed 2026-06-15 (branch `doc-review/followup-minors`): `listProjects` returns `status:"unknown"` (not `"active"`) when the value is missing or the status read fell back to the no-status query, and `ProjectLibrary` renders a neutral "Status?" placeholder for an unknown status (still settable) вАФ so a failed read no longer silently reports every project as "active." (Group-consistency is unchanged: status is group-wide per B7, so newest-row stays a fair representative.) Status is read from whichever group row sorts first by `updated_at`, and if the `status:data->>status` select errors the fallback query omits status so every project shows the default "active" вАФ silently misreporting lifecycle. Fix: resolve status group-consistently and surface "unknown" rather than defaulting to active on a failed status read.

### B37 вАФ Cloud/auth hardening `[Site Planner / auth]` (bug) вАФ low/minor
`[x]` рЯФІ partially fixed in audit PR. (a) **fixed:** `cloudDelete` now scopes by `user_id` AND `id` (was RLS-only). (b) **fixed:** the autosave cloud push had no `.catch`, leaving the save badge stuck on "SavingвА¶" on a rejected upsert. (c) **fixed:** `metaRef` omitted `county`, so a save whose merge-base lacked county could normalize it to null вАФ now self-contained. (d) **fixed:** `testConnection` now accepts any https origin (custom Supabase domains) вАФ PR #27; the `pullCloud`-failure-empty-library half was fixed separately as B54 (#21).

### B39 вАФ PDF.js documents are never `destroy()`'d вЖТ growing memory leak across a review session `[Document Review]` (bug) вАФ leak, high
`[x]` рЯФІ fixed 2026-06-15 (branch `chore/audit-safe-fixes-b39-b45`): the prior doc is destroyed before swap (DocReview `setPdfDoc` helper) and the Stitcher destroys docs as they leave state via a diff effect, plus an unmount cleanup in both. `loadPdf` returns a `PDFDocumentProxy` (worker + retained ArrayBuffer); every replacement just overwrites `pdfRef.current` / `pdfs[].doc` (openFile, load, resetSingle, resetStitch, loadStitch) with no `.destroy()`, and there's no unmount cleanup. A repo-wide grep for `.destroy()` in doc-review is empty. Heavy construction sets leak MBs per open; the stitcher holds N docs at once. Fix: destroy the prior doc before replacing, destroy each removed/replaced source in the stitcher, and add an unmount effect that destroys the live doc(s). (Deferred from the audit PR only to avoid editing files a parallel agent was reading вАФ will fix in the consolidated pass.)

### B40 вАФ Superseded PDF render tasks are never cancelled `[Document Review]` (bug) вАФ perf, high
`[x]` рЯФІ fixed 2026-06-15 (branch `chore/audit-safe-fixes-b39-b45`): `renderPageToCanvas` now exposes its `RenderTask` (an `onTask` callback); `render()` keeps it in a ref, `cancel()`s the prior one before each render and on unmount, and swallows `RenderingCancelledException`. `renderPageToCanvas` creates `page.render(...)` and only awaits its promise; `render()` discards the stale *result* via the `renderTok` token but never calls `task.cancel()`. Rapid page/zoom changes pile up overlapping renders and can hit PDF.js's "cannot use the same canvas during multiple render operations" (throw/torn output). Fix: return the `RenderTask`, keep a ref, `cancel()` before starting a new one and on unmount; treat `RenderingCancelledException` as a no-op.
> **Amendment вАФ residual same-canvas race, fixed 2026-06-21 (branch `claude/modest-turing-wixo1y`).** (Folded in from a coworker-chat note, not a new item.) The B40 fix had a hole: `renderTaskRef.current` is only populated AFTER `await pdf.getPage()` inside `renderPageToCanvas`, so during render #1's getPage await, render #2 starts, finds `renderTaskRef.current` still null (nothing to cancel), and both proceed to `page.render()` on the same canvas вАФ the exact "Cannot use the same canvas during multiple render operations" error B40 targeted, swallowed, leaving the canvas on a superseded sheet. **Fix:** `renderPageToCanvas` now takes an `isStale` predicate and checks it right BEFORE `page.render()`; `DocReview.jsx` passes `() => tok !== renderTok.current`, so a render superseded mid-getPage bails (returns null) before it touches the canvas вАФ only the newest render draws. Verified: lint 0 ¬Ј 802 tests ¬Ј build green; headless `ui-audit/verify-b322-b40.mjs` shows 0 same-canvas errors across rapid switches (V85). Shipping via PR #240 вЖТ `main` (with the B326вАУB328 batch).

### B41 вАФ Global keydown effects have no deps array вЖТ re-subscribe on every render (hot path) `[Document Review]` (bug) вАФ perf, high
`[x]` рЯФІ fixed 2026-06-15 (branch `chore/audit-safe-fixes-b39-b45`): both now bind the `keydown` listener ONCE (`[]` deps) and dispatch through an `onKeyRef` refreshed each render, so the handler keeps live closures without re-subscribing on every render. DocReview.jsx and Stitcher.jsx register their `keydown` listener in an effect with no dependency array (the `}); // eslint-disable-line` pattern), so the handler is removed+re-added after *every* render вАФ and `onPointerMove`вЖТ`setCursor` re-renders dozens of times/second while drawing. Fix: register once with `[]` and read `draft`/`sel`/handlers from refs inside `onKey`.

### B42 вАФ `SitePlannerApp` rebuilds `siteGroups` (a Map over all sites) every render `[Site Planner]` (bug) вАФ perf, medium
`[x]` вЬЕ already addressed (verified 2026-06-15): `siteGroups` is already `useMemo`'d on `[sites, activeSiteId]` in `SitePlannerApp.jsx` (with a "stable identity" comment) вАФ the IIFE the audit flagged had since been converted, so no code change was needed. `const siteGroups = (() => { вА¶ })()` runs unconditionally each render, allocating a fresh array passed as the `sites` prop to `MapFinder` вАФ O(n) per render and a referential-stability hazard that defeats child memoization. Fix: `useMemo(вА¶, [sites, activeSiteId])`. (Safe, small вАФ will fix in the consolidated pass.)

### B43 вАФ `applyUser` auth-event handling has no sequence guard вЖТ races on fast auth transitions `[Site Planner / auth]` (bug) вАФ correctness, medium
`[x]` `applyUser` is async (`setActiveUser` вЖТ `await pullCloud` вЖТ `refreshSites`); overlapping auth events (INITIAL_SESSIONвЖТSIGNED_IN, or fast sign-out/in) can interleave so `prevUid.current`/`clearCloudCache` run out of order and clear/point at the wrong user's cache. Fix: capture a monotonic token before the await and bail stale completions (the file already uses a `live` guard elsewhere).

### B44 вАФ Doc Review async refresh/flush lack in-flight guards `[Document Review]` (bug) вАФ minor
`[x]` рЯФІ fixed 2026-06-15 (branch `doc-review/b19-resume-resave`, alongside B19): (a) the flush now gates its cloud upsert on a `dirtyRef` (set on a real edit, cleared on a successful write), so a singleвЖФstitch toggle with no change no longer re-upserts; (b) `ReviewsBar.refresh` is token-guarded (latest wins) and its outside-click listener moved to its own effect; (c) `ProjectLibrary.refresh` is token-guarded too, so an overlapping/late refresh (incl. `fileDrop`'s) can't clobber newer state. (a) `useReviewPersistence`'s unmount cleanup unconditionally fires a cloud `upsert` on every singleвЖФstitch mode toggle (wasteful double-write even when nothing changed) вАФ gate on a dirty flag. (b) `ReviewsBar` re-runs `listReviews()+listProjects()` on every `signedIn` flip while open and has no in-flight guard, so a slow resolution can clobber newer state; (c) `ProjectLibrary.fileDrop` calls `refresh()` in `finally` even if the drawer closed, and overlapping refreshes can interleave. Fix: split outside-click vs fetch effects and add an `ignore`/AbortController guard; `useCallback` the refreshers.

### B45 вАФ Stitcher keeps large PNG data URLs for every placed sheet in state `[Document Review]` (bug) вАФ perf, medium
`[x]` рЯФІ fixed 2026-06-15 (branch `chore/audit-safe-fixes-b39-b45`): `renderPageToImage` now returns a `URL.createObjectURL` blob URL (data-URL fallback), and the Stitcher revokes URLs as sheets leave state via a diff effect + unmount cleanup. `renderPageToImage` returns `canvas.toDataURL("image/png")` at scale 2 and each placed sheet stores that multi-MB base64 string in `placed[].href`; reloads/re-binds regenerate them without releasing the old ones (data URLs can't be revoked). Fix: use `canvas.toBlob` + `URL.createObjectURL`, track and `revokeObjectURL` on remove/replace/unmount.

### B46 вАФ `LayerPanel` Mapillary token desyncs across its two instances `[Site Planner]` (bug) вАФ minor
`[x]` The token is seeded once via `useState(() => mapillaryToken())` in each `LayerPanel` (map + planner both render one); typing in one doesn't update the other's local `tok`, and an externally-set token isn't reflected on reopen. Fix: lift the token to shared state (alongside `overlays`) or read from a subscribable source.
> Progress 2026-06-15: deferred from the map/GIS robustness PR вАФ minor. Clean fix = either lift the token to shared app state (thread alongside `overlays`) or add a tiny pub/sub in `evidenceLayers.js` (`setMapillaryToken` notifies listeners; each `LayerPanel` subscribes via an effect and updates its `tok`). Left Open for that small refactor.

### B47 вАФ ArcGIS `where`-clause hardening (LIKE wildcards + auto-detected field names) `[Site Planner]` (bug) вАФ security, medium
`[x]` рЯФІ fixed 2026-06-15 (branch `site-planner/map-gis-robustness`) вАФ **part (b)**: the parcel-lookup `where` builder now validates `idField`/`addrField` against `/^[A-Za-z0-9_.]+$/` before interpolating, so a hostile/compromised (or user-pasted) layer's metadata can't inject a field name that escapes the `scopeWhere` county confinement. **Part (a)** вАФ escaping `%`/`_` LIKE wildcards via an `ESCAPE` clause вАФ is **deferred** (must verify Harris/FBCAD accept `ESCAPE` before shipping; low risk вАФ read-only public data). A security pass found the rest of the app **clean** (Supabase queries are parameterized with no injection surface; RLS/storage policies sound; secrets handled correctly; all text/SVG render paths are React-escaped). The one item: the parcel-lookup `where` builder escapes the user *value*'s quotes (`'`вЖТ`''`, blocks the realistic breakout) but (a) does not escape LIKE wildcards `%`/`_` (a value of `%` enumerates rows вАФ minor, public read-only data; the statewide TxGIO/Chambers layer is still confined by `scopeWhere`), and (b) interpolates `idField`/`addrField` **unescaped** вАФ and those come from live layer metadata (or a user-pasted "Service / layer URL"), so a hostile/compromised endpoint could inject a field name that defeats the `scopeWhere` county confinement. Read-only/public so not critical. Fix: validate the detected field name against an identifier allowlist (`/^[A-Za-z0-9_.]+$/` and/or `meta.fields.some(f=>f.name===idField)`) before interpolating, and escape `%`/`_` with an `ESCAPE` clause (verify the CAD datasources accept `ESCAPE` before shipping вАФ don't break Harris/FBCAD search).

### B48 вАФ Client-side Anthropic key (title reader) + reusable HTML-escape helper `[Site Planner]` (bug) вАФ note, low
`[x]` `lib/titleReader.js` instantiates the Anthropic SDK in the browser with `dangerouslyAllowBrowser:true` and the user's own key from `localStorage` (`planarfit:anthropicKey`). This is the documented BYO-key, no-backend pattern (not a committed/bundled secret), but the key is localStorage-resident and reachable by any script on the origin. Acceptable for a personal tool; harden later by moving the call behind the planned `/server` (key stays server-side) or keeping it in memory only. Also: `printPDF`'s `esc` helper only escapes `&`/`<` (fine for its text/title contexts today) вАФ make it also escape `"`/`>` before reusing it in any attribute/style context.

### B49 вАФ Document Review file-input validation `[Document Review]` (bug) вАФ crash/correctness
`[x]` рЯФІ partially fixed in audit PR. (a) **fixed:** the single-sheet viewer's open/drop accepted ANY file and read the whole thing into memory via `arrayBuffer()` before failing (OOM risk on a huge/non-PDF drop) вАФ now validated by type + non-zero size before `loadPdf`, mirroring the stitcher. (b) **left for review:** the stitcher sniffs only by `.pdf` extension, and its multi-file load loop is in a single `try`, so one bad file silently skips the rest вАФ wrap each `loadPdf` per-file and size-check.

### B50 вАФ Export/print & prompt robustness `[Site Planner]` (bug) вАФ minor
`[x]` рЯФІ partially fixed in audit PR. (a) **fixed:** the per-edge setback `window.prompt` treated an empty/whitespace confirm as `0` (`+""===0`) instead of cancelling вАФ now requires a non-blank numeric. (b) **left for review:** `exportPNG` swallows raster failures (an `image.onerror` rejects with no `.catch`/feedback; `canvas.toBlob`вЖТnull silently produces no download) and `printPDF` can leave a stranded blank print window if serialization throws after `window.open` вАФ wrap both in try/catch with a user alert (and `win.close()` on failure). `titleReader` base64-encodes with no size/type guard. (Export filename sanitization, object-URL revocation, empty-state guards, and calibration numeric guards were all audited and are clean.)
> Progress 2026-06-15 (branch `site-planner/export-robustness-b50`): part (b) done вАФ `exportPNG` now alerts on an image-load / canvas-taint / `drawImage` failure (was a silent no-op + unhandled rejection) and on a null `toBlob` result; `printPDF` wraps its post-`window.open` work in try/catch and calls `win.close()` on failure, so a serialization/inlining throw can't strand a blank "PreparingвА¶" window. Remaining: the `titleReader` base64 size/type guard (BYO-key path, low priority).

### B51 вАФ Stitcher async handlers have no in-flight guard вЖТ re-entrant interleave corrupts placed sheets `[Document Review]` (bug) вАФ data-loss, high
`[x]` рЯФІ fixed 2026-06-15 (branch `doc-review/async-safety`): `loadStitch` sets a `loadingRef` while it rebuilds `pdfs[]`/`placed[]`, and `openFiles`/`addSheet` bail when it's set вАФ so a click during a load can't have its sheet clobbered by the load's blind `setPlaced(out)`. (`bindSource` stays unguarded; it's internal to `openFiles`.) `openFiles`/`addSheet`/`bindSource`/`loadStitch` each `setBusy(true)вА¶awaitвА¶finally setBusy(false)` but none *reads* busy as a re-entrancy guard, and they mix functional updates (`addSheet`: `setPlaced(arr=>[...arr,вА¶])`) with snapshot overwrites (`loadStitch`: `setPlaced(out)`). Clicking "add sheet" while a load is mid-await lets the load's blind `setPlaced(out)` clobber the just-added sheet. Fix: `busyRef` guard at the top of each, or disable the tray/open while busy; prefer functional updates / reconcile rather than overwrite.

### B52 вАФ Doc Review load/open paths lack a cancellation token вЖТ opening B while A loads mixes the two `[Document Review]` (bug) вАФ correctness, high
`[x]` рЯФІ fixed 2026-06-15 (branch `doc-review/async-safety`): both load paths capture a `loadTok` at start and bail before each post-await `setState` if a newer open superseded them вАФ `loadStitch` before `setPdfs`/`setPlaced`; `loadSingleReview`/`fetchSourceBytes` before `setPdfDoc` (destroying the late doc) вАФ so opening B while A loads can't land A's PDF/sheets on B. `loadStitch` (Stitcher) and `openReview`вЖТ`loadSingleReview`вЖТ`fetchSourceBytes` (DocReview) run long await chains (download + loadPdf + render) and then unconditionally `setState` (reviewId, meta, markups, pdfRef, placed) with no "is this still the requested review?" check. Open review A then B quickly and A's late resolution overwrites B's PDF/sheets while ids/markups are B's вАФ and the autosave then persists the mix under the wrong id. Fix: capture a token (the requested `rec.id`) in a ref and bail before each post-await `setState` if superseded (mirror the single-sheet `renderTok` pattern). Related to B19.

### B53 вАФ In-planner `identifyAt` lacks a token вЖТ second click shows/adds the wrong parcel `[Site Planner]` (bug) вАФ correctness, medium
`[x]` рЯФІ fixed 2026-06-15 (branch `site-planner/map-gis-robustness`): `identifyAt` captures an `identifyTok` at call start and bails before `setIdentifyRes` if a newer click superseded it (matches the single-sheet `renderTok` pattern). `identifyAt` (SitePlanner) sets `{busy:true}`, awaits `resolveLayerUrl`/`queryAtPoint`, then unconditionally `setIdentifyRes({attrs,ring,вА¶})`. Clicking P2 before P1 resolves lets P1 overwrite P2's result, so the panel/`addIdentifiedParcel` use the wrong lot. (Distinct code path from the already-logged MapFinder `handleClick` race, B22.) Fix: a token captured at call start, checked before the post-await `setState`.

### B54 вАФ `pullCloud` overwrites the per-user cache with `{}` when a cloud fetch errors `[Site Planner]` (bug) вАФ data-loss-shaped, medium
`[x]` рЯФІ fixed 2026-06-15 (branch `site-planner/b54-cloud-pull-guard`): `cloudList` now THROWS on a real fetch error (vs. a genuinely-empty result); `pullCloud` catches it, SKIPS the cache write, and returns `{ ok:false }`, so the cache (the user's last-known sites) is preserved; `applyUser` then shows a dismissible "showing your last synced copy" banner instead of a silent empty library. B18's separate half (merge-by-`updatedAt` + `sendBeacon`-on-pagehide) stays open вАФ it carries a delete-resurrection subtlety, so it's deliberately left under B18. `cloudList` returns `[]` on *error* (cloudSync.js), so `pullCloud` can't tell "no sites" from "fetch failed" and blind-writes an empty map to the per-user cache; signing in while offline/unreachable thus shows "no sites" and wipes the local cloud cache to empty (data safe in Supabase, but a scary empty state that the user might start recreating into). Fix: have `cloudList` throw/return a status on error; `pullCloud` must skip the cache overwrite on error and surface a "couldn't load" state. (Sharpens B18/B37d into a concrete fix.)

### B55 вАФ Fire-and-forget promises without `.catch` вЖТ unhandled rejections; async continuations touch torn-down objects `[Document Review / Site Planner]` (bug) вАФ minor
`[x]` `uploadSource(...).then(...)` (DocReview + Stitcher), the `usePersistence` unmount/visibility `flush()` cloud upsert, and the `probeService(...).then(...)` overlay continuation all lack `.catch`, so a rejected Storage/DB/network call is an unhandled rejection. The `probeService` continuation also does `lyr.addTo(map)` after the await with no map-teardown guard (can throw if the map was removed mid-probe). Fix: add `.catch(()=>{})` to the fire-and-forget calls (matching the `pushSiteToCloud(...).catch` convention) and guard `addTo` with `map._loaded`.

### B56 вАФ Assorted async UX/robustness `[Site Planner / Document Review]` (bug) вАФ minor
`[x]` Grouped: (a) `goAddress` double-submit вАФ Enter isn't gated by `busy` (only the Go button is), so two geocodes can race the `flyTo`; (b) transient `overlapWarn` messages each schedule their own `setTimeout(()=>setOverlapWarn(""))` with the id discarded, so a stale clear blanks a newer warning (and `runXSection` has no in-flight guard); (c) `setProjectStatus` upserts group rows serially and ignores per-row failure, returning `ok:true` even if one plan kept the old status (inconsistent group status) вАФ use `Promise.allSettled` and report partial failure; (d) the evidence layers drop `moveend` events that arrive while a fetch is in flight (no trailing-edge refresh), so the last view may never load; (e) the doc-review mutation handlers (`del`/`onStatus`/`fileDrop`) call `refresh()` after an await with no open/mounted guard.
> Progress 2026-06-15: (a) shipped in #30, (d) in #33; **(c) done here** (branch `chore/audit-tail-grind` вАФ `setProjectStatus` now writes the group's plans in parallel via `Promise.allSettled` and returns partial-failure counts); (e) covered by the B44 in-flight guards (PR #32). **(b)** вАФ the `overlapWarn` stale-timer вАФ left open: the clean fix is a single timer-ref `flashWarn` helper across ~12 call sites (or a uniform auto-clear effect that would flatten per-message durations); minor UX, not worth churning 12 sites.
> **(b) done 2026-06-17 (branch `claude/keen-curie-2ic2cg`) вАФ this closes B56 (a/c/d/e already shipped).** A single timer-ref `flashWarn(msg, ms)` helper now owns the warning toast: it cancels any pending auto-clear *before* showing a new message, so a stale timer from an earlier warning can no longer blank a newer one. All 32 message-setting `setOverlapWarn(...)` sites route through it вАФ transient ones pass their duration; sticky instructional prompts pass `ms=0` (no auto-clear, but they still cancel a prior timer so a stale clear can't wipe them either). The bare `setOverlapWarn("")` clears (Escape, Cancel, toggle-off) stay as-is: a later `flashWarn` cancels any lingering timer, and a fired timer just re-blanks an already-empty toast. Also fixed the second half of (b): `runXSection` got the missing in-flight guard (`xsecBusyRef` bails a second cross-section run while one is still sampling, reset in `finally`), plus an unmount cleanup that clears the pending timer. lint 0 err ¬Ј 174 tests ¬Ј build green ¬Ј lazy split intact. Browser-verify logged as **V23**.

### B58 вАФ Ditch cross-section drops no-data DEM samples without preserving position вЖТ wrong pond depth `[Site Planner]` (bug) вАФ correctness, high
`[x]` рЯФІ fixed 2026-06-15 (branch `site-planner/b58-b62-planner-correctness`): `sampleProfile` now keeps no-data as `null` (position preserved), and `ditchStats` places each surviving sample at its true fractional distance and takes banks from the end-most VALID samples. `sampleProfile` (elevation.js) does `.filter(v=>isFinite(v))`, discarding position; `ditchStats` then assumes uniform spacing (`d = i/(n-1)*lenFt`) and takes `bankFt = (elevFt[0]+elevFt[n-1])/2`. 3DEP commonly returns no-data over water/low ground, so surviving samples aren't evenly spaced вАФ the profile x-axis is distorted, and if the true endpoints were no-data the "bank" is taken from interior points, so `depthFt` (the headline number applied to the pond's available depth) is wrong. (Distinct from the B23 1-sample NaN.) Fix: map each sample to its fractional position BEFORE filtering; treat leading/trailing no-data as missing banks rather than substituting interior points.

### B59 вАФ Parking render/count/panel ignore per-element `cfg` вЖТ "Drive aisle on the far side" toggle is inert `[Site Planner]` (bug) вАФ correctness, high
`[x]` рЯФІ fixed 2026-06-15 (branch `site-planner/b58-b62-planner-correctness`): all three `carStalls(...)` calls now pass `cfgOf(el)` (which merges `{...settings, ...el.cfg}`), so a field's per-element `flipDepth`/depth/aisle/angle take effect in count + render вАФ the "Drive aisle on the far side" toggle works. The renderer, metrics, and panel all call `carStalls(el.w, el.h, settings)` with the GLOBAL settings, never `cfgOf(el)`, so a parking field's per-element `cfg` (notably `flipDepth`, and side-parking strips created with `cfg`) has no visual/count effect вАФ the panel's "Drive aisle on the far side" checkbox writes `cfg.flipDepth` but nothing reads it for drawing. Trailer rendering correctly uses `el.cfg`, so it's an inconsistency. Fix: use `cfgOf(el)` (which merges `{...settings, ...el.cfg}`) in the three `carStalls(...)` call sites.

### B60 вАФ Detention bottom area spuriously non-zero when the basin over-tapers `[Site Planner]` (bug) вАФ correctness, medium
`[x]` рЯФІ fixed 2026-06-15 (branch `site-planner/b58-b62-planner-correctness`): `areaAt` now compares the offset ring's SIGNED area to the footprint's and returns 0 on a winding-sign flip (over-taper), so the bogus positive bottom is gone and the "tapers to a point" guard fires. `detentionStorage`'s `areaAt(down)` returns `offsetPolygon(ring, slope*down)` area; when `slope*depth` exceeds the footprint's inradius, `offsetPolygon` yields an inverted (flipped) ring rather than null, and the self-check uses `polyArea` (abs value), so a bogus positive "bottom" passes. Result: overestimated prismoidal volume and the "Basin tapers to a point вАФ reduce depth/slope" guard (`aBottom===0`) never fires. Fix: detect collapse via a signed-area sign flip (or offset distance вЙ• inradius) and return 0.

### B61 вАФ Two-click road drawn shorter than it is wide mis-assigns the length/cross axis `[Site Planner]` (bug) вАФ minor
`[x]` Road creation sets `w:len, h:roadWidth+2*curb`, but downstream infers the cross axis from `min(w,h)` (curb render `el.w>=el.h`; `roadTravel` `min`; resize `el.h<=el.w`). A stubby road (`len < cross`) has `w<h`, so curbs draw on the wrong edges and the length/width fields control the swapped axis. Fix: tag an explicit length axis at creation and key rendering/resize off it (or clamp `len>=cross`).
> Progress 2026-06-15: deferred from round-2 вАФ a complete fix needs an explicit length-axis tag threaded through render/resize/roadTravel; a creation-time clamp alone leaves resize able to reproduce it. Left Open for that focused change.

### B62 вАФ Utility-route corridor leaves a visible gap to the fitting pad `[Site Planner]` (bug) вАФ minor, cosmetic
`[x]` рЯФІ fixed 2026-06-15 (branch `site-planner/b58-b62-planner-correctness`): the route now includes the pad centre (`pts=[source, entry, padC]`), so the corridor reaches the fitting pad. `buildUtilRoute` buffers `pts=[source, entry]` where `entry` is on the wall, but the pad sits outside the wall (`entry + normal*(padSize/2+3)`), so the drawn corridor never reaches the pad. Fix: include the pad center in the route (`pts=[source, entry, padC]`) before buffering. (Math/easement-width/overlap checks are otherwise correct.)

<!-- Filed 2026-06-15 from a parallel chat's backlog (its provisional B13вАУB16 were reassigned here; B1вАУB12 + protocol deduped against existing items, which already shipped). -->

### B67 вАФ Attach & mark up a site-plan drawing on a parcel `[Site Planner]` (feature)
`[x]` **Done 2026-06-16 (browser-only tranche complete: MVP + increments 2a/2b/2c).** Let the user attach an existing site plan (PDF or JPEG; CAD/DWG out of scope for v1) to a selected parcel and draw on top of it with the full existing markup/element toolset, saved as a persistent, named file tied to that parcel. The pattern mirrors Document Review's **immutable-backdrop + editable-layers-above** model and its Supabase persistence вАФ reuse those patterns, don't stand up a parallel drawing engine or store. (Related to but distinct from B14, which files drawings under *projects* in the Document Review workspace; this attaches to a *parcel* in the Site Planner and marks up with the planner's own tools.)
- **Entry point.** After clicking a parcel (e.g. the Schiel Road site), offer "Attach drawing" / "Open markup." Allow **multiple drawings per parcel** (a parcel may have several plan sheets).
- **Backdrop = immutable layer.** The imported PDF/JPEG is the locked backdrop (architecture invariant: imported drawing = immutable; user content lives on editable layers above). PDF вЖТ rasterize the chosen page to an image for display; if multipage, let the user pick the page.
- **Markup layer = editable.** Reuse the current `els` + `markups` suite (lines, polylines, polygons, text, dimensions, freehand вАФ whatever the suite already supports), not a separate drawing engine.
- **Anchoring v1 = pixel-relative to the backdrop.** Store markup coordinates **normalized to the backdrop's intrinsic pixel dimensions (0вАУ1 fractions, not screen pixels)** so zoom/pan can't corrupt geometry. Nothing may assume the backdrop is screen-sized.
- **Forward-compat for georeference (deferred).** Persist the backdrop's **intrinsic dimensions** and (for a PDF) **page size/DPI** alongside the markup вАФ the minimum needed later to compute a pixelвЖТTexas-State-Plane (EPSG:2278) transform without re-marking. No georeferencing UI in v1; just don't discard the data that makes it possible.
- **Persistence.** Save as a named file/record associated with the parcel through the existing Supabase save/load + RLS path (**private by default**). Reopening restores backdrop + markup layer.
- **Out of scope v1 (follow-ons):** CAD/DWG import; real-world georeferencing; and **overlaying the marked-up plan onto the live map/aerial** вАФ that last is the "overlay onto site" goal that converges with the вШЕ north-star ("map вЖТ drawings вЖТ latest set") and the shared coordinate spine. Flagged here as a follow-on, not v1.
> Cross-ref 2026-06-15: the deferred "overlay onto the live map/aerial" follow-on noted just above is now a filed item вАФ **B72** (drag-drop a site-plan PDF onto the map, place by hand) + **B73** (scale calibration / precise alignment). B67 stays distinct (parcel-attached markup in *pixel* space), but shares the immutable-backdrop + PDF-rasterize + Supabase machinery вАФ build them on the same primitives.
> Progress 2026-06-16 (branch `claude/laughing-babbage-hrxgct`): **browser-only MVP shipped + screenshot-verified.** Select a parcel вЖТ Parcel panel вЖТ **"пЉЛ Attach a drawing (PDF / JPG)"** вЖТ it rasterizes the file (reusing the B72 `openOverlayFile` engine вАФ PDF.js via dynamic import, off the main thread; image path too) and opens a full-screen **`ParcelDrawing`** markup modal: the imported file is an **immutable backdrop** and you draw on an editable layer above it with **Select / Pen / Line / Box / Text**, a colour picker, delete, fit/zoom/pan. **Markups are stored PIXEL-RELATIVE (0..1)** of the backdrop's intrinsic dims, so zoom/pan can't corrupt them (verified: a seeded rect + text land exactly on the backdrop). **Multiple drawings per parcel** (listed in the panel, open/delete). **Persistence:** additive Site Model field **`parcelDrawings`** (`SITE_MODEL_VERSION` 4вЖТ5, `parcelDrawingsOf` selector, `slimForCloud` strips the raster like the overlay/underlay); saved via a `saveSite` MERGE + debounced cloud push, so it needs no new wiring through the autosave path and **existing sites are unaffected** (empty field = no-op). **Forward-compat:** the backdrop's intrinsic dims (PDF points) ride with each record for a future pixelвЖТEPSG:2278 transform. The modal **portals to `<body>`** so its toolbar clears the shell header (B66 stacking floor). **lint 0 ¬Ј 56 tests (incl. a new parcelDrawings test) ¬Ј build green.** вП≥ **Deferred to a focused increment 2 (B67 stays `[ ]`):** (a) the **multipage page-picker** (page 1 only today; `pageCount` is stored); (b) **Supabase Storage backing** of the source file so the raster reloads cross-device (today the raster is local + stripped from the cloud row вЖТ a re-login shows a "re-attach to view; markups saved" placeholder, exactly like B72's first increment; **markups always persist**); (c) richer markup parity with the planner's full suite (dimensions/measure, freehand smoothing) and on-backdrop markup editing/move (today: draw + select + delete + recolour). Runtime-verified headless via `ui-audit/screens/parcel-drawing.png`; please also try it on planyr.io with a real PDF.
> Progress 2026-06-16 (increment 2a вАФ page-picker, branch `claude/laughing-babbage-hrxgct`): **multi-page PDFs now prompt a "Pick a sheet" dialog** at attach (lists all `pageCount` pages; the chosen sheet rasterizes via the B72 `rasterizePage`, reusing the already-loaded PDF for page 1; the record is named `"<file> вАФ p.N"`). The PDF proxy is kept alive only for the pick then destroyed (no leak). Single-page PDFs and images skip the dialog. Removes limit (a). lint 0 ¬Ј 138 tests ¬Ј build green.
> Progress 2026-06-16 (increment 2b вАФ Storage backing, branch `claude/laughing-babbage-hrxgct`): **the source file now backs the backdrop in Supabase Storage for cross-device reload.** On attach, the original PDF/image is uploaded (background, fallback-safe) to the existing private `doc-review-files` bucket at `<uid>/parcel-drawings/<siteId>/<drawingId>.<ext>` (new `uploadParcelDrawingFile` in `overlayStorage.js`, uid-first so the existing Storage RLS holds); the returned `storageKey`+`ext` persist on the record (kept through `slimForCloud`, which only strips the raster). Opening a drawing whose local raster is missing (cross-device вАФ the cloud row's `src` was stripped) **rehydrates** it: download bytes вЖТ `rasterizeStoredPdf(bytes, page)` for PDFs, or `downloadOverlayDataUrl` for images, with a "Loading the drawing from the cloudвА¶" state. Delete now also best-effort-removes the stored object. All fallback-safe (logged-out / >50 MB / error вЖТ keeps the local raster, no regression). Mirrors B72's overlay Storage-backing exactly. This **closes limit (b)**. Remaining for B67: (c) richer markup parity (dimensions/measure, move/edit existing markups). lint 0 ¬Ј 138 tests ¬Ј build green; **cohort to confirm the cross-device round-trip live** (`VERIFICATION.md` V9) вАФ can't be exercised headless (needs a signed-in session + Storage).
> Progress 2026-06-16 (increment 2c вАФ richer markup, branch `claude/laughing-babbage-hrxgct`): **closes limit (c); B67 вЖТ done.** In `ParcelDrawing.jsx`: (1) **move** any existing markup вАФ in Select, press-and-drag a shape/text to reposition it (cursor shows в§Іmove; a transient `moving` overlay avoids a save per pointer-move, commits once on release, pixel-relative throughout); (2) **edit text** in place (double-click вАФ preserved); (3) a **Measure tool + one-time Scale calibration**: draw a **Scale** line and enter its real length вЖТ sets feet-per-pixel; the **Measure** tool then labels each line's true length in feet (teal chip), live while drawing. The calibration is stored as a `type:'calib'` markup, so it **persists through the same `onSave(markups)` channel** вАФ no extra plumbing. Verified headless (`ui-audit/screens/parcel-drawing.png`: a 0.26-wide measure line reads **124 ft** against a 200-ft / 0.42-wide scale вЬУ). Optional future niceties (not blocking): resize/rotate handles on a selected shape. lint 0 ¬Ј 138 tests ¬Ј build green.

### B69 вАФ Paving "+" over-increments from a single-loaded bay `[Site Planner]` (bug)
`[x]` Repro: start from the ~42вАУ47вА≤ paving cross-section (one parking row + one drive aisle вАФ a single-loaded bay = parking on one side of the aisle only) and click "+". **Observed:** it added two parking rows plus another drive aisle (a full double-loaded module). **Expected:** "+" adds exactly one parking row вАФ from a single-loaded bay it converts to double-loaded (parking both sides of the existing aisle, ~60вАУ65вА≤); a new drive aisle is inserted only once the current aisle is already double-loaded; each click steps by one row, never a two-row module. (Filed from a parallel chat as provisional "NEW-1"; minted **B69** here вАФ B67/B68 were already taken on `main`.)
> Done 2026-06-15 (branch `claude/nice-wozniak-2k2v9c`). **Root cause:** `growParking` stepped depth by a whole `stallDepth+aisle` band per click, but the renderer/counter (`carStalls`) re-flows the field into *double-loaded modules* (2 rows share 1 aisle), so a single band of added depth re-striped into ~2 extra rows + an aisle вАФ the jump the report saw. (Distinct from the already-fixed B29/B59, which were per-element `cfg` plumbing in the same area, not the increment model.) **Fix:** two pure helpers вАФ `parkDepthForRows(n)= n¬ЈstallDepth + вМИn/2вМЙ¬Јaisle` and its inverse `parkRowsForDepth(h)` вАФ model double-loading explicitly; `growParking` now reads the current row count and sets the depth for `n¬±1`, so the increment alternates +stallDepth (singleвЖТdouble-loads the last aisle) / +stallDepth+aisle (adds a new aisle) exactly as specced. `setParkCfg`, `splitParkingRows`, `canShrink`, and the two "Split into rows" `вЙ•2` gates were moved onto the same row model so depthвЖФrows stays consistent; the "+" button/tooltip relabelled "пЉЛ Row" / "Add one parking row" (was "Row + aisle"). Verified: 42вЖТ60вЖТ102вЖТ120вЖТ162 (rows 1вЖТ2вЖТ3вЖТ4вЖТ5, +18/+42/+18/+42), round-trip `rowsвЖФdepth` clean for n=1..8; build + tests pass.

### B70 вАФ Curbs: derived auto-placed bands with visual / calc / dimension rules `[Site Planner]` (feature)
`[x]` Curbs are derived auto-placed thin bands вАФ not user-placed, draggable, or deletable; they float to stay attached to their surface as rows are added/removed. Default = 6вА≥ mono curb ("mono" = single monolithic pour, no gutter pan), occupying 0.5вА≤ of plan-view width. **Placement:** terminal (the outermost band of every section gets a curb on its far/back edge); sidewalk transition (a curb between a sidewalk and the parking/drive it abuts вАФ sidewalk behind, pavement dropping at the curb face); never a building-side curb. **Three-way representation, one rule for all sections (standard / truck court / trailer alike):** always *drawn*; always in the *calculations* (area, yield, paving SF, the width feeding any math вЖТ 18вА≤ stall + 24вА≤ aisle + 0.5вА≤ = 42.5вА≤; a 135вА≤ court = 135.5вА≤); never in the *displayed dimension* (reads 42вА≤, 135вА≤, 185вА≤ вАФ to the face of curb; the 0.5вА≤ lives only in geometry + calc).
> Inspection first (what already existed): **roads already implemented the exact three-way contract** вАФ a road's footprint includes its 6вА≥ curbs (`h = travelW + 2¬Јcurb`), the curbs are drawn as lines, area uses `w¬Јh` (curb included), and the on-canvas dimension shows `travelW` (curb excluded). So the *pattern* was proven; the gap was that **parking, paving/truck-court, and trailer carried no curb at all** (no draw, no calc, no rule). Built only that gap, generalizing the road contract to the other paved types.
> Done 2026-06-15 (branch `claude/nice-wozniak-2k2v9c`). A single derived-curb model (`curbEdgesOf(el, allEls)`, a **module-level** helper вАФ no `cfgOf`/component scope, so it's safe inside `renderElPx`; cf. B68) is the one source feeding both the drawn band and the math: terminal curb on the edge pointing **away** from the host building (so never building-side); a sidewalk-transition curb on the inner edge when a sidewalk/landscape strip sits between the pad and its host; both depth ends for a free-standing field. The element's `w/h` stays the **face-of-curb** size, so (a) the displayed dimension already excludes the curb with no change, and (b) the curb is derived on top and *floats* to the terminal edge as rows change вАФ no stored geometry. **Calc:** `curbAreaOf` (ќ£ edge-length¬Јwidth) is added to the element's paving/parking/trailer bucket and thus to impervious вАФ so a 200вА≤ bay reads 8 500 sf (eff. 42.5вА≤) and a 300вА≤ court reads 40 650 sf (eff. 135.5вА≤), while the on-canvas label still reads 42/135. **Draw:** a thin band whose width *scales* (so the 12вА≥ option visibly doubles the 6вА≥), kept legible by its stroke when the 0.5вА≤ is sub-pixel at low zoom. Roads untouched (excluded from the new model; they keep their own curbs). Build + tests pass.
> Deferred nuance (kept minor, not blocking): the sidewalk-transition and free-field-both-ends cases are geometric heuristics (same-host + inboard; ¬±depth ends) rather than an explicit stored curb edge; polygon (irregular) pads are out of scope for the auto-curb. Revisit if a future case needs a hand-placed/overridden curb edge.

### B71 вАФ Per-element curb override on trailer parking (6вА≥ вЖТ 12вА≥) `[Site Planner]` (feature)
`[x]` Selecting a trailer-parking element exposes a curb selector: default 6вА≥, option 12вА≥ (heavier curb to take trailer-tire/dolly abuse). 12вА≥ = 1.0вА≤ of plan-view width (double the 6вА≥ curb's 0.5вА≤) вАФ real plan width, not a taller face/reveal (height unchanged). Flows through the same three-way rule as B70: drawn in the visual field, included in calculations (a trailer section with a 12вА≥ terminal curb counts the full 1.0вА≤ in area/width math), excluded from the displayed dimension (185вА≤ still reads 185вА≤). Build the property globally underneath (any band could carry it) but surface the control only on trailer parking for now.
> Done 2026-06-15 (branch `claude/nice-wozniak-2k2v9c`). The width is a global per-element field `el.curbW` (`CURB_6 = 0.5` / `CURB_12 = 1.0`) read by `curbWidthOf(el)`, so any band *could* carry it; the **6вА≥ / 12вА≥ control is surfaced only in the selected-trailer panel** (`setCurbW`). It rides the B70 model end-to-end: the drawn band scales to 1.0вА≤ (visibly double), `curbAreaOf` counts the full 1.0вА≤ in the SF/width math, and the displayed dimension is untouched (still face-of-curb). Trailer fields show no on-canvas dimension number today, so there's nothing to wrongly include the curb in; the rule holds the moment one is shown. Verified: a 12вА≥ curb on a 300вА≤ edge = 300 sf vs the 6вА≥ 150 sf; build + tests pass.

### B74 вАФ "New plan, same parcel" drops the site's county вЖТ identify/jurisdiction defaults to Harris `[Site Planner]` (bug) вАФ medium
`[x]` Fixed 2026-06-16. `newPlanSameParcel` (`SitePlannerApp.jsx`) copied origin/parcels/settings/underlay but **not** `county`, so a Fort Bend/Chambers iteration plan normalized to `county:null` and the planner fell back to Harris for click-identify, jurisdiction utility layers, and easement rules. Added `county: src.county || null` to the payload (matches `goPlanFromParcels`). (`duplicatePlan` already spreads `...src`, so it was fine.)

### B75 вАФ Chambers county-acreage check ~10.76√Ч wrong; flags every correct parcel as a huge mismatch `[Site Planner]` (bug) вАФ high
`[x]` Fixed 2026-06-16. The TxGIO statewide source (Chambers) names its already-in-acres fields `GIS_AREA`/`LEGAL_AREA` (with a sibling `*_UNIT`), which the `countyAcres` acres-regex didn't match вЖТ it fell through to a projected `st_area` in m¬≤, √Ј43560 (ft¬≤/ac) вЖТ ~10.76√Ч too small; the old "tenx" m¬≤ guard also corrected the wrong way (√Ј instead of √Ч). `countyAcres` now prefers `gis_area`/`legal_area` when the sibling unit says "Acres"; the geometry-check badge detects an m¬≤-misread Shape area and shows the **corrected** acreage (a correct lot reads вЬУ, not "900% off вЦ≤"). Badge-only вАФ never fed the yield math (which uses the drawn polygon).

### B76 вАФ Cross-county OBJECTID selection-key collision mis-toggles parcels `[Site Planner / map]` (bug) вАФ medium
`[x]` Fixed 2026-06-16. `MapFinder.handleClick` keyed selected parcels by bare `OBJECTID`, which is unique only within one CAD layer вАФ a multi-county assembly with two lots sharing an id would toggle each other off (and corrupt the assembled acreage). Key is now namespaced `"<county>:<oid>"`. (Distinct from the B22 rapid-click race; the dedupe/hilite guards there are unchanged.)

### B77 вАФ `fileNewReview` ignores upload failure вЖТ silently files an unopenable document `[Document Review]` (bug) вАФ medium
`[x]` Fixed 2026-06-16. A non-oversize `uploadSource` failure (network/RLS/transient 5xx) was stored as a normal source (`storageKey:null, oversize:false`) and `fileNewReview` returned `ok:true` with no feedback. It now returns `{ uploadFailed }`, and `ProjectLibrary.fileDrop` collects failures and alerts ("filed, but the upload failed вАФ re-drop on open to view"). (On load a null key already showed the re-drop banner/placeholder; the gap was no warning at file time.)

### B78 вАФ Parking/trailer stall layout can infinite-loop (freeze) on a degenerate config `[Site Planner]` (bug) вАФ critical (latent)
`[x]` Fixed 2026-06-16. `carStalls`/`trailerStalls` compute `mod = rowDepth*2 + aisle` then `mods = floor(h/mod)` and loop `mods` times; `mod===0` (0 stall-depth + 0 aisle) makes `mods` Infinity вЖТ an unbounded band loop that hard-freezes the tab (and a 0 stall-width/`tw` made `perRow` Infinity вЖТ unbounded render loop). The current UI clamps these inputs (`min` 1/8/1), so it's **not reachable from the fields today** вАФ the live freeze a sibling audit saw was a transient mid-deploy regression вАФ but legacy/`cfg`-merged data could still hit it, so added an early-return guard (`mod>0 && pitch>0`; `tw>0`) to both.

### B79 вАФ Negative/zero Grid size infinite-loops the grid render; size fields have no upper bound `[Site Planner]` (bug) вАФ high (latent)
`[x]` Fixed 2026-06-16. `gridLines` used `step = settings.gridSize` directly; a 0/negative step made `for (xвА¶; x += step)` never terminate (freeze). Clamped `step = Math.max(0.1, +gridSize || 10)`. The Grid field's `min={1}` already blocks it from the UI; this hardens the loop itself. Also added `max={MAX_DIM}` (100000 ft) to the element Width/Depth fields so a fat-fingered/pasted size can't produce absurd geometry or SVG-coordinate stalls.

### B80 вАФ Underlay calibration divides by zero on a 0 ft/px underlay `[Site Planner]` (bug) вАФ low
`[x]` Fixed 2026-06-16. `applyCalibration` guarded `knownFt>0`/`measured>0` but not `underlay.ftPerPx>0`; a degenerate underlay вЖТ Infinity/NaN placement (image flies off-canvas). Added `underlay.ftPerPx > 0` to the guard (covers the derived `sy` too).

### B81 вАФ Self-intersecting / near-zero polygons accepted everywhere вЖТ silently wrong area `[Site Planner]` (bug) вАФ medium
`[x]` Fixed 2026-06-16. Parcel/element/measure-area close handlers only gated on vertex count; a bow-tie outline closes and `polyArea` (abs shoelace) returns the *net* area (lobes cancel) with no warning, corrupting siteSqft вЖТ coverage/FAR/parking/detention. Added `polySelfIntersects` + `flashPolyWarn` on close (parcel / drawn element / measured area): warns on a self-crossing or ~zero-area outline (accepts but flags, so the number isn't trusted silently).

### B82 вАФ Calibrate tool is a silent no-op with no underlay `[Site Planner]` (bug) вАФ low
`[x]` Fixed 2026-06-16. Calibrate sits in the main toolbar (selectable with no underlay); clicks hit `if (!underlay) return` silently. Now flashes "Calibrate needs an underlay вАФ drop an aerial/screenshot first."

### B83 вАФ Copy/Duplicate carries dangling host/court metadata `[Site Planner]` (bug) вАФ low
`[x]` Fixed 2026-06-16. Paste/duplicate stripped only `attachedTo`, keeping `truckCourt`/`forCourt`/`dogEar`/`oppSide`/side-park/sidewalk tags вАФ so a copied child carried court metadata pointing at nothing (refit/trailer logic reads it). Added a shared `detachClone` that strips all relational tags on clone. (Copying a host building's whole attached assembly is a separate enhancement вАФ noted, not done.)

### B84 вАФ Metes/POB plot silently cancels when no bearings parsed `[Site Planner]` (bug) вАФ low
`[x]` Fixed 2026-06-16. `anchorEncumbrance` returned silently when the description produced 0 calls (e.g. an unreadable format). Now warns "No bearings were recognizedвА¶", with a separate message when the calls can't form a shape. (The underlying curve/dash-DMS parser gaps stay under B25/B26.)

### B85 вАФ Empty callout left on Escape; zero-length cross-section makes a degenerate profile `[Site Planner]` (bug) вАФ low
`[x]` Fixed 2026-06-16. The global Escape cleared `calloutDraft` but not an in-progress empty *new* callout вАФ now calls `cancelEditCallout()` (added `editCallout` to the keydown effect deps so the closure stays fresh). `runXSection` now requires `lenFt > 1` (a same-point cross-section produced NaN profile distances).

### B86 вАФ Split tool corrupts area on concave parcels `[Site Planner]` (bug) вАФ high
`[x]` Fixed 2026-06-16 (complements B31). `splitPolygon` keys off the extreme-`t` crossings, so a straight cut across a concave parcel (4+ crossings) can yield overlapping/omitting halves whose areas don't sum to the original вЖТ wrong siteSqft + every downstream yield. Added an **area-conservation + self-intersection guard** in `performSplit`: if the two pieces don't conserve area (¬±2%) or come out self-intersecting, the cut is rejected with "that cut crosses the parcel ambiguously вАФ try a straight cut between two opposite edges," instead of saving corrupted geometry. (A full polygon-clipping rewrite for multi-piece concave cuts stays deferred per B31.)

### B87 вАФ `Infinity` / scientific-notation in a numeric field bypasses the min-clamp вЖТ NaN geometry, persisted as null `[Site Planner]` (bug) вАФ high
`[x]` Fixed 2026-06-16. `NumInput.commit` rejected only `isNaN`, but `parseFloat("1e999")`/`"Infinity"` return `Infinity` (not NaN) and `Math.max(min, Infinity)===Infinity`, so a non-finite value slipped through вАФ Grid=Infinity made `snap` return NaN (every new coord NaN), a size=Infinity drew nothing, and `JSON.stringify` then persisted NaN/Infinity as **null** (permanent corruption). Now requires `Number.isFinite(n)` and applies a default `1e7` upper cap when no explicit `max`; `snap` also guards a non-finite/вЙ§0 grid (falls back to 10). Closes the persist-as-null source (B91).

### B88 вАФ Type confusion: a record whose `parcels`/`els` isn't an array crashes the whole app `[Site Planner]` (bug) вАФ medium
`[x]` Fixed 2026-06-16. `createSiteModel` kept any truthy value (`p.parcels || []`), so a tampered/legacy/bad-sync record with a non-array collection flowed into `parcels.reduce(...)` вЖТ `TypeError` вЖТ blank app on load. Now coerces every collection (`Array.isArray(...) ? ... : []`) and `settings` to an object. Added a unit test (40 tests pass). (The B68 error boundary already contained the blank-screen; this stops the throw so the site actually loads.)

### B89 вАФ "Travel widths" free-text feeds road geometry вЖТ NaN roads `[Site Planner]` (bug) вАФ medium
`[x]` Fixed 2026-06-16. The road-width preset list `.split(",")` of the free-text field offered any token (e.g. `abc`) as a selectable width; drawing with it did `+"abc" = NaN` вЖТ a NaN road persisted as null. The preset list now keeps only finite, positive numeric tokens.

### B90 вАФ No cross-tab reconciliation: a second tab's finder list goes stale `[Site Planner]` (bug) вАФ mediumвЖТlow
`[x]` Fixed 2026-06-16. Added a `window` `storage` listener that refreshes the finder list when another tab changes the site store. **Re-scoped on inspection:** the audit's "whole-store clobber" doesn't actually reproduce вАФ `saveSite`/`deleteSite` already read-modify-write the latest store per call, so a second tab editing a *different* site can't wipe the first's work; the real symptom was a stale list, which this fixes (logged-in tabs now also pick up each other's cloud-cache writes).

### B91 вАФ NaN/Infinity coordinates persist as `null` (corruption amplifier) `[Site Planner]` (bug) вАФ low
`[x]` Addressed-at-source 2026-06-16. The non-finite *sources* are now closed (B87 NumInput/snap, B89 road widths, plus the B78/B79 freeze guards), so no path feeds a non-finite coordinate into a save. A deep on-save geometry sanitizer was deliberately NOT added вАФ rewriting stored points risks corrupting valid geometry, worse than the rare amplified case it would catch.

### B92 вАФ Unbounded text/emoji/RTL in annotations bloats the SVG/record `[Site Planner]` (bug) вАФ low
`[x]` Fixed 2026-06-16. Callout/text annotations now cap at `maxLength={2000}`. (Injection was already safe вАФ XSS payloads render escaped.)

> **Triaged but NOT changed (still open / deferred, by decision):** building bump-outs aren't clamped when the host shrinks (medium, geometry вАФ risk-deferred); `deleteSite` cloud delete stays fire-and-forget (zombie only if the delete fails вАФ B-class edge); over-quota save still drops the underlay and reports success (graceful-degradation, minor); `currentSite` pointer global-not-per-user (low). County straddle/out-of-coverage messaging stays under **B13/B36**; metes curve + dash-DMS under **B25/B26**; bundle size / Anthropic-SDK / Mapillary-token / Nominatim / deploy-churn remain LOW/infra.

### B93 вАФ Jurisdiction identify: city limits, ETJ & county `[Site Planner / GIS]` (feature) вАФ SHIP target (promoted from deferred 2026-06-17)
`[x]` Click any point вАФ or, **on explicit request**, run on the active parcel вАФ and get back which jurisdictions it falls in: incorporated city (or "unincorporated"), any city **ETJ** (extraterritorial jurisdiction), and county (Harris, Fort Bend, Montgomery, Galveston, BrazoriaвА¶). **Trigger: click / explicit request only вАФ NOT auto-loaded on every parcel.**
- **Interaction:** a map click runs a point-in-polygon "identify" against the loaded boundary layers; also identify-on-demand for the active parcel. **Test the whole parcel, not just its centroid** вАФ flag boundary-straddle (e.g. partly City of Houston, partly unincorporated Harris Co.) and list *every* jurisdiction it touches rather than forcing one answer.
- **Coverage:** Houston-metro priority cities (Houston, Baytown, Missouri City, Sugar Land, Pearland, вА¶), but driven by a **source registry**, never per-city hardcoded logic вАФ adding a city = adding a registry row, not new code.
- **Source-priority chain (the crux):** query in fallback order per layer вАФ authoritative city source where it publishes good GIS (e.g. Houston / COHGIS) вЖТ regional backbone (**H-GAC**, the Houston-Galveston Area Council, whose GIS covers the 13-county region) вЖТ statewide backbone (**TxDOT Open Data**, which publishes city limits + ETJ statewide). **One generic ArcGIS-REST connector** parameterized per source; a registry row stores endpoint URL, layer ID, and a field map. (Same connector serves **B94** вАФ build it once.)
- **Field mapping:** every source names the city field differently (`CITY_NM` / `NAME` / `MUNICIPALITY` вА¶). The registry normalizes each source's schema into one internal shape so the UI is source-agnostic.
- **Reuse existing GIS infra вАФ do NOT build a parallel system:** same cache (**B96**), same per-layer honest status + visible data-age, same ~45 s self-heal re-probe, same Texas State Plane frame.
- **Screening-only framing:** ETJ is volatile (Texas law now lets landowners petition out of a city's ETJ; annexations move city limits) вАФ label results screening-only, always show source + age, never present as a legal/official determination, keep a visible "verify with the jurisdiction" note.
- **Build step before wiring (evidence-first):** confirm each candidate endpoint actually responds and carries the expected fields, then calibrate against a few parcels whose jurisdiction is already known. Don't assume an endpoint/schema exists вАФ verify it.
> **Relationship to B13 / B36 (county-resolution theme) вАФ not a duplicate, but adjacent.** B13-pt1 and B36(a)/(d) have been *waiting on a county-boundary polygon dataset* to replace the coarse per-county **bbox** pre-filter (true point-in-county CAD routing + straddle merge). B93 introduces exactly that data path вАФ county boundary polygons loaded via the new source registry + point-in-polygon. So B93's county layer **is** the dataset those items need: land it and B13-pt1 / B36(a)/(d) can be closed or folded in. They're still distinct items (B13/B36 = *internal CAD-routing*; B93 = a *user-facing* city/ETJ/county identify) вАФ build them aware of each other so the boundary data loads once, not twice.
> **Endpoint verification needs network egress (2026-06-15, filing session):** the build-before-wiring step above is blocked from a default web session вАФ outbound to the GIS hosts (`server.arcgisonline.com`, `services.arcgis.com`, `gis.h-gac.com`, TxGIO/TxDOT) returns `403 host_not_allowed` from the environment egress proxy. Recipe: in the environment editor set **Network access вЖТ Custom** (keep "Also include default list of common package managers" checked so npm/GitHub still work) and add, one per line: `*.arcgis.com` (TxDOT + city AGOL services), `*.arcgisonline.com`, `gis.h-gac.com` (H-GAC), `*.geographic.texas.gov` (TxGIO), plus `www.gis.hctx.net` + `gis.fbcad.org` (HCAD/FBCAD, for calibrating against known-jurisdiction parcels). **The proxy is fixed when a session starts**, so the change applies to a NEW session вАФ not the one that saved it. Verify the hosts respond, then do the verify/calibrate pass before wiring.
> **Progress 2026-06-15 (branch `claude/festive-davinci-0oco2n`): egress unblocked вЖТ endpoints verified + calibrated вЖТ connector built, tested, wired.** The allowlist recipe above took effect in a FRESH session (the proxy picks up the policy at session start, not mid-session): all GIS hosts now reachable вАФ `server.arcgisonline.com` / `services.arcgis.com` (AGOL) / `feature.geographic.texas.gov` (TxGIO) / `www.gis.hctx.net` all 200; H-GAC + FBCAD are *allowed* but upstream-503 right now (not a proxy block). **Verified + calibrated against known ground:** city limits = TxGIO `City_Boundaries/Texas_City_Boundaries/MapServer/0` field `city_name` (downtown Houston вЖТ "Houston"); county = TxDOT `Texas_County_Boundaries/FeatureServer/0` field `CNTY_NM` (same point вЖТ "Harris" / FIPS 48201). **ETJ has no statewide layer** вАФ only per-city / regional publishers (H-GAC for the metro); kept as a registry row that honestly reads "source not wired" rather than faked. **Built `src/workspaces/site-planner/lib/jurisdiction.js`:** ONE generic, registry-driven ArcGIS-REST connector on the B96 SWR cache вАФ `JURISDICTION_SOURCES` rows (url/layer/field-map/query-kind), `normalizeFeature` (each source's schema вЖТ one internal shape), and `identifyJurisdiction(lng,lat,{ring})` which tests the WHOLE parcel via a polygon-intersect so a boundary **straddle** lists every city/county touched (point fallback when no ring); honest per-source status + visible data-age; screening-only. **Wired** into the planner's Identify panel as an explicit-request "вЪЦпЄО Jurisdiction & road authority" button (never auto-loaded, per spec). **23 unit tests** (`test/jurisdiction.test.js`, injected fetch + cache); `lint` (0 errors) / `test` (68 pass) / `build` green; lazy chunks still split. **Remaining (kept `[ ]`):** wire a real ETJ source (H-GAC when its server recovers, or per-city COHGIS rows); **live browser confirmation** (CORS from the app origin + on-map render вАФ same handoff as B96); and the **B13/B36 fold-in** (this county layer IS the boundary dataset those items were waiting on вАФ close/merge in a follow-up so the data loads once).
> **ETJ leg wired 2026-06-15 (same branch):** B93's third leg is no longer a gap вАФ wired to the City of Houston's own COHGIS ETJ (`COH_ETJ_view/FeatureServer/1`, reflects SB2038 releases), verified + calibrated (Aldine / Spring, unincorporated near Houston вЖТ in the ETJ ring; downtown / in-city вЖТ not). Houston-only by design (the priority metro); other cities' ETJ are additive registry rows. `normalizeFeature` gained a `nameConst` fallback so a single-jurisdiction layer with no city-name column still resolves ("Houston"). So **all three legs (city + ETJ + county) are now wired against verified sources**; what remains is live browser confirmation + the B13/B36 fold-in.
> **Amendment 2026-06-17 вАФ disposition: DEFERRED вЖТ SHIP as a released, user-facing feature** (status/disposition change folded into B93 per the arriving note; **no new B#**). Promote B93 from "deferred until the GIS-caching foundation is solid" to a production capability on planyr.io: ship the **full** item вАФ the boundary layer(s) + click/explicit-request identify вАФ as a real **user-facing** tool, not dev-only/experimental. (The connector, all three legs, and the tests already exist вАФ see the progress notes above; what's promoted is the *intent to ship*, gated only on the points below.)
> - **Build order unchanged:** **GIS layer caching (B96, stale-while-revalidate) stays the immediate predecessor.** Ship caching + jurisdiction identify **together as one unit** rather than leaving jurisdiction open-ended. *Owner option:* if Michael confirms standalone-first, drop the cache dependency, ship against live endpoints now, and retrofit the cache later.
> - **Screening-only contract carries into the shipped feature** (already specified above under "Screening-only framing" вАФ restated as a ship requirement, not a new ask): a per-layer **data-age stamp** + a visible **"verify with the jurisdiction"** disclaimer are always shown; **never** present ETJ or city limits as authoritative.

The honest-fallback-disclosure sharpening (show which source answered) is also carried forward under those.
> вЬЕ **ETJ is no longer Houston-only (2026-06-17).** Owner pushed back that the feature isn't finished while ETJ is Houston-only вАФ fixed. Confirmed there is **no statewide ETJ layer** (TxGIO has city limits + county, not ETJ), then swapped the ETJ source from the City-of-Houston-only layer to **H-GAC's regional ETJ layer** (`HGAC_City_ETJ_Boundaries` on AGOL `services.arcgis.com/su8ic9KbA7PYVxPS`, CORS-clean), which carries **every city's ETJ across the 13-county Houston-Galveston metro** (Houston, Sugar Land, Missouri City, Pearland, Richmond, Katy, Baytown, Conroe, Texas City, вА¶). County / City / Road were already statewide (TxDOT / TxGIO), so the whole identify is now metro-wide. lint 0 errors ¬Ј **206 tests** (33 jurisdiction; 2 new: title-case + non-Houston ETJ) ¬Ј build green. **Remaining ETJ follow-up (smaller, separate):** cross-REGION coverage outside H-GAC вАФ e.g. Dallas via **NCTCOG**'s ETJ layer вАФ is another additive registry row when a deal needs it (would benefit from a tiny multi-source-per-role tweak); the **B13/B36 fold-in** is still the other open thread.

Done, with **region routing** so it can't: ETJ is now a bbox-scoped **list** (`ETJ_SOURCES` + `etjSourcesForPoint(lat,lng)` in `jurisdiction.js`), and a click only queries the metro whose box it falls in вАФ a **Houston click still fires exactly one ETJ query (H-GAC), unchanged**; Austin/DFW servers are never touched from Houston. Investigated the data honestly: there's **no statewide ETJ** and, unlike Houston (H-GAC's clean regional layer), Austin/DFW publish ETJ **city-by-city** and some authoritative servers aren't CORS-open (Fort Worth's own `mapit.fortworthtexas.gov` is CORS-blocked; NCTCOG has regional city-limits but **no** regional ETJ + no CORS).
