### B129 вАФ [HAND-OFF] GIS overlays: NWI wetlands CORS + the cached-vector experiment вАФ needs a real browser to finish `[Site Planner / GIS]` (bug/task)
`[x]` **The probe-resilience fix below LANDED via PR #60 (2026-06-16); this item now tracks the REMAINING browser-only work** (confirming FEMA renders, the NWI CORS question, and the reverted vector experiment). **Written for a future session that HAS a browser.** This session had none (CI container), and the GIS hosts are egress-blocked from it (`curl вА¶?f=json` вЖТ HTTP 403 "Host not in allowlist: hazards.fema.gov / fwspublicservices.wim.usgs.gov"). So map *rendering* could only be judged from the owner's screenshots вАФ which repeatedly misled me into saying "it works" when it didn't. **Do not trust a layer's green "loaded" status as proof of rendering: it is set the instant the layer is attached, BEFORE the image loads.** Only a human/browser confirms a visible overlay.

**Symptom (owner-reported on planyr.io + the PR #60 preview):** toggling **Wetlands (NWI)** throws a layer error. First `network / CORS error` (the health *probe*), then after a fix `Could not parse response as JSON вА¶ CORS` (esri-leaflet's internal *metadata* fetch). **FEMA flood zones** seemed to load (green status; faint hatching in one screenshot) but its *visible* rendering was never actually confirmed вАФ the owner's pushback ("what makes you think it's working?") is the honest state.

**Root-cause analysis (UNVERIFIED in a browser вАФ confirm before acting):**
- NWI host `fwspublicservices.wim.usgs.gov` appears to refuse cross-origin browser requests (CORS): both the `?f=json` health probe AND esri-leaflet's metadata/service-info fetch fail. Its `f=image` export *should* still paint via a CORS-exempt `<img>`, but esri's metadata `requesterror` fires regardless. FEMA host `hazards.fema.gov` appears CORS-clean.
- The (now-deleted) `kind:"vector"` overlay never rendered. Strong suspicion: an esri raster/image layer must be added **directly to the map**, not nested inside an `L.layerGroup`. Reverted rather than debugged blind.

**What PR #60 MERGED (the safe, shippable part of branch `claude/nice-dirac-029jok`). Net diff vs `main` = just `layers.js`:**
1. `probeService` returns `unreachable:true` on a CORS/network throw; `syncOverlayLayers` then adds the image layer anyway вАФ a CORS-blocked *probe* no longer kills a layer.
2. A layer `requesterror` no longer drops the layer or fires the red toast вАФ just a quiet per-layer "failed" status; `'load'` flips it back to "loaded".
FEMA/NWI are on the proven `dynamicMapLayer` (`f=image`) path. `lib/vectorLayers.js` (pure fetch/paging/style/decide engine, 31 tests, from #58) is on `main` but **UNWIRED groundwork**. (The branch's MapFinder/SitePlanner edits were dropped at merge вАФ they pre-dated and would have undone main's B105/tab work; only the `layers.js` fix landed.) `lint` 0 / `test` 138 / `build` green.

**Questions a browser settles in minutes (DevTools вЖТ Network / Console):**
1. Does **FEMA** draw a *visible* flood overlay on the preview? (Confirm/deny вАФ ignore the "loaded" status.)
2. Does the **NWI** `export?f=image` request fire, return 200, and produce an `<img>` *despite* the metadata `requesterror`? Or does esri block the export?
3. NWI response headers вАФ is `Access-Control-Allow-Origin` present on `/MapServer`, `/export`, `/0/query`? Is the block total or endpoint-specific? Did it change recently (the DONE list says wetlands once worked)?

**Next steps (after browser triage):**
- **FEMA:** confirm it draws a *visible* overlay (the merged probe-resilience fix should keep it alive even if its probe is blocked).
- **NWI:** (a) swap to a CORS-clean wetlands endpoint (browser-test alternates вАФ a USFWS ArcGIS Online hosted layer, a tiled service, etc.; edit `STATEWIDE.wetlands.url` in `lib/layers.js`); or (b) route via the `/server` proxy (the documented durable fix for flaky agency hosts вАФ serves through our own origin, no CORS); or (c) leave it (screening-only).
- **Vector engine (`lib/vectorLayers.js`):** if revived, render via **direct map-add** and browser-test. Remember these overlays are used at area-scale, where the server-rendered image is the right tool; vectors only pay off zoomed in tight. The deleted `vectorOverlay.js` is recoverable from git (branch commits `49e2a1b` / `2f89c19`).

**Key files:** `lib/layers.js` (`STATEWIDE`, `syncOverlayLayers` dispatch, `probeService` `unreachable`, softened `requesterror`), `lib/vectorLayers.js` + `test/vectorLayers.test.js` (unwired engine), `VERIFICATION.md` V20 (the live-test item for the merged fix).

> **вЬЕ DONE 2026-06-17 вАФ verified in a REAL headless browser (Chromium/Playwright, live on planyr.io), branch `claude/gallant-wright-c3sjwd`.** Prior sessions had no browser and guessed; this one settled the open questions with evidence.
> - **FEMA flood zones вАФ CONFIRMED RENDERING.** `/export?f=image` вЖТ **HTTP 200 `image/png`**, `<img>` paints (sampled **25.9%** non-transparent at zoom 15: teal `(0,224,224)` Zone AE, orange `(224,128,0)` floodway, red `(224,0,0)` boundaries вАФ standard NFHL symbology tracing Buffalo/White Oak Bayou through downtown Houston). **CORS-clean:** `Access-Control-Allow-Origin: https://planyr.io` on the metadata GET, `/export`, AND the OPTIONS preflight. **Scale caveat (the source of prior "is it even working?" confusion):** NFHL sublayers 27/28 are gated AT THE SOURCE to `minScale ~1:36,112`, so they draw nothing at city-wide zoom (вЙ§~z13) and only appear at ~zoom 14+. Blank-when-zoomed-out is expected, not a bug вАФ added a user-facing layer note + a code comment so it isn't re-misdiagnosed.
> - **NWI wetlands вАФ root cause is NOT CORS (the original hypothesis was wrong); the USFWS service is DOWN (HTTP 500).** The configured host `fwspublicservices.wim.usgs.gov/wetlandsmapservice/вА¶` returns **HTTP 500 across its ENTIRE catalog** (metadata, `/export`, `/query`, REST root, `/info`), confirmed three independent ways: sandbox `curl` (3/3 persistent), planyr.io in a real browser (layer errors, no `<img>`, zero successful responses), and an out-of-band fetch on a different network (also 500). Genuine **agency-side outage**, hitting production users too. esri-leaflet's "could not parse JSON / CORS" text is a misleading catch-all.
> - **The configured URL is canonical & correct вАФ confirmed NOT to swap it.** The official USFWS "National Wetlands Inventory" ArcGIS web map (arcgis.com item `da9a3343вА¶`) uses this EXACT MapServer. The only alternates are `www.fws.gov/wetlands/вА¶` (older mirror, egress-blocked from the test sandbox so not in-browser-verifiable) and non-authoritative state re-hosts вАФ swapping to either would repeat the blind guess this item exists to stop. **Decision: option (c) вАФ keep the canonical URL** (it returns when USFWS restores the service) and make the failure honest.
> - **Shipped (this branch):** `lib/layers.js` вАФ the `requesterror` status now reads a plain *"the map service is not responding вАФ it may be temporarily unavailable (screening only)"* instead of esri's misleading CORS text (the `'load'` handler still flips it back to "loaded" if the image lands, so a healthy-but-CORS-blocked layer is unaffected); documenting comments on FEMA's source-side scale-gating and the NWI canonical-but-outaged endpoint; and the user-facing FEMA "zoom in to see flood zones" note. **lint 0 errors ¬Ј 175 tests ¬Ј build green.**
> - **Browser now persists for future sessions** (STEP 3): Playwright Chromium is installed to `/opt/pw-browsers`, a repo SessionStart hook (`.claude/hooks/ensure-browser.sh`) re-ensures it on every web session, and egress to the GIS hosts + `cdn.playwright.dev` is open. Evidence screenshots committed under `gis-verify/`.
> - **вЦґ FOLLOW-UP вАФ owner found a LIVE sibling host (2026-06-17):** the official USFWS Wetlands Mapper renders fine from `fwsprimary.wim.usgs.gov` (sibling of our down `fwspublicservices`). So the data is live вАФ only our specific host is erroring, and the fix is likely a one-line URL swap. Handed off as **B130** (pending an egress allowlist + in-browser verification). `lib/vectorLayers.js` stays unwired groundwork (unchanged).

### B105 вАФ Remove the "Drag to move the map" hint card `[Site Planner / map]` (task)

live view. (If a specific popover is still observed on the live site, reopen with a repro вАФ couldn't find
one in the code.) Original spec:
inside parcels constantly, so it fires far too often and gets in the way; the on-parcel overlay is also
busy/unclear (line + vertex handles + length labels all at once). **Expected:**
- When a **draw/measure tool is active**, clicks go to the **tool** and do **NOT** open the popup.

  **double-click**, or a small **"i" button** вАФ and shows in a **side or pinned panel** rather than a

  behind an **expand**.

### B139 вАФ Detention pond "Expand this pond" mode (replaces B132's "Lock as existing pond") `[Site Planner]` (feature)  *(arrived as "NEW-1", filed B133вЖТB137 in chat; renumbered B139 вАФ B137 collided via a concurrent merge with the already-done "Fort Bend parcels" bug, which keeps B137; this is the next free ID. Companion labels item is B140.)*
`[x]` Done 2026-06-17 (branch `claude/practical-noether-ln1f46`). Reframed pond enlargement around the goal and fixed the two confusions the owner hit (a second "Lock" button + no visible way to expand). Reuses B132's volume math + ghost вАФ no schema change.
- **Entry point:** replaced the buried "Lock as existing pond" with a primary, accent **"Expand this pond"** button directly under the Stored-volume readout, above the caveat. Clicking auto-snapshots the current pond as baseline (geometry + depth/freeboard/slope) and draws the dashed ghost вАФ baseline capture is now an automatic side effect, never its own button.
- **Explicit expand controls (steppers primary, drag secondary, one readout):** "Push banks out (ft)" applies a uniform OUTWARD offset of the footprint from the baseline вАФ new `expandPolygon()` (outward sibling of the inward-only `offsetPolygon`, with a self-intersection fallback вЖТ "drag instead") for irregular ponds, and `w/h += 2N` about the baseline centre for rectangles; "Dig deeper (ft)" raises Total depth (derived = depth вИТ baseline). Free drag still works and feeds the same ExistingвЖТProposed delta. "Reset to existing" reverts geometry + depth to baseline; "Done" exits keeping the new size (feeds downstream coverage/detention) and clears the ghost.
- **Naming-collision fixes:** the only "Lock" left is the generic element pin, relabeled **"рЯУМ Pin"/"рЯУМ Unpin"** (panel + right-click menu) вАФ no "lock" verb near the expansion entry; footprint plan dimension **"Depth" вЖТ "Length"** for ponds (so dimensions read Width / Length; "Total depth" is now the only "depth", and it's vertical).
- **Guards (amber, non-blocking):** warns when the expanded footprint overlaps a building/parking/trailer (`ringsOverlap`) or extends past the property line (new `pointInRing` vs. parcels); the over-taper case reuses **B60** (bottom area 0) and now surfaces "Side slopes meet before full depth". Steppers work even when the pond is pinned. Honest one-liner "Screening estimate вАФ confirm with your engineer" under the gain.
- **Verified (self, headless browser, 2026-06-17):** Expand button shown / old button gone / "Length" label / Pin relabel; enter mode вЖТ steppers + Existing/Proposed/gain 0; push banks out 40вА≤ вЖТ uniform grow + ghost even on all four sides, **+18.33 ac-ft**; dig deeper +6вА≤ вЖТ **85.17 ac-ft**; Reset вЖТ 0; Done вЖТ keeps size; Pin toggles; **zero console errors.** lint 0 errors ¬Ј **202 tests** ¬Ј build green ¬Ј `SitePlannerApp` lazy chunk intact. Browser pass recorded as **VERIFICATION V30** (supersedes V25).
- **One deviation from the brief:** Pin/Delete kept as the existing buttons (relabeled), not relocated into the Section header вАФ that's a shared all-element-types layout change, deferred as not worth the regression risk for this pond feature.
> Replaces **B132**'s entry point (B132 stays Done as the original). Companion **B140** (on-map pond area labels) stays Open. The "Length" rename + Pin relabel touch the shared element panel вАФ coordinated with **B121**.

### B100 вАФ Active / Inactive parcels driving calculations `[Site Planner]` (feature)
`[x]` Done 2026-06-16 (branch `claude/blissful-babbage-liboyn`). Per-parcel `active` flag (default
**active**; missing = active, so existing sites are unchanged until a parcel is toggled off). New
`activeParcelsOf` selector + a unit test. `siteSqft` now sums **active parcels only**, so every
downstream metric (coverage, FAR, impervious, detention %, open space) follows automatically. Added an
**вЬУ Active / вЧѓ Inactive** toggle in the Parcel panel (beside Lock) + `toggleParcelActive`; inactive
parcels render **dimmed + dashed** on the canvas (visible for context, clearly excluded) and show
"¬Ј inactive" in the saved-parcel list; the Yield panel notes "Excludes N inactive parcel(s)." No
`SITE_MODEL_VERSION` bump вАФ `active` is a per-parcel field (defaulted at read, like `locked`/`fill`),
so no migration is needed. **Scope note:** the *map's* site-acreage label (MapFinder) intentionally still
shows the full footprint (all parcels) вАФ B100 targets the planner's yield/coverage/detention math.
Original spec:
- Add a per-parcel **Active/Inactive** toggle.
- **All area-based calculations вАФ yield, coverage, detention, and similar вАФ count ONLY active parcels.**
- Inactive parcels stay **visible for context** but render **dimmed or with diagonal-line shading** so
  it's obvious they're excluded.
- **New parcels default to Active.**
- Expose the toggle in the **parcel info panel (B98)**, and ideally **inline** on the parcel itself.
> Cross-ref: independent of lock (**B99**). The "active only" rule must thread through the
> yield/coverage/detention math (the `siteSqft` / `developableArea` inputs) вАФ additive Site Model field
> вЖТ bump `SITE_MODEL_VERSION`, extend `migrate`, expose via a selector; the self-intersection/area
> guards from **B81/B86** feed the same totals, so keep them in step.
